Akli Ǧutamazirt Hǧcine. M Hǧcine. M
Am yal aseggas, igduden imaziɣen ttebdaden i usfugel n umenzu n useggas Amaziɣ. Yal tamnaḍt d acu n wansay s wamek i d- yettili usfugel-agi. Annect-a yemgared si tama ɣer tayeḍ. Lɣerẓa n unamek n usfugel n yennayer teqqen ɣer tedyant n umezruy yeḍran 2963 n yiseggasen aya. Agdud amaziɣ yettaga azal i wass n 13 janḍier acku azemz-agi yerra lwelha ɣer taggara n ṭrad i d-yellan gar tiserdest n yimaziɣen d tin n yiferɛunen n Maṣer anda agellid Cicnaq yekcem akal n taxlijt n Nil akken ad yessali tigelda tis XXII tmanaɣt-is tella d Bǧubastis. Ihi, Yennayer yeqqen ɣer tikkelt tamezwarut deg ugdud Amaziɣ yettwensex deg umezruy imi ula deg «la Bible" tettunebder tedyant—agi.
Maca, asteqsi-nneɣ , ur icud ara ɣer sseba yeǧǧan imaziɣen ad ssalin tafada-nsen 950 n yiseggasen uqbel talalit n Ɛisa. Annect-a iban unamek- ines, amezruy yewwi-d fell-as. Tuttra i nebɣa ad nger ɣer unnar n tidmi d tayeḍ: acimi asfugel n yennayer, sani i tejbed lɣerẓa –ines?
Igduden n ddunit meṛṛa bnan timadit-nsen ɣer wamud n yiferdisen: akal, tutlayt, ddin, amezruy. Maca akken ad ilal ugdud,yernu ad yebnu aɣlan –ines izeggir i lsas n lebni n taɣerma ɣef wacu ara isenned wayen umi neqqar «tanfust timsuddest"  le mythe fǧndateur.
Ulac agdud neɣ talɣant ibedden yerna tquzem akud s txidas-is, ur ntekka ɣef «tanfust tameslalit" yellan d azamul yeṭṭfen ajgu n tilin ines. Tinfusin- agi zemrent ad ilint d tidyanin yeḍran akka s tidet deg umezruy neɣ d tid i d -tesnulfa tidmi n tmeti n yal agdud. Anamek n wawal iban: am wakken yal agdud yeḥwaj irebbiten, ddin, akal, tutlayt akken ad yili, yeḥwaj diɣ izamulen ara yesfugel akken «Nek" n tmeti yellan d aqnaḍri n yixef n ugdud ad yezgu deg umḍiq-is. Ulac aḍu ara t-yessenquqlen.
Deg wakka, ad naf belli  ma newwi-t d amedya tamdint n Rǧme is- ilasen d Remus akked Rǧmulus akniwen i d- trebba tuccent. Tamurt n Suisse tesbedd lɛezza-s ɣef yiwen waṣaḍ  hẓrǧs Guillaume Tell yeddren di temnaḍt n Uri di lqarn wis XIV. Si tama nniḍen,mi ara neddem tamurt n Franṣa ad naf dakken timadit-nsen tebna ɣef yiwet n tenfust i d- yeqqaren d akken nutni d les Gaulǧis  awal yuzzel deg yilsawen n ugdud- agi, imi yezga yettuɣal-d ɣer-sen u qqaren lejdud-nneɣ les Gaulǧis. Ɣer tama n tenfust-agi, rnan asfugel n yiwen wasaḍ i ḥesben d ameɣras amezwaru yeɣlin ɣef wakal n Fransa, wagi d Vercingẓtǧrix.
Ihi am wakken i aɣ- id- yettban, yal agdud yeḥwaj izamulen ara yezdin taswin n uɣref ɣer yiwen n yiḍelli, ɣer yiwen n wass-a, ɣer yiwen n uzekka. Azday-agi yettili-d  d leḥtum akken ccetla ad temyeɛqel, akken ad tger isufar s wacu ara tegmu wa ad tennerni s usfugel n wasaḍen, n tedyanin n umezruy, d ṭrad yekcem ugdud-nni yerna irebbeḥ-it. Asfugel- agi anamek ines d asbucceɛ n yixef n tmeti  amer ḥurent wussan akked tyita n umezruy akken «nekk" n yiɣermaniyen yeččuren aɣref-nni ad yili d win yezdin d win yekkren. S usfugel n yizamulen-agi i teksent tfiriwin ɣef yixef akked «nekk" n yal aɣref di ddunit.
Akken izamulen-agi  neɣ tinfusin- agi yesseftayen ljedra n tjaddit n yal aɣref, timura –agi, nnig n usfugel i asen- ttgen yigduden di lawan  imuliyen n yal asaḍ neɣ tadyant rennun-asen di ccan, deg wazal s ttawil n tira, amezgun, sinima, ccnawi…
Deg wakka, ad naf dakken mačči d yiwen n udlis neɣ yiwen n usaru neɣ yiwet n tceqquft i yettwasudsen akken ad tuɣal tisemɣert n yizamulen-agi  ɣef tebna timadit-nsen d tin ur yettḥaz uɣebber n tatut. Lebni n timadit yessutur diɣen aktayen. Aleqqem n waktay yezga d lḥir ɣer tɣermiwin-agi akken tuccar n zzman d awezɣi ad nnalent lsas ɣef wacu sendent akken ad ilint yerna ad dumment.
Si tama nniḍen, asfugel ur yeqqim ara d agujil icud kan ɣer tidet n umezruy, imi ɣer yigduden- agi  yesbedden tiɣermiwin inumren lawan ula d aṣaden i d- tesnulfa tsugent-nsen gan-as ccan. Anwa deg-neɣ ur nessin Rǧbin des bǧis, Iḍanhǧẓ Lancelǧt, Buffalǧ Bil, Gẓrẓnẓmǧ, Sindibad, Sttatracus, Ulyss, Achile….?
Annect-a yakk, yessenɛet azal yekseb uzamul di lebni n tjaddit. Igduden yettun asaḍen-nsen yellan s tidet neɣ wid i d -tesnulfa tenfust ɣebbun, kečmen deg uzabuq n nger.
Am yal agdud di ddunit, Leqbayel  imaziɣen ula d nitni sɛan izamulen-nsen, iten- yerran ttemyeɛqalen gar-asen belli ttikin ɣer yiwet n ccetla, iten- yerran ggaren tamawt d akken yezdi-ten umezruy, yezdi-ten umha, yezdi-ten yimal. Cicnaq, Gaya, Massnsen, Yugurten, Syfax, Takafarinas, Dihya,Kuseila, Faḍma N Sumer, Si Muḥend U Mḥend, Krim Belqasem, Ccix Muḥend u Lhusin, Lalla Xlija Tukrift, Mqidec bu lehmum, Lunja, Anẓar, aɛeqqa yasawalen,Ḥmed Umeri….. d aṣaden yensex uktay akked umezruy ɣef tewriqin-nsen i lebda. D nitni i d lɛezz s wacu yezdi ssenjeq n nnekwa-nneɣ . Asfugel-nsen d netta ara yerren timadit-nneɣ ad tewwet s ugerz akken ad tezdi lqedd, ad nwali iṭij-nneɣ yuɣ di tignawt n tmura akked leǧnas.
Yennayer umu nettara asfugel si leqdim n zzman, yekcem di lɣerẓa-agi: d yiwen n lsas yettekkin di tenfusin i d- yexleq ugdud-nneɣ akken am netta am wiyaḍ ad yaɣ amur –is di talsa.
Ait Slimane Hamid
Zik illa yiwen ugellid, d bab n lḥikma ikseb tamusni, isεa yiwen mmi-s ittuṛebba s lεezz, armi ibweḍ d ilemẓi.
Yiwet n tikkelt inna-as: -A mmi tura aql-ik d argaz ilaq ad txedmeḍ.
Mmi-s: -A baba acu ara xedmeγ?
Baba-s: -A mmi ayen ara k-d-yawin asurdi.
Mmi-s: -A baba acu akka ara d-teqqareḍ?
Mmi-s n ugellid ad ixdem γer medden, aεni xussen-aγ yidrimen?
Baba-s: -Ala a mmi lxudma d tacrift ttif frank n tidi-k wala amelyun n wiyaḍ, tegra-d γer medden, ulac wi illan γer yiman-is, ula d nekk d agellid γer medden, lemmer ulac-iten ur ttiliγ ara d agellid.
Tenṭeq-d yemma-s: -Ay argaz ur qbileγ mmi a t-sxedmen medden, ma tebγiḍ ad ixdem, ad ixdem γur-k icbeḥ.
Baba-s: -Susem a tameṭṭut wagi d ccγel-iw, mi ijeṛṛeb lxudma γer medden imir ad ixdem γur-i, qqaren yimusnawen: " tannumi d ṭṭbiεa tis snat «. Bγiγ mmi ad yaγ tannuni d lxudma.
Asmi iṭṭef ugellid di ṛṛay-is, iqbel uqcic ad ixdem, iruḥ tefka-as-d yemma-s asurdi, mi id-tewweḍ tmeddit, ikcem-d baba-s: -A mmi txedmed?
Mmi-s: -Xedmeγ a baba. "
Baba-s: -Acḥal id-tewwid?
Mmi-s: -Wwiγ-d asurdi.
Baba-s: -Zzi-d ziγ ad waliγ asurdi-agi.
Ifka-as uqcic, baba-s mi iṭṭef asurdi-nni inna-as: -Awah! Asurdi-agi a t-ḍeggreγ ar lebḥer si ṭṭaq-agi.
Iḍegger-it, aqcic ittmuqqul, azekka-nni kifkif, yiwet n tikkelt, ikker-d uqcic iruḥ γer uḥddad inna-as: -Bγiγ ad xedmeγ γur-k.
Aḥeddad ifhem tamsalt inna-as: -Iẓra baba-k?
Aqcic: -D netta i ibγan ad xedmeγ.
Aḥeddad: -Ṛwaḥ ad txedmeḍ.
Ibda uqcic axeddim s laεtab d tidi, almi d tameddit, iwwi-d asurdi n tidi-s, ikcem γer baba-s: -A baba aql-i xedmeγ atan frank.
Iṭṭef baba-s frank-nni, iruḥ ad illi ṭṭaq akken a t-id-ideger γer lebḥer aqcic ibda ittru iqqar-as: -Ttxil-k a baba ur ṭeggir ara laεtab-iw, si ṣṣbeḥ nekk ttqabaleγ times d wuzzal fell-as.
Yuγal baba-s ifhem belli s tidett mmi-s ixdem, inna-as: -A mmi acuγer frank n yiḍelli d win n seldiḍelli, ur tecliεeḍ ara mi ten-ḍeggreγ?
Aqcic isusem ifhem tamsalt akken ilaq.
Inna-as baba-s: -Tura a mmi teẓriḍ acu swan yiṣurdiyen, zemreγ a k-sxedmeγ γur-i, ttekleγ ur txelluḍ ara baba-k. Yahia Yanes
Tamacahutt s wazal-is, qqaren: « Ma fkiγ-ak kilu n sserdin seččeγ-ak yiwen wass, ma slemdeγ-ak amek ara tseggdeḍ, seččayeγ-k yal ass ".
Asfuggel n wass amezwaru n yennayer n yimaziγen yettili-d am yal tikkelt deg tesdawit n Lmulud At Mεemmer, s-γur "agezdu n tutlayt d yidles amaziγ”. Asfuggel-agi yella-d s wussan idelsanen seg 7 armi d 10 deg waggur –agi.
Ahil yebda s wawal n yiεeggalen n le cǧmitẓ n yinelmaden, syin tebda temsikent n yidlisen n yal taγult i yeddan deg teγzi n wussan-agi. Rnu γur-s lbiε s ubuddu s-γur Muhand ARKAT i ungal-is "abrid n tala”.
Ahil ikemmel s usarag i d-yewwi Mass Abedennur Abdeslam s uzwel " tazγent tamaziγt 1949 «. Ass wis sin yella-d uskan n usaru « ur kkat a gma inetteḍ " i d-yesuffeγ. Ma d ass wis tlata, tella-d tceqquft n umezgun « yenna-yi jeddi " i d-turaren tarbaεt « Macahu ". Ass aneggaru tella-d temsizwert n seksu gar tnelmadin n ugezdu, dγa d tid n useggas wis tlata i d-yufraren.
Akka, ihi, s ufraq n warrazen I d-wwḍen wussan idelsanen γer taggara nsen. D.said lhadj
Di taggara tanemmirt tameqqrant i wid akk I d-iheggan leqdic-a aseggas ameggaz i yal amaziγ anda yella.
Ilmend n tmeγra n yennayer, aseggas amaynut n yimaziγen 2963, aṭas n tmeγriwin i d-ittewhegan γef demma di deqs n temnaḍin n tmazγa.
Dγa tidukla tadelsant Alma n taddert n Yigersafen n tγiwant n At-yeğğar tsudes-d yiwen n leqdic s wazal-is s yiwen n wahil d amarkati, ideg llant temzikniyin yegaraden n tqendyar leqbayel, ṭṭebqat n wučči i tt-gen imaziγen-nneγ γef demma n yennayer, tiγawsiwin tiqburin, idlisen d ttsawaṛ d waṭas niḍen.
Akken daγen i d-yella yiwen usarag s usentel " Yennayer ", i d-wwin ssin imusnawen isdawiyen, wigi d mass Zindin Kacimi akk d mass Mǧqran Taguemǧunt, syen tella-d lweεda meqran « imekli n yennayer ".
Syen jarden deg ahil-nsen yiwet n tmeγra n zwağğ aqbur γef iεudiwen, anda imezdaγ n taddert-agi igersafen ad-ddun merra d iqeffafen akk d tarbaεt n yiḍebbalen γer wemḍiq iwmi qqaren Alma, anda ara d-sudsen tameγra γef demma n yennayer. Islam Bessaci
Γer tagara ad yilli usenεet n waddal n yimenγi n waḥric n Karatẓ syen ad-ffken arazen d igardasen usebγes i warac id-yufraren di temzizla yemgaraden n wadal deg ussan-nni imuras yezrin.
Anekruf: Mačči d kečc ara d yerren ttar, anef-as ayen texdem ad taf, am ass-a ad temlil d wayen d i txeddem, ass-n ad txelles lexlas n tuccent. Tin yernan ɣur-s mačči d kečč i d juj anefray
Anekruf: Juj ur yettfiq ara i nbuc-is, ur yettaweḍ ara ad iwali tidet-is, ala nekk i tt-yesnen, ala nekk i as ifaqen, ala nekk i d yewwin s lexbar i tmenqas-is, ayen akk ara tt-id ibegnen ata ɣur-i, wamma wiyaḍ ad turar ad teffeɣ, acku d stut m lebhut
Amejjay: Wayi d axemmem ynek, d kečč i tt-yettwalin akka
Anekruf: ur d qqim ara deg xemmem, d ayen yellan
Anekruf: S liɣ-as akken iwata, d ayemi i d nniɣ akka
Amejjay: Lammer ik teḍlim ur cukkeɣ ara ad terzu ɣur-k, kečč akkiya s tmad-ik akka i d tenniḍ
Anekruf: ala k qqareɣ ulac win i as izemren, tus-ad akken kan ad tbeggen amakken acemma ur yelli, ad tesmsawi ayen i d yeqqimen, wa ad tesfeḍ ameslay deg yilesawen n wid ara as yinin "ihuh argaz-as ad yemmet, ur tezmir ara ad truḥ ad t-id wali?!” ɣaf waya i d tusa wamma mačči d nekk i tt-iɣaḍen
Amejjay: Anef-as ad tessebgen, anef ad tt-id ẓren medden
Anekruf: Tessen amek i tettkellix, mačči d tikelt tamenzut i texdem akka, ula d argaz-is amezwaru mačči akka i as tga, alammi i tegla s uqerruy-is, tessen-asen i yimeṭṭawen …akka ar texdem ula i nekk imi ara mteɣ
Amejjay: Akken tebɣu tili, ttxilek ur ….eğğ-itt, erra-yak yiwet n twaɣit
Anekruf: Tawɣit tamezwarut ɣef wudem-is, anef meqqar taneggarut-a i wudem-iw
Amejjay: Ttxilek ur semsax ara ifassen-ik, ur telliḍ ara deg qettalen, kečč d amejjay, d ragaz ifehmen yeɣran, ih akken "qqaren ad yili yiwen yelha ad tafeḍ idhem-it wayeḍ, ɣas ma yella kra i txedmeḍ, txdmet ilmend n talsa
Anekruf: yettadṣa ih! Tesmektaḍ-iyi-d ɣaf wudem n talsa, ḥnineɣ aṭas, ula d ayen i d tenniḍ yettwakkes-iyi. Tettuḍ d acu id nnan fell-i? win yenɣan mačči d aceffar a d argaz-is, d amejjay, telha tikli-s, ur tfaqeḍ ara i tkellax-nni? i win yettwanɣan ur yuklal ara, dya i d-iyi- swehmen din-a id faqeɣ bell-i tekreh argaz-is, tameṭṭut ara kerhen argaz-is ad as-d yettban d ilat lweḥc, d ayemmi i d iyi-d beggen bell-i tḥemmel-iyi, imir faqeɣ-d ur d-iyi-tḥemmel ara, uɣaleɣ d arelluc deg ufus-is d ufus n n umeεcuq-is, ih! uraren yess-i almmi i d-iyi-tessaweḍ semḥesseɣ i tasa-w wwiγ tamgerṭ.
Amejjay: Maca ttuγaḍin ik tɣaḍ! imi tumneḍ s waya, acuγer ara tuɣaleḍ d wayeḍ ttxilek qim kan akka ḥnineḍ.
Anekruf: wa d cɣel-iw Amejjay: yid-wen!?
Anekruf: sell ur k ẓriɣ ur ak d-nniɣ, ettu ayen imi tesliḍ, lammer ur k umineɣ ara, ur ak d qqareɣ ara acemma, twalaḍ! yeqqim-d kan tura ad iyi-teffɣeḍ sya ternuḍ xemsa ɣef yimi daya.
Anekruf: Ih yid-neɣ, nekk akk d nettat di sin
Amejjay: I yiman-iw anida ara terreɣ, neɣ ad ula d netta tneṭleɣ yid-wen
Anekruf: yettxemmim ahat …d azref-ik ad txemmeḍ kan ɣef yiman-ik ma d anezgum-iw ala nekk I yeyerza, mačči am nekk i yegren akken ad selkeɣ tameṭṭut di tballaɣt. aziɣen tḥemmleḍ iman-ik aṭas, azref ɣur-k d azref yekkaten ar tama-k,win ara k yesdarin, win ara k yerren d amzerfu ar yiman-ik, win ara k id begnen ar wiyaḍ, d tidet ad tεeğbeḍ i yiman-ik wa ad tεeğbeḍ i wiyaḍ, d ameggaz yiman-ik a mass! Iman-ik d azref-ik d yiman-ik….iman-ik! Maca sarameɣ ad tettuḍ iman-ik, d lwajeb-ik axxi tagnitt, wa ad terreḍ lmendad-ik ar wiyaḍ ad ak-d sutreɣ ad-iyi-teffɣeḍ sya d xemsa ɣef yimi ma yella wamek, tettuḍ ayen i ak d-nniɣ.ttxilek ddu-iyi di lebɣi, i nekk yellan d ameddakel-ik yettwarẓen, yettwasexnunsen, yettubehdlen …ur tufiḍ i as d yeqqimen azekka tafejrit ad tenγen
Taḍatt si berra
Anekruf: ad taya…
Amejjay: d acu ara xedmeɣ?
Anekruf: dureqq, teğğeḍ-iyi nekk yid-s
Amejjay: s rxifan ihi atan wanisa kkiɣ
Tawwurt telli iban-d unemhal netta d yiwen yewwi-d yid-s tiwriqin
Amejjay: iger-d nnehta mačči d nettat
Anekruf: s reffu anida-tt? anida-tt?
Anemhal: newwi-ak-d asali yugaren ayen-nni s waṭas, d asali ara y beddlen tagnitt fella-k
Anemhal: Ta d tamsalt nniḍen, yella-d umaynut wammag axnaq-ik iban-d melmi, maca ur zmireɣ ara ad ak d ferheɣ melmi, u terna d ayen ara d yilin anect tebγu tekk-it i tura d ayen?!
Anemhal: Ma yella tqebleḍ ayen ayen ara k d sutreɣ, timenɣiwt-ik ur d ttili ara
Imwekkel: yuẓa ar umeḥbus yettmuqul-it maca tamsalt-a d tuffirt
Anemhal: aya ekkes anezgum*
Imwekkel: akka meqqar ad nruḥ srid i temsalt, nebɣa ad n serreḥ i tnaεurt ar tegnawt maca yessefk ad yili win ara tawi, tettwaheyya i tiwin n wemdan akken ad t-id njerreb,tura ma yella tqebleḍ, ayen i ak ḥekkmen ad d yeɣli
Anekruf: yella kra neṭmeε akken ad zziɣ?
Anekruf: ma yella ugiɣ xusseɣ, axir n win yessaramen wala win igezmen liyas, yiwen wala ulac, neɣ ala?
Anemhal: Imi tqebleḍ, stenyi aɣ-d da
Imwekkel: irfed-d tiwriqin ihi stenyi da
Anekruf: Bɣiɣ ad ak id steqsiɣ ma ulac fell-as, icimi d nekk i d tefernem?
Imwekkel: D taseqqamutt i tt-igezmen d ṛṛay, belli win ara n seddu ad yili d yiwen ɣef iḥekkmen s lmut, wammag aṭas n wid i d sebblen iman-nnsen akken ad d ruḥen
Imwekkel: ur nezmir ara ad nweddef yiwen kan akka ma wer yelli deg-wi i d ak-d nniɣ.
Anekruf: Γas ma yella, d netta i ken-d sutren?
Imwekkel: ulac takebbanit naγ tama deg udabu ara yesseflen kra n yiwen ar tmenγiwt n yiman-is
Anekruf: Ula d nekk akka meqqar ad irtiḥeɣ, imi sertaḥeɣ taɣdemt, tura d nnuba n tseqqamtt n tussna akk d tamiwin yetḍebbiren
Imwekkel: Ula d nekkni nefreḥ imi d nufa yiwen umssnaw akka am kečč, acku mačči d cɣel n ukellex, mačči εeddi kan ad tafeḍ win ar d yeffken liqin s ttawil n usiwel war tellqa akk iy imaṭṭafen akk d tiliẓri.

Ma yeqreḥ mmi-s ad yefreḥ.
Mǧulǧud Feraǧun d amaru Azzayri s tenfalit tafransist, ilul deg 8 meɣres 1913 deg Tizi Hibel, yettwanɣa deg Lezzayer deg 15 meɣres -D anelmad n uɣerbaz amagnu n yisalmaden n Buzerriɛa yesselmed aṭas n yiseggasen s wudem n usalmad, yuɣal d anemhal n uɣerbaz, diɣ n temsirin tisemmadin send ad t-rren d amaswaḍ n yigensen n tmetti. Lmulud At Caɛban yebda yettaru deg useggas -Ungal-is amenzu, Mmi-s n yigellil, amahil i izul uzɣan, yuwi arraz ameqqran n uɣrem n Lezzayer. Amaru yettwanɣa ass n 15 meɣres 1962 deg lezzayer, ukkuẓ n wussan send aḥbas n lbarud n ttrad n Lezzayer, s tama n yiwet n terbaɛt n ǦAS Tuddsa n Tredsa tuffirt n Fransa Timenɣiwt n Chɛtɛau-Rǧyal.
Mǧulǧud Feraǧun d amaru Azzayri s tenfalit tafransist, ilul deg 8 meɣres 1913 deg Tizi Hibel, yettwanɣa deg Lezzayer deg 15 meɣres -D anelmad n uɣerbaz amagnu n yisalmaden n Buzerriɛa yesselmed aṭas n yiseggasen s wudem n usalmad, yuɣal d anemhal n uɣerbaz, diɣ n temsirin tisemmadin send ad t-rren d amaswaḍ n yigensen n tmetti. Lmulud At Caɛban yebda yettaru deg useggas -Ungal-is amenzu, Mmi-s n yigellil, amahil i izul uzɣan, yuwi arraz ameqqran n uɣrem n Lezzayer. Amaru yettwanɣa ass n 15 meɣres 1962 deg lezzayer, ukkuẓ n wussan send aḥbas n lbarud n ttrad n Lezzayer, s tama n yiwet n terbaɛt n ǦAS Tuddsa n Tredsa tuffirt n Fransa Timenɣiwt n Chɛtɛau-Rǧyal. Tabrat-inu Deg-s awal
Mǧhamed Rǧugie d amedyaz amaziɣ si tmurt n Rrif. Tamedyazt-ines d tamḥadit. Illul deg aseggas 1977 di « Temsamane " akal anda i d- yella trad n Anwal akked d win n Dhar Ubaran anda irrifiyen rẓan tiserdest tasbanyulit. Mǧhamed Rǧugie nnig tamedyazt –ines, yella d amdan n talwit yesazalen iguma n tayri deg isefra-ines. Leslaḥ s wacu yettaqazem Mǧhamed Rǧugie lehlak iḥuzen timeti, yetteceliḥen deg idles amaziɣ d imru ines akked d awalen- is. Awalen-is yeččuren d timedyazt. Mǧhamed yefka azal meqran i timsal yettrabin ixef am tayri n talwit, leḥmala n ugama, tilleli., tawaculut. Yegga azal i tawacult acku yettwali-tt d netta-t i d-lsas ɣef acu tettsenid timeti. Mǧhamed yattaru di snat n tutalayin: tarifit tamaziɣt n Rrif akked tafransist. S tumert meqran id yuzen awalen-is i yimeɣriyen n uɣmis n imaziɣen.
S wur d acemrar
I kečč ay amdakel
I kečč a tawamet
I kečč a mmis n udrar
Tettaruḍ s tmaziɣt  tarrifit akked tefransist, amek yettili ufran n tutlayt di lawan n tira? Awal-inu
Tira ur telli ara d aqaṣer. Tira d tugra n yiman ɣer ugni n umenuɣ. Di tillawt ur smenyafeɣ-ara tutlayt ɣef tayeḍ. Tarifit d tutlayt-iw tamezwarut, yis i ttemesawaleɣ akked d atmaten-iw imaziɣen. Ttaruɣ yis akken ad tidir wa tuɣal am netta-t am tutlayin nniḍen d tutlayt n taywalt cǧmmunicatiǧn. S tirifit ṣawaḍeɣ i yimeɣriyen-iw iḥulfan-iw ama d lferḥ neɣ d leḥzen, d taḍṣa neɣ d imeṭṭi. S tewzel n wawal,s trifit ttalseɣ-d i tikta iceɣben ixef-iw s umata. Tafransist d tutlayt s wacu teɛradeɣ ad cebheɣ tidmi n tmaziɣt akken ad tḥaz talsa i meṛṛa. Di tillawt ulac amgared ger tutlayin imi yal yiwen yesɛa azref akken ad yaru s tutlayt i-iḥamel.
Deg-s tanwact n tafsut Deg-s anebdu Deg-s tafukt
Nekk akked kečč
A tawmat inu
Anwi idlsen id tezrargeḍ ɣer tura u d acu i d- isentel n yal yiwen?
Deffir amud n isefra-inu « lehmali n isefra- les rafales de la ttǧẓsie " ɣer tizrigin « ǧasis des artistes ", rniɣ-d « ddew nhati- au rythme des sǧuffles " ɣer tizrigin « mǧn ttetit ẓditeur ". Anagaru i d- yefɣen d win umu semmeɣ « rwayaḥ n temdyazt- les fragrances de la ttǧẓsie ". Targit iyi -zedɣen tagara-agi d asezrireg n wamud n isefra s trifit. Ma yalla, ar tura, ur d sufeɣ ara s tmaziɣt tella sebba. Ttemjadaleɣ akked ṛṛay-iw u ttnadiɣ anwa abrid ilaqen, anwa udem ilaqen akken ad nawi amaynut i uɣanib n tira s tmaziɣt. Ttnadiɣ ɣef umaynut, acku ayen yakk i d- yettnulfun s trifit yekcem deg yiwen lqaleb, yeglugel. Nekk bɣiɣ ad rẓeɣ asalu ɣer wayen nniḍen. Ilaq ad neffeɣ deg iberden n tanumi akken ad nexleq amaynut. Deg isefra-inu s triffit, ttnadiɣ isental iceɣben talsa akked d umdan s umata: tayri,tadukli, tudert, lmut, timadit tamaziɣt, akked tameṭut. Liḥala n tmaṭut iceɣeb-iyi aṭas,acku deg timeti-neɣ tettweɛzel, yettwakes-as uzref, rran aqarif ɣef izerfan-is.Neẓra yakk belli d tmaṭut i d-tasarut n tanfalit. D netta-t id aɣerbaz amenzu i yal yiwen seg-nneɣ . D netta-t id aɣ- yeslemden tikli. Deg tamdyazt xedmeɣ rriɣ-as tisemɣert i tuklal.
Tudert d taqudbdat Ay amdakel
A tawmat siwel Axmi ɛamer-as
A tawmet inu Ur neqqim
  ɣer ij n wanḍu axmi ɛamer-as
wer neswi seg yij n wanu
Amek tella tamedyazt tarifit, anwi i d-imedyazen itt-iɛeban deg abrid n unerni ines? axmi ɛamra-as ay amdakel
Di tillawt tamedyazt tarifit tufrared akken ilaq deg isaggasen n tmanyin s demma n umedyaz Saɛid El Musawi. Isefra-ines aṭas n icenayen iten-yecnan am tarbeɛt « itran ", El Walid Mimun. Tamdyazt-is thuz ixfawen-nneɣ s imeslayen-is yeččuren d sser akked lmeɛna. Amedya asefru-ines « necrin ssa- aqleɣ-da ". Di, lǧera-s, aṭas n imedyazen i d yernan, ḍefren abrid-agi n tanfalit id yewwi Saɛid am « Mayasa Rachida " yezdin di tmedyazt-is snat n tutlayin: taqbaylit akked tarifit. Yella diɣ « Amnus Ḥarfuf ", « Lhanis ". Ass-a tamedyazt tarifit tufrar s tuget n imedyazen akked tmadyazin id as yellan d lmendad.
wer neqqim deg tiri unebdu
sad it-tecubeḍ n wartu
Amek tella liḥala n tizlit tarifit?
Mi ara d nemeslay ɣer ccna n rrif ulamek ur d nettebder ara « El Walid Mimun ". D acenay-agi i -irefden senjaq n ccna amaziɣ atrar di rrif. D netta id-as yerẓan asalu. Ur nettu ara diɣ acenay Allal, Ayawen, terbaɛt « Itran ", d waṭas nniḍen yefken lemqud i tizlit tartrart n rrif.
Mǧḥand Amɣar d tanfust, d aṣaḍ di Rrif. Yezmer ad yili usaru ara d yelsen n ugarawli –agi ameqran?
Mulay Muḥend amɣar d yiwen uzamul n tilleli, n timunent n yegduden n ddunit meṛṛa. Deg akken ccan-is meqqer ula d Che Gueḍara yezdew ɣef tikta-s tigrawliyin. Maca di tmurt-is  Rrif- Lmaruk, tamazɣa isem-is muggad. Kra n yemdanen ttkukrun ad bedren isem-is. Xas ulama akka yemmut, lexyal-is yeshab-iten. Ilaq asaru ad yewwin ɣef waṣaḍ-agi n timuzɣa akken tizumelt-ines ad ttesmendig tirget n tirugza deg ulawen n yal amaziɣ anda ma yella. Akken ibɣu nniɣ-d ɣef Mulay Muḥend, awalen-iw meẓẓiyi-t zdat n temɣert akked ccan yekseb deg ulawen n yal amaziɣ di Rrif neɣ di tamazɣa wakali.
Amek yezmer ad yilli umṣaweḍ ger imusnawen Iqbayliyen akked Irifiyen?
I tazwara ilaq ad inniɣ ulac umgared ger tarrifit aked teqbaylit. Snat n tutlayin -agi d takniwin. Ttemcabin-t aṭas.. s tanumi yal yiwen yezmer ad yezgi tutlatyin -agi. Nekk asen -inniɣ i watma iqbayliyen ḥamleɣ-ten aṭas aṭas. Idles aqbayli d idles inu am netta am tarifit. Mi ttmeslayeɣ akked leqbayel, ttafeɣ iman-iw. Awal yettezririg ger-nneɣ s shala. Ayen ala? Nekni nesɛa adrar n Dhar Ubaran kunwi tesɛam adrar n Jerjer. Idurar-nneɣ yiwen-nsen. Adar d ixef-nneɣ . Azul-iw i ccna n teqbaylit yeggan abrid i tmaziɣt akken ad tuɣal d tutlayt n taywalt akked tmusni d tusna.
tayri ɣer –nneɣ ma ur teqqim
niɣ tenɣi-ḍ-tt, yeffeɣ ixef-is s adrim?
Ait Slimane Hamid
Tessudsed texxamet n lhirfat ufus, d lehirfat tiqburin n lwilaya n Titi wezzu s lemɛawna n lwekala taɣenawt n ureṭṭal amecṭuḥ, d lewkalat niḍen yettukelfen s lemɛawna n yilmeẓyen, yiwet n temzikkent deg usalay n Tizi wezzu, anda ttikkint wazal n 50 n tlawin I d-yusan si yal tamadṭ n tmurt n leqbayel iwakken ad d-senaεtent leḥirfat yemgaraden deg-i I qedcent, ama d azeṭṭa ama d afexxar, d teqendyar n leqbayel, s ittwasnent tlawin iεeẓẓugen d iwaḍiyen d lejihat niḍen, ayen yeṭṭfen lwelha deg tmezikkent-agi, d asenulfu I yeǧǧan taqendurt n leqbayel ad sukkes amkan_is gar iselsa imaynut ɣef I yeṭṭuqet usuter di lawan n unebdu. Timzikkent-agi I d-yusan I usfuggel n wass agraɣlan n tmeṭṭut I d-yettuɣalen deg ass n 8 meɣres seg yal aseggas, tmeyyez-it tirza iṭṭuqten n tlawin ɣer usalay anda d-tella yiwet n temlilit meqqren gar- asent, d tagnit I umbeddel n tektiwin, yal yiwet deg uḥric deg I tettuxeṣe&amtt;ucirc,; ladɣa imi tameṭṭut ass-a teṛza asalu tesaweḍ ad tger iqudimen di tmetti deg I tettidir, imi ad t-id-naf tekcem ula di leḥirfat I ixeddem urgaz, ama d lfeṭṭa neɣ lḥelfa d wayen niḍen, si lejiha-s mass ɛebd lekrim Belqasem imkellef n texxamt n tejara, yenna-d d akken tilawin I iqdcen deg uḥric n lxudma n tzarbay sfaydint-d s yiwen wass n ukewwen deg sensu n Balwa, anda I d ḥefḍent udmawen imaynuten n uzeṭṭa n tzarbit, iwakken ad d-tekcem leḥirfa –agi deg usnerni n tdamsa n tmurt sya d afella, ass –agi n ukewwen ɣef leḥsab n yimḍebbren taɛna temsalt yusa-d imi yeṭuqet ucetki sɣur iḥirafiyen imi ssleɛa-nsen tettɣimi ur tettnuz ara s sseba n lexṣas n leswaq di tmurt n leqbayel, ɣef aya ilaq ad d-afen leswaq niḍen akken sselɛa n iḥirafiyen-agi ad tenz. Malika Kebaili
Yetturaǧu di taggara n waggur-agi n meɣres ad ifak ustensex n yizmamen yerzan tiferkiyin yemxallafen i tetteḥwiji twacult di teɣiwant n Tizi wezzu, aya ɣef leḥsab n yisali iɣ-id-yuwḍen seg wid ixedmen dina, id-iqqaren d akken ar tura ssawḍen yimḍebbren n tɣiwant ad d- stensexen azal n 435 alef n tferkiyin yerzan tiwaculin n tmazya n Tizi Wezzu. Asurif-agi i t-ger tɣiwant yetturaǧu seg-s ad d-yer tilas i uεeṭṭel i d-yettilin i usuffeɣ ama d tiferkiyin n leεmer neɣ t-i d –yerzan tamezduɣt d wayen niḍen, imi ineggura-agi ttidiren yiwen n uɣbel d ameqqran s sebba n uεṭṭel i d-yettilin deg usuffeɣ n wayen ibeɣan ladɣa taferkit n leεmer uṭun 12, anda d-ttafen yimzdaɣ n Tizi iman-nsen, ilaq ad reǧun azal n ddurt s lekmal-is i wakken ad d- yeffeɣ yiccer-agi n lekaɣeḍ, tikwal ɣef sebba n wanct-a yettili-d imenɣi ger ixeddamen akked yimezdaɣ ayen yettaǧǧan iɣallen n laman zgan dina iferru n tmesal icban tigi, maca sya ɣer taggara n waggur- agi ad ifakk leḥif ɣef yimdanen i d-irezzun ɣer tɣiwant n Tizi Wezzu, am akken daɣen ad tifsus taεkemt ɣef ixeddamen mi ara yekcem tawil n lanfurmatiq ɣer umḍiq-agi n uxeddim. Mǧkrane Chikhi
Amawal-a n usisleg neɣ n ddublajdǧublage s tmaziɣt, d yiwen n leqdic s wazal-is i yexdem mass Smail Abdenbi, i d-ssufɣent teẓrigin n Tfaska Taɣelnawt n Usaru Amaziɣ FCNAFA. Ameskar n umawal-a d yiwen n wudem i iqeddcen deg uḥric n tesliẓrantaudiǧḍisuel s tmaziɣt, netta daɣen d amyaru d amedyaz s tmaziɣt, ladɣa yetwassen aṭas s yimagraden-is i d-yeffɣen deg yiɣmisen d tesɣunin n tmaziɣt am: ABC Amazigh, Le Pays-Tamurt, Racines-Iẓuṛan,…Deg tezwert n udlis mass Smail Abdenbi, yura-d ɣef tixuṭṭert i yesɛa usisleg deg usnerni n yidles d tutlayt; « Taẓuri n usisleg d tawwurt yeldin s idles n yiɣerfan n umaḍal. D taɣawsa izemren, seg tama ad tenjer abrid ara yesseddun tutlayt-nneɣ deg tmetti s useqdec n yisalalen n uḍebsi DVD, tiliẓri,..atg. Seg tama-nniḍen, ad teldi allen i uɣref-nneɣ , acku imesli akked tugna d aɣerbaz ideg ara tzemreḍ ad tlemdeḍ war leɛtab ". Mass Smail Abdenbi, akken ad isemmed amawal-a i d-yessufeɣ, inuda di akk imawalen n tmaziɣt yellan ama d wid i d-yettwaẓergen neɣ wid ur nessaweḍ ara ad d-ffɣen, am umawal n tusnakt i yemmugen deg yiseggasen n 80 deg tesdawit n Tizi Wezzu s ufus n yiwet n terbaɛt n yiselmaden yellan daɣen d imeɣnasen. Nnig n wawalen yellan deg yimawalen n tmaziɣt, ameskar, yeɛreḍ yessumer-d kra n wawalen imaynuten iss yezmer win iqeddcen deg unnar n usisleg s tmaziɣt ad yessenfali tignatin d tɣawsiwin icudden ɣer taɣult-a d teywalt s umata. Amahil yecban wa, iban ad d-yeglu s lmenfiɛa i wid iqeddcen deg uḥric n ssinima n tmaziɣt, imi ad afen deg-s akk awalen i uḥwaǧen, daɣen d asnerni i tnedlist tamaziɣt, i yuḥwaǧen ugar n yimawalen uzzigen n yal taɣult n tudert.
Liḥala n tmeṭṭut tamaziɣt, uguren tettmagar di tudert-is, asirem-is deg tmazɣa wakali d tuttriwin i ɣef nebɣa ad d-nawi tiririt. Akken ad d- yili wannect-a neqseḍ Silya Tanazart akken ad aɣ-d- tefk tamuɣli-s ɣef temsalt-agi. Silya Tanazart d tamejjayt n wul, tlul di Agadir di 13 Yunyu 1988 di Lmerruk. Tura, tettidir di Marikan anda teɣra la biǧchimie di tesdawit n Richmǧnds di Verginie. Silya d tameɣnast deg umussu adelsan amaziɣ, d taɛeggalt deg tiddukla n yimaziɣen n Marikan Amazigh American Assǧciatiǧn ǧf the Grɛater Washingtǧn DC  yesɛan leqrar di washingtǧn. Gar yiswiyen n tiddukla-agi asnerni n yidles amaziɣ akked uḥareb ɣef timadit tamaziɣt n ugdud n tferka n ugafa.
Amek tella liḥala n tmeṭṭut tamaziɣt di Lmerruk?
Di leɛwayed n yimaziɣen, tameṭṭut, si zik, tesɛa leɛnaya. Tettiki deg uskasi icudden ɣer yiɣeblan tettidir tmetti s umata, awal-is yettɛeddi u yesɛa leqrar. Deg umezruy-nneɣ , d tameṭṭut i yettleqqimen ilugan n yidles-nneɣ i tarwa. Leqdic n urgaz akked win n tmeṭṭut xas yemgared, timetti –nneɣ taqburt tga-as yiwen wazal. Tesseɛdel-iten, wa ur d- yekki nnig wa. Di leqdim n zman, tameṭṭut tamaziɣt tesɛa azal meqqren, tikwal tella ɣef tgelda n kra n temnaḍin. Ass-a, tallest tamaziɣt tettwaweḍ. Tenquqel lɛezza-s. Tettwaweḍ deg yixef-is iɛebban tuntayt fẓminitẓ am wakken i tettwaweḍ di tmuzɣa- ines. Mačči kan ilaq-as ad tennaɣ ɣef yizerfan-ines d tmaṭṭut, ilaq-as diɣ ad tennaɣ ɣef timmuzɣa-ines. Ilaq-as ad tennaɣ ɣef timuzɣa ines, akken ad teqqim dima d nettat i d dduḥ amezwaru deg tettnekkar u tettnerni tmaziɣt. Ilaq-as ad tennaɣ akken ad tẓerreb ɣef uhamaj deg yixef-is i d- yewwi yidles aɛrab-ineslem ɣer tmura –nneɣ . Deg umussu adelsan amaziɣ di Lmerruk ur gtent ara tlawin iqeddcen deg uḥric-agi. Tuget n tdukliwin timaziɣin yellan di Lmerruk i tent-iɛemren d irgazen. Drus n tlawin i yellan deg unnar, ḥala tid yeččuren d tasa, d tid yumnen s yidles amaziɣ. Tullas yellan d timeɣnasin ɣef yidles amaziɣ, d tid i d-yugmen tabɣest di lliqa n timmuzɣa yettazzalen deg yixef-nsent. Sebba ɣef wacu drus i yellan n tullas deg unnar n timeɣnest yeqqen ɣer watmaten-nneɣ s timad-sen, acku atmaten-nneɣ imaziɣen mazal sɛan yir tamuɣli ɣer tilawin yettnadin tilelli n wawal akked leqdic. Deg tudrin neɣ deg temdinin tuget n tyestmatin-nneɣ ur ssinent ara izerfan-nsent. Ttkukrunt ad qazment taluft. D nutenti i d timezwura akked dderya-nsent i yettḥaz waṭṭan icudden ɣer tuẓuft. Liḥala-nsent reqiqet, acku lḥif akked lmizirya srewten deg yixfawen-nsent….lqella n leqraya, yir tamuɣli n tmeti ɣer ljiha-nsent, ur tent-iɛawen ara akken ad ilint d iferdisen s lekmal di tudert n yal ass. Tid yeɣran ttemḍarkalent ɣef yidelsan ijenṭad am taɛrabt akked tefransist. Liḥala-agi  tunḥist ɣef tmeṭṭut tefka iɣisi i timadi-nsent… yetteɛraq-asent anwa i d nekk. Di tilawt, liḥala n tmeṭṭut tamaziɣt di Lmerruk ur tessefraḥ ara.
Anti tilawin irefden asafu n timmuzɣa di tmurt n Lmerruk?
Di Lmerruk neɣ di tmazɣa irkelli, ur nessin ara anta taddart ideg d argaz i yeggaren azeṭṭa. Leqdic-agi yellan d taẓuri s tehri n wawal d ayla n tullas. D nutenti i as- yellan di lmendad, i as- yeẓḍan udem. Deg-s i srusuyent iḥulfan-nsent. Tilawin timaziɣin si zik ggarent azeṭṭa s yiwen uɣanib deg sedduyent kra di tecriḥt-nsent. Azeṭṭa d tizumelt n tmeṭṭut. Azeṭṭa ɣer-sent d yiwen wudem n taywalt i kesbent nutenti kan. Tuget n tullas –nneɣ yeggaren azeṭṭa, d tinaẓurin di teklut anda i d- ssebganent tidmi-nsent lqayen. Amedya, Najat Akazum yellan d tanaẓurt di teklut i as- yennan: « rreqm-iw d azamul n timadit-inu ". Tella diɣ Fatima Tamlalt i tewlen nezzeh deg uzeṭṭa akked teklut, xas akken ur teɣri ara. D nettat i yeldin aɣerbaz n teklult akken ad lemdent tullas taẓuri-agi id -yekkan si zman aqbur, am wakken diɣ i tella deffir tlalit n tiddukla « tmalalt " yettnaɣen ɣef yizerfan n tmeṭṭut tamaziɣt. Ass-a, Fatima d yiwen n uzamul n tlawin yugin kennu, yugin lbaṭel, yettnaɣen akken ad ilint. Fatima Tamlelt mačči kan txeddem taklut, meɛna s nmara i tesɛa tuɣal tettmeslay nnig tamaziɣt tutlayin nniḍen am tefransit s wacu i d -te ttɛeggin i tmuɣli-ines akked tikta- ines ɣef tudert akked yiɣeblan-is.
Anwa i d abrid iwulmen akken ad tili tneflit n tsekla taywamit tamaziɣt?
Tasekla taywamit di Lmerruk txuṣ mačči d kra. Nnig n tmedyazin am Tabuɛemrant, Talbensirt i ikecmen annar n ccna akken ad ssiwḍent amazan-nsent i ugdud wakali, imyura d temyura-nneɣ ur ttwasnen ara s waṭas. Akken ad tefti tsekla taywamit, tamaziɣt ilaq ad tekcem deg tenfalit n tdamsa n yidles akked tmetti. Ɣef waya, ilaq yal yiwen ad yissin izerfan-ines akked walsen-ines deḍǧirs.
Acu-ten wuguren i d- tettmagar tmeṭṭut tamaziɣt di Lmerruk?
Ccek-iw, iɣblan tettmager tmeṭṭut din ɣer-neɣ d wid i tettmager tmeṭṭut di tamazɣa irkelli. Tameṭṭut tamaziɣt akked tlawin n umaḍal s umata mazal yella fell-asent lbaṭel.Mazal-itent ddaw tekriḍt n yirgazen, imi ttuneḥsaben llan nnig-sent. Di Lmerruk, « la mǧudawana " yellan d lqanun, ireṣṣa leɛli n urgaz ɣef tmeṭṭut. Xas akken yettuɛawed zeɛma deg useggas n 1993, di tilawt kra ur ibeddel ɣef tmeṭṭut. Xas akken iṣuḍaf i as-igan miḥiyaf zeɛma ttwaksen, di tudert n yal ass, tameṭut tettwaḥqer, tettqazam rregmat, asebxes n yirgazen deg ubrid neɣ deg uxxam. Tameṭṭut tamaziɣt tettwaɛzel acku, di tmura yesburren tacḍat tineslemt, ulac azref i tmeṭṭut. Di tmetiyin-agi, tameṭṭut iqeddcen di tmusni, yebɣan ad tezdi s lqedd tettuneḥsab d yir nettat. Ma ur tt-sseɣlin, ad as-id- jaben ticrurin sya d sya akken ad tt- ssimsen!
Amek i as- ilaq iwakken ad tbeddel liḥala-agi fell-as?
Ilaq imenɣi ɣef yizerfan-ines. Ilaq ad nessegrireb aɣrab n ẓẓur i d-isers urgaz fell-as d ẓẓur yerran tullas ddaw ugerz n yirgazen. Ilaq diɣ tasnekla taɛrabt-tineslemt ad terr aḍar, acku seg-s i d- yekka wannect-a n tmuḥeqranit mgal tameṭṭut. D nettat i d ajgu n uxxam akked tmetti. Ilaq argaz amaziɣ ad yegzi belli skud tameṭṭut tettuḍerref, agdud amaziɣ s lekmal-is ad yaf iman-is di rrif. Aṭas n yimeɣnasen imaziɣen i d- yettawin inaw agrawli ɣer yizerfan n tmeṭṭut, meɛna nutni s timad-nsen d imezwura i yetterkaḍen izerfan-agi s wacu i ttgallan. D ahdum! Akken ad aɣ -d- ḍsen wussan, ilaq lemqadra gar urgaz akked tmeṭṭut, ilaq tikli idis ɣer yidis di yal aḥric n tmeddurt tatrart. Ilaq izerfan n tmeṭṭut ad as- ttuḥarben, am wakken ilaq unekcum n tmeṭṭut ɣer ugni n tsertit akked yidles…
Acu iwumi zemrent tullas timaziɣin yettidiren beṛṛa n tmazɣa ad t-id -awint i yidles amaziɣ?
Ugur ameqran yellan, d akken nekni s yiɣriben yegzem umrar gar-aɣ d yidles-nneɣ . Di tmura tiberraniyin, ur nettidir ara idles-nneɣ akken nebɣa. Ɣef waya, tuget seg-neɣ tettun aɛdil n tnaslit, keččmen di lqaleb n tudert tatrart n tmura tiberraniyin ideg ttidiren. Ayen i tezmer ad tawi tmeṭṭut tamaziɣt yettidiren di lɣerba, d tikta timaynutin, d lɛeqliya tajḍidṭ ara tleqqem ɣef tin i aɣ- d- ǧǧan lejdud. Tilelli i d- tettemagar di tmura, yeddan di tenfalit, yefka i tmeṭṭut tamaziɣt ttawil akken ad tesɛu tamuɣli lqayen ɣef yidles-nneɣ akken ad ttani seg-s ayen ikerfen ad as- tezwi tindal daɣ ad tḥareb ɣef wayen i ittellin lqid i umdan akked tmetti.
D acu i d izen n Silya i tulawwin tiqbayliyin s umata?
Ayen zemreɣ ad t-id- iniɣ i tyisetmatin-iw tiqbayliyin neɣ timaziɣin s umata, d akken ilaq aseḥbiber ɣef uktay-nneɣ yellan d imezdi. Ilaq tasuta ad t-id- teǧǧ i tayeḍ akken aẓar-nneɣ d awezɣi ad yenger. D wa kan i nesɛa d asirem akken ccetla tamaziɣt ad tennerni u d awazɣi a tt-yeɣḍer lawan, imi akken neẓra: nnekwa-nneɣ , idles-nneɣ , tutlayt-nneɣ aten-in d tadla zdat idelsan ijenṭad i aɣ-d- yezzin ama si daxel n tmurt neɣ beṛṛa n tmurt.
Ait Slimane Hamid
Taɣiwant n Beclul i d-yezgan tama n usammer n Tubiret tezmer akka deg useggas neɣ sin ad tbeddel udem deg uḥric yerzan tanezduɣt. 350 n tnezduɣin i yellan akka tura d ahil di tɣiwant- seg-sent qrib dɣa ad fakkent s lebni, tigi d tid yettwaheggan i widak ara yeggaǧen seg yixxamen yehtutan d wid daɣ yenḥafen. widak ara d-yeggaǧen ad naf deg-sen wid izedɣen akka ar tura deg uɣerbaz amenzu aqdim Cherarak Slimane. Ɣef leḥsab n yimeslayen n uselway n tɣiwant Mass A. Ammǧuche, drus n lecɣal i mazal iwakken ad d-asen imezdaɣ. 100 n tnezduɣin nniḍen anda i bdan lecɣal n lebni-nsent ɣef yiri n ubrid aɣelnaw wis 5 ssawḍent ahat ɣer 30 di lmeyya. Ma d 150 tineggura, ata-n akka tebda tezrawt-nsent, d tid ara yilin di ṣṣenf n LSP. Yettwahegga-d umkan ideg ara ttwabnunt, meɛna mazal kra n lecɣal ara yettwakemlen deg wussan-a i d-iteddun.
Idurar n Ǧerǧer yessan s udfel d win i d-yefkan yiwet n cbaḥa i temnaḍt. D ayen yeǧǧan aṭas n yimezdaɣ n temnaḍin i d-yezzin i Tubiret ttasen-d yal taggara n yimalas iwakken ad kksen lxiq. Ula d tiwilayin yecban Sṭif, Burǧ Bu Ɛririǧ, Bumerdas, Lezzayer tamaneɣt, Msila d tiyaḍ nettwali imezdaɣ-nsent di Tikjda. Lkiran i d-yettawin inelmaden mačči d yiwet neɣ d snat, almi ur yeshil ara uɛeddi ɣer waṭas n yimukan s tkerrust. Taggara n yimalas-a yezrin, imi tignewt d tin n tefsut, aṭas i d-yusan ɣer umkan-a n tmerrit mebla ma ṣṣawḍen ad d-ẓren ayen akk i bɣan. Tikerrusin mseḍfarent ta deffir ta ɣef wazal n nnig n 3 ikilumitren, d ayen yeǧǧan tuget n yimdanen ddan ɣef uḍar. Tiwaculin d yigerdan ufan akka tagnit i umerreḥ, imi adfel mazal-it deg tqucac-a n Ǧerǧer. Si tama-nsen, iɣallen n laman d wid ibedden akken iwata, ttḥaraben ɣef lehna n yimerriyen.
Iɛeggalen n tejmaɛt n twilayt n Tubiret sqerden deg temlilit n yimalas yezrin i yekkan azal n tlata wussan sin n yiḥricen i yettemxelbaḍen deg wurrifen. Mbeɛd mi sɣerblen timsal yerzan lakul, anda i d-sseknen tugniwin n kra n yiɣerbazen yenṭerren, d wuguren i d-tettmagar tmaziɣt, zzin s aḥric n tezmert. Tasqamut yettwasbedden yakan tezzi-d ɣef waṭas n sbiṭarat d tzeɣwa n tujya, tuɣal-d s yiwen n rrabul n wazal 35 n yisebtar anda i d-jerden akk ayen ixuṣṣen deg 122 n yimukan i d-ẓran yiɛeggalen n tesqamut-a. Ulamma tadrimt yewḍen ɣer 06 imelyaren n yidinaren i yettunefken deg useggas yezrin i uḥric-a mačči d tin ixuṣṣen, meɛna lixṣas n ttawil d win yeswehmen mačči d yiwen. Tezdeg, imejjayen d wid yetxeṣsen, lixṣas deg umagar n yimuḍan d liḥala n wid yimuḍan yettnusun di sbiṭer d iɣeblan i d-ssuksen yiɛeggalen n tejmaɛt n twilayt i d-yerran tuttra yecban ta: "Ɣer melmi ara yennerni uḥric-a n tezmert?”. Taɣawsa yesserfan wid yellan di temlilit-a d astehzi deg ttawilat yeswan tadrimt tameqrant mebla ma yettunefk-asen kra n wazal, imi qqimen di rrif, yuli fell-asen uɣebbar. wigi, ɣeg leḥsab n wid i d-ixedmen rrabul-a d ayen iwumi neqqar Scanner. Dɣa d ayen i d-ijebden lwelha n yimazen, imi sin seg ttawilat-a ɣlayen i d-tḥella Tubiret, meɛna ar ass-a ur ttwasexdmen ara, imi ulac wid ara ten-yesseddun!! Ɣef leḥsab n wayen i d-nnan di temlilit-a, ttawilat-a n scanner tekfa ṭṭmana-nsen uqbel ad ttwasxedmen. Taluft yessekren ahetwir d tin icudden ɣer yimejja yetxeṣṣen ixuṣṣen s waṭas labeɛda di temdint n Tubiret. Meɛna, ayen i yessewhamen dakken di sbiṭer n Lakharia, llan 7 seg yiwet n lḥirfa! Ɣer taggara n temlilit, s kra n wid akk i d-yemmeslayen gren tiɣri i yimḍebber n uḥric-a iwakken ad yeɣseb tikli deg wayen akka yellan d asenfar ama di M’chedallah neɣ Bǧrdj Ǧkhris iwakken ahat ad d-ɣermen seg wayen yekbel facal. Malika Kebaili
Tuɣal-as ass n ssebt 30 deg wayyur n meɣres, tejmilt tameqqrant i yiwen gar wudmawen mucaεen deg uḥric n tẓuri. Wagi, d Qasi n Tizi wezzu i ilulen di 1831 di Beni wartilan, di lwilaya n Sṭif. Deg uxxam n umezgun Kateb Yasin, i d-tella tmelilit-a anda i ḥeḍren yimdukkal d leḥbab n unaẓur-a i yuran isem-is s yisekkilen n wureɣ deg umezgun, imi yessaweḍ, netta d yerfiqen-is, ad d-rren taḍsa ɣer daxel n twacult tazzayrit, s usekles n wazal n 6000 n tceqqufin n umezgun d tedwilin n teḍsa ama di tilizri neɣ di rradyu n lezzayer. Aṭas n wudmawen yettwasnen deg uḥric-a i ixedmen yid-s wid yecban, Hasan Lḥasani neɣ Bubegra, Qriqec, Salaḥ Sadaǧui d wiyaḍ nniḍen. Tajmilt-agi i as-yuɣalen I tgejdit-agi n umezgun mi akka yessaweḍ 82 n yiseggasen di lɛemr-is, tejemε-d aṭas n yimdanen i t-iḥemlen ɣer tzeqqa anda i d-tella tmeɣra tameqrant ɣef ddemma-s, gar-asen Farida ṣabunji, ṭaleb Rabeḥ d Mama Mesεuda, i yerran tajmilt-agi d tagnit i teḍsa d unecraḥ yal mi ara d-uɣalen deg umeslay ɣef cwiṭ si tudert n Qasi n tizi wezzu.
Tawacult n tẓuri taqbaylit terra tamuɣli i tikkelt taneggarut i yiwen seg yiɛeggalen-is yewḍen leɛfu n Rebbi deg wyimalas yezrin. Mulud Ḥabib, imi d wa i aɣ-yeǧǧan, d yiwen seg wudmawen yettasnen s tezlatin-is yezuzunen.
Ukkuẓ tuɣalin ar Lqaεa
Deg yiwet n TAMANIT iɣraben-is ttaken anzi ar djaj tiɣemmar ttwaɣumment s lḥufat yettwzewqen deg yiwet n tama taqcict d tacebḥant s tmelsa tamadwant abstraite
Zdat umras n usekles enregestrement d tiliẓri….tletha d uheggi ines
Weεli: ikcem-d yettfay iẓid yiḍes! Waqila aṭas i ttseγ!
Tuzyint: yuder akin i waṭas…azal n krad trǧis temrilin swayeε
Weεli: d aya! iḍes mačči i usgenfu kan, maca d ddehwat
Tuzyint: d ddehwat?!
Weεli: ihi, akka i d as nḥus mi nella deg ubluɣ-nni amcum
Tuzyint: ahat kra yellan at-id tesedduḍ deg rabul rattttǧrt ara d taruḍ, iḥulfan-ik d wayen akk i teddrem din?
Weεli: ma ulac fella-s…awi-iyi-d taɣerfit n lqahwa
Tuzyint: suref-iyi! Attan anida i ak tt-id serseɣ, naɣ s uyefki i tt-tebɣiḍ, d ayen fesusen fell-ak ad tesseweḍ lqahwa akken i tt-tebɣiḍ, ad tafeḍ di tnewalt cuisine ijeεbuben n waman iṣemmaḍen d yeḥmayanen ad tafeḍ wiyaḍ s unuɣen yemgaraden: yiwen n lqahwa, wis sin n tay wis krad n uyefki wis ukus quatre n yiẓem jeu, ad telliḍ tabernint ad teffiḍ ayen texseḍ, anect i texseḍ
Weεli: akka di yal tazeqqa?!
Tuzyint: akka …imgusen-a acide uɣalen am waman
Weεli: ahat aṭas i d yesqam!
Tuzyint: ala … drus akkiya, d addad i yettxellisen
Weεli: d lewhayem!
Tuzyint: ulac aya di tallit-nnwen? Weεli: sḥasfeɣ.
Tuzyint: d tidet deg tezrawin etude inga nufa-d mačči d kra i yemgarrad ɣaf wass-a, 300 n yiseggasen aya
Weεli: 300 iseggasen! mačči d lewhayem! anida nella akk tisutiwin-a, nekkni ɣur-neɣ ad as t-iniḍ d yiwen wass
Tuzyint: ihi ma yella texseḍ akkiya akkiya, tekka-m krad twines d ṣa d aseggas
Weεli: d ṣa?
Tuzyint: akkiya…ɣaf uṣṣimeḍ n tuddsa ǧrganasitiǧn n yimassanen γef INEKKASEN n tussna iqbuburen
Weεli: ass-n i yebran i tnaεurt ahat, d ass ameqran, yettwura deg umezruy, maca afrayen-iw sentiments
Tuzyint: ih d afrayen-ik ɣaf ara d meslayeḍ di rabul-inek
Weεli: s wuden n tussna, akkud n di yemgarrad ɣaf win n da, maca ihulfan-iw d ayen nniḍen … d acu ara geɣ yes-sen?!
Tuzyint: ihi ɣas glem dicrire aseglem iwatan, d tarmit exttẓrience igerzen, imdanen akk d ay i tganin di yal tamnaṭ deg umaḍal mǧnde,ur teḥsiḍ ara dayen ara yilin d asentel theme i tezrawt etude n yimassanen?!
Weεli: yirbeḥ….ihi uɣaleɣ awen d aɣerda n tqerεtt akken ad tgem fell-i exttẓrience tirmitin naɣ Mačči akka?!
Tuzyint: isem-ik yuɣ di yal tamnaṭ, aqel-ak d aqdacc n umaḍal, ula d ddula terra-yak azal ameqran
Weεli: d tidet kra ur d iyi-xus, ladɣa kemmini
Tuzyint: s wecmumeḥ tanemmirt
Weεli: i tarcelt-iw ẓttǧuse, wissen ma teqqim ar tura?!
Tuzyint: 300 n yiseggasen?! Anida teẓriḍ?! Weεli: amek?!
Tuzyint: ih! tura ahat d tamγart, neɣ ḥacama temmut send aḍant tanfalit deḍlǧttttement n tujya mẓdicine, tura llan wid yernan nnig 80 d 90 n yiseggase ɣef 100 yerna haten deg tdawsa igerzen
Weεli: d tisewham! s weḥrurid attttrǧximatifAcḥal yezmer ad yidir yiwen?
Tuzyint: nekkni da, alamma ifel yiwen i 150 n yiseggasen, neɣ 200 n yiseggaseni i tebeddu tettağğa-t temzi-s
Weεli: temẓi! i temγer ihi Melmi?
Tuzyint: tem  ɣer tebeddu seg 300 n yiseggasen,
Weεli:d ayen igerzen!
Tuzyint: i, belli send 300 n yiseggasen, nesla d akken atemmun age yettwaeḍ ar 80 neγ ar 90 n yiseggasen, drus neγ ala?
Weεli: imir ar ɣur-neɣ 80 iseggasen aṭas!
Tuzyint: I nekk, acḥal akka ara d -iyi-tmuddeḍ?
Weεli: kemmini? Gar 20 d 25 n yiseggasen
Tuzyint: teḍsa-d ɣur-i 60 iseggasen a mass
Weεli: amek! Aha ur tmesxir ara fell-i!
Tuzyint: twehmeḍ, da bu 60 iseggasen mecṭuḥ
Tuzyint: akka lliγ akka tura i lliɣ
Weεli: d acu i t-ttgem akken ad tezgem akka?
Weεli: llan waṭṭanen, d taḍnent, iẓuran ttkawen, amwi akk akka….
Tuzyint: nekkni alamma tzeggreḍ 200 i d iḍerru tikwal waya, Akli Ǧutamazirt
"Xerṣum d yiwen ad d-yegri
Ad aɣ-id-ismekti azekka
F lǧerḥ iqcer ad yali
Ad d-enban ger tmura
Tarwa-nneɣ ad tennerni
Xas akken deg irebbi n tlufa”
Ilul-ed s waṭṭan. Asm’ala yettimɣur, lehlak-is yettimɣur yides, ur s ittaxer ara ar almi yewwi rruḥ-is. Aṭṭan-is d amennuɣ: amennuɣ ɣef tutlayt lal angue, amennuɣ ɣef tugdut, amennuɣ ɣef tlelli, d izerfan n wemdan. Deg iseggasen yedder, Matub Lwennas warǧin yekna i wuguren d-yemmugger, ulamma tewweḍ, acḥal n tikkal, tfidi ɣer yiɣes, maca yezga yettkemmil ɣer zdat-es. Ayen yellan deg wallaɣ-is, yeqqar-it-id yimi-is. Ur yettḥaci yiwen. Ula d lmut ur s yeggi ara ccan, axaṭer yeḥsa d akken ilaq-as ad iqabel ula d lmut akken ad yaweḍ ɣer yeswi-is, akken yaqqar Hijel” s usebbel n tudert i nettaweḍ ɣer tlelli”. Lwennas d-yenna-n: " Ssarameɣ ad mteɣ d ameɣras s tektiwin-iw, wala ad mteɣ deg wussu s lehlak neɣ s tewser", iwweḍ ɣer lebɣi-s, yemmut d lefḥel, d agrawliw, d’ameɣras.
Matǧub Lwennas ilul di 24 yennayer 1956, di Tewrirt Musa deg At Dwala, di lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu. D netta i d argaz n wexxam, baba-s yella di Fransa, yemma-s ur tesɛi ara arrac-nniḍen. Deg 1961 yekcem s aɣerbaz, maca ur yufi ara iman-is maḍi. Xas yemma-s teddez abrid n llakul, iselmaden-is zgan ttceyyiɛen-as-id acku ihedder aṭas, ur iserkad ara iman-is deg yiwen n wemkan, ur yetteḥsis ara daɣen i temsirin. Tbukkemmelt asmi yekkes tira n taɛrabt u yura deg wemkan-is s tmaziɣt. Lwennas izgel temzi-s, ilul-ed d argaz, yedder d argaz, u yemmut d argaz. Deg wasmi yella d aqrur yebɣa ad yexdem lecɣal n yergazen. Yiwen wass, mi d-usan imǧuhad s axxam-nsen di lweqt n ṭṭrad, yemma-s tsureg-asen lqahwa. Mi kfan uqbel ad kken tawwurt, inṭeq Lwennas ɣer yiwen deg sen yenna-yas: bɣiɣ ad dduɣ yidwen ɣer wedrar. Amǧahed yugi ad t-yawi, inna-yas mazal-ik mezziyeḍ. Lwennas ur t-iqenneɛ ara wawal-agi. Imir kan yemmeɣ ɣef ufenǧal n lqahwa yellan ger ifassen-is, yebbeɣ iḍudan-is di ttelwa, imir irṣem yissen claɣem.
Lwennas yebda ilemmed cna asmi yella d amezian. Di tazwara yella yesmuzgut kan i yemma-s mi tcennu deg wexxam. Tuɣal tekcem-as deg idammen. Asmi ɣur-es tsɛa iseggasen,yesmeckukel-ed agambar-is amenzu s tcabcaqt n zzit. Yebda s ucewwiq n Awḥid Yusef:” Uh a Muḥend a madam serbi latay”.
Matub yecna i tikkelt tamenzut di yiwet n lqahwa di Fransa, yewwi-d azal n 4 000 FF. D ayagi dɣa is-yefkan affud akken ad ikkemmel deg webrid-agi n ccna. Imir yuli ɣer Lttari. Ikkemmel icennu di leqhawi ladɣa anda ṭṭuqten leqbayel iminigiyen, dɣa imir id d-imuger Yidir. Aneggaru-agi yewwi-t akken ad yecnu lak d icennayen nniḍen. Imlal-ed lak d snat n tgejda n ccna n teqbaylit, ḥnifa lak d Sliman Azem. Syen yewwi-t akken ad isekles tasfift-is tamenzut umu isemma "Ya lferḥ-iw” deg useggas n -"62 ma as-necfu
Nɣil d amzeyyed n lehna
Nerfed leɛlam ncennu
Aqlaɣ nessufeɣ Fransa
Bu waɛmam asenni i ten-ettu Yesmar burekku
Yeṣṣenṭeḍ di mkul lǧiha
Yeffeɣ-ed leḥzen am wabbu Yeqqim-ed uɣurru
Tirrugza tenza s rrxa”
Syagi i bdan-t temḍellas, si 1962, mi tewwi tmurt n Lezzayer azarug-is  sǧn indettendence. Aɣref  le tteuttle yella yettraǧu "amzeyyed n lehna", talwit, tayri, tilelli, yiɣil ad d-yerr nnehta, maca I tṣebḥit n tmunnent l’indẓttendance, agdud iḥulfa i yiman-is yetteɣraq cwiṭ cwiṭ deg temda uɣurru, asirem-is yewwi-t waḍu. Yeffeɣ-ed di ṭlam u yekcem qbala ɣer ṭlam-nniḍen. Urɛad id d-yerri nnehta mi yesseɣli azaglu urumi, yufa-d iman-is yettwarez s uzaglu n tiɛurrebt.
"Cfiɣ-d immel iyi-d baba
ɣef asmi tefra
Si Maṣer id d-iṣub waḍu ” "Ileḥq-ed zhir ɣer tudrin-nneɣ
Lebṣel isuffeɣ anaṣli, tabuciṭant n tiɛurrebt d tin isqumcen agdud azzayri acku tiyita ur tt-iḥtam ara, yella yettraǧu ussan mellulen, ussan n talwit, maca targit-is ur teffiɣ ara, zman ikmes-as-id tarzebt iɣilifen d lehmum, d aṭṭan ur n-esɛi ddwa. D wagi i d asentelsujet iceɣben, s waṭas, Matub Lwennas. Yezga yettezzi-d fell-as di tezlatin-is. Yenna-d deg-sent ansi d-yekka, anwa t-id-yewwin, iswi uneggaru-agi, amek i ylaq aten-qabel.
Ayen yak n dir aɣ-ihemj iseɣ
Taluft tdegger-ed tilas
Tufa-d allaɣ teksa yas
Si zik tuder lqima-s
Bgayet lbaḍna-s tefreɣ Qessiḥ uzekka
Iban-ed i tmeddit
Ur d-nemyuzga ara f ujeggu n teqbaylit”
Izdeɣ-it lḥir m’ur d-yufi s wayes ara yejji taqbaylit-is yettnazzaɛen di tesga n ṭlam
" Terrez teqbaylit deg iferr
Wissen ma ad tekker
Lǧerḥ ikcem-it ssem”
Yeggul ur yeḥnit ur isers izen ɣer lmaɛun alamma yemmut xas akken yettwargem, yettwaḥqer, yettwakker, yettwawweḍ u yettwajreḥ acḥal n tikkal.
" Yerra-iyi zman deg umehraz
Mi d-eɣli tyita ayi-d-ḥaz Teddegdeg ṣṣura”
Ayen i tyerḥan d taqbaylit, d tutlayt, tilelli, d idurar. Ulamma tudert-is d tin ur nɣezzif ara, maca iṣaweḍ ad d-yini, ad yaru, ad yeḥku, w’ad yecnu timsal t-iceɣben. Iḥureb ɣef teqbaylt-is s wuglan d tuɣmas. Yennuɣ s wawal. D wagi i d leslaḥ s wayes iqubel tixnanasin n yeɛdawen n tudert d iṣeggaden n tmusni, lewḥuc teǧǧa leḥnana. isefra-s d rrmug ihuzzen idurar, i yceqqen igenwan. Ayen ttxemmimmen leqbayel s tsusmi, yenna-t-id s leǧher. Yaɛreḍ acḥal n tikkal ad d-yekkes acḍaḍ- nni n tegmatt d timmuzɣa yeḥweṣ umeṣbaṭli.
Matub Lwennas yerra, deg tezlatin-is, tajmilt i ymusnawen, i wid iqeddcen di tmusni, d yemǧuhad ar …almi qarṣen fell-as s rrṣaṣ deg yiwen wass, yir ass, ass n 25 di yunyu 1998, deg uzal lqayli, di Tala Bbunan, deg webrid n At Dwala. Asenni- yeddem tibalizin-is, iruḥ ar wanda ur d-yettuɣal. Ibeddel tansa l’adresse. Tuɣal tansa-s d tin n Tahar ǧaut, Smaɛil Ybṣaḥ, Racid Tigziri, Busebsi, Rabeḥ Sṭenbuli d wiyyaḍ, d yiwet. Iɛdawen-agi n tmusni, ur nfehhem siwa tutlayt n leslaḥ, ɣeḍlen aṭas imusnawen, imeɣnasen jǧurnalistes d inazuren id d-ibedden deg wudem-nsen u nnan-asen ala i leḥkem ameṣbaṭli, maca akken teqqareḍ: "Xas neqḍen acḥal d itri, igenni ur inegger ara”.
Asirem n Lwennas d akken tarwa n tmazɣa ad teddukel, acku ala s tegmatt ara izmiren ad d-kken nnig n wid izarrɛen isennanen. "Yiwen wass limmer ad d-neddukkel, tamurt-nneɣ ad tt-id-nḥell, ad nekkes azaglu ɣ-yeqqnen”. D tagi i d tirga n Lwennas, tadukli, asirem d tegmatt, d wigi i d leslaḥ s wayes zemren imaziɣen ad awḍen ɣer lmerɣub-nsen:
"D lwaǧeb asirem ad yili
Deg wulawen ad yefti
Xas akka lwaɛd la yteqqes
Ma wteɣ di gma ass-agi
Tassa-w ur tugi
Bɣiɣ kan ad yefriwes” "Win iwen-inna-n
D acu i d tafat
Inet-as d iɣallen yedduklen” Tiziri Zinya
Tucḍa n yixef mačči d yiwen i d-udem-is. Amdyaz  dagi Lwenas yegren ixef-is am uqajmur s-asif akken ad iḥareb ɣef cetla, yeẓra belli, tikwal, tawecḍa tettili d ttin yeɛnan amdan weḥdes kan netta d yiman-is, am akken tettili tikwal-nniḍen d ttin n ugdud wakali. Matǧub deg waṭas n isefra yexdem yezdi tucḍa n yixef-is ɣer tin n ugdud ansi id yefruri. Anect-a nettaf-it deg isefra ɣezifen yexdem, amedya « terwa n Lhif ", « fkiɣ ɣer ssuq isem-iw " « ad regmeɣ deg iman-iw ", « tisirt n ndama "… Anect-nni ur d yelli ara s ugacur imi Matǧub yewwid tecriḥt deg timeti ansi id yefruri, am akken netta s-timad-is yella d tecriḥt s-wacu tettidir timeti-nni. Ger Matǧub Lǧunes akked ugdud Aqbayli ur yekki unẓaḍ d tilist ger asen. Netta s timad-is yenna: Tuḍen tmurt-iw
La tteḍneɣ yides
Ugadeɣ d laṣel-iw
I d-asfel ines….
Di tigzirin n tudert, ihi teqqen tawenza n umdan ɣer tin n tmurt, ɣer tin n ugdud. Anda akken teɣli timiṭ i umdan i ɣelint tiseqar n tudert n uɣref. Tiwenziwin yellan ger yiwen d waṭas, ger kra d xilla ggent tiregwa yettawin urfan, lemḥayen, lehmum seg yiri ɣer yiri. Aɣilif n umdan yettɛemir seg iɣilifen n tmurt, ahdum n tmurt yettenser-d seg tucḍiwin n umdan. Deg unamek n wawal yenna umedyaz:
Assen ad tfehmeḍ kulci
Ameqyas deg i tweḥleḍ
Zher n zher-ik ayen-nni
D tamurt andi i d t-lluleḍ
Netta-t zher-is yerwi
Amek tebɣiḍ a tt-rebḥeḍ?
Tadyant-agi icuden tudert n umdan ɣer wakal anda id yefruri &amtt;nbstt,; Matǧub ifeser-itt-id akken ilaq deg usefru ines « terwa n lḥif ". Deg ixef n usefru –agi yebna Matǧub am akken d tanfust yettawin amdan alama d tilist n yiman-is yebda s tuzma deg atmaten yekcem waḍḍu n lexdaɛ akked d yir aseḥseb. Atmaten-agi wukud, nniqal, tagrawla tebda tegger imɣi, ziɣen d nefs kan i yeččuren. D zhir ur nemɛin kan i yesṭuqten! Wama deg annar n imenɣi, ssan amzun d ixmir, seɛraqen lǧera i ṣṣwab acku d ttnefxa akked ucufu n uqendur i ttawin yid-sen d aɛwin: « ttzuxun hedren/ kran n yemdanen/ad bedlen aggus i tmurt ". Zux, aburef, taggalit s aḥeq nekk d wigi i d-iferdisen s wacu ččuren lfuci ttawin ger ifasen-nsen: « Leḥbas ad zemmen/ neɣ aten hudden/ cetwa as ksen tagut " neɣ diɣ: « ggulen ur ḥenten/ tamalalt a tt-id ksen/ ur tettnekkar tsekurt ". Xas akken teɛjajat n leɣrur id yettṣudun terra aɣebar s allen, werǧin tedrig tidet ɣef umadyaz, imi akken qqaren at zik: « yettban usigna s wacu tekkat ".
Lyafuxa n umdan yemɛabaren akked tidet d aken ines lekdeb, xas teḥḍem, tezga akken ibɣu iḍul lḥal d telqa n telqaq iccuden ixef n yal yiwen ɣer timadit-ines. Ulac tikelax deg urar n tudert akked lmut. Amdan neɣ agdud mi t-id rran yiɣerban ur yeṭuqet ara ufran zdat-as. Yiwen ubrid i wullem: asburu n tlaba n tɣisit neɣ tuṣra s tlaba n yiseɣ. Amdyaz yeẓran d akken ulac lebni ɣef yijdi, ulac tayerza ɣef agris,ulac anṣib di tɣerɣart, yesawel i tarwa akken ad aten isteqsi ma yella ṭamaɛ deg ulac neɣ ma ad yarrew ubudu lexrif?
Maca, di tebḥat n usemɛenter ger tidet akked tikerkas, tucḍa tesenta tucar-is deg ixef n ugdud. Tetteceliḥ di tinekit-ines am akken yettceliḥ lḥif di « Nekk " n umedyaz ur nezmir ad yerwel i taluft neɣ ad yeqqen allen-is fell-as. Lemwaji id iḥamlen si yal tama, ur tezgilent ur zgilent timeti wuɣur iccud yiri-is. Di lhejna n lḥir i-itenḍen ɣef tasa-s, yunnag ɣer ugni n tuzmiwin. Tikwal nettaf-i tezzem deg iman-is, tikwal deg wid yerra d atmaten, tikwal ula deg imawlen. Yekfa uqili, ifuk udari imi tidet ur tessin ara asefran ger wa akked wihin:
« fkiɣ ɣer ssuq isem-iw
  ɣer reḥba iẓẓayriyen
ad yezenz imaṭawen-iw
ma llan wid a ten-yaɛen… "
neɣ « Ɣef yisem-iw id mǧazen/ as ḍlen qerḍren/ win i s-yeslan ad yesmumi " anda nniḍen d asḥisef: « a nneɣ a baba d yemma/ ur ken- cbiɣ-ara/ tili ass-a aqli ger-wen ". Simmal yettendekwi yixef ɣef tuṣda n zzman, leɣder n watmaten simmal yesiqisiḥ umedyaz deg awalen-is. Udem-is umu yeḍla iselwan, yezwi leḥya akkin, ideqer aḥazeb ur d nettawi akken leɛyub yellan ad ufraren nnig wadal n tikerkas yessan ɣef tiswin akked ulawen: « rniɣ deɛwessu imawlan/ tewwi-yi ger ifarawen-is " neɣ « ad regmeɣ uqbel iman-iw / uqbel a neziɣ ɣurwen ", « ass-a udem-iw jerdeɣ s useɣwen ", « iles-iw yesfujuɣ ", « iḥcer lbeḥr-iw "….
Times n reffu tzeher, teseknef deg ifyar, deg awalen alarmi yuɣal usefru d teḥbubt yettfegiḍen s yiẓra n wurɣu. Tidet yecbek uẓeṭṭ-as. I wakken ad iban ixef-is ilaq lexlas. Yerhan umedyaz lehna n yixef-is, yefka-tt d asfel i lebɣi n tidet. Lmenṭaq si zikk akka, nnbi ur yettwaqbel di tmurt-is yettawi-d cḥani. Bab-is a tɣunzun medden. Leḥbab uqbel ixṣimen deg-s ad hemjen. A tesɛun d cɣel neɣ a t-ḍerfen: « yezga uḍad yesweɛdi-yi ", « mazal-iten deg-i a katen/ anda diɣ ayi sweɛden " « qqaren-as aqcic-nni d imciṭan " « Tekfa tiɣimit n lǧema/teɣlid lɛica/ agris a igezzem iḍaren " neɣ diɣ « anda akken id ufiɣ leḥbab-iw/ id tt-nejmaɛen yiɛdawen ".
Temxebel tagnit, uguren ssan deg abrid yeggunin uḍar. Timlalay nnig uqaru taxatalent di bab-nsent. Amezdyaz yeẓra du leqrar a teṭṭef ticeket i s- undin wussan. Di ccew yemderkal ɣef ayen yellan. Temẓi thud d iceqfan. Axam yettwebnan, s tidi d leɛtab, irab. Tayri thujer imeḍqan. Tagmet selaw uɣdu-ines. Tmaɛ-nni n zik yemḥa: « tuzenzeɣ s rxa ", « s adaynin ad yiqnan ", « yettwaqecem ubuqal n ddunit-iw " d tugniwin yesexdem Matǧub akken ad immel telqay n wanu wuɣur yerdem yixef-is. Yewɛer lɛum di tmedwa iluɣen. Igefuren, i d-yewwi yir asigna, gland s leḥmali n ineẓman: « Lbabur id i -yewwin/ ɣef lebḥer n tismin/ yeqṣed temurt n wammus ". Amɛaber akked timsal tid umu ur zmirent tuyat i uɛebbi yegger ṣṣura deg yir tisirt. Ixef yenɣed yeftutes, yegla s ṛṛuḥ, ur yezgil ṛṛuḥ n ṛṛuh: « ǧǧiɣ acwari n tirgin/ i ẓẓwaǧ-iw d aɛwin/a tt-kemel i tebrek ma txuṣ ". « nedḥed am igerfiwen-rẓan wafriwen… ", « rri-yi ɣer wid iruḥen/ mi sen d sawlen/ asmi akken id tewweḍ lgira ", « rriɣ ul-iw deg uffus-iw/ hemjen seg-s yakk medden " …
Imararen n ẓẓur, am ucengal, ggunin ixef n umedyaz yugin kenu. Lɛaz win it –yebɣen tewwid ad yecrew tidi yerɣan. Amedyaz ɣef ur drigen-t timsal, yesni tiɛaqucin n tillawt ɣer ṭelqa n tidet. Ixef-is yuɣal d lemri deg id tettuɣal tugna n timeti deg yettidir. Tucḍa wuɣur yemɣebas yiri-s d lewhi n tucḍa deg tedda timeti. Matǧub yettenjeɛ deg meslayen akken ad innin nnig wayen umu zemren. Nhuden-t tisas, yekna leqder ɣer umilus. Yebḍa lebɣi d ifataten. Ɣelluy yewweḍ ɣer akkin i tagara-s: « leqḍeɣ lebwent deg iberden ". Allaɣ ur nuksen iḥulfa s lehlak i d- izedwen ɣef ṣṣura. Iḥulfa s ifaden yulwan yuggumen i tikli: « s kra n win ihelken yeḥla/ aṭan-iw yuggi ad yeḥlu/ lhem fell-i id yesteɛfa/ ihamej deg-i irennu ". Yegrurec umdan si tsadarin i d-yebna lmektub am akken tegrurec timeti seg usebdad i d-yenǧer umezruy: « nḥamel dderz netɛegiḍ/ nettkaw am uceṭid "neɣ « iluḥqed zhir ɣer tudrin-nneɣ , ur nesɛi-ara lḥir akken a t-nesufeɣ ". Astehzi akked berru n yiman anda ur ilaq d iferdisen id yetteǧwan ddel ama i umdan ama i wagdud: « atten atten deɛwesu/ ceyɛen-tt-id ad tzur tudar " neɣ « imesdurar n twaɣit, tawaɣit tezi-asen ", anda nniḍen « s lḥif i nemuger cetwa/ ur aɣ terri tamara/ talwit mi id t-qareb a tterwel ". Ammus iḥara amkan di tesga. Tizelgi tuɣal d tarigla yesenɛaten abrid ɣer yifri i wagdud neɣ i umdan. Mi i yufgen iḍumen, deg asrifeg –nsen ur yemniɛ ḥedd seg unezgum: « xas yurad yixef-iw/ leɛyub fell-i ɣman ".
Yezga wul ad yettiẓif
D idamen iyi-d yesneṭqen
Greɣ-d am uqajmur s asif
Ait Slimane Hamid
Aḥric n tmerrit  le tǧurisme d win yesnegmayen tadamsa l’ẓcǧnǧmie n tmura. Llan-t kra deg-sen-t d tayejdit ɣef ayeg tbedd tdamsa-nsen-t, d tagi ɣef ayeg sɛukkuzen-t akken ad d-skecmen-t ameṣruf acku i ḥricen-nniḍen akk n tgemmi-nsen-t, lexdami, tafellaḥt, ṣṣenɛat, d wid ur nennerni ara s waṭas neɣ ur gman ara maḍi. Ger tmura-agi ad d-n-ebder Tunes, Lmerruk, Maṣer, Lyunan, d tiyyaḍ. Aṭas n tmura-nniḍen glan-t akk yissen-t, anerni n tdamsa d unerni- n tmerrit. D agi nezmer ad d-nini d akken gmmu n tdamsa yetturar azal d ameqran deg usnerni n tmerrit n tmura, acku taneggarut-agi teḥwaǧ adellel La ttublicitẓ akken ad tessaɛlem imdanen ɣef ugerruj ay sɛan-t tmura w’ad d-ejbed tamuɣli iḥewwassen. ɣef ayagi, timura yegman, ladɣa tid n lɣerb, srusuyen-t-ed ɣer wennar yak tiɣawsiwin ara ywenɛen anerzi n iḥewwassen ɣur-sen-t, am wallalen uṣiweḍ, tu ččit, llebsa… Dehhun-ed daɣen s usizdeg n tuddar d temdinin. Ayagi mebla ma n-ebder-ed leqdic-nsen-t deg wayen yeɛnan adellel. L’Internet, tilizrit, idlisen, tidukliwin, ixxamen n yedles d wid n yelmezyen ttaken-as afud d ameqran i tmerrit. Tamurt n Lezzayer ɣas akken tesɛa aṭas s wayes ara tzux deg wayen icudden ɣer tmerrit, lameɛna ur s tefki-ara azal meqren i weḥric-agi. Leqdic deg wayen yeɛnan tamsalt-agi d win ur n-ettembiwil ara s watas. Tarwa-s s timmad-is ur t- ḥsi ara d acu tesɛa tmurt-is. Dɣa mi tebda tallit imuras les ḍacances, imdanen ad ten-t-afeḍ refden tibalizin-nsen ɣer tmura akin i yillel agrakal. Di 48 n lwilayat tekseb tmurt n Lezzayer, yal yiwet deg-sen-t tesɛa ayen tt-isemxallafen ɣef tayya ḍ. Yal yiwet s thuski-s s ccḥbaa-s. Yal yiwet d acu tt-id- iṣebḥen deg wayen is t-id freq twennaṭ  la nature, d wemdan, acku aneggaru-agi yesbedd, s iffassen-is, aṭas n lebni yessawḍen ad tfen-t iman-nsen-t d leqrun adɣa di tallit n rruman d iṭerkiyen. Melba ma newwi-d awal ɣef wayen yella-n di twennaṭ am idurar, illel la mer, tizgwa les fǧrḥts, ṣṣḥari, tiftisin, … Ger temnaḍin umu yeǧhed aṭas weḥric n tmerrit tella lwilaya n Batna, tamanaɣt la cattitale n wawras. Tezga-d deg ugafa-asammer nǧrd-est n Lezzayer. Biskra tḥud-itt-id deg wenzul sud, lwilaya n M’sila deg umalu ǧuest, Xencela deg usammer, ṣṭif, Mila d Sirṭa deg ugafa. Batna tesɛa azal 11 n la dayrat: 3in Tuta, Arris, Barika, Batna, El Madhar, Marwana, N’Gawes, Ras Laɛyun, Tazult, Tniyat El Abad, lak d Seriana. Batna tesɛa azal n 61 n tɣiwanin les cǧmmunes. Ger imeḍqan n tmerrit id d-yufraren di lwilaya n Batna lla-n wigi.
Ɣufi neɣ ibalkuyen n ɣufi: Aẓekka Imedɣasen
ɣufi d yiwet n temnaṭ n tmerrit  site tǧuristique id d-yezgan deg wenzul n Batna. Wagi d yiwen umedḥuḥ d’aɣezzfan canyǧn umu semman asif amellal i yzegren di tama umu qqaren Tifelfel alami d M’cnunec ɣef teɣzi n wazal n 3-4 n les kilumitr. ɣufi d yiwet n temnaṭ iqerben aṭas ɣer lwilaya n Biskra, tawwurt n ṣṣeḥra. Asif amellal ma čči d win yewwi-n abrid-is qbala, yezzi u yenneḍ acḥal n tikkal. Aman-is d izedganen, ttecruruden am nebdu am cetwa. ɣef yiran n wasif, mɣint-ed tzantin, iruhen akka tura deg igenni. Wid izedɣen zzik di temnaṭ-agi zzan aṭas n tebḥirin isekla les arbres ladɣa tiremmanin, tizemrin, tittefaḥin, tineqlin, tiberquqin, ddayla, timecmacin s wayes mussan-et lwilaya-agi,… Asif amellal, umi zzin-t tebḥirin isekla, kkan-d nnig-es igadiren les falaises yewwḍen di kra n imeḍqan 200 n lmitrat. ɣef tneggura-agi ttwabnan-t xemsa n tuddar: Hitesla, Iddaren, At Mimun, At Yaḥya, At Menṣur neɣ tawriret. Ixxamen n tuddar-agi ttwabnan deg lqern wis rebɛa. D tizeɣwa timecṭaḥ yebnan s yezra de wakal d wesɣar, ttwaseqfen-t s lqermud. Ixxamen-agi yebnan ɣef ibalkuyen n wezru mqabalen. kra si lǧiha tayfust n wasit, kra nniḍen si lǧiha tazelmaḍt. Tizeɣwa-ya ur ttwazdɣen-t ara akka tura. Xas ɛeddan aṭas n leqrun fellasen-t maca mazal-iten-t bedden-t. Rnan-t as-d ccbaha meqren i wemda n ɣufi. Tezdeg, tizzeyzewt, lebni aqbur aqdim, tizantin, asif amellal, ibalkuyen mlalen-d u fkan i temnaṭ-agi yiwet n tmuɣli ifazzen. Imḍebren n tmerrit, akken ad sishlen aṣubbu n iḥewwasen ɣer wasif amellal yellan ddaw ixxamen, bnan ṭruj. Aẓekka Imedɣasen Imedɣasen d yiwen uẓekka anumidi yellan di tɣiwant n Bǧumia di lwilaya n Batna. Aneggaru-agi yettwabna di lqern wis krad uqbel talalit n Sidna ɛisa.
Aẓekka n Imedɣasen d ameqran, d aɛlayan, d imdewwer. D netta akk i d aẓekka ageldan  rǧyal aqbur aqdim di Tefriqt ugafa. Isem-agi s fkan, lahsab n imazrayen les histǧriens am Ibn Xaldun, Ibn Hazm, Salluste, Hẓrǧdǧte d isem n yiwen ugellid n la Numidi, Madɣis. Akka tura, azekka Imedɣasen yella ger 100 laterat yebgha zman ad yemḥu. Aẓekka-agi ageldan yesɛa 59 n lmitrat di tehri-s, 18,50 n lmitrat di teɣzi. Yettwabna s udɣaɣ lmenǧur. Sqef-is ɛlayen yebna d tiṭarjtin. Amazray amaṣri, Al Bakri, di lqern wis XI yella d’amezwaru id d-igelmen aẓekka-agi. Yenna-d d akken Madɣis yella d agellid n tmurt. Ibn Xaldun, netta, yenna-d, di lqern wis XIV, deg wedlis yura « Histǧire des BerbAres " d akken Madɣis d ababat n imaziɣen.
Timgad, Zana, Tǧbna,… Thiziri Zenia Yasin Zidan
Timgad d yiwen wemḍiq s wayes tettwassen lwilaya n Batna. Timgad neɣ tamdint n rruman, d tin yebnan deg useggas n -Tettwassen ladɣa s unezgum-is yesɛan azal n 4 000 imekwan lak d temkerḍit-is  la bibliǧthAque. Zana d amekkan nniḍen n tmerrit id d-yezgan ger ɛin ǧasser d temdint n Batna. Dagi i llan laterat n temdint n Diana Veteranǧrum n la Numidi. Tǧbna d yiwet n temdint taqdimt n wawras. Tezga-d deg umalu n Barika deg wenzul n Batna. Di tallit n rruman tamdint-agi qqaren-as Tǧbuna negh Tubǧnis. Ass-agi qqiment-ed kan deg-s tkemmict n laterat yuklalen ad n-erzu ɣursen-t akken ad ten-t-id nwali.
Danwa-t Smaɛil Ṭaleb?
Smaɛil Ṭaleb: D anelmad n tmaziɣt deg tesdawit n Bgayet, luleɣ deg useggas 1986 deg temdint n yemma Guraya, ḥemmleɣ ayen akk icudden ɣer timmuzɣa, alq-in d aselway n uqusis club ussnan n tmaziɣt anda i nxeddem aṭas n tɣawsiwin.
Dacu-ten yimahilen i txedmem deg uqusis?
Leqdicat-nneɣ nezmer ad ten-nefren ilmend n snat n tɣawsiwin: ayen yellan d ussnan d wayen yeɛnan idles. Yelha ma nesmekta-d belli abrid i d-newwi yettkemmil deg wayen neǧren imezwura i yeṭṭfen tanarit n uqusis-a, amedya deg wayen i xedmen ya deg tesɣunin akked tfaskiwin n tsekla, aseggas-a, newwi-d ttiɛadat n usfuggel am umenzu n Yennayer, amager n tefsut s seksu d uderyis, tafsut n Yimaziɣen … Akken daɣen i nxemmem amek ara neg kra n temliliyin tussnanin deg wayen yerzan annaren n tesnilest akked tsekla tamaziɣt, ɣef waya ahil i d-nessujed i useggas i d-iteddun ad yili d amerkanti deg wayen yerzan tussna. Akken daɣ ara nefk ttiɛad yal aseggas s tfaska n unelmad ara d-nessajed i teɣzi n ddurt s leqdicat yemxalafen.
Tufrareḍ-d taggara-ya s warraz wis sin n tsekla, mmeslayaɣ-d ɣef tira-inek?
Tamazwarut, nekk ttḥacaɣ tameslayt ɣef leqdic, aṭas ur nwala belli ttaruɣ tullisin, aṭas i yettmeslayen mebla ma ssawḍen, nekk seg wid yugin anect-a, axir ad yexdem yiwen mebla ma yehḍer aṭas, akken qqaren irumiyen "ibelheddaren ur llin d ixeddamen", ferḥeɣ mi wwiɣ arraz wis sin, dayen i d-yesbeynen aswir n tira-w, ur ilaq ara ad ttuɣ lxir n wid akk i yi-d-yesseɣtan kra n tullsin-inu, ḥemmleɣ seg zik tasekla, ɣef waya i ḍefreɣ taɣult-a deg tmaziɣt, ḥemmleɣ ad ɣreɣ ayen akk uran s teqbaylit ladɣa mi ara yettwaxdem s lewqama d lekyasa.
Ssarameɣ ɣer sdat ad ssufɣeɣ ammud n tullisin-ynu, ssarameɣ dayen ara iɛejben i yimeɣriyen.
Amek i tzemreḍ ad tessemlileḍ gar tɣuri, tira akked leqdicat n uqusis? Awal aneggaru?
Mi ara twaliḍ ayen nneɛtaben yimyura yenḥafen deg tallit n ṭṭrad am Mulud Ferɛun fell-as yeɛfu yerḥem ad as-tiniḍ I yuɣen irgazen susmen! Maca s ttawilat i aɣ-yettunefken ass-a, yuɣal asdukkel n wanect-a mačči d awezɣi. D tidet ahat kkseɣ anezzeh d uferrej deg lweqt-iw, kkseɣ lqahwa d leḥbab deg berra, yal mi ara sɛuɣ tagnit ttfaraseɣ-tt i tɣuri.
SBɣiɣ ad wessiɣ, deg usebter-a, inelmaden: berka-ken deg usmesxer deg tesdawit, tasdawit d amkan n ulmad mačči d adeg n zzhu d uqesser! Aṭas i yeṭṭsen war ma ẓran, aṭas i ixesren war ma ḥsan, ilaq ad d-yuɣal uswir, ilaq ad fken azal i uẓayer n unelmad yakan, yettɣiḍ mi ara nettwali deg yinelmaden ṭṭafaren "ṣṣafa walmarwa", ad ttɛiwiden i yiseggasen, neɣ ad ttkuttyin deg yikayaden.
Ilmend usmekti n umuli wis 51γef timunent n tmurt n Lzzayer, id-yettuγalen yal ass n 5 yulyu di yal seggas, i yellan daγen d ameγra n yelmeẓyen, deqs n leqdicat id-ittewhegan γef dema di yal tamnaḍt n tmurt.
Dγa taddert n yigersafen, taγiwant n At-Yeğğar yetabaεen dayra n Wizgan, tesfaydi-d s wecεal n lgaz n temdint i lfayda n nnig n 400 n yexxamen.
Γef dema n waya tella-d yiwet n tmeγra meqren id-sudes tdukla tadelsan ALMA n taddert n yigarsafen s lemεawna n tesqamut n taddart-agi akk d yimezdaγ-is. Ahil i ittewjarden d amarkanti, anda llan temzikniyin yemgaraden γef umezruy azzayri d tegrewla n 54 akk d isaragan, cnawi d waṭas niḍen.
Ilmend umuli wis 51 γef tmunent n tmurt n Lzzayer, deqs n leqdicat id-ittewheggan γef dema di 04 tγemmar n tmurt.
Dγa tamnaḍt n Wizgan tella di ttiεad, anda imḍebren n tγiwant n Wizgan, s tallelt n tudsa taγelnawt n lmujahidin d tesqamut n tadert n At-Sidi Σmar heggan-d yiwen n leqdic d amesbaγur u swazal-is, anda id-yella usemmi n yiwen uγarbaz alemmas γef yiwen n umaγras n tadert At-Sidi Σmar, i yeγlin deg wegni n liser ass n 02 yunyu 1959, wagi d Muḥemmadi Areẓqi. Islam Bessaci
Tamesbanit-agi tamazrayt tella-d s leḥdur n yemḍebren n temnaḍt n Wizgan, ger-asen iselwayen n dayra d tγiwant n Wizgan, tawacult n yigrewliwen d deqs n yimezdaγ n temnaḍt-agi. Ahil i jarden d amarkanti u s wazal-is, anda id-yella userussu n tmeqnin n yijeğğigen γef uẓekka n umaγras Muḥemmadi Areẓqi d wemḍiq ideg yeγli, d usebdad n yimeγrasen n tegrewla Lzzayer d uẓekka n kulunel Muḥend Welḥağ i yellan d yiwen n imḍebar aneggaru n lwilaya tis 03 tamazrayt. Akken id-yella usenεet n temzikniyin yemgaraden γef umezruy n tegrewla d isaragen niḍen. D tagnit yelhan i yemdanen, xarṣum ilmeẓyen akken ad-isinen azal n timunent n tmurt n Lzzayer d warfad umezruy lqayen tesεa tmurt n Lzzayer.

Tuzyint: Ih muqel ɣar webrid, ad twaliḍ umrisen n tunḍa s war imesnayen amsedduyen, muqel ar tegnawt ad twaliḍ lkiran isakkacen n tegnaw teddun s war imesnayen imsenharen …kra yellan yetwasedday s tqeffilt yerna di tnedlibin tadiganin d tlemmasin administratiǧns lǧcales et centraux

Weεli: yyah…ih ih aya sneγ-t….dayen i snermiγ jerbeɣ…ih i yakken ẓẓay yilem ɣaf wemdan

Tuzyint: sanwa…arağu tekker ar teɣmert n texxamt tketta i tqeffilt dɣa tban-d tugna ɣaf tfelwit ah wayi d ameddakel-ik

Ʃli: deg umris tukiḍ-d? tesswiḍ lqahwa?

Ʃli: ihi akka cwiṭ Akli Ǧutamazirt
Tedder, teḥka, tura, tecna, Marguerite Taǧs Amrǧuche, tlul di Tunes, deg useggas n -Aseggas-a yezzem lqern,ɣef tlalit-is. Taǧs tekker-ed deg yiwet n twacult taqbaylit, deg Iɣil Ali, di lwilaya n Bgayet. Tawacult n yemyura d tmusni. Yemma-s n Taǧs d tin yuran ungal ” Histǧire de ma ḍie” 1968, agzul n tudert n tmeṭṭut taqbaylit, Faḍma Nat Mensǧur, ilemden deg yiwen uɣerbaz ẓcǧle n teqcicin yellan ger imezwura yeldin tiwwura-nsen di Lezzayer. Marie Lǧuise Taǧs, ula d nettat, tewwi-d yid-es azar-agi n tira. D nettat i d tamyarut, tamenzut, taqbaylit, ineǧren asalu i temyura nniḍen id tt-id-iḍefren deffir-es. Tenǧer-it-id s wungal umu tsemma « Jacinthe nǧire” -Weltma-s n Jɛan Amrǧuche, teswa-d deg ssin idelsan  cultures, aqbayli d ufransi. Taǧs Amrǧuche tella tettxalaḍ imyura imeqranen n tmura-nniḍen, ladɣa wid n Fransa, gar-asen Andrẓ Gide d Jɛan Giǧnǧ. D wid ukkud tella tettbeddil tiktiwin deg uḥric yeɛnan tira. Deg wungalen rǧmantura, Taǧs tsers-ed deg-sen amur ameqran deg wayen tɛac di tudert-is n yall ass. Ladɣa ayen icudden ɣer lyerba, tinna tt-isbeɛden ɣef wanda i d-lul, ɣef tamurt-is, Lezzayer. Deg idlisen-is, tewwi-d awal ɣef waṭas isental-nniḍen  sujets, tayri, tagmatt, temzi, ansayen d leɛwayed, tudert izzayriyen di timetti la sǧciẓtẓ yellan tettwarez s snasel umnekcem arumi,…Maca win umu tefka azal d ameqran, win tesqerdec s telqey, win ɣef ayeg tesseɣzef awal, d win yeɛnan tameṭṭut. Tameṭṭut yellan tettwakbel s leɛwayed n tmetti. Tameṭṭut ur nezmir ara ad d-niq zdat iɛeggalen n twacult xas akken d izerfan-is i yettwaɛefsen. Tameṭṭut daɣen ur nezmir ara ad d-ehder ɣef iḥulfuyen-is, lebɣi-s, …Iswi-s sǧn but d aseɣli n uzaglu yuɣalen ɣef tlawin yettwaḥeqren.
S tebɣest, Taǧs Amrǧuche terfed imru akken ad d-eslek isefra, inzan d tmucuha, yettawin ttarran ger imawen n yemdanen, deg tittin, acku, melba ma nesmekta-d d akken tasekla n Tefriqt ugafa tella d timawit ǧrale, maci d tirawit ẓcrite.
S taɣect-is qessiḥen am lbeq, tecna, tessaweḍ, ɣer tmezzaɣ n wid ur nessin ad n-  ɣer, ayen tettxemmim, ayen ilaq ad slen. Di ccna, tufa d yiwen webrid yettawin qbala ɣer umezzuɣ n yemɣaren, ilmezyen d imecṭaḥ. Deg useggas n 1939, tebda tgemmer-ed, sya wesya, icewwiqen n leqbayel. Wid terna ɣer wid is-d-eǧǧa yemma-s yakan. Zenia T.
Taǧs teqdec daɣen ula di radiǧ. Tebda di Tunes -Deg useggas n 1944, tuɣal-ed ɣer Lezzayer anda tkemmel ahil-is deg tɣamsa. Tewwi abrid-is di tira, cna, taɣamsa ar almi yewweḍ lmijal-is deg -Tettwamḍel di Fransa.

Qqaren-as Muḥ Afenyan
Kra ufayan akenni
Ma d aglim-is d acebḥan
Ulac acu yettmeni
Ur t-ttḥazen iɣeblan
Efk-as kan učči d tguni

A d nek i d MuḥAfenyan

D aɣrum-nni i ten-yenfan

A sen-d-iqim i tili
I netta d acu i t-yehman

I keč a Muḥ Afenyan?
A sen-yini: nekkini
D nek i d Muḥ Afenyan
Ur tezrim ara kunwi
Aglim-inu d acebḥan?
Mi s-nnan: i keččini?
I keč a Muḥ Afenyan?
Acu ɣ-d-tewwiḍ akkagi?
Tura iwezzan kfan Inna-yasen: nekkini
D nek i d Muḥ Afenyan Tessenm-iyi nekkini
Aglim-inu d acebḥan…
Ass_nni rfan dayennni
Beṛṛa n wexxam i t-ǧǧan
ɣlin-d fell-as s iɛekzan
almi t-rran d aberkan Muḥya Mǧkrane Chikhi
Tamurt n Lezzayer tesfuggel ass-a amulli wis-57 n wegraw n Sumam, i waṭas n yimulihen d tadyant tameqqrant ay d-yellan ass 20 di ɣuct 1956, qrib azal 2 n yiseggasen seld mbaεed tagrawla n Lezzayer « mi tendeh tegrawla «. agraw-a d tasarut ara yesrebḥen, daɣen ara iseggmen abrid srid ɣer timunent n wegdud Azayri, ara yekksen fell-as taɛkumt d tmeḥqranit n uṛumi. Timlilit-a n Sumam i yeṭṭfen azal n 10 wussan i d-yellan deg tmiṭ n tegrawla, ɣas akken imir-n aṭas i iwalan dakken d awezɣi ad d-yili usirem n timunent, acku deg wannar, iɣallen n ucengu aṛumi llan deg yal tiɣmert rnu sɛan xirella n wallalen di lawan anda tagrawla ala ulɣu n 01 di wenbir -Imeɣnasen n tidet ẓran dakken timunent ilaq ad tili acku sɛan tamuɣli lqayen ar sdat, d tamuɣli n yimeɣṛasen imeqqranen yecban Σebban Remṭan d Lɛerbi Ben Mhidi imi d nutni i yisɛan tikti d tmuɣli d wamek ara telḥu tegrawla ɣer timunent, tikti-nsen d tin swacu sreḥben izalukken akked yimḍebbren n waṭas n leǧwayeh n tmurt.
Deg wallen n yimazrayen histǧriens akked yimjuhad yeddren tallit-n ẓran dakken tiɣerɣert n "la Summam" tesɛa azal d ameqqran yerna d tamsalt i yeɛnan lebni n tmurt akked tmetti, agraw-a iseggem tama taserdasant iseggem-as tasertit. Di tazwara timlilit-a tella ad d-tili deg tama n Suq ahras, sey-in ɣur-s deg Skikda maca di taggara tella-d deg tmurt n yizmawen d laman, tamurt n Yizwawen, di taddart n Ifri deg uzellagen deg waɣir n Bgayet amkan-a yettwaɛus sɣur umeɣṛas ameqqran Ɛmiruc d terbaɛt-is. Mi yemmug wegraw-a yeffeɣ-d s waṭas n tezmilin gar-asent:
– Astaɛref s tmurt n Lezzayer s lekmal-is  d awelleh i tikti n Lezzayer Tafransist i tezraɛ Franṣa deg wallaɣ n kra ixuniyen….
– Aserreḥ n yizzayriyen d tzayriyin i ttwaḥebsen ɣef leqdic asertan neɣ aserdasan.
– Astaɛref s FLN d netta i yettmettilen agdud Azayri.
– Asezwer n ṛṛay yettwaṭṭfen daxel n tmurt ɣef win ara yettwaṭṭfen beṛṛa i tmurt awelleh i tdellalt n Ǧamal Abdenaser….
– Asezwer n tsertit ɣef tserdast.
– Asbed n tedbelt administratiǧn ara yesselḥun leqdic gar yimdanen rrcel, timsal ger yimdanen, ajerred n yimsnerniyen, ajmaɛ n tebzar….
– Abṭaw n tmurt n Lezzayer ɣef waṭas n lwilayat.
– Lebni n tigduda n tugdut d tmetti.
Akka ay llant temsal alammi d 19 meɣres 1962, seg yimir ar ass-a tella-d timunent yeffeɣ ufṛansis yekcem-d waɛṛab… d ayen i yeǧǧan targit n yimeɣṛasen-nneɣ teqqim d azgen; Fṛanṣa teffeɣ ma d asbed n tagduda mazal yettnaɣ fell-as Bu tissas… Mhenni Xalifi
Gar temsirin n Zarathǧustra, s yiles n ufelsafi n tmurt n Hitler, l’Allemagne, Friedrich Nietzsche, i d-yessemlal deg udlis umu yextar azwel le titre "Akka i d as-yenna Zarathǧustra", i d-yessuffeɣ ɣer temkarḍiyin les librairies deg useggas n 1883, nextar-ed tuqsa n llifɛa. « Yiwen wass, Zarathǧustra yeṭṭes ddaw tili n tneqlett. Lḥamu tɛedda tilas. Yewwi-d afus-is, isers-it ɣef wallen-is, imir iruḥ deg-sen-t. Llifɛa tusa-d, teqqes-it deg umegre ḍ. Zarathǧustra yuɣwas deg wayen yesɛa deg taɣect-is. Ssem yewwweḍ ɣer wul. Mi d-yekkes afus-nni isers ɣef wudem-is, iwala azrem ɣer tama-s. Aneggaru-agi, ula d netta, yaɛqel allen n Zarathǧustra. Llifɛa yettlen, tebɣa ad terwel. « Ala, i s-yenna Zarathǧustra, mazal ur m-enniɣ ara tanmirt! Tsakiḍ-iyi-d di lawan. Abrid-iw mazal-it ɣezzif ". « Abrid-ik d win wezzilen", i s-tenni llifɛa, le ḥzen yuɣ allen-is. Ssem-iw ineq. Zarathǧustra yebda yettezmumug. « Melmi yemmut "le dragǧn” s ssem n wezrem?", i s yenna. Err-en ssem-im! Imir talafsa tettel ɣef umegreḍ n Zarathǧustra, tessers imi-s ɣef umekkan-nni n tuqsa, u tejbed-ed ssem-is. Yiwen wass, mi d d-yewwi Zarathǧustra awal ɣef tedyan-agi i s-yeḍ i ynelmaden-is ses discittles, ineggura-yagi seqsan-t. D acu i d tamsirt n teqṣiṭ-agi a Zarathǧustra?. Tiririt n Zarathǧustra d tagi: Wid yelhan d iḥeqqiyen qqaren-iyi amhuddu n tsanit. Ma tesɛam aɛdaw, yiwen wass, ur settarrat ara lxir i teqriḥt i wen-yexdem, neɣ m’ulac ad yuɣal di ddel, ad yeḥqer iman-is. Sbegnet-as-id d akken ixdem-awen ayen n lɛali. Ur ttdullut ara, axir ad tfeqɛem w’ad tɛgḍem. Ma yseɣli-d dunnit ɣer lqaɛa, u yebda yttreggim, ur susumet ara, erret-as ṣṣerf s iwulmen.
Ma dagella rran-d fell-awen lbaṭel meqren, erret-asen xemsa nniḍen. Teḥṣam? Lbaṭel yettwabḍan d azgen n wezref demi-drǧit … Di tagara, ay atmaten, ad ken-weṣṣiɣ ad tili-m d iḥeqqiyen lak d iwḥiden les sǧlitaires. Amek yezmer wewḥid ad yettu? Amek yezmer ad yerr?
Awḥid am lbir leqqayen. Yeshel ad tḍeggreḍ ablaḍ ɣer daxel, maca ma yewweḍ ɣer lqaɛ inet-iyi-d anwa izemren ad tt-id-isali. Ur ttawḍet ara awḥid, ma tewḍemt, ihi, arnu neɣ tett.
Akka i s yenna Zarathǧustra.”
Friedrich Nietzsche ilul di 15 tuber aseggas n 1844 di Röcken. Yeggujel asmi yesɛa semmus xemsa n iseggasen. Trebbat-id yemma-s. Yelmed tafelsafit di tseddawiyin n Bǧnn d Leittzig anda id d-yeffeɣ d aselmad ttrǧfesseur n la tthilǧlǧgie taqburt  classique. Yebda yesselmad yesɣar di tseddawit n Bɛle asmi yesɛa rebɛa uɛecrin n iseggasen. Tazmert-is d tin ur nwenneɛ ara maḍi. yesɛa ladɣa ugur n tmuɣli lak d uqraḥ uqerruy la migraine. Taswɛt tḥers-it s waṭas, ɣef ayagi i yeǧǧa axeddim-is deg useggas n 1879, Mi yesɛa xemsa utlatin n iseggasen. ɛecra iseggasen ɣer zdat, teṭṭef-it « une dẓttressiǧn nerḍeuse ". ur s tettaxer ara ar almi yemmut di 25 ɣuct -Zenia T.
Akka i s yenna Zarathǧustra d yiwen wungal ger wungalen yura Nietzsche, anda d yewwi awal ɣef waṭas n isental. Win yebɣan ad yinig lak d Zarathǧustra, ala andemmi ur ittnedemmay ara.
Tamedit n yiḍeli tesuli tedwilt tis 02 n tfaska n ukarmus id-suddes tdukla tadelsant n taddert n saḥel s lemεawna n tdukliwin-nsen yemgaraden d tesqamut n taddert-agi. Leqdic d win yebdan s wudem unṣib ass n 22 almi d 23 γuct yezrins teγzi n 02 wussan. Islam Bessaci
Tafaska-agi tella-d s ddaw laεnaya n wesqamu aγarfan aγiwan n Wizgan, asqamu aγarfan n ugarzu n Tizi-Wezzu d mahla n yedles n lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu, ayagi yella-d s leḥdur n yemḍebren n temnaḍt n Wizgan, ger-aseniselwayen n tγiwanin, Wizgan d Yillulen Umalu, imḍebren n lwilaya nTizi-Wezzu, γef uqaru-s mass Ḥussin Harun aselway n wesqamu aγarfan n ugarzu n Tizi-Wezzu, akk d yemḍebren n yeḥricen yemgaraden. Akken llan di ttiεad iεeggalen n yikkubar n tsartit, ger-asen mass Mǧussa Tamadartaza, aεeggal n wagraw n lluma ukabar n tirni iγallen inemlayen, mass Azǧuaǧu akk d mass tiyeb Mǧkadem, iεeggalen n wesqamu aγarfan aγelnaw i yettmetilen akabar n tsartit Agraw Aγelnaw n Tugdut d waṭas niḍen. Tamesbanit-agi yesduri-tt-id uγarbaz amezwaru Bakuc Muḥend Waεmar n taddert n saḥel, anda i yukkan s nnig n 20 n yemzikniyen id-yussan si temnaḍin yemgaraden n lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu. Ahil id-heggan γef dema d amerkanti yerna d amesbaγur, anda llant temzikniyin ukarmus s leṣnaf-is yemgaraden, timliliyin d isaragen anda id-wwin awal γef azal yesεa ukarmus di temnaḍt leqbayel d wamek ara d-yilli uḥareb fell-as akken ad-teqqim d lγella n lebda, asenεet n zwağ aqbur, d temzikniyin niḍen n lḥirfat ufus, am talaxt, aẓeṭṭa, d wayen icuden γer useḥbiber γef twenaḍt. Dγa tameddit n wass n 23 γuct yezrin, tessuli tezrigt tis ssnat n tfaska ukarmus s yiwet n tmeγra meqren anda i ccnan icennayen meqren n tezlitt taqbaylit, ger-asen Ǧulahlǧu, Lekhdar Sennan, Tanina, Hǧcine Fidili d tarbeεt n ccna n tdukla n taddert n Saḥel, syen tella-d tikci n warazen usebγes i kra n wid yukkan di tfaska-agi. Iswi n tfaska-agi d tikci n tebγest d wafud i wuẓẓu ukarmus akken ad-yenarni yedles n teqbaylit, d tikci n wazal i tgemi. Akken tella d tagnit yelhan i yemdanen akken ad-sεun tamuγli yelhan γef lγella ukarmus d uḥareb fell-as. Leqdic d win iεeddan di tegnatin yelhan nezzah.
Ɛlaḥsab ineɣmisen i d-yekkan seg tmehla tamatut directiǧn gẓnẓrale n AADL deg APS, iwellihen meṛṛa i ara ad tḍefreḍ deg internet d azdam n uneɣmis n wermas accusẓ de recetttiǧn akked ccuṛuḍ n weqbal, d lekwaɣeḍ i yettunefkayen d taseɣṛut n yiseɣ dẓclaratiǧn sur l’hǧnneur. Akken i d-teqqaṛ dima tmehla tamatut n AADL ayen akk i d-yettwaceyyεen sɣur uɣerman citǧyen ad yettwassefqed s telqey, win i d-ibanen ixulef tiwtilin cǧnditiǧns n usuter neɣ yeskaddeb atan ad yebṭel wayen yebɣa yerna ad yettwaεaqeb sɣur teɣdemt justice. Mhenni Xalifi
Taggara ad nerr awellih dakken AADL tessefhem-d s cedda belli tisutriwin yewwi-d ad ttwaḍelbent deg twilayt anda yezdeɣ win terza temsalt, daɣen ala yiwet n tsutert i yettwasemḥen i ubusin cǧuttle.
Mebεed imi d-yerra acḥal d asaru γer teqbaylit, tikelt-a, Samir Ait Belkacem yessezga-d adattter, netta d terbaεt-is, BEBE LILLY γer teqbaylit.
Leqdic-a dayen igerrzen nezzeh imi dγa yeεna arrac imecṭaḥ. Amek wakken neẓra, amur ameqqran n wayen i d-itteffγen s tmaziγt yecγeb imeqqranen. Leqdic am wa, yezmer ad yili d yiwen wallal gar yifassen n yiselmaden n tmaziγt ma bγan ad slemden i warrac idles amaziγ s umata imi ayen i d-yewwi usaru-a icudd γer tmetti ines. Akka, dγa, ara naf kra n tmucuha timeẓẓyanin, kra n tezlatin akked wurar s yisteqsiyen ifessasen γef yidles amaziγ s umata aya akk s ṣṣut n Bellali Fella, nettat d yiwet n teqcict i yuraren deg yisura i d-yerra γer tmaziγt Samir Ait Belkacem i aγ-d-yemmeslayen γef yiswi n ussezgi-agi, yenna-d:’’Bebe Lilly, yuγal-d γer waṭas n tmeslayin, i wacuγer ihi ur t-id-nettarra ara nekni γer teqbaylit ladγa imi annar-agi n ussezgi ha-t-an d asuki? Tis snat, nebγa ad yili i warrac imecṭaḥ d yiwen n ttawil s wayes ara lemden idles d tγerma nsen s wurar akked neccraḥa…’’ Hǧcine.M Bǧusbaine Samir.
Tamhalt n yiniliyen d tin i d-ixelqen lxuf d ccek gar yimjuhad. Tella-d s lmendad n cattitaine Lẓger‶ ass 01 meɣres n useggas n -D yiwet seg temhal i tessemres temhersa tafransist, i wakken ad temḥu tagrawla deg waɣir wis kraḍ, acku twala d akken imezdaɣ n waɣir-a ttwasnen s tebɣest akked leḥmala n tmurt-nsen. Ihi tamhalt-a, tella-d mbaɛd mi i tessexdem temhersa inelmaden akked yigumiyen deg yigen n uslelli aɣelnaw. iwakken ad sɛun issalen ɣef yimjuhad. Maca, imḍebber n waɣir wis kraḍ « Ɛmiruc Ayt Ḥemmudda " ifaq i temhalt-a asmi i t-id-yewweḍ lexbar seg yiɛeggalen n temnaḍt tis ukuẓ, dakken agensas asertan " Si Lḥusin Salhi " iḥemmel aṭas iruḥ ulac isali fell-as. Dɣa, iruḥ " Ɛmiruc " ɣer din yemlal-d aɣellachef n temnaḍt-a « Si Ḥsen Meḥyuz " akked unmaẓul-is « Si Lɛerbi " wekkden-as-d dakken agensas « Si Lḥusin " ur d-iban ara. Anect-a yessekcem asudru ccek deg « Ɛmiruc " belli llan wid i yettaken isallen ɣef yimjuhad i yigen n Fransa, ladɣa mi i yeẓra dakken sani ara yerren ad afen lɛesker iɛuss-iten-id. Rnu ɣer waya, yufa-d deg yiwen n useqqif abri snat n teqcicin i d-yusan seg temnaḍt tilellit dakken imḍebbren n temnaḍt-nni ceyyɛen-tent-id ɣer temnaḍt tis ukuẓ iwakken ad tent-skecmen ɣer tegrawla, acku tamsulta n Fransa tettnadi fell-asent mbaɛd mi i d-rewlent seg lḥebs n Serkaǧi.
