Maca, anect-a ur iseḥḥa ara imi yiwet seg-sent isem-is « Ruza " tbeyyeɛ-d dakken d ″ cattitaine Lẓger″ i tent-id-iceyyɛen iwakken ad as-fkent isallen ɣef tuddsa n yimjuhad deg tmurt n leqbayel, rnu daɣen wekkdent-d dakken « Si lɛerbi " i yellan d anmaẓuladjǧin n yimḍebber n temnaḍt tis ukuẓ n waɣir wis kraḍ ixeddem akked « cattitaine Lẓger " yerna d netta i d ssebba n lmut n ugensas « Si Lḥusin Salḥi " acku d netta i t-ibeyɛen i yirumyen nɣan-t. Ɣef waya, tadyant-a teǧǧa-d aṭṭan meqqren gar watmaten imi ruḥen azal n 400 n yimjuhad deg leɣlaḍ, llan wid i yemmuten llan wid i iɛettben s tiyta ɣas akken ur uklalen ara ayen i asen-yeḍran. Ma d imeḥbas uɣalen imḍebren n waɣir-a ɣef uqerru-nsen "Muḥend u Lḥaǧ serḥen-asen acku faqen d akken d tamhersa i asen-ixedmen tamhalt-a iwakken ad d-xlaq lxuf d ccek d umennuɣ gar watmaten n tegrawla.
Zrin kra n wussan, Ddayxa tettuɣal-itt-id tezweɣ n wudem-is ɣef waya i yerfed ṭṭbib rray ad s-yekkes aceṭṭiḍ-nni amellal yedlen udem-is. Igezzem-it-id s lemḥadrat s temqessin netta ihedder i tmuḍint am wakken d yelli-s tamecṭuḥt: "Ur ttagad, tura ad m-kkseɣ akk ayen yesburen anzaren-im, tura ad ten-twaliḍ, ḥṣiɣ ad m-d-zgen deg lxaṭer”. Lehdur akk i s-yeqqar tejɣem-iten am waman mi ara teffad, ssedhan-tt almi i d-tufa iman-is mebla kra iɣummen udem-is. Teṭall ɣer win n ṭṭbib twala-t yecmumeḥ-d, d ayen i isneqsen cwiṭ seg uɣilif-is. Iweddeɛ-as umsuji s leɛqel lemri, udem-nni daxel-is yettẓiẓi-d ɣur-s cwiṭ cwiṭ almi d-yewweḍ azal n ɛecrin n yiṣenṭimen sdat-s. Mi akken i twala iman-is, imi-s yeqqim yeldi yettaḍsa, allen-is cerɛent teddunt d imeṭṭawen n lferḥ. Temmeɣ ur tuki ɣef ṭṭbib-is tessuden-it deg leḥnak, deg unyir acḥal d abrid nettat teqqar tettales-as i wawal: "Tanemmirt a ṭṭbib! Tanemmirt a ṭṭbib!” Lemri-nni i ɣef trewwel seg wasmi i d-tekker yuɣal ur yeṭṭixir ara fell-as, teṭallay deg-s mebla ɛeyyu. Ad s-ɛerqent kan ad t-id-terfed ad tesmuqel deg wudem n tin i d-yettaḍsan ɣur-s. Teqqar: "Ahat d targit i ttarguɣ, ad d-akiɣ kan seg yiḍes ad waliɣ widak yezgan deg tlemmast n wudem-iw ṭallayen-d ɣur-i s ujqejqej. Din din ad d-terr i yiman-is: "Mačči d targit i tettrguḍ a nneya, cwiṭ-nni n tanzarin yeqmumsen rnant deg ccbaḥa i wudem-im, d ayla-inem, ma d igejduren-nni i tɛebbaḍ azal n tlatin n yiseggasen dayen ddan d yiḍelli. Temmekta-d assen i d-usan yimawlan n Wakli ad tt-xeḍben d wass n uɛeyyen-is. Sin wussan-a ɣazen takwat i lebda deg wallaɣ-is, ur tezmir ara ad ten-tettu. Imeɛraḍen ggten, kra n win yettilin i Dda Ɛacur n At Yiɣil ddan-d d iqeffafen ad fken tiẓri. Akka i d lɛada, win iwalan tislit ad s-ikemmes, ad s-yefk ayen i s-d-tefka nneya-s.
– Ǧttawa/Gatinɛau: 1 TIREGWA – 1519-1112 R.At Bucnan
Buḥu: Atan wwḍen-d d acu ara yeḍrun? Beẓẓa: ad t-ṭṭerḍeq ad ilal ulamek, Aya ziɣ ulac akk deg-k, ma ilul-d ulamek a nniya, dɣa ad teḥbes din,win i d yukin ad yuɣal ɣar yiḍes, tamuɣli ad tiḍyiq, tamussni ad t-idyiq, ulamek ad iger ifurkan, deg wamek ad nuɣal ɣar deffir.
Beẓẓa: Win ur nettaẓ ɣar zdat, ɣar deffir i yettuɣal…a yettwexxir.
Beẓẓa: Akka i yaɣ-d qqaren, yal abrid ara ad aɣ-nehren
Buḥu: Atan diγ wa yebɣa ad aɣ-yessufeɣ leɛqel, ad neffeɣ aglim-nneɣ .
Beẓẓa: Win yeffɣen yeffeɣ, ad yebdu asefreɣ, am wegris ad yessaɣ, amzun zeddig ur yexdim kra. Ur yečči, Ur yesswi, Ur yeṛwi, ulac amdan am netta.
Buḥu: D lekteb ihi, amzun yella win i t-yecban amzun tifeṭ, teṣṣawḍeḍ-as naɣ yesssaweḍ-as win yellan am kečč naɣ am nekk?
Beẓẓa: win yellan am kečč ala win yellan am nekk wamma netta d igenni wi sebɛa yiwen ur yezmir ad as yaweḍ.
Buḥu: d acu i t-ttelliḍ deg uxenfuc-ik ih?
Beẓẓa: tesmektaḍ-iyi-d aṭas aya ttnadiɣ-as-d taziba ara as-d- yekfun ɣar w ass-a ur as-d-ufiɣ ara.
Buḥu: uẓum awal, uɣal d agugam, maca…iiih ad mneɣ ad d ssusmen at tregwa d at ẓegwa, ma d wa xaṭi.
Beẓẓa: Amek tebɣam ad nessusem ima ara tettwaliḍ: imelliẓ yettseddiq i win yerrrwan. Lefḥel yewḥel, leɛqel yehmel, ṣwab yeqqel ɣar lembuqqel d wuffiɣ n leɛqel d win yellan d lɣafel. Amek tebɣam ad nessusem ima ara tettwaliḍ: tadist aɛebbuḍ tugar allaɣ yessaweḍ ɣar uɣunzu n laṣel, win im twehad ad d yeddu d inigi, ad d yeggal amzun yella netta ulac-it, amek ara nessusem ima ara tettwaliḍ: nesenṣel taglimt nsedda adif, nḍegger ticlemt negla s nnif, am win yesɛan am win ur nesɛi, am win yeɣran am win ur neɣ ri am…kif kif lḥasun ur yefri wudi ɣaf yiɣi
Buḥu: d acu n weɣbel i k ikecmen? Akken yebɣu yili: ass-a d ass-a, iḍelli d iḍelli.
Beẓẓa: Ah! Ass-a d ass-a, iḍelli d iḍelli aya ẓriɣ-t! a diɣ netta aqel-aɣ: ula d nekkni am ass-a am yiḍelli anida i aɣ yeğğa yiḍelli i aɣ d-yufa wass-a, nettɣama alama yuɣal wass-a d iḍelli imir ad as neqqar: ah aniwa ara d yerren iḍelli d ass-a, xas neẓra iḍelli ur yezmir ad d yuɣal d ass-a, naɣ ass-a ad d yuɣal d azekka.
Buḥu: amek i yettissinen ih?
Beẓẓa: deg wassen i d nella d nekkni neqqar-as anef ahat ad nissin…akka ara n issin? win nenɣa ad aɣ-d-slalen wis sin naɣ sin nugi ad nissin.
Buḥu: aniwa i ak yeẓran ahat tikelt-a d tagara n lmerta ad d ḥlun wussan-nneɣ ala d ttawin imusnawen.
Beẓẓa:-amzun uqan ɣur-neɣ ima ara ffɣen ɣar lberrani.
Beẓẓa: d tidet, maca wida ass-a fella-k azekka fella-k ma terbeḥ iynes ma texser iynek, a tamusni ur tettwarḍal ara, ur tettnuz ara ma wer tt-tesɛiḍ ara xas ass-a ad tɣilleḍ tuɣeḍ-d azekka ad tafeḍ iman-ik tenziḍ ula d win yuḍnen tabeɛuct…amek ihi? ma ad nwexxer amek ad nqerreb amek ma neqqim di tlemmast ulamek, akken id as-nnan refdeɣ-t yujjaq serseɣ-t yujjaq amek ara as xedmeɣ aya xellaq amek ara nqabel qabel aseggass-a bezzaf i ɛeṭṭel!Ih! teqqarem kan nezdeɣ igelman-nneɣ netta d leḥya i tessetḥam ad tinim neɛya deg-yiman-nneɣ
Buḥu:-Ad aɣ tɛegceḍ kečč-i
Beẓẓa:-Ih nekk amzun ṛwiɣ yegra-d kan kečč ad ak id-rnuɣ iy iri-w ula d nekk lluẓeɣ, ffudeɣ…
Buḥu: ma tebɣiḍ ad teččeḍ susem d taɣ awal anɛam yirbeḥ, awal aẓidan i teṭṭeḍ ula d tasedda, i teg abrid ula deg lebḥer. ah!ad mteɣ d dwa tella! ttnuzun medden nezz, ttderɣilen medden dderɣel, ma yess-i ara twenneɛ a wer s yeg Rebbi akken ara at wenneɛ
Beẓẓa: yaak nniɣ-ak ulamek
Buḥu:-Atan ah ssawḍen-d! ata limer d lebɣi, a wi yufan waqila! Ddan-d akk… amek ay ilaq?
– Aqel-aɣ akk da
-ansuf yes-swen ɣar da ɣur-neɣ amek alammi i ten-id sdukleḍ!
Ilaq: akken twalam nekkni d atmaten, lebɣi-nneɣ yiwen xas ma nemgarrad deg wasmiwen, imi uwḍeɣ nniɣ-asen tazwara kkren-d ɣer-i ad iyi-uwten d wissen id iyi-selken
Buḥu: am i k-id-isellek wissen?
Ilaq:-lebɣi n terwiḥt: yenna-yaɣ-d iwacu ara tennaɣem, kunwi di wissen, ruḥ-t, ass ara temlilem ayen yellan ad teẓrem ssin akin uɣalet-d ɣar wissen
Ilaq: akken ad d-naf amek Ilaq ad imzel waqila.
Limer d lebɣi: limer ilaq i aɣ-d-issefhem tilli i d nedhem wissen
Win yufan: D acu ara k-iniɣ, xas neẓra d atmaten, yiwen wudem, maca ismawen mgarraden nekk d win yufan,win yebɣan ad iyi fhem ad imeyez isem-iw ad yaf d acu-yi.ad d ɣaf d acu i d lebɣi-w.ma d wi yufan yufa yezger ihenna ma d wayeḍ yeṭṭurfa ur yezmir i talwit wala i lfetna win ɣar ittiliɣ efekk-as imi xas ḍlant-tt cwami ifassen-is uɣen d lḥenni
Buḥu: I kečč a limer d lebɣi limer d lebɣi: nekk ur sseɣzafeɣ ara awal, ibeddu-tt-id yilaq yal tamsalt ara d innulfun d netta i d isiɣi, ilaq ima ara yessaɣ, ad d ilal wi yufan, ssin ad d irnu limer dlebɣi, waqila ad d yeḥlelli d netta id gellun s wamek, ulamek ima ara d irnu ɣur-neɣ yettlala-d ulamek, ulamek i teg abrid i wissen, wissen xas yeẓra, yeqqar kan wissen twalam daya i yessen
Buḥu: I tura amek ara d-naf amek, akken ur nettaweḍ ara ɣar ulamek?
Ilaq: akken ad d naf amek ilaq ad nezlu waqila
Limer d lebɣi: acimi ara nezlu waqila
Ilaq: yal abrid ara tt-id sekreɣ d waqila i tt-yesnusuyen d wa id yeslalayen cekk. S kra i ttenɛettabeɣ wa yessenɣal-it
Waqila: ay ilaq a mačči deg yiles igi nxus. Yal yiwen deg-neɣ iwala anida i texreb, ulac win ur neẓri, macca akken nnan a wwah a tasa, azraɛ nessen-as akk, awi-d aniwa ara ymegren, aserwet nessen-as akk, awi-d aniwa ayessizedgen. nekk d aḥezzeb i d-iyi-nnɣan, ttxemmimeɣ ɣaf umenṭas ima ara yeḥsel, wammag mačči d aqedder i d ay-iweɛren
– awal nat wawal, ima ara-d yeffeɣ deg at wawal yessawal i wuzzal, awal yetɣimi d awal timecki ulac aberrez n temsal i wumi-t wawal? Akli Ǧutamazirt x.Y
Yessen Ddayxa m wanzaren n lbaṭaṭa, d tin i d-iɛeyyen, ma d tin ara yeddun d tislit s axxam-is urǧin i tt-iwala. D tin yesɛan tanzarin tiqmumsanin. Nettat terfed aqerruy-is s igenni tessenhaz-is seg zzuxx. Ihi sya d tasawent d kunemti d yemma ara iyi-d-iqedcen. D kunemti deg snat ara icebbḥen i teslit. Ilaq yiwen seg taddart ur iḥeṣṣu amek i giɣ. Assen ara dduɣ d tislit udem-iw diɣen yiwen ur t-ittwali, ad t-iɣumm uqelmun n ubernus ara lseɣ. Amdan wis ukkuẓ ara iyi-iwalin d Akli deg uxxam-is sdat n yinbgawen n tmeɣra mi ara nɛeddi ad nṣewwer deg sin akken ad nesɛu tiwlifin n tissulya-nneɣ i usmekti n wass-nni. Din ara iẓer i tikkelt tamezwarut udem-iw amaynut mi ara iyi-ikkes aqelmun n ubernus-iw. Deg yedra-s akk i giɣ aya wanag wiyaḍ ur iyi-tuqiɛ ara deg-sen. Akli yuklal nnig waya, ḥemmleɣ-t am leɛmer-iw, netta diɣen mačči tikkelt i iyi-d-yenna iḥemmel-iyi. Aṭas i iḥar ɣer temlilit-nneɣ n dima. Malek Hǧud
Ass n tmeɣra yewweḍ-d, d ass n ssebt. Imawlan n Wakli usan-d deg yiṭaksiyen. Irgazen wwten lbarud, tilawin slalwent, Melɛez d Melxir grent-d gar-asent tislit i iɣumm ubernus amellal seg tqacuct n uqerruy-is almi d timceḍt n yiḍarren-is, grent-tt daxel n yiwet n tkerrust i icebḥen am teslit. Deg ubrid ssekkren s tkerrusin-nsen d tyitiwin n lbarud d uslilew yiwen uhetwir annect-ilat. Tameɣra n Wakli ad s-cfun medden, ad d-teqqim deg umezruy n taddart n Tewrirt. Aserbabuɛ-nni n tkerrusin, mi yewweḍ s axxam n Dda Ɛacur, rsen-d akk yiqeffafen d tqeffafin, tislit d tamezwarut. Send ad tezger amnar n uxxam ara yuɣalen d ayla-s tdegger ɣer deffir urawen n waman, terna urawen n leḥlawat d lkawkaw d waṭas n tẓidanin i warrac d teqcicin yeggten deffir-s, akken ad iẓiden wussan-is. Tekcem axxam n urgaz-is dima gar snat-nni n tɛessasin n xwalti-s, s lbarud d uslilew. Tezger afrag awesɛan terra srid s axxam n yinebgawen yebbuḥran imi ldin sin n yisfuyla-ines, teɛna tasga teqqim din. Zenia T.
Zik, akken kan ara d-udum tiqit n lehwa tamezwarut, di tallit n iweǧǧiben, imdanen yak ad fɣen ɣer lexla akken ad cerwen lqiɛan n tzemrin-nsen uqbel ad d-yeɣli uzemmur. Ayagi yessishil-asen ajmaɛ n lɣella-yagi. Tizemrin d-yezgan di tlemmast n teẓgi lɣaba, tteksen-asen-t yak ayen ara sen-d-yasen d aɛewwiq: iḥinṭeḍ, anajjel, tiɛeffert, abuneqqaṛ, azzu, adles, d yemɣan nniḍen d yekren tama n ledra. Tizemrin d yusa-n deg usawen, mi yekfa wefras-nsen-t, xedmen-asen-t aḥeǧǧeṛ, ddaw-nsen-t, s wakal, akken azemmur-nni d iɣelli-n ur yettṛuḥ ara mbaɛid. Akken kra n ledwaṛ, imdanen ak, ameẓyan d umeqṛan, irgazen d tlawin, ad refden tiṣennajin lak d imextafen-nsen akken ad leqḍen azemmur. Tilawin ilaq-asen-t ad kren-t tafejrit akken ad heggin-t imekli ara awin-t ɣer lexla. ṣbeḥ, akken kan ara d-yali yiṭij, lɣaci ad d-efɣen deg ixxamen-nsen. Mkul yiwen anda ara yerr. Wa yettṣubbu ɣer uzaɣaṛ, wa yettali s yinna ɣer wedrar. Iberdan zeɣzɣen, wa yessawal i wa, wa yettṛaǧu wayeḍ. Azemmur, zzik, d tagnitt i yemdanen ur nemzer ara di teɣzi n useggas akken ad mwalin, ad mseqsin ɣef tezmert d tarwa-nsen. Irgazen d nutni i yettezwiri-n ɣer lexla. Mi bḍen ad rnun tirni, ma d asemmiḍ, ladɣa ma tewwet nda deg yiḍ-nni, ad-sbuḥten kran n yesɣaṛen s wayes ara d-caɛlen times uɣur ara qden iḍudan-nsen yerẓa wegris. Mi d-ebḍen yak iɛeggalen n twacult, as mḥajajin i lqaɛa. Mi kfan, ad alin akken ad d-ezwin tazemmurt yellan yuɣ lḥal teḥma. Mi yenṣef was, iṭij di tlemmast n igenni, ad tesleḍ kan i zhir n umextaf d uzemmur m’ara d-iɣelli ɣer lqaɛa, aman yettregrugen deg iɣezṛan, asčewč n yefrax yettferfiren sufella n isekla ṭjuṛ d itercucen, d-ittekken nnig n teḍṣa d laɛyaḍ n yemdanen ileqḍen azemmur. Mi urwen-t tzemrin, imdanen xedmen tiwiza gar-asen, akken ad d-jemɛen lɣella-nsen, ttgabaren igelfan n zarẓuṛ, uqbel m’ad d-eɣlin ideflawen.
Asmi id -as yenna Ccix Muḥend U Lḥusin bab n tmusni i Si Muḥend U Mḥend bab n wawal : «ṛuḥ ak- ineɣ rebbi d aɣrib ", yerra-s ufṣih n yiles: «a nɛam a ccix, deg asqif n ṭmana, ncallah!". S ugacur neɣ s tbut tamusni tenwa, tawenza tufa, dɣa din yemlal wuffir akked uciri, yemlal lweɛd d ummeni! Akka itt-iccer bab n tmuɣli wer teḥbis tillist, akken itt-yebɣa bab n yisefra ur tekbil teswiɛt! Din di Taqa Nat Aḥmed yemlal usekud leqayen akked cihwa n tasa yezan akken ad yilli yinnig ɣer yiwen umṛaḥ yellan d taxamt n leqder akked sser: Asqif n Ṭmana.
Asqif n Ṭmana, lxelwa deg iman n wid yecgen di tregwa n lawan, yewten s telqay di tɣuza n leqrun, yella d taxatemt deg ttemyfkan tamugent leṛwaḥ yesnan d acu i d-innig yifen innigan, ixfawen yesnan abrid yettawin seg yixef ɣer yixef n tmedurt. Asqif n Ṭmana ɣer wid yeɣran tadaxlit, yesnan ad annin adrugen mystAre, ur yelli ara d taqenuzṭ neɣ d tamacahut yesganayen allaɣ, yettaren tidmi deg ugris n waglugel. Asqif n Ṭmana  ɣer wid yesefruyen lbeḍna d tasarut i tellin tiwura i tmuɣliwin akken ad neflent i ddiq n teswiɛt, ad nessrent i tmara n umḍiq. Asqif n Ṭmana ɣer ibaḍniyen yeṣɛa ay din d inumak, ay din d lemɛani. Ula ɣer leǧnas nniḍen, Asqif n Ṭmana yella d lqibla n wid yettnadin ɣef tigelda n yixfawen-nsen akken yid-s ad mlilen amer ad ttaren ddew lebɣi n lebɣi-nsen. Ttnadin fell-as acku ẓran mi tegursel leḥmala n tudert deg ul, sebba-s d akken «Nekk" n umdan yenqedwa ɣer uzabuq n tmerzuga. Deg abrid yettawin yal alles ɣer yiman-is, yewwid umyaru Paulǧ Cǧelhǧ ɣef yinnig it-yeṣawḍen ula d netta ɣer Usqif n Ṭmana yecehwa wul-is ikenfen s tirgin n wayen yellan d udrig. Innig-agi yellan d innig n tudert  neɣ n yal tudert yemeslay-d fell-as deg ungal-ines angaru «Aletth" i d-yefɣen ɣer tizrigin « Flammariǧn". Ahat win ur nessin  inumak n tudert yemzer ad yinni: «D acu i d- l’ Aletth"? Aletth d anamek nniḍen n lexlwa wuɣur tunnag tidmi n Ccix Muḥend U Lḥusin, tin deg yezdew Si Muḥend U Mḥend akken ad tesemlil deg yirebi-s imedyazen, izemniyen, imusnawen yecban Sliman Azem, Yusef U Qasi, Lala Xedija tukrift, Ccix Ccrif n temlilin, Sidi Ḥend U Yusef, Ccix Ameqran…. Yuɣ lḥal Jǧrge Luis Bǧrges  d amyaru, d amedyaz n tmurt n l’Argentine yefka-d anamek n l’Aletth yenna: « l’Aletth d taxatemt tubrint, akdu diametre ines ur tettɛeddi-ara di tehri azal n ssin neɣ tlata isentimen, maca tujma tigenwit tekcem s lekmal deg umeqyas-is. Di reḥba-agi tudert tettcali s lqed n teɣzi-s akked d telqay n tehri-is. Kra yellan d taɣawsa ijebden ɣer wer tagara tuffa leqrar di reḥba-s, tettban ay ansi itt-id yemuqel yiẓri si yal ixef n ddunit". Deg ungal Paulǧ Cǧelhǧ, yegger deg yiwen yinnig ara t-yawwin seg yixef n l’Eurǧtte alarmi d wul n la Sebẓrie, akken ad ijab Asqif n Ṭmana  win id as -iwulmen ɣef tecweḍ tasa-s. Anadi n Cǧelhǧ yesmendig-it lḥewj n tusna akked d fad n tririt ɣef tuttriwin i tezzin deg alaɣ-is yettfurun, yecehwan tidet melulen am lekfan. Innig n Cǧelhǧ iswi-s d tegelda n yixef-is akken ad yuɣal fell-as d netta i d-agelid. Di tmacint id at yewwin akken ad yemlil d twenza-s, tesemlal-it lqedra netta d yiwet n tlemẓit « Hilal " ara s yeldin tabrujt s wacu ara yedlu ɣef kra n tufirin yellan di tmedurin-ines yezrin. Innig-a  ur nefki anzi i wiyaḍ yesɛa tazwert deg tallit n yimir, yeṣawwaḍ ɣer yiḍeli, yesmirjiḥ ɣef uzekka, yettraṣi leqrar deg ass-a. Am yiḍeli, am ass-a,am uzekka d lḥewj n tusna n yiman-nneɣ acu i d – Nekk i- yesmendigen tikli-nneɣ ɣer tira n twenza akken ad nemlil d lemri ur neskidib, ur nezuzur tikerkas ɣef akal n yiman id- aɣ izedɣen. Iman yellan d imezgi, iman yellan nnig urar n wussan, nnig timurṣaḍ n lawan. Tikwal deg ubrid n tudert nettiḥwij win ara neɣ tin ara yesiɣen tafat tafat n yal taɣawsa, n yal aḥulfu, n yal tamusni akken akukru d temlilit d yiman-nneɣ ad yer aḍar amer ṛuḥ imir ad taf tilleli ara s yillin d abeḥri s wacu ara d teceɛcaɣ tirget n tudert yegunin di lkanun n lebda! Tirget ur nxetti, deg Asqif n Ṭmana id- as yegga leqrar Ccix Muḥend U Lḥusin. Din id-as-iweha nafex  azwu yesmendigen isufa n lebɣi. Tirget yettaren ṛuh d amudir i lebda, deg Asqif n Ṭmana i- yenwa Si Muḥend ad yid-s yemlil. Tirget n tmusni deg «l’Aletth" i –inudda fell-as Paulǧ Cǧelhǧ, akken d yixef n yexf-is ad yezdi. Mi tebren tasarut, ayen yellan, yettifrir-d am zit ɣef waman. Win yenwan tudert tesḥurejdul, wina yegger iman-is deg yir iɣilifen yefka lmendad i tiyersiwin ixenqen iman. Izuraz yeqnen tidmi ɣer ufurk n ustehzi, am anza, sutren- andaq! Tabɣest yettawin ɣer tilleli yiwen id udem-is: d tamuɣli wer akukuru si txatemt deg tetturar ddunit ɣer wudem n Yiman anamek aḥeqqi n «Nekk". Asqif n Ṭmana d texlijt yettawin iman n wid yebɣan talwit,di yal tudert, ɣer tidet n yiman-nsen.. ddin i yella L’Aletth,d ttin i d -Asqif n Ṭmana, din i d- Tafuɣalt, din i yezdeɣ leqrar.
Amek i tesneɣ d tamacahut, amek yid-s lḥiɣ d tamacahut, ɣef acu nelḥa d wayen ɣef i nemdarkel teɣzi n wussan d tamacahut. Netta d Saɛid Iɛamrac amedyaz, amyaru, aseqqat sculttteur, ameɣnas n tmurt n leqbayel tamnaḍt n At Jennad.
Awal i tezzin deg immi-s seg assen deg i t-sneɣ d win-a n Sliman Azem: « azger yeɛqal gma-s/ d win wukkud yetmaḥen ". Asekkud wuɣur yezzi yiẓri-s: d tamazɣa, d tamaziɣt, d tugdut akked izerfan n umdan. Ayen si tneggi tasa-s d-isefra, d-aẓawan, d-aselqqat ɣef usɣar, d-amezgun. Amek i tedda tikli-s d timeɣnast, d ameyyez akked tira.
Akked Saɛid Iɛamrac, nella seg wid ihaḍren i tllalit n ukabar n RCD akked Mǧhand Ixerban, Rafil Meẓian, Daḥman Nafaɛ, Ɛali ideflawen. Lwaḥid nnega lsas i ukabar -agi deg At Jennad, imi tuget n tigezmiyin n ukabar sectiǧns d ssin yidneɣ isen-t nella di lmendad. Ayen-nni n leqdic yella-d acku Saɛid Iɛamrac yumen s tugdut, s tatrarit mǧdernitẓ s tilaysiyit  laicitẓ akked tmaziɣt. D wigi i d-isufa i t- yesmendagen akken ad yefk leɛtab i terwiḥt amer lbaṭel yesburen akken tamurt si 62 ɣer yimir ad yezwi ucḍaḍ-is.Leqdic am win mebla cceḥa i-yeṣawḍen Saɛid Iɛamrac ad yettwafren sɣur imeɣnasen n ukabar i tugdut akked yidles akken ad nettawafen ɣer tama n Ixerban, Rafil Meẓiane, Mǧhand Tiwcicin ɣer uswir cǧngrAs amezwaru n ukabar id yellan deg aɣram aɣlan ttalais des natiǧns di club des ttins.
Akked Saɛid Iɛamrac, nebedd ɣer tifranin timenza id yellan menbaɛd tulya ɣef tugdut, d-asget n-ikabaren multittartisme akked tilelli n tisertit. Lwaḥid i nella u deffir tufɣa n ukabar awḥid FLN seg tɣiwan n Timizart i tikelt tamazwarut.
Nnig timaɣnest tasartit, Saɛid Iɛamrac yella diɣ d anaẓur. D acennay   ɣer ass-a ttmektayeɣ-d ccna-nni id yessuli zdat-i umu yeqqar: « ay afrux-iw/affeg ɛalli d asawan/ ay afrux-iw /siwel i wigad-nniḍen. " Meḥsub ad yesiwel i yimaziɣen n wawras, n Ɣerdaya, Imuceɣ, Irifiyen…. Yella diɣ d-amedyazamek ara nettu asefru-ines « salima tineslemt ",neɣ « acu yellan deffir lemri "…. Yella daɣen d-aseqqat mačči d-izli n tisbediyin id yeǧǧer ɣef lluḥ . Saɛid Iɛamrac yella diɣ d-amyaru imi yura yerna yesazreg ungal umu yeqqar « tasga n ṭlam "  yellan deg ungalan imenza id yefɣen s taqbaylit .
Leḥmala-ines ɣer idles, teǧǧa-t ur yettwexir-ara zdat lwajeb. Cfiɣ amek yefreḥ asmi id as-nnena nekk akked Nuredin: « ayen akka aɛami Saɛid ur d-nesllalay-ara ula d nekni yiwet n tadukli tadelsant ara yillin am tin id yenulfan di Micli tadukli Si Muḥend u Mḥend i-yellan deffir tafeska tamazwarut n tmedyazt tamaziɣt deg At Iraten, Micli, Tizi Racced ddew leɛnaya n tadwilt leqlam d umedyaz id yettheggi di radyu tis snat di lawan-nni Agaruj Rabaḥ. Dɣa akken i teḍra, ur nɛaṭel-ara nesbeded yiwet n tadukli i mazal teqdec ɣer ass-a n wussan deg uḥric n yidles umu nefka isem n-umedyaz n At Jennad yettwasnan Yusef u Qasi. Tadukli-agi tesnejmaɛ azal n 400 iɛagalen asmi akken id tellul, u tezdi yakk lɛarc n At Jennad imi tasqamut id as-yellan d-aqaru tesɛa iɛagalen seg Aɣrib, Freḥa, Timizart. Asqamu –agi d netta id ifernan Saɛid Iɛamrac d aselway amezwaru n tidukla id illulen Yusef u Qasi.
Di lhejna n leqdic n yimir xas akken xuṣen wallalen akked Saɛid Iɛamrac nesbeded diɣen yiwet n tarbaɛt n umezgun « Tacemlit " id yuraren i tikelt tamewarut tacquft: « aqcic d uɛatar " id yettwaksen si tizlit tecna terbaɛt n Imziɣen Imula. Tamezgunt-agi yewwin arraz di tfeska tamenzut n umezgun amaziɣ « Sliman Azem " deg Tizi-Uzzu, yella-as di lmendad ɣer tama-nneɣ Mustafa Nat Daḥman, Ibucicen Ɛacur, Nuredin At Sliman deg uraran izaffanen: Ait Ggeni Saɛid Husin, Ɛarqub Ɛabdela, Izuran Mǧḥamed, Rihan Meẓiane, Igerɛisi Saɛid, Hamduduc Ɛumar.
Akked Saɛid Iɛmrac, nemmeɣ tamurt n Leqbaye tirn. Ur neǧǧi amdiq. Si Lerbaɛ Nat Iraten ɣer Bgayet ɛadi seg uẓeffun ulac anda ur d neɣ ri ara isefra, ur nexdim ara isaragen ama ɣef tugdut ama ɣef yidles. Maca aṭan yegguni amadyaz-nneɣ . Xas akken yettemɛaber yid-s, yal mi ara tesemlil tagnit awal-is i tezzi ɣef « tesga n ṭlam ". Ṭasga n ṭlam d-ungal id yettheggi yakken si teqriḥt n lqerḥ-is. Yettawi-t deg allaɣ -is anda yedda am akken tettawi tmeṭṭut mmi-s di taddist. Am win yettumelken anda yelḥa yewwi lɣerza-s yid-s.
Aṭas n tikwal is-uɣalen tijmilin i Saɛid Iɛamrac. Ayen-nni d lawajeb i wakken kra n win id yewwin tafa ara yesnernin ijujaḥ n yidles aqbayli d awezɣi ad teseblaɛ tatut. Tadukli tadelsant itran n taddart Imalusen  d taddart n Sɛid Iɛamrac tesmakted amdyaz-nneɣ durt-agi yezrin deg yiwet n tajmilt is yuɣalen s demma. Tajmilit-agi tjemɛad kra n wid yesnen anaẓur n At Jennad Saɛid Iɛmarc gar-assen Arkǧub Abdellah yellan d anelmad-is deg aḥric-agi n yidles  Ɛabdslam Ɛabdenur, Nuredin Nat Sliman, Dahmani Belɛid, iselwayen n tiɣiwant n Uɣrib, Freḥa akked Timizart, imdebran n yidles n Tizi-Uzzu akked waṭas n yemdanen i t-iḥamlen. Deg tajmilt agi tella-d timzikent id yewwin ɣef leqdic n unaẓur akked isurag ɣef win yedran tudert n uferṭetu. « Aferṭetu iḥamlen tudert deg iḥarqen, yetthimin seg urti ɣer wayeḍ, yesmirjiḥen ɣef ifurkawen n tayri akked leḥmala. Awecriḍ yesudunen tiǧeǧǧigin yeccucfen s liqa n thuski. Afarṭetu teɣwa cbaḥa, alarmi d-asmi i-iwella amcirqi n lamba yettreqriqen, deg akken tettfeǧǧig yenwa-tt d tageǧǧigt n tamsunt. Yemmeɣ umeɛcuq n thuski akken a tt-yesriḥ, ziɣ d tafat m lesmum tewtit ɣef leɣder, din ifarawen-is tesɣar. Rɣan ifariwen, uɣalen d-iɣiɣden, ddan d tɛajajt id ṣuḍen.. ullin ɣer tignawt anda ṭalayen ala wid id yettmakatayen 1 ".
Ait Slimane Hamid
Ait Meslayen yessaweḍ leɛfu n Rebbi ass 21 deg waggur n dujember 2000, mbeɛd 56 n yiseggasen n ccna d yinig exil. Yettwamḍel deg taddart-is, ddaw lemqam n Yemma Tagenturt, anda tella tiddukla tadelsant tanaddalt i yeddmen isem-is, i yuγen tannumi tettarra-as tajmilt yal aseggas. Sytthax Y.
Gar wayen yecna: ’Wa ad d-yerren zzman-ik ay ajenwi; ad ak-nketti; alama tewwḍeḍ s iγes; wa ad d-yerren Ʃmiruc ad iwali; Ḥmed Umerri; nnif deg tuddar yekkes; tamurt-nneγ teqqel i lefḥel d ilili; mi ara t-id-yali wawal; ad t-neɛzel weḥd-s; mmuten akk yirgazen iγer nettcekti; neggra-d nekkni; ur nemzil ur nemmurḍes’’ … T Larbi Hǧcine M.
Deqs n tmeγriwin id-ittewheggan aseggas-a sγur tidukliwin yemgaraden ama di tmurt-nnaγ ama di tmura n lbarani d tmura n tmazγa sumata, ilmend n useggas amaynut n yimaziγen -Dγa tiddukla tadelsant Tiεwinin n taddert n Wizgan, thegga-d yiwen n leqdic s wazal-is, s yiwen n wahil d amesbaγur γef teγzi n 02 wussan, ideg llant temzikniyin yegaraden am ṭṭebqat n wučči i tt-gen imaziγen-nneγ γef demma n yennayer, tiγawsiwin tiqburin, idlisen d ttsawaṛ d waṭas niḍen.Ass n 11 yennayer, i yellan d imensi n yennayer, tella-d sbaḥ temzizelt n tzaburt i yinelmaden n yeswiren amezwaru d ulemmas, syen yella-d yiwen usarag γef umezruy n yennayer id-yefka uselmad n tmaziγt mass Brahim Bessaci. Tamedit n wass tella-d llweεda meqran « imensi n yennayer ", anda imezdaγ n taddert n Wizgan fursen tagnitt-agi ideg temlal tasa d way turew.
Ma yella deg ass wis 02, ass n 12 yennayer i yellan d ixef n useggas amaynut imaziγen 2964, tella-d yiwet n temlilit n tmedyazt sγur imedyazen ger-asen, Fahim MessaǧudAne, Sǧuad Akǧu, Said Hamǧum, Amar Akkǧu d massa Bellabas n temnaḍt n Wizgan, akken illant 02 n tmedyazin niḍen tigi d Tala n wawal n temnaḍt n Tubiret, d massa Attǧuchi Assia yiwet n tmedyazt u d tamyarut n temnaḍt iεeẓẓugen i ixedmen ibudan s uzenzu i wedlis-is n tmedyazt. Leqdic d win i ikemlen tamedit n wass, anda id tella usenεet n yiwet n tecquft n umezgun n tarbaεt n At-yiraten. Γer tagara, yella-d tikci n warazen usebγes d igardasen usenmar ikra n wid yukkan di leqdic-agi, xarsum inelmaden yukkan di temzizilt n tzaburt n tmaziγt, i usebγest n tutlayt-nnaγ.
Acu i d yennayer?
Yennayer d ass amezwaru n useggas imaziγen, yebdan lewhi n 590 uqbel talalit n sidna Σisa, aseggas-nni i yerbeḥ ugellid Cacnaq ṭrad i d-yellan gar-as d ifarεunen di Maṣer, mbaεd tagelda tis -Yennayer d agur yefilliten i lxir, rrbeḥ, lerẓaq, talwi, imi t-sfuggulen imaziγen. Amek i d-yettili usfuggel n yennayer? Aṭas n wansayen i d-icudden γer yennayer, xeddemen imensi n yennayer neγ llan wid yeqqaren imensi bu sebεa isufar. Zellun iyuzaḍ, dγa zik yal aεeggal s uyaziḍ-is, yernu yal yiwen deg-sen ma yewweḍ 17 neγ 18 iseggasen ad yezlu i yiman-is. Xeddmen lwaεda swayen zemren. Mačči d aya kan, llan wansayen nniḍen am ttesḍila tamezwarut i weqcic amectuḥ akken ad yeğhed ucebbub-is. Xeddmen taswiqt anda aqcic ad yawi aqerru n wezger akken ad yuγal d aqerru n wexxam. Islam Bessaci
Ihi aseggas-nwen mara d-amegaz i yal amaziγ anda yella, anda yebγu yilli.
H. Tassadit, s wurfan, tcerreg tamesmizwert ǧrdǧnnance  i s-d- yura umejjay n tlawin, terra-t d tawamust gar iḍuḍan-is imir t-deqqar-itt akkin ɣer lebɛid. Argaz-is, yellan deffir-s, ula d netta, yettban ɣef udem-is yefqeɛ. Isaɣ igirru, ɣefumnar n tawwurt n umejay, ibedd yesikid akkin akka yetḥayer amzun ɛarqent-as. Tassadit teneqlab ɣer ɣer-s tenna-as: "tlezmi tkefart ad-as tinniḍ si tmaɛamert id neffeɣ neɣ ɣer ccix n lǧemaɛ mačči seg axxam n tadawsa neɣ ɣer umejay. Ṛṛuḥ kečč-nni ad tfehmeḍ kra ɣer wigi! Ur ẓriɣ ara nekk acu-tt leqraya-agi ɣran, neɣ amek ttxamimen. Lhem-nsen ak-sneṣlen deg texriṭ-ik wama aselak si lhija-nsen ulac! ”.
Taluft n Tassadit d talluft n waṭas n tullawin izewǧen yemdarkalen ɣef uggur n uɣri n -taddist aḍǧrtement dagi di tmurt-nneɣ . Tassadit di lɛamer-is 46 isaggasen, limer d lebɣi tili teḥbes tarwa imi tewweḍ ɣer leɛmer anda tullawin teɛqarent menǧttause , meɛna netta-t tella seg tid- mazal ttarwent xas akken teselḥa di leɛmer. Argaz-is Mǧhand yesɛa 59 isagassen. Iban kan ɣef leḥsab leɛmer-nsen di ssin yidsen yeẓay fell-asen ad rrnun dderya ɣef widen sɛan yakka. Amek ara d rrabin aqrur nutni ibedden ɣef umnar n tawser? Di tmurt irebḥen anect-a kan tikli di leɛmer weḥdes gelɛum akken amejay ad ɛiwen Tassadit ad teɣri taddist-is…lemeɛni aya iḍeru-d kan di di tmura irebḥen anda zegiren leɛqal ɣef timucuha nniḍen.
Nnig leɛmer, Tassadit tuḍḍen. Ul –is yesxenfat, tleḥu s ddwawi. Idamen ḥerṣen iɣerbn n-izuran-is, la tensiǧn-ines ur terkid-ara.tikwal tettali tikwal tettṣubbu. Di tmurt-irebḥen, anda d ṣṣwab i-tt-iḥekmen mačči d timucuha nniḍen, ɣef aya kan  aṭan tesɛa Tassadit amejay n wul i tt-yettdawin as-id yefk iccer n lkaɣeḍ akken a tawwi ɣer uxxam n tdawsa akken as sḥebsen taddist-nni… meɛna i gar-nneɣ akked ṣṣwab d lmeɛqul di tmurt-nneɣ ! Mi seqseɣ Tassadit nniɣ-as amek akka? Tenna-k s nehta: " mi rziɣ ɣer umajay n wul iyi-ttdawin, akken kan id as ḥkiɣ, yebda yettraru ɣef yicer n lkaɣeḍ. Nekk ɣileɣ d tebra-tt ara y-id yarru akken ad seɣliɣ taddist, ziɣ netta d ddwawi i yebɣa ayi- ɛiwed. Asmi id –as sefehmeɣ acu ttraǧǧuɣ s ljiha-s yenna-yid s wurfan:” ala anect-a ur xeddemeɣra nekni. I ma ikteb-am a ttemteḍ, mačči d nekk ara kem-id yesuksen, wig d lecɣel n Ṛebbi!”
Ayen tettqabal Tassadit, aṭas n tullawin nniḍen I yemdarkalen ɣef uɣbel-is. Kra seg-sen-t  t-id ur neɣ ri –ara, neɣ tawacult-nsen ur tweɛa-ara  ma yella ur mmuten-ara s taddist-nni, ttesriḥint ṛṛiha n lmut s lqerb.Cedda sɛdayent ala win yewten d win yettewten i yeẓran acu-t.Ɣef aya tuttra teḥalalid iman-is kan: "Iwumi amejay, ma yella ur d uffin-ara ɣer-s imuḍan lejwab ttraǧǧun i wuguren-sen akked tifrat i saramen s ljiha-s?” Hakima B, tenna-k: " armi yemmut llufan deg tɛabut-iw i qeblen imejayen n terwa a-tid seɣlin, meḥsub selḥeɣ s taddist ugar n setta waguren, nutni zṛan si tezwara ad yemmet meɛna uggin ad xedmen ttawil akken, ayi ɛetqen si leɛtab meskud ur yegma-ara. Ɣef aya assen deg i-tid seɣlin wallaɣ lmut zdat wallen-iw, ur ẓriɣ ara amek ara tedṛu yidi limer ur yemmut ara lufan-nni, limer yeṣaweḍ ṛṛuḥ ar d- illal ccek-iw ad yeglu yis-i!”
Timsal am tigi mačči yiwet mačči snat. Tawes netta-t s ljiha-s ksed anda ur tuzzilara akken ad teɣri, ur teǧǧi Bgayet, Tizi-Ǧuzǧu, Lẓẓayer, anda tbedd ala asɛezeg ɣef i tecceg. Zdat-as medlen tiwwura. Xas akken netta-t tettdawi deg ṣbiṭar akaram dǧssier tettawi yid-s ur as-d yelli ara d tesriḥ akken a teɣri. Tadyant n Tawes fell-as tura rebɛa n-isaggasen. Mi ttesteqseɣ amek texdem tenna: " cwi kan yella ttawil n Net. Nnudeɣ di gǧǧgle ufiɣ ziɣ llant tiɛaqucin mi ten-teswa tmeṭut yallan s taddist, lufan yellan deg uɛabud-is ad yeɣli. Maca dwa-agi ur tettnuz ara di tmurt-nneɣ , armi ceyɛeɣ ɣer Franṣa iyi-tt-id wwin. Iḥattem fell-i lḥal teɣri taddist-iw s yiman-iw deg axxam. Cwi kan aragaz -iw yeṭṭef-iyi-d tama, yella yiǧdi di lmendad.”
Aya irkel acku amagrad  article 304 n tangalt n usaḍuf yeqqar: " kra n tmeṭṭut ara yeɣrin s rḍa-s neɣ melba lebɣi-s neɣ kra n win ara tt-iɛiwnen akken a teɣri &amtt;nbstt,; ama s uɛaqar neɣ s ddwa, neɣ takriḍt lexṭiya-s d lhebs azal n useggas ar xemsa n-isaggassen.” S waka ihi kra n temeṭṭut yellan s taddist ma yella tegzem-itt d ṛṛay a teɣri ay akken tebɣu tella sseba I –ihattmen fell-as anect-ten, yegguni lḥebs akked lexṭiya. Ahat d lqanun-agi i-yeǧǧan tuget n tlawin ad ɛamden ad ṭiwlent tudert-nsent wala ad ɣrint taddist xas akken ṣṣeḥa-nsent ur tezmir ara i wayen-nni i terwa. Maca, xas lqanun yeseḥres, llan-t diɣen tid akken yebɣu yilli s tufra seɣlayen taddist-nsen-t imi mu mačči akken iban kan d tudert-nsen s wacu ttqemirent.
Xas akkan aɣeri igedel-it lqanun di tmurt-nneɣ , di tillawt dayen nniḍen. Ɣef akken id qqaren leḥsabat unṣiben  statistiques ǧfficielles  azal n 8000 n uɣeri i- yettilin deg useggas di tmurt n Lẓẓayer. Gar anect-a yak 200 ɣer 300 s yettili s- tufra. Azal n 20 n tlawin i yettmattaten acku ɣrint taddist-nsen-t berra n leɛnaya n imajayen yetukelfan s wenect-a. Ihi ɣef akken nettwali xas lqanun iḥarem aɣeri aṭas n tullawin i tettrara tamara akken ad ɣrint taddist-nsent. Sebba-t iten-t yettawin mgaradent. Tikwal d-aṭṭan iten-yetṣawaḍen ɣer din. Tikwal diɣ ɣer tilmeẓyin ur nezwij –ara  d leḥya imi agrud id sɛant di tɛabbut-nsen yella-d berra n umetṛaḥ neɣ ahat yettuḥatem fell-asen-t s tɛedya. Di tmeti-nneɣ anda lɛib akked usweɛdi yezga yeṭṭafer tameṭut, anquqel n yixef n tullawin terra tamra ad ɣrin d- anquqel ur nesɛi tamtil. Tikwal, anec-ten,yeṣṣaweḍ-iten-t ɣer timenɣiwt n yiman-nsen-t. Tuget di lawan, tettefed tmeṭṭut iman-is wehḍes i tettqazem uggur-agi, imi ur d ttaf leɛnaya la ɣer imawalen-is, la ɣer leḥbab-is. Aɣeri yecba lɛar di dhen n tuget deg lɣaci. D lɛar? Izmer lḥal skud nebɛed ɣef talluft! Qarren i yeẓran ala win ijerben, qqaren diɣ win yeṭtṣen di trekna yeqqar-as cetwa ḥalwet. Timsal akken ibɣu seɛbent, ala s lemɣiḍa, s leɛaqel, akked rẓana id ttafent tifrat. Timsal akken ibɣu qeriḥit, ala s tayri i ttnefsusint. Deg anect-a yakk ahat d tayri i-ixusen di tmeti-nneɣ armi nettuɛalaq ɣer ifurkwan n regmat akked ustehzi s wid ur nuksen iten-yuɣen.
Ait Slimane Hamid
Aṭas n yizzayriyen yeqqaren lakul-nneɣ yeḥfa. Aṭas daɣen i inudan ad ẓren d acu i t-yesseḥfan d wamek ara s-yekkes sḍiḍ. Wa iwala tlaq la refǧnte, wayeḍ yenna-k tamsalt-agi tcu-d, carrẓment, ɣer ttrǧjet de sǧciẓtẓ…
Wigi ǧnt tǧut faux!
D timqerqert i yesseḥfan lakul! Heureusement, faqen-as ineɣmasen n Ennahar, ad ten-iḥrez, Rebbi. Selǧn ineɣmasen-a, tecrured, s tufra, temqerqert en questiǧn alarmi d-ḥella amkan deg wedlis n weswir wis-4 n uselmed alemmas. Yewham Ennahar amek i ɛessasen n tuqubet ur faqen ara i la dẓesse grenǧuille Imi d-terwel seg la mythǧlǧgie, terra s aɣerbaz azzayri ad tessexseṛ ṭbiɛa i warrac d tullas.
Mais tura, ifuk rebbi lḥif. Si sya d afella ad nesɛu lakul d nnefṣ d xemsa uɛecrin. Ladɣa imi d-gren iman-sen Cheikh Chemseddine, d jemɛiyet el ɛulama el muslimin.
Terminẓ ad tuɣal temqerqert s amdun. Ula d iselmaden ad uɣalen s axeddim: yefta-yasen-d Uneɣlaf n lumur n ddin, belli la grAḍe-agi d leḥram.
Cukteɣ belli tella temqerqert-nniḍen d-inesren seg la mythǧlǧgie, terra s allaɣ n Uḍebbal en chef n FLN.
Cukteɣ daɣen, tefrurex temqerqert-a. ma dɣa d sseḥ tefrurex, atan ihi d taqeḍit n temqerqrin
yettenfufuden am tmest ddaw walim..
Ad yeṣṣer Rebbi tameddit!
T. Ǧuld amar
Afus d afus kan ur yelli d ayen nniḍen. Am wakken i t-id- yesefhem usegzawal, afus d agman ǧrgane i d-yezgan ɣef yixef n yiɣil, agman-agi yella i unerfud neɣ i useqdec n tɣawisiwin yetteḥwiji umdan di tudert-is. Akkagi i d as-tga tudert udem. D wagi i d ameqyas deg nniqal tenwa a tecbek. Maca afus ur yeqqim ara kan d alqaf aḥerfi am akken i d as-tega tillin ddunit, imi timeti tbeddel-as azal, teskecm-it deg urekti n lebɣi yetthuzun neɣ yesnuɣnuyen amdan di tmeddurt-is. Deg akka, ɣer yal agdud ad nnef mačči d-izli n inumak i-yewwi uffus, mačči d-izli n tugniwin wuɣur yeṭṭeqir lewhi. Affus yekcem, melba iḍaren, ɣer yal aḥric iccuden ɣer tudert n umdan ama deg ayen yeqnen ɣer tasertit, ɣer ddin, ɣer tayri, ɣer tadukli, ɣer lexdaɛ d wayen yakk yefkan lmul i temɛict n yemdanen. Affus yetturar netta d imdanen urar n tudert akked lmut, yecfag tillin-ines ɣer tillin n imadanen d yegduden akken bɣun illin anda bɣun ddren. Deg akka ad nnef ulac tasekla ur nesxdem affus akken ad bnun tugninwin ara yegen udem i lḥir akked lhejnat yesmendigen iɣerfan. Lḥir d lhejnat yeṣawaden tikwal timetiyin ɣer cwal akked trad. Affus ma yeẓẓel ijemɛed ɣer-s yal asafer yeggan lmendad i tudert, yeqqar yiwen unzi aselti: « ma neldi ifassen, iɛaqayen n ujdi n ṣeḥra merra ad kecmen. Ma nekres ifassen ala kra iɛqayen ara d yeqqimen ". Dima deg unamek n wawal yeqqer yiwen anzi ataram: « akken ibɣu yeẓmed uffus, ijdi iragel si gar iḍuḍan". Yella diɣ anzi nniḍen si tmurt n Jattǧn id-as yeqqaren: « ttif xir affus yeččuren d tayri wala affus yeččuren d cci ".
Di tmurt n Maṣer qarren: « acmumeḥ n udem yif acmumeḥ n- ifasen " am akken qarren diɣ Irusiyen: « wiyak ad teǧǧeḍ lmus gar ifassen n-umdan yesḍen". Deg aḥric nniḍen qarren diɣ irusiyen: « ifasen mellulen ḥamlen lqdic n wiyiḍ ". Di tmurt n Lhend qarren « argaz melba leḥab am uffus aẓelmaḍ melba ayefus". Si ljiha-nsen udayen qqaren « ur ttek-ara affus i yir derya, annef-as a tɛum weḥdes ". Ihi ulac lǧens ur nesexdem ara "affus” deg lemtul-is akken ad yebnu iɣerban n tidmi-ines i waken as- id iban ubrid yettawin ɣer yimal. Tasekla taqbaylit ula d netta-t tesexdem u teseqdec awal n " uffus” deg izli n yeḥricen. Dɣa neqqar ula d nekni ɣef win I tewlen di lebni « affus-is d abenay", neqqar ɣef taqcict i tawlen deg leqdic: «d tumɛint ifassen ", Afelaḥ iteẓun s lmun neqqar fella-s: «affus-is yettleqim", neqqar diɣ ɣef win ibedden ɣer cɣel: «affus yettnawel deg lerbayeḥ", neqqar diɣ «affus yettaru" neɣ diɣen «affus-is teẓẓu". Yal tikelt amek nesexdem di tutlayt-nneɣ awal n-uffus akken ad nesllal inumak leqayen ara yekken nnig tigzi, nnid iḥulfan amer ixef ad yedlu ɣef tidet tuffir ur yezmir ad iɛabbi wawal n menwala, wawal n kul-ass. Tikwal ɣer leqbayl seg "uffus” id yekka lbaṭel, d netta i t-yettnawalen. Akken ad tban tikti-agi akken ilaq neqqar-as: «affus yakaten". Neqqar diɣ akken ad tebni n tixubta n umdan:: « yiwen uffus ad ak yeslef, wayeḍ ad ak-yewwet ". Amdan yekcem facal ur nezmir i dunnit neqqar fell-as: « affus-is yettwarez" neɣ: «keblen ifasen-is". Yal tikelt anta telɣa neɣ tugna deg nettera affus akken ad nesenɛat tidyanin yettḥazen, ixef-nneɣ . Imi tudert tebna ɣef tidukla akked beṭṭu, ɣef laman akked lexdeɛ nettaf leqbayel qqaren ɣef win ixeḍɛen: « yefka affus ". Anect-a a t-nnef di tsadarin-agi n Lǧunis Ait Menguellet: « Fkan affus / wid-ak si numen iḍeli/ weṣṣan si zikk ɣef temɛict n ddew uḍar/ akken anagaru ad yerr ṭṭar ". Deg tikti -agi n lexḍaɛ id yekkan sɣur atmaten Matǧub Lǧunes si ljiha-s yeqqar-as: « Lerbaɛ Nat Iraten/ irumyen imi i tt-id kecmen/ d nekni i yefkan affus / mazal timsal nniḍen / ɣeẓẓifit am yemraren/ wama id nniɣ drus ". Lexḍaɛ am waken yettili di tisertit, yettili diɣ di tayri. Yeqqar Lǧunis Ait Menguellet: «tewwi-yi-d iḥder n ukermus/ texdem-iyi-d tirkasin/Armi tefka deg-i affus/ tmedleḍ kan tawwurt yellin ". Tikwal diɣ d amdan i yettɣurun iman-is s yiman-is, anect-a at neff deg ifyar agi n Matǧub Lǧunes anda is yeqqar: « di ljib-iw mi id yella kra/ ayi yekker uffus-iw ". Anda nniḍen s telɣa n tuzmiwin yeqqar: «s uffus-ik id uɣeḍ aṭan ". ihi am akka nwala lexdaɛ tikwal yezmer ad yekk sɣur wiyaḍ am akken yezmer ad seg-nneɣ ara d yettnulfu. Mi nemderkal ɣef uguren, mi teccud fellaɣ amek akken ur t-fetti neqqar s nuqma: « affus yekka-d deg-nneɣ ". Anamek n wawal d nukni i-iɛamden i wayen id aɣ-yuɣen, d nekni s timmad-nneɣ i- yellin tiwwura i lemḥayen id kecmen ɣer tasga. Lmeɛna agi nettaf-itt deg aṭas n yifyar di tmedyazt taqbaylit amedya: « s-uffus-iw I yettewteɣ ". Awal n " uffus” sxadement diɣ leqbayel akken ad sneɛtan azal n tdukli. Qarren « yiwen uffus ur yekkat cqar " neɣ «dduklen am iḍuḍan n uffus ". Deg usefru ɣuri "yiwen umdakel” yecna Ferhat akked idir llan yifyar-agi id yesenɛaten telqay akked ljehd yezdin ssin yemjuhad: « deg iberden mi ara n lleḥu/ ɣer tama-w id teddu/ am iḍuḍan n uffus". Akken ad dukkeln watmaten neqqar diɣ: «affus deg uffus/ teɛkemt yeẓayen a tifsus "acku ma fraqen yemdanen yettiɛib ula d ayen isehlen. I lmend n waya neqqar: «yiwen uffus ur yekkat cqar ". di tagni-tt n diq, mi yewḥel umdan yetteḥwiji tallelt ɣef aya neqqar: « fka-s affus"meḥsub ddlu fell-as akken at-id tesukseḍ seg uɛawiq deg yella. Tikwal lux ikerref imdanen. Tabɣest akken ibɣu tella terna-t tugdi. Di tagnatin am tigi amdan ilaq amdan ad iḥader iman-is.Ilaq ad iẓer acu id yeqqar neɣ acu ixeddem imi tiyita tezmer ad teṣemhel ansi fella-s ur yebni. Ɣef aya leḥder d lwajeb. Awal neɣ tiɣawsiwin ara d yawwin cwal i bab-nsent s tufra kan id ttilint. Ɣef aya neqqar:: « s ddew uffus ". Anda nniḍen xas ma neqqar: «isusfan d awal kan ", neẓra d texmam i d-tidet mačči d lefɛayel. Anamek n wawal yettifrir-d deg anzi-agi:: «affus yesḥalfen amzun yewwet ". si ljiha nniḍen neẓra belli yal amdan s tikti-ines, s lɛaqliya ines. Mgaraden yemdanen di tmuɣli, deg usewaq, deg leqdic di yal taɣewsa iccuden ɣer tmeddurt s umata. Tikti –agi nega-as lmendad deg lemtel -agi: «iḍuḍan ur ɛadilen ". Deg akka llan yirgazen yettqazem tagnit s lejher melba adari, llan wiyaḍ d uffiren; smenyafen tiherci ɣef tirugza taḥerfit. Tugna-agi nettaf-itt deg anzi is yeqqaren: «yeffer tiḥjurin deg uffus ". Anzi yesexdem Sliman Azem deg usefru-ines dǧminǧ imi is yeqqar: « feqqeɣ-ak tleɛbeḍ s lḥir/ tefreḍ tiḥejurin deg uffus".
Tikwal, ɣef kra n yegduden yerwan lemrar d ṣsber akked tasusmi i d ddwa n tlufa. Maca am akken tenfeɛ tsusmi i tettili diɣ,di kra n tagnit, d neqma. Mi yuɣal uffus ɣef yimmi, zzun akken nerra takmamt i lmenṭaq. Tikti-agi id yesenɛaten tugdi akked uzuzen n ddel ɣer lqum tetuɣaled deg anzi-agi: « nerra xemsa ɣef yimmi". Tudert ur telli d telqa yelwan neɣ d amrar yezdin iferdisen n temɛict s lqis. Anda tella talwit id tettnulfu cceda. Anda i tefka aẓar cceda i t-meqqi talwit. Kra yellan yettidir s nned-is. Ayen inefɛan ass-a yettuɣal d aɣbal azekka. Ayenid d yettbanen d-tidet tura, yenebren d tikerkas ar deqal.
Tudert tettsenid ɣef iɛawiqen akken ad ttawi amdan ɣer liser. Aḥulfu yekmen deg ixef, lqerḥ ireṣa di ṣṣura. Mi yenekbel wul, mi tezzi fell-as tcerket, yiwen ubrid iwulem: laqqen iseflan, ilaq amenuɣ. Ɣef aya akken ibɣu aɛziz cci, i lmend n tlelli, i lmend n lɛaz akked yiseɣ ilaq ad yettwerhen am akken is yenna Lǧunis Ait Mneguellet: «I wakken awen –tebru ticerket/ sɛut tasa gezmet afus ".
Ait Slimane Hamid
Ass-nni n 7 deg furar 2014 i d-yella usmekti wis 54 n tmettan n IMACHE Amar deg taddart n Ait Mesbah i d-yezgan deg lεerc n Wat Dwala. Leqdic-a, theyya-t-id tiddukla n taddart i yewwin isem n urgaz-a s lemεawna n twacult IMACHE akked tenmehla n yidles n Tizi Uzzu. Hǧcine.M Mhenni Xalifi
Aṭas n yimdanen i d-yerzan γer Wat Mesbah sbeḥ n wass n lğemεa. Gar-asen, yella uselway n useqqamu aγerfan n lwilaya, aselway n tenmehla n yidles n Tizi Uzzu, aselway n tγiwant n temnaḍt-nni, Abdennǧur Abdeslam d wiyaḍ. Mebεed mi ssersen tameqqunt iseğğigen γef uzekka-s, tesmekta-d twacult-is amecwar n IMACHA Amar anda i ṭṭalaben asteεref s urgaz-a imi d netta i d tigejdid n umussu aγelnaw u d netta i d-yeslulen ENA. Σlaḥsab n wid i d-yemmeslayen, nnan-d d akken deg umussu-a i d-bedren i tikelt tamezwarut azarug n Lezzayer. Maca, aṭas i yessḥasfen imi amennuγ n urgaz am wa iγellet-it Messali Hadj wehd-s. Γef wanect-a, dγa, i d-llan yisarugen deg uxxam n Mulud Mεemmri ass-nni n ssebt 8 deg furar.
Yelli-s n yiεiqer d tamacahut i d-yefγen deg ussan-agi iεeddan, γer tezrigin El Amel, sγur TǦUATI Zǧulikha. D tamacahut tis snat i tura mebεeb mi d-tessufeγ tamezwarut ’Inuda γef zzher-is, yufa-t’’ ilindi. Lferq gar tmezwarut d tis snat d akken taneggarut-a d nettat i tt-id-yesnulfan. Γef wanect-a, dγa, tenna-aγ-d:’’ḥemmleγ ad d-siwleγ timucuha. Meεna tikwal ur d-ttafeγ ara tin ara d-siwle&amtt;gamma,; dγa snulfuyeγ-d imi ilaq ad d-ḥkuγ. Akka i d-tusa tikti-agi n tmacahut ’Yelli-s n yiεiqer’’. Ihi, tamacahut-a tewwi-d awal γef yiwet n twacult i iεemren kan s tullas, baba-tsent d amγar, teğğa-t tezmert meεna yelli-s ad as-taf tifrat… Hǧcine.M Mhenni Xalifi Mhenni Xalifi
Belɛid Izarar, yettwasnen s yisem n Belɛid At Ali, d netta i yerẓan asalu i yemyura n teqbaylit. Yekker-ed deg lmizireyya, tinna t-iḍefṛen am tili-s ar almi s medlen-t wallen. Yennemḍaṛ ar almi ḥfan iḍaṛṛen-is. D mmi-s n tselmadt, Belɛid yelmed tutlayt n tṛumit akken kan d-yeffeɣ di dduḥ. Ayagi, mi ara tmuqleḍ, d ayen ara s isishlen tudert-is, maca, abrid d-yebbi, yettemcabin aṭas ɣer win n si Muḥend U M’ḥend, yeččuṛ d iɛekkiṛen. Ceɣlis ala anemḍeṛ. Adeg yettak-it i wayeḍ. Ur yetterkad ara deg yiwen n wemkan. Tissit tefka-yas axeṣṣaṛ, d nettat i yellan deffir yak iɣelliyen-is, yir tamɛict d waṭṭanen t-yeṭfen. Ula d tamettant-is tella-d sebba n waṭṭan n turin-is lak d wawi yerr i s yeskawen ifadden-is. Belɛid Izarar ilul deg useggan n 1909 deg Weẓṛu Uqellal, llan wid nniḍen d-yeqqaṛen d akken ilul deg Tugirett anda tella yemma-s tesselmad. Belɛid d agrud wis setta deg yiwet n twacult yesɛan xemsa n tullas d tlata n warrac. Deg 1915, yella yesɛa setta n iseggasen. Yemm-as teǧǧa aselmed, tebbi-d tawacult-is ar Weẓṛu Uqellal, di tama n Aïn El Hammam. Aseggas-nni kan yekcem ɣer uɣerbaz n taddart anda d-yufrar ger tezyiwin-is, acku netta yella yessen tutlayt n tṛumit d waṭas n wayen nniḍen s tselmed yemma-s. Di tazwaran umecwaṛ-is n tira, yedha-d kan s tira n tmucuha s tutlayt n teqbaylit. Ger tid ijerred, ad d-nebder izwal-agi: Tamacahutt uwaɣzniw, tamacahutt uɛeqqa yessawalen, tamacahutt n Bu-Yedmim, tamacahut inisi d wuccen, tafunast ibujilen, lwali n wedrar, aẓidan d umerẓagu,…Deg imir tuɣal tezzi lwelha-s ɣer tira n wungalen. D netta i yxedmen aquddim warǧin xedmen, ula d wid d-yekren deffir-es, Ben Sedira lak d Bǧulifa, yellan sbuḥuten-d, ula d nutni, inzan, isefra, d tmucuha yettawin ttarran ger umeẓẓuɣ d yimi. Belɛid At Ali d netta i d amyaru amenzu i yebdan tira n wungalen s tutlayt n teqbaylit. D netta i ysersen imɣan imezwura deg wennar n tsekla yella-n d asuki. Deg useggas n 1950, Belɛid At Ali yebbeḍ laɛfu n Ṛebbi.
Uqbel ad d-yers uɣamac n unbdu, imdanen ttagan kra n ttawilat akken ad sɛeddin tallit-agi n weẓɣal akken iwata. Izenqan yak ad ten-t-afeḍ ttwacerwen. Tizergatin ittwakkes-asen-t leḥcic akken kan tɛedda tefsewt, aceku angaru-agi, mi ara yeḥḍem ijebbed-ed iḥermemmuḍen, ladɣ izerman. Imdanen ttneqqin yak lḥala tama n leḥwaṛi-nsen akken ur tettnekkar ara tmes. S daxel n yexxamen daɣen yettili-d uqeɛed, uqbel anebdu. Tilawin, mi d tafsewt, ad rzun-t, d tirebbaɛ, ɣer wanda ara d-awint tumlilt  d akal d acebḥan s wayes ara d-begḍen-t sqef wad d-selɣen-t leḥyuḍ. Ma d win s wayes ara d-selɣen-t tiɣerɣert rnun-t-as zbel n tfunast ajdid, llan wid s irennun ula d imezuren n weɣyul, lak d cwiṭ n walim aṛeqqaq, acku win n lqaɛa, ɣef ayeg tqewwu lǧeṛṛa, ilaq ad yeṭṭef akken ur yettnekkar ara uɣebbaṛ. Tumlilt mi tt-id-ɣzant, ad tt-id-ṣawḍent s axxam. Uqbel ad tt-sxedment serkamen-t-ett, kra n wussan, deg waman, acku ur ilaq ara ad d-tt-eddu d tikebrurin lawan n ubeggeḍ. Mi terkem akken iwata, tumlilt-nni ad tili tefsi yak deg waman. Abeggeḍ maci d ayen isehlen. Leḥwal lak d iceṭiḍen ilaq yak ad d-tt-wasefɣen ɣer beṛṛa akken ur ttamsen ara. Deg waṭas n tikkal, mi ara ilin-t tzeɣwa meqrit, tilawin tteḥwiǧin-t afus n tallelt n tǧiratin. S uɣectu n tuzzalt, d aɣezfan, win ara ttebɣen-t ɣer lḥila anda terkem tumlilt, id d-yettili cɣel-agi. Akken kan ara d-sufɣen-t aɣectu deg wakal amellal irekmen ad zebḍen-t yas sqef yettwaxdamen s uɣanim. Mi kfan-t lak d sqef, ad zzin-t ɣef leḥyuḍ. Dagi sexdamen-t d ačelliq deg wemkan n uɣectu. Ilaq kan ad yettwabbeɣ akken iwata deg tumlilt, imir ad tesɛaddayen-t ɣef leḥyuḍ n tzeqqa, wid n tkanna, lemdawed, ikufan… Mi kfan leḥyuḍ lak d sqef, d nnuba n tɣerɣert. Aslaɣ n lqaɛa yettili-d s ufus. Mi yekfa ubeggeḍ d weslaɣ, axxam ad yuɣal d azedgan, d asemmaḍ.
Seg wasmi ideg d-yeflali yitri Matǧub Lǧunes deg yigenni n ccna aqbayli ur yeḥbis wawal fell-as. Udem n ccna s wacu d-yekcem annar-agi n ccna d amaynut, d win si ur nnumen ara medden uqbel tissin n Matǧub Lǧunes. Ccna id yewwi d win yezdin deg yiwen uxelxal ljehd n wawal tamedyazt lqayen akked aẓawan d-yedmen nneɣ ma-s seg tala n wurfan yeččuren ul-is mgal timcukal deg tella tmeti taqbaylit deg isaggasen-nni. Di lawan-nni bexlaf kra n yicenayen d yimedyazen, am Lǧunis Ait Menguellet, Idir, Ferhat Imaziɣen Imula, Ben Mǧhamed i yecqarwen lbatel n ukabar awḥid n yimiren, tasusmi tekbel ilsawen, tesgugem imawen, tesgen ulawen. Cna n Matǧub yussa-d di lawan akken ad yesihriw iɣisi deg uɣrab n ukukru imi awal-is ur yeffir timsal, ur yenneḍ ɣef tidet yellan. Ɣef aya yal mi ara d bedren medden Matǧub Lǧunes deg umeslay qerna-s d aɣawaɣ rebelle. Xas ṣṣifa-agi n tiɣeweɣt yeddan am tayuga akked isem-is d ttin yelhan, d ttin yesburen s tlaba n yiseɣ maca Matǧub lexṣayel-is kkan-d nnig ṣṣifa-agi wuɣur zedwen yemdanen akken ad sneɛten anwi d Matǧub Lǧunes. Iberden yettawin ɣer timadit n umedyaz gten…yal yiwen anwa udem wuɣur yesufuɣ, anta lexṣla id yesbgan. Deg adris-agi nefka nnuba i wawal akken aɣ yeṭṭef affus aɣ yawwi ɣer lexlawi nniḍen n ucenay nḥamel Matǧub Lǧunes.
Am win yetseqin i wassif
Kra ur t-yeṭṭif
Yesenzeh deg-s laɛrac…
Uqbel ad tegrem asurif
Ad tezwirem nnif Ma ulac…
Tamaziɣt.. ulac.. ulac … ulac…
Yal wa amek id yenna fell-as, Yal yiwen amek i t-yettwali. Kra ttawalint- d aɣawaɣ, d bab n tabɣest, d bab n tirugza, d argaz bu tisas. Ɣer waṭas n yemdanen Matǧub yella d win ur neddaray ara timsal. Ayen yellan deg ul-is aten ɣef yiles-is Akka i tt-nettwali… akka i nḥamel a t-id nebder. Akka i-yuzzel fell-as wawal.
Ksed amek ur d wwin fell-as awal. Yal tamacahut tenneḍ ɣef yisem-is, armi tuɣal leḥmala isen-budd qrib iɣ-teseɛaq lewhi ɣef tidet tamenzut yellan imi uqbel ad yilli d ayen nniḍen Matǧub Lǧunes yella d amdan!
Nettu belli Matǧub Lǧunes uqbel kulci yella: d tasa, d ul, d iḥulfan, d ccek, d- amajadel netta d yiman-is. Amezwaru id cehden ɣef aya d Matǧub Lǧunes s timad-is:
Imi lwaqt ur d iyi ḥacem
Xas ayi yeɛdem
Yefka-iyi aɣrum deg isefra
Yal yiwen anta tugna is- yefka i Matǧub Lǧunes. Yal yiwen anta tiṭ s waci i t-yettwali. Wa yeqqar-as d agrawliw, wa d-ameɣnas, wayeḍ iwaṣef-it d-izem bu tisas, wayeḍ yecna ɣef lhiba-s ur yeksib ḥedd. Mačča nettu belli Matǧub Lǧunes uqbel kulci yella d amedyaz!
D amedyaz i neǧǧren isefra. D aḥadad n wawal yesefrurin ifyar. D amedyaz yesqdacen awal, ineǧǧren tira ɣef lluḥ s tedwat n thuski akked tayri.
Fkiɣ ɣer ssuq isem-iw
Ɣer reḥba n iẓẓiriyen
Ma ad yezenz imaṭṭawen-iw Ma llan widen a ten –yaɣen Jeɛleɣ ad qḍuɣ lebɣi-iw Ziɣen teqlab tewriqt-iw Anda akken ufiɣ leḥbab-iw
Id nejmaɛen yixṣimen-iw
Ɣef tɛakazt n wawal i-isened Matǧub Lǧunes akken ad yini t-id it yerḥan. Ɣef tagmert n isefra i- yedda akken ad yezuzer ayen yenwa n tidet. Tedra-tt yid-s am umedaḥ yettebdaden tawwurt tawwurt akken ad yesbin i medden acu iten-yuɣen d wanida i ttuɣen.
Abrid yeḍfer Matǧub Lǧunes mačči d win yessan d iǧeǧǧigen. Abrid yeḍfer yessa d iɣebla, d urfan, d lḥir, d-iɛaqiqen. Abrid yuɣ ur yelli d win iḍemnan. Ayen i t-yewwin ɣer iberden yesawnen, ayen i t-yewwin ɣer igudar ur tettmagger lluḍa d tiɣri n idamen:
Fkiɣ laman gar medden
Tagara wwiɣ-d aɣilif
Iles-iw yuɣal d isyaxen
Yezga wul a d yettiẓif
D idamen iyi-d yesneṭqen
Ggreɣ-d am uqajmur s- asif
Yedda uḍar deg abrid xas akken uguren uṛgan aḍar. Iɛawiqen ggunin ixef. Tugdi yettxatalen tassa akked d wul di yal tiɣmert ala awal is-yettaren lqid akken bubrak tenwa teḍlaq ɣef yixef n umedyaz d yemdanen ad yerr aḍar. Acqirew win it –yedman yeḥwaj ṣda n leɛnaya. Matǧub Lǧunes inuda leɛnaya deg idurar anda id yuɣ aẓar:
Idurar nedhen yisen
Ṣṣut-iw anwa ur as nesli-ara
Xas akka kawen ifaden
Zarɛeɣ awal yenerna
Acu n tamara yettaren amdan ad iqazem ayen umu ur yezmir? Ad inamer ayen i t-yugaren? Tuttra ɣer Matǧub ur teḥwaj ara aṭas n umjadel imi:
D idamen iyi-d yesneṭqen
Greɣ-d am uqajmur s-asif Acku:
Nekk nniɣ-d ayen iyi-qarḥen
Xas lḥebs yegguni-yi
Neɣ ma ulac:
Am win yetseqin i wassif
Kra ur t-yeṭṭif
Yesenzeh deg-s laɛrac…
Uqbel ad tegrem asurif
Ad tezwirem nnif
Ma ulac…tamaziɣt.. ulac.. ulac … ulac…
Acu id yesentaqen amadyaz..? Ayen i t-yettawi ubrid ɣef wanda zedwen ticrurin yettnawalen cwal i yixef-is? Matǧub Lǧunes Yeẓra belli awal id yeger yiles ɣer tabḥat n usmeḥsas, tikwal igelud s umenuɣ. Matǧub Lǧunes yeẓra belli lexlas n tmena d regmat. Tikwal sɣur wid yettqazam. Tikwal sɣur wid yettɛuzzu. Tamselt si tazwara i yemdarkel fell-as:
Xas ḥarni rebɛa leḥyuḍ
Xas lfinga a ttettwaliɣ
Xas lḥif ayi-id iṣṣuḍ
Xas yecceḍ ubrid awiɣ
Ma nnan-iyi s-anda i t-tteduḍ
Asen-inniɣ nekk d Amaziɣ
D lebɣi i yesmendagen lebɣi deg ulawen. Deg akken ireṣa lḥawj n tilelli akked fad n tudert deg ul n umedyaz, wi cqa ayen ara s –id teǧǧew nmara-s.Ɣef anect-a tikwal nettaf-it yettqazem tamara s neqma. Tikwal nettaf-it yedaray tarzeg n wussan s tirga. Tikwal nettaf-it yettexalis zzman s idamen-ines:
Kecmeɣ di ssuq n tlufa
Qdiɣ-d leqsadi n lmeḥna
Deg-sen hamjeɣ kul-ass
Ɣef ul-iw ur tnuqqel cetwa
Lebraq rɛud d usigna
Rniɣ ṭlam d imeḍelas
Lmut fell-i ur tnuda
Yifi-t limer id tesqsa
A tɣum leɛyub-iw meṛṛa…
Ɣef ufagag n isefra, yesni Matǧub Lǧunes awalen id yeddem si takurt n lxiq-is, si takurt n wurfan-is akked d lhejnat izedɣen ul-is….
Lebḥer- is yezga yenhewal. Mačči d yiwet n lmuja i yettraǧǧimen iɣerban n yixef-is. Dagi d tilufa n tagmet, dihin d talfut n yidles yettmattaten. Dagi d taluft n isertiyen yezzin s waɛrur i tidet, dihin d lbaṭel id yeɣlin ɣef lqum. Dagi d lḥif yessasayen lemḥayen deg iqera n imeɣben, dihin d tirget n tayri yeseknafen deg ul-is teɣzi n wuḍan akked wussan. Dagi d tadyant n yemdukel i hemjen deg ul-is yettawi gar ifasen-is, dihin d tamselt n leɛcaq yeserɣayen ifarawen n lferḥ-is:
D teɛjajt n lmut-a
Idi yesxelḍen temẓi-w
Ruḥen kan baba d yemma
Teɣli tigejdit n lfreḥ-iw
Ajgagal n lmizirya
Yuɣ amdiq di ddunit-iw
Tefreɣ lkas d ljebba…
Tewet rrba deg axxam-iw
Hamid Ait Slimane yettkemmil Mhenni Xalifi Hǧcine.M
Ddurt yezrin mi d-yerza lwali n waɣir n Bgayet imezdaɣ drus i yeḥsan taswiɛt-n ahat acku imi ass-nni ur yettak anzi aṭas i wass n tirza, ma neẓra dakken ddeqs n ugeffur ay d-yeɣlin ass-n, d ayen dɣa i yeǧǧan lwali ad yesseɛjel timuɣliwin-is deg tal tamnaḍt anda yeḥbes. Lwali tazwara yesres iḍarren-is deg Tdayra n Yiderginen anda ara d-yili yella-d umeslay ladɣa ɣef taluft n uxeddim i beṭṭu n teɣbalut n waman, rnu yerza ɣer yiwen n uɣerbaz anda llan ttmaggan ikayaden n BAC. send ad iḍil ɣef lǧamaɛ n umkan-n. Mi tekfa tirzi n lwali deg tdayra ilḥem-d ed wid dɣa yedakkalen yid-s, ama s yinemhalen n umeqyas-is neɣ s unmazul-is, ɣer tɣiwant n Tsexriwt, din yeḥbes ladɣa sdat n wadeg n tzeqqa n usileɣ fǧrmatiǧn, syin akkin yella umeslay ɣef tesnawit n Maɛuc Idris. Taggara n tirzi, imḍebber amezwaru n Bgayet yuli-d i Udrar n Fad, ɣer tɣiwant n Ayt-Smaɛel imi d tisin i d-yusan deg teswiɛt teḥres, abaɛda ɣef taluft n tesnawit n Ayt-Smaɛel ed wawal merra i yuzzlen fell-as ma ad theggi tikkelt-a i Ctember neɣ uhu. Sadeq Rebbaɛi, anmazul n uselway n tɣiwant s leḥdaqa i ak-d-yefka isallen ɣef wamek teffeɣ s umata tirza-a n lwali i Ayt-Smaɛel. « Akken teẓram merra, ama s imezdaɣ n Ayt-Smaɛel neɣ s wid yettafaren isallen n tɣiwant-a, ayen i aɣ-iceɣben s waṭas d abellez n yiqeddicen n tesnawit. Lwali iɛeyyen tirmisin entrettrises ara yesɛejlen lxedma akken i t-id-yenna s timmad-is, bac ad nessiweḍ ad neldi tasnawit xersum i yiseggasen amenzu ed wis-sin n ulemmud asnawan ". Mi d-isub lwali seg tesnawit yella-d umeslay ɣef temkarḍit n tɣiwant acku ula d tin sebken lecɣal-is seg tulacit n tedrimt ara yesnedhen ixeddamen. Taggara maḍi imḍebbren n tɣiwant n Ayt-Smaɛel utlayen i lwali ɣef taluft n unqal n unaray n yijadarmiyen ɣer sdat n tɣiwant.
Akken i d as-yenna Mǧhya deg yiwen gar isefra-ines: « Iw ḍellaɛ mi yesselqaf, d acu ad as-d- gen ifassen? ". Akka ihi i tḍerru d yimezdaɣ n tɣiwant n yimcedallen, ma yella ad nebder kan tama-agi, segmi i d-yekcem waggur n Ṛemḍan, tiwaculin ur ṣiwḍent ara ad sduklent sin n yifassen. Acku leɣla n kra n yifarisen n tuččit ttrǧduits alimentaires yekkes lbenna i Ṛemḍan. Gar tuččiyin-agi, yella weksum. Ɣas ma yella iguma fruits lakked izegza lẓgumes ur ulin ara aṭaṣ deg ssuma, aksum, ur d-tudir ara ssuma-ines. Dayen yeǧǧan imezdaɣ ur ufin ara s anda ad rren iqurra-nsen! Cerba tettibnin s weksum, wagi ɣlay aṭaṣ ɣef imezdaɣ, yagi tiwaculin ur nelḥiq ara iman-nsen-t! Ula d-aksum uyaẓid, neɣ aksum igellil, yessemɣi-d afriwen yufeg alarmi d 350 idinaren i l’kilu! Aksum yekunǧlin γiande cǧngelẓe anegaru deg ikesman ur d-yettader ara s daw n 650 idinaren. Ma yella win n tmurt, abaqri yettnuzu kra n 850 idinaren. Ma d win n-uɣelmi, ulayɣar ad nahḍar fella-s, imi iɛedda akin i 1300 idinaren! « D ttidett, izegza lakked d-igumma ur ɣlay-it ara aṭaṣ deg Ṛemḍan n-useggas-agi, maca aɣbel d-aksum yeɣlayen aṭaṣ! Ur s zmir-ɣ ara! ". Akka iɣ-d yenna yiwen n Mas, bab n t’wacult. Leɣla-agi, yeddemir tiwaculin akken ad cuḥen-t i weksum, as-t-ini-ḍ akken d-uraɣ l’ǧr. Tilawin ggaren-t cwiṭ cwiṭ n weksum ar teccuyt, akken kan att-sɛu lbenna. Ɣas akken tamurt nneɣ d ttin izemren att-sekfu iman-is ɣef ayen yeɛnan aksum n myal nuɛ, imi tesɛa allalen akal n teksawt, tadrimt, imeksawen,… maca ur texdim ara taserṭit ar tanila-agi. D-ayagi yeǧǧan tamurt nneɣ t ttaɣ-d aksum yekunǧlin ɣer timura nniḍen. Yerna aksum-agi ur yesɛi ara lbenna laked lfayda i tezmart n yimsuddar cǧnsǧmmateurs. Akka ihi, aḍellaɛ n twaculin izedɣen deg Mcedallah « yesselqaf ". Ass n lɛid amecṭuḥ ahat ad yemmet, at nɣen iselsa n yigerdan! Sytthax.Y Mhenni Xalifi
Zzik, ɣef wakken d-eqqaṛen, yella yiwen n ubabat lak d mmi-s ttemḥellin-d deg wawal ɣef yemdukal-nsen. Mmi-s yeqqar-as i baba-s d akken aṭas n yemdukal i yesɛa, ma dagella yewḥel yiwen was, ma ur s-id-yeṭṭif yiwen afus, ad yaf wayeḍ. Ur yettfakka ara awal fell-asen. Winna ixdem-iyi aya. Wayeḍ yenna-yas ma tsutreḍ-iyi-d tiṭ-iw ak ttefkeɣ. Wayeḍ nniḍen yenna-yas mi iyi d-egreḍ tiɣṛi ayi-d-afeḍ ɣef yidis-ik ayfus, d waṭas nniḍen yal wa deg-sen d acu s yenna. Ababat ur tyeɛǧib ara lḥal. Yiwen was mi yebda mmi-s iskuffut awal yeqqaṛ mazal ɣef yemdukal-is, yenna-yas: Deg tegnitt n ddiq id d-ettbanen yerfiqen n tidett. Nek sɛiɣ kan yiwen. Ma d keč, ɣef leḥsab n wayen d-eqqaṛeḍ, gten. Yaṛeq leḥsab i tifin. Ihi, ass-a, ma tebɣiḍ, ayen yellan deg tasilt ad t-id-yessali uɣenja. Tura ad-nerr iman-nneɣ nebbi tamegṛeṭ. Rzu ɣer wemdakel deg ayeg tesɛiḍ laman, in-as i yellan i yellan, baba-k yenɣa yiwen n wergaz id d-iẓedmen s axxam. Tura atan deg tesga i tneḍleq. Akken ad yettwamḍel, mebla ma ifaq yiwen, ilaq-aɣ afus n tallelt. Ilemẓi yebbi abrid zdat-es qbala ɣer weṛfiq-nni s d-yesebbayen tifeswa. Yeḥka-yas-d tadyant akken s-d-yenna baba-s. Mi yekfa, winna s d-yemuzguten yebda yettettel wawal deg yimi-s. Yeqqel ar almi d-yeffeɣ ala nni. Ur yezmir ara acku yettagad tilufa yagi n tmegṛaḍ. Yeča tiyita ɣer daxel, aqcic yuɣal ɣer baba-s ad s-yini d acu yeḍṛan. Aneggaru-yagi ur yessewhem ara d acu s-d yenna mmi-s, yerra-t kan ɣef tebburt ad yerzu ɣer wayeḍ. Ula d tikkelt-agi ur d-yesli ara d acu yebɣa. Ababat yefka-yas i mmi-s tagnitt akken ad d-yezzi yak ɣef yemdukal-nni s wayes yettzuxxu. Ilemẓiibda ikečem-it ccek, maca mazal ur yeqḍiɛ ara layas. Tibbura n yemdukal-is yak iṣṭebṭeb fell-asen-t. Inna-yasen yak tiyita ten-yuɣen ar almi yeḥfa yiles-is deg uɛawed n lehduṛ. Si tama-nsen, yal yiwen d acu ara d-yaf d sebba akken ur yetteddu ara yid-es s axxam. Tiyita yeča-tt ɣer daxel teḥma, ula d yiwen ur t-id-yufi ɣer yidis-is akken ad t-iḥami deg tegnitt-agi n ddiq. Zzin-as-d ak s warur. Mi yekfa awi yerr, iceggeɛ-it baba-s ɣer wemdakel-is akken as-yeḍleb afus n lemɛawna. Akken cwiṭ yezzi-d yid-es. Mi d-iekcem s axxam, iseqsa anda yella winna nɣan akken ad tmeḍlen uqbel ad yali was. Ababat imuqqel mmi-s s wezmumeg yenna-yas: « Twalaḍ a mmi, akken qaṛen menyif takemmict n tzizwa wala aglaf n warẓaẓen. Sarameɣ d akken tagnitt-agi tella-yak-id d tamsirt ur tettettuḍ ara ". Mi yekfa awal lak d mmi-s, yezzi ɣer wemdakel-is akken ad s-yemmel anda yella winna nɣan. Amdakel itbeɛ qbala aḍad-nni s-d-yemlen anda tella tfekka n win yemmuten. Mi yebbeḍ ɣer taṛust yerfed aɣummu i wayen yufa yeddel, yufa d ikerri i ymezlen. Irfed-ed aqerru-s yezzi-d ɣer wemdakel-is iseqsa-t d acu ixeddem ikerri imezlen sufella n taṛust. Ababat s wezmumeg yerra-yas: d mmi ɣef ayeg ugadeɣ. Yezga iheddeṛ-iyi-d ɣef yemdukal-is. Ittxalaḍ aṭas mači d kra. Dɣa nniɣ-as ass-agi ad d-isali uɣenja ayen yella-n yezder deg lqaɛ n tasilt. Akka tettwaliḍ ala keč id d-yusan. Iqim-iyi-d kan ad k-iniɣ s tezmert-ik. Di tlata yid-sen zzin i ykerri sebbayen, setten ar almi ṛwan.
Yal yiwen amek yettwali tamsalt-agi. Llan wid yettamnen s tugett n yemdukal. Win sen-d-yeḍṣan yegla s wul-nsen. Llan daɣen wid yettarran tilas i wxaleḍ-nni ur nesɛi lmeɛna. I waṭas umu d-ḍeṛṛun-t temsal am tigi. Mi tweḥleḍ s ṛebɛa wid tesneḍ ad k-d-ezzin s warur.
Ajemmaɛ n lmal n taddart n Tɣalaḍt meqqer, d aqḍar. Yal axxam yekki deg-s s yiwen n yixef neɣ ugar. Ilemẓiyen n taddart kessen s nnuba almend n umḍan n waxfiwen i sɛant twaculin-nsen, ma ɣur-sent yiwen n yixef n lmal am taɣaḍt neɣ tixsi d tayessawt n yiwen n wass, ma ɣur-sent sin waxfiwen d tayessawt n sin wussan…atg.
Imeksawen iwimi d-tewweḍ nnuba ttnekkaren-d zik send tafrara, ttɛeddayen-d ɣef yixxamen si tama wadda alamma d tin n ufella n taddart. Yal axxam i ɣef d-kkan berrun-d wa i taɣaḍt wayeḍ i txsi d warraw-is, dɣa netta ajemmaɛ skudmal yettimɣur, yettuɣal d aqḍar ma yelḥeq ɣer ubrid aneggaru nnig taddart, win akken yettawin srid s adrar. Yidir d Leḥlu d nnuba-nsen, yal yiwen iɛleq-d leǧbira n wusran anda i d-iger aɣrum aquran d kra n yiniɣman d zzit n uzemmur. Asɣar n uẓebbuj aquran deg ufus ayeffus yis-s sɛukkuzen neɣ ttwehhin ɣer wulli ad d-uɣalent s abrid ma ffɣent-t. Leḥlu yezwar sdat n uqḍar ma d Yidir d sin yiḍan ggran. Aydi yetturebban yeẓwer i tyessawt, yessen ad d-yerr izimer neɣ iɣid ma yeɛzel ɣef tqeḍɛit ma ulac ad t-izu  ɣer wuccen ɣer yiɣẓer ad t-yečč. Mi ara awḍen yimeksawen ɣer wadeg anida ara ikes lmal ttserriḥen i tɣeṭṭen d wulli ad calint akken ad d-nadint ɣef yimɣi i iḥemmlent ad t-ččent. Rrbiɛ yegget acku deg tsemhuyt n tefsut i nella.
Imeksawen ad d-bedden mebɛid ad ttɛassan ma ur d-ixutel wuccen iɣid neɣ ma ur yewḥil ara yizimer deg yinijel. Kra yekka wass d tagi i d lxedma-nsen. Imdanen imeksawen ssexdamen allen-nsen deg tyessawt ma d iḍan imeksawen ssexdamen allen d wanzaren-nsen, seg wanda i d-tejba rriḥa n wuccen ad tt-mmagren s useglef. Biccuḥ, akken i s-qqaren warrac, yeḥṣa ur yezmir ara i uqjun dɣa ad yerwel d taffugt. Maca ala tuɣalin ara d-yuɣal, wissen kan melmi. Ad yeǧǧ alamma yeɣfel uydi ad yeḥweṣ izimer amecṭuḥ, ad t-yawi ɣer wabɛaḍ icudax ad t-yečč deg lisser. Ḥacama kan dayen wanag imeksawen d yiḍan ur yettɛedday ara fell-asen uzaylal, aɣfal ur t-ssinen, zgan dima ukin, kra yeḍran sdat-sen ɣef tiṭ-nsen.
Mi ara izeggen wass, Leḥlu d yiḍan ad d-dhun d tyessawt n lmal ma d Yidir ad iɛeddi ad d-iẓẓeg ulli alamma yeččur-d snat neɣ kradet n al ad d-ikkes aqurḍaɛ seg tenqelt ma yella neɣtegdurin n uyefki ad yu ifer-is. Liqa-nni tamellalt i d-iɣellin seg-sen ad isiqi snat ar kradet n tmiqwa seg-s ɣer daxel n uyefki-nni, wagi ad yuɣal yebbugla. Liqa n uqurḍaɛ ɣur-s tigawt takrurant ɣef uyefki, tbeṭṭu-t ɣef sin n yiḥricen: aman d tedɣart. Tadɣart-agi neqqar-as abuglu. Lmal ad t-id-gren s asensu anda ara ixeggel deg laman ma d nutni ad d-ssersen ad ččen imekli. Ad d-qqimen i sin ad d-rnun yiḍan, ad d-refden leǧbirat-nsen ad d-kksen seg-sent tiḥedrin n uɣrum-nni aquran d zzit d man. Ttǧewwizen aɣrum s ubuglu i d-ihegga Yidir. Aseggri dyini tibxsisin neɣ d tizwal ma wwant. Tameddit ad d-ssuffɣen lmal-nni seg yisensa, ad rnun cwiṭ n tyessawt alamma alaḥal ad yeɣli yiṭij imiren ad d-aɣen abrid n tuɣalin. Mi ara d-awḍen ɣer taddart, yal ixef yessen tawwurt n uxxam-is, yettarra srid ɣer din. Ma d azekka-nni ad d-tezzi nnuba n yimeksawen-nniḍen. Wissen n Mḥend, wissen n Mejɛer, wissen…
Aḍris-a d tukkist seg tullist «Tadukli " i d-yeddan deg ummud n tullisin
«Timsirin n yiḍ " n Malek HǦUD
Ass n 11 di tuber 2014 ay fkan, s wudem unṣib, isem n Slimane Azem i yiwen umekkan di temdint n Paris, deg tγiwant n. Leqdic-a i d-heggant kra n tdukliwin s lemεawna n tγiwant-a, yella-d tajmilt i umecwar n ccna n Slimane Azem.
Deg wahil, ad naf: tisfifin tiqdimin d yiḍebsiyen-nni n zik n ccna-s, kra di leḥwayeğ ines. Teṣwirat n twacult-is ur ẓrin medden yakan, isefra sγur arrac imecṭaḥ.Am wakken ad yili, di&amtt;gamma,; uwali n yiwen ufetray dǧcumentaire s yisem ’Slimane Azem, une lẓgende de l’exil’’ syin, ad d-yili umeslay γef usaru-agi.
I usmektu, Slimane Azem ilul ass n 19/09/1918 deg Ugni Geγran, di tmurt n Leqbayel. Yedder di twacult n 5 warrac d 2 n teḥdayin. Yunag deg useggas 1937 γer gma-s Ǧuali. Deg useggas 1945, yekra lqahwa u yesbedd-d yiwet n terbaεt n ccna. Yessekles i tikelt tamezwarut tasfift i wumi isemma ’ Ma ad tedduḍ ad nruḥ’’ deg useggas n -Syin i yebda umecwar n ccna-s yettnerni u yettmuccuε armi yewwi aḍebsi n ddheb, netta d tcennayt Nǧura, deg useggas n -Yemmut Slimane Azem ass 28/01/1983 di tmurt n lγerba, di Mǧissac anda yesεa tibḥirt n tneqqlin d tzemrin i as-yellan d rriḥa n tmurt. Seg wakken sugten fell-as awal, yenna-d:’’xir ad idireγ d Azzayri di berra wala d aberrani di tmurt-iw.’’ Hǧcine.M
Tamaziγt di Maruk Anda i tufeg i ters! Hǧcine.M Sytthax.Y
Deg unebdu-nni, akken kan i ifuk waggur n Remḍan, yewwi-d baba lkunji. Dɣa nniɣ-as, ad neṛwu acali d umerreḥ: ad nruḥ ɣer Tgejda ad ẓreɣ iddawen, ɣer la ttlage ad sbezgeɣ timeccacin-iw, ɣer taddart ad rwuɣ aɛrur n yaya, ɣer Lina ad nemmyeḥku tilufa n yibibiḍen… Rien de tǧut cela! En fait, yewwi-d baba lkunji bac ad…yexdem. Ih, yerra-yaɣ axxam d chantier. Remarkiɣ, seg wasmi nernaɣ s kra n les neurǧnes, belli ttaqa deg les adultes xeddmen mara yilin kunji. Ljar-neɣ, ttar exemttle, yeznuzuy les glaces. Et cǧmme netta d ccix n lakul, lkunji-s iḍul. Mais, tura imi yenerna lexlaṣ-is, ad yeḥbes ur yeznuzu ara lakrim. Akka i as-yenna i baba: "tura, lḥemdulelah, dayen ur znuzuyeɣ ara les glaces! Ad tt-dewṛeɣ d…akraren”. Nniɣa-awen belli les adultes-agi d lewhayem! Tǧujǧurs deg unebdu-nni, et sǧus ttressiǧn n yemma, yeddisidi baba ad aɣ-yawi ɣer lebḥer ttǧur une jǧurnẓe. Aussitṛt dẓcidẓ aussitṛt fait. sbeḥ zik neddimari ɣer la ttlage. Et cǧmme di tmurt-agi ula tagnawt teteddu nneqma, ass kamel ur teḥbis ara lehwa. "D acu tenniḍ lukan ad nruḥ ad d-nẓur imaziɣen-nni, dagi i nejmaɛen?", i tttruttuzi yemma i baba. "Gẓniale tǧn idẓe!", i d as-yerra baba. Akka, ḥala ɣef tmaziɣt i ttemsefhamen. Mi newweḍ s axxam unejmuɛ, naf-n nna Crifa tecarji d ittafttaren, temmal i yinebgawen dǧnt nekni amek ara ddunt temsal. D nna crifa i timḍebbert n ujemuɛ. tenna-k: "deg temlilit-agi ilaq ad mmttafaqen imaziɣen n tmurt ɣef tira!”. Zzin-d iṭabla inebgawen n nna Crifa. Gar-asen dda Allaǧua, dda Meḥmud, dda meksem, dda Yǧucef, dda remḍan d wiaṭas n yimaziɣen nniḍen. Llan daɣen icawiyen. ula d nutni d imaziɣen. Maɛna, ur fehmeɣ ara mara d-heḍren. et cǧmme aṭas ur ten-nefhim ara, uɣalen hedren akken ttarun tamaziɣt. c’est à dire s taɛrabt. Et mǧi qui ttensait belli imaziɣen akk ttmeslayen taqbaylit!? Et ben nǧn! llan mḥme imaziɣen yettmuzuɣen s tɣumit! Yeffeɣ-d Mhenni Xalifi
Aneɣmis infǧrmatiǧn yella kan d ameslay gar yimezdaɣ n Ayt Smaɛel seg waṭas d aseggas tura. Meḥsub iɣermanen-is citǧyens llan ɣilen belli taɣiwant-a, i yeggugen ibeɛden s wazal n 60 n yikilumitren ɣef Bgayet, ur tettɛeṭṭil ara ad tettwiqqen s lgaz n temdint neɣ n lḥiḍ. Maca ddurt yezrin yuɣal-d wawal-a n wacḥal-aya d unsib ǧfficiel. Mi akken rgen yimḍebbren n tɣiwant ed kra n yimezdaɣ n taddart ɣer temnaḍt mu ssawalen « Aswel " bac ad walin annar ed ubrid ansi yezmer ad d-yekk ugazuduk. « Nelḥem ɣer umḍiq anda nga yiwet n tezrawt ɣef wansi ara d-iɛeddi uteyyu-nni, syin akin, kra n win yettsayalen akal din, nessawel-as bac ad yestenyi turagt n uɛeddi ". Aya yenna-aɣ-t-id unmazul n uselway ḍice-ttrẓsident n tɣiwant n Ayt-Smaɛel mass Sadeq Rebbaɛi, send ad d-yernu ɣef ssmamat i d-yettak usenfar i yimal. « Ar tura aṭas i yestenyan yakan, llan d tidet werɛad, mazal steqsayen, maca yettban-aɣ-d ur d-nettmagar ara ugur seg tama-ya, skud asenfar d ayen ara yekksen taɛkemt i yimezdaɣ merra ". D tidet, ur ilaq ara akk ad d-tmager tɣiwant tiririyin n « uhu " sɣur imezdaɣ, ḥaca ma yella smenyifen aqaɛ ed ubellaɛ akken qqaren, rnan ttun lmeḥna-nni n yennayer n useggas 2012, asmi rewwun leɛtab, aḥeyyer, adaxel, ed uḥebber bac ad afen tabutayt n lgaz. Ad d-nesmekti dakken taɣbalut n lgaz-a ad d-taweḍ Ayt-Smaɛel seg temnaḍt Tala n Yifassen i yettabaɛen tawilayt n Seṭṭif, dɣa syin ad d-tekcem Buyman anda ara tettwasbedd teɣsert-nni statiǧn de dẓtente, seg wansi ara ttwasseččent ihi akk tuddart n Ayt Smaɛel, send mara tesdaffel amḍiq « Aswel ". Mara yekfu umgar n tzemmilin, ad yettwasres ukaramdǧssier n tezrawt iwakken ad yettwajerred usenfar deg tazwara n useggas-a ara d-ikecmen n -Dɣa, rnu kra n wakud ad bdun yiqeddicen, i nessaram ur ttaɣen ara amecwar bac ad kfun. « S lferḥ d agaɛmir ay nlaqa lexber-a, nessaram kan ur yekkat xilla n yiseggasen bac ad yekfu ". I d-yenna yiwen n uɣerman n Ayt-Smaɛel.
Tutlayt akken yebɣu lḥal atteqim d ttutlyat, mači d-aɣbel. Yelha i wemdan akken ad yissin akk tutlayin n-umaḍal. D-acu kan, asmi ara attres deg weḥric n t’sartit tettuɣal dayen nniḍen. Dayen yaɛnan tutlayt taɛrabt deg t’murt nneɣ . Adabu seg wass n timunent ar ass-a yesnulfa-d tasertit n-uɛareb. Tasertit-agi « teḍla " ɣef t’metti nneɣ , ama deg uɣerbaz neɣ deg weḥricen nniḍen. Akken ẓran wid i faqqen i t’sertit-agi n-udabu, iswi-ines d-aɛerreb n weɣref Amaziɣ, acku ur yettmeslay ara tutlayt n-udabu. Tikta n « el umma el ɛarabiya " tewwi abrid-is…Arrac imaziɣen uḍenen deg yiɣarbazen. As-tini-ḍ ttidiren snat n tudartin. Deg wexxam, neɣ deg berra ttmeslayen s teqbaylit, ma deg yiɣerbazen ttbeddilen tutlayt akken ad meslayen s taɛrabt. Akken i ngar tamawt, arrac nneɣ uɣalen garen-d aṭaṣ n yimeslayen s taɛrabt, cennu-n cna s taɛrabt, llan kra zemren ad ak-inin: " d-acu-tt akka tamaziɣt-agi? ". Ayagi yusa-d seg t’sertit n-uɛarreb! Adabu ur yaḥbis ara dagi kan, yewweḍ alarmi id yesnulfa yiwwet n lɛefsa akken ad « yemḍel " aɣref Amaziɣ. As mi yewweḍ ad « izaɛzaɛ " allaɣen n warraw nneɣ s t’sertit-agi n-uɛarreb, yewwet lsas n t’metti taqbaylit s yiwwet n tikli yecban tin n lafɛa. Aɛerreb yewweḍ tura ɣer yimɣaren d temɣarin nni ur nekcim laɛmar nsen ɣer uɣerbaz. D wigi kan id yegran deg t’metti nneɣ ttmeslayen taqbaylit yeṣfan, s tikta n teqbaylit n zik. D wigi id yegaren lemɛun lakked d yisefra n Si Muḥ Umḥand, lakked Ccix Lḥusin, tagi d Tassekla taqbaylit taqburt, tin ur lemden ara warraw nneɣ deg uɣerbaz aɛrab! Lukan mazal Muḥya ad yini: " Ah a ddin uqabac! ". Akka, myal aseggas, iɣerbazen ssawalen-d i yimɣaren akk d temɣarin akken ad lemden tira d-umeslay n taɛrabt. Tagara-agi, ssiwlen-d deg taddart n Tuɣezza, id yezgan deg t’ɣiwant n Cerfa deg lwilyaya n Tubirett, timɣarin akken ad ruḥen-t ad mmarkin-t iman-nsen-t deg uɣerbaz akken ad lemden-t taɛrabt! Akka ihi, timɣarin nni tiḥninin i ḥarzen taqbaylit n lejdud ad ruḥen-t ad lemden-t taɛrabt ɣer tagara llaɛmar nsen-t, akken « ad s’hetrifen-t " s tutlayt n El Mutanabi! Nutenti yennumen isefra n zik nni lakked d timucuha, ad bedlen-t tikta akk d yidles i yiles! N’na zwina attelmed « ellif d-elba ", netta-t yennumen tettgalla s « waḥeq n Sidi el mufaq "? N’na Ǧeǧiga attaru « baba " d « mama " s taɛrabt, netta-t tennum t-cerru azemmur akken at ssisen zzit d yiniɣman? N’na Megduda yennumen icewiqen s taqbaylit attecnu « ṭalaɛa elbadru ɛalayna "? Ṛuḥ a a taqbaylit ṛuḥ… Sytthax.Y
Lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu teṭṭef amḍiq amenzu deg usefti deg waḥric n uyefki. Annect-a yettased s tebγest n yifellaḥen i yefkan laεtab iman-nsen akken ad-refden aḥric-agi, i wesnarni n tdamsa n tmurt. Maca deg seggasen-agi ineggura, ifellaḥen ttmagaren-d ugguren iwmi ur zmiren-ara, sebba n leγla n yisufar n wučči n lmal naγ lεelf, leγla n dwawi, rnu lexṣaṣ id-yettbanen di ttawilat, am trisiti, amman, ibardan d waṭas niḍen. Γas akken gten wugguren, maca ifellaḥen yettrebin lmal xarṣum wid yeseftayen deg uyefki dduklen afus deg ufus, xelqen-d tiddukliwin akken ad-mεawanen ad-affen tifrat s tdukli i wugguren-agi merra. Si tama niḍen, Tafidiralit n yifellaḥen yettrebin lmal tameqrant « Aksum azeggaγ d uyefki ", n lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu, tesḥasef aṭas γef yiεewiqen d wugguren id-ttmagaren yal ass. Γef aya sutren timliliyin akked yemḍebren taεna temsalt, ad-qqimen wa ad-sqardcen iγeblan s telqay i tifrat-nsen, s wudem yelhan. Tasqamut taγelnawt n tiddukla ifellaḥen izzayriyen, sḥasfen ula d nutni γef iεewiqen-agi id-ttmagaren yal ass ifellaḥen yettrebin lmal n lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu, imi tugget seg-sen ur-zmiren-ara i taεkkemt, dayen i ideggren kra seg-sen zenzen lmal-nsen. Γer tagara, ifellaḥen yettrebin lmal n lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu, sutren deg yemḍebren εlayen taεna temsalt, akken ad-ggren iman-nsen i tifrat n wugguren-agi s lεejlan ilfayda usnarni n tdamsa n tmurt Islam Bessaci Mhenni Xalifi
Ahat tura ugar n sa sebɛa n yiseggasen segmi tettwajerred deg yisenfaren n tɣiwant. Tamkardit n Ayt Smaɛel atan sebken lecɣal-is s wacḥal d ayyur tura almi qrib tettwattu. Ɣas ma yella, iban dakken, tamkardit-a tettwarǧa aṭas seg tal tama: mačči ala sɣur kra n yilemẓiyen i iḥemmlen taɣuri, wanag, ula seg yisɣuren iɣerbazanen ẓtablissements scǧlaires i ara sɛun taɣbalut s wazal-is seg wansi ara d-ssawaḍen idlisen iwatan i yinelmaden. War ma nesha, belli tamkardit ad tili daɣen d aɛwin n Tidukkla Tadelsant Adrar n Fad i yekkaten dima amek ara tessedles ilemẓiyen, ad ten-id-tesker deg tayri n tira akked tɣuri. Mi tettwaserref dayen tedrimt i yellan tettwar-as i tesga, ifares uselway n tɣiwant n Ayt Smaɛel tagnit, mass Ɛebdun Nasir, bac ad yessuter azal n tedrimt tayeḍ deg lwali n Bgayet ass mi d-yerza ɣer tɣiwanin n Yiderginen – Iderginen, Tasexriwt, Ayt Smaɛel – ass n 2 seg yunyu yezrin, swayes ara kemmlen yiqeddicen deg tebnayt-a i yeqqimen akken d tajmamt, skud ala iɣraben d sseqfat i yellan deg-s, umma aql-itt d ilem s tidet. Maca, akken i aɣ-d-tenna teɣbalut-nneɣ , ulac ssmamat i d-yeskanayen dakken ma texḍa taɣiwant n Ayt Smaɛel ad ttwasemmden yiqeddicen n temkarḍit-a. Hǧcine.M
I tikelt tis snat, aseggas-a, i ttuwtent tselmadtin deg uγerbaz Mimǧun n temdint n Tizi Uzzu. Tikelt-a, glan ula s unemhal. Amek teḍra temsalt? ddurt iεeddan, γef wakken i aγ-d-yenna unemhal n uγerbaz-a d akken yusa-d gma-s n yiwen n unelmad γer uγerbaz, yekcem γer tselmad n gma-s, yessawel-as teffeγ-d γur-s, dγa yewwet-itt. Syin yekker wahraḥu gar yiselmaden d yixeddamen. Mi d-iruḥ unemhal ad iwali d acu yeḍran, yemmuger-it yilemẓi-agi s tyitiwin ula d netta. Tekker ddunit ad telḥu. Iselmaden ḥefsen γef uxeddim s uzekka-nni ass-nni n larebεa ufan-tt-id dγa d sebba i wakken ad d-rnun γur-s liḥala taberkan ideg yettidir uγerbaz-nsen. ’Aγerbaz ixus si yal tama. Tiqit di yal tazeqqa, ammus γer tama n tneγriyin, lexsas n waman…atg. Lḥasun mačči d yiwet’’ i aγ-d-nnan yiselmaden. Win yewwten, ha-t-an akka tura di lḥebs n leεḍil. Llan wid i d-yusan, ssutren deg unemhal ad as-isemmeḥ, yella gar-asen ula d baba-s n yilemẓi-agi. Am wakken i d-usan, di&amtt;gamma,; yimḍebbren, yinemhalen n yiγerbazen-nniḍen akked sandika. Tamsalt tebda, γef wakken d-nnan imi taselmadt-a tewwet anelmad-nni syin yugi ad d-yas γer uγerbaz. Islam Bessaci
Aẓru d win yesεan amezruy meqren di tmurt n leqbayel, u dwin iwmi fkan azal imezdaγ-is, imi ixxamen n sser d lḥerma ttwabnan s weẓru, s yiwen n lqaleb, d ayen id-yernan cbaḥa meqren i tudrin leqbayel. Lḥirfa n wid yettruẓun aẓru di temnaḍt n leqbayel, ur telli-ara n wass-a, telḥad di seggasen, maca tura tenqes lxedma-agi s waṭas, sebba n laεtab meqqren id-ttmagaren deg-s itarasen, imi zik ttruẓun aẓru s wefḍis d tuẓẓal, dayagi id allalen yellan, rnu aṭas n yemdanen yettruẓun aẓru wexṛen i lḥirfa-agi sebba n waṭan meqqren id-taṭṭafen deg-s, wagi d aṭṭan n yedmaren la silicǧse, d aṭṭan i yesrewten acḥal d amdan. Γas akken tawilat n lxedma d wallalen gten tura, am tmacinin, rnu ttawilat i saxdamen i uḥareb γef tezmert-nsen, maca aṭas i irewlen γef lxedma-agi tamentilt yemdanen ur nesaxdam-ara aẓru di lebni, imi yuεar rnu γlay aṭas di ssuma. Macca, ass-a deqs n yemdanen i yesaramen ad-bnun s weẓru, imi yesεa cbaḥa d sser swayes ijebbed tamuγli. Dayen i yeğğan deqs n yemdanen n lwilayat yemgaraden n tmurt n Lzzayer, am Lzzayer tamanaγt, Blida, Tittaza, Wahran, tteqsaden-d timnaḍin-agi n lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu ger-asent Wizgan, Ifiγa, Iεeẓẓugen, ttaγen aẓru inejren. Si tama niḍen aṭas n yemdanen i yesḥasfen γef wid yettruẓẓun aẓru, imi xelqen-d ugguren meqqren i twenaḍt, am wesyax d wayen niḍen, dayen iyeğğan imsebriden ttkukrun aṭas i uεeddi xarṣum s ṭumubilat, amedya deg webrid n lwilaya uṭun wis 251 i icuden ger snat n tγiwanin, Wizgan akked Yiεeẓẓugen, anda iẓra γellin-d s waṭas, isyaxen sebba n yemdanen yettruẓun mebla tesriḥ, berra lqanun. Akka wa maεdur wa d lḥeq-is, llan yemdanen id-yessasayen amεic-nsen s truẓi n weẓru, acu kkan yewwi-d lḥal akken ad-ḥadren γef tezmert-nsen xarṣum aṭas n yedmaren. Γer tagara akken yeqqar yenzi « Aḥezzeb yugar leqḍaε ", yewwi-d lḥal γef yemdanen yettruẓun aẓru, akken ad-harben ama γef tezmert-nsen akken id-yewwi lḥal ad-ḥarben γef twenaḍt d wayen id as-d-yezzin.
Assegas amaynut n yimaziɣen ɣef tewwura. Deg umenzu n yennayer ad ibedd yal amaziɣ ɣef timadit-is akken ad yemekti anwi i t-illan, ansi i d-yekka, sani i iteddu, amek i d-teḍra d s teqbaylit-is. Akken ad yefti ugdud, ad iqazem tixidas n zzman ilaq-as ijga ɣef acu ara isenned. Ilaq-as tiliwa ansi ara d yeggem aman yetteksen fad i yiman. Ilaq-as akufi anda ara d yeddem lqut ara yefkken afud i "Nekk” ines yesmirjiḥen gar yir lemwaji: tid ara t-id yesufɣen ɣer rrif  lisser / lemnaɛ neɣ tid ara t-yezuɣren ɣer yimmi n nnger. Ayen yettqqawiten iman n umdan, ayen i tekksen fad ɣef ṛṛuḥ, ayen yettcuddun " Nekk” ɣer yiman-is d idles. Agdud melba idles am umdan melba iles id nnan imezwura. Ɣef aya i neɛreḍ ad nsuk tamuɣli ɣef yidles aqbayli seg asmi tewwi timunent tmurt ɣer ass-a n wussan.
Liḥala n yidles aqbayli deg issgasen n 60:
I wakken ad illal kra, ilaq ad yilli kra. Di tagara n isaggasen n ssettin tasekla taqbaylit tbedd ɣef yiwet n tqejirt: "tamedyazt”. Amur ameqran n wayen iccuden ɣer timsal n tidmi id yettnulfun s teqbaylit di lawan-nni yella s udem n isefra akked tezlatin. Wid is yefkan azal i unect-a, ɛarḍen ad leqmen isufar itararen i tmedyazt-agi d Slimane Azem Akked Cherif Kheddam, wama ayen nniḍen yella kan d isefra n tallit id tezzin ɣef isental ur d nettawi kra i tusna n umdan am tayri temeɛlalt, leɣrba, d kra n wugguren iccuden ɣer liḥala n twacculin di tallit-nni am zwaj, berru, iḥeckulen….
Tazwara n isaggasen n 70
Kra –nni id yellan, i-ibeddelen tagnit ɣef tasekla taqbaylit, d tizlit n Idir " baba inuba”. Aya yella-d di ttnaṣfa n isgassen n sebɛin. Timlilit yellan gar umedyaz Ben Mǧhamed akked uccenay Idir tbedel udem mačči kan i tizlit taqbaylit terna ula i lqaleb n tmedyazt taqbaylit. Ssin inaẓuren-agi segrewlen liḥala n yidles aqbayli s –umata. Seg assen-nni uɣalen imedyazen n teqbaylit ttemɛanaden anwa ara d yawwin ugar n tatrart ɣer tira –ines. Wakali, isental ɣef I t-tezzi tmedyaz-agi beddlen. Lqaleb n tira yembeddel, lhejna n twefɣa nnig uglugel treṣṣa iman-is di tesga n usnulfu s teqbaylit. Ahat Lǧunis Ait Menguellet d netta i-ineǧren asalu ɣer tanfalit deg tira s isefra-ines mechuren am "igenni-m trekeb-it tewla", " nnuɣeɣ yid-k ay yul-iw",” teseḍlemeḍ-iyi",” acu  ɣer", "ixef yettrun", "anida teǧǧam mmi” …Yuɣ lḥal widen yecfan I tallit-nni ttmektayen-d timzizlit yellan gar Lǧunis Ait Menguellet d Idir Ait Meslayen ɣer usnulfu n tezlatin yesduqusen lexwaṭer.
Ɣer leqruba n Mǧulǧud Mammeri
Kra agi id yellan, i-yefkan udem nniḍen I temedyazt taqbaylit ur d yekki ara s -ugacur imi inaẓuren-agi id yewwin abeḥri amaynut I yidles aqabyli i merra llan ɣer leqruba n Mǧulǧud Mammeri. Amezruy yura d akken d aragaz-agi is id ijaben aɛiwed n tllalit i yidles-nneɣ yellan ɣef yiri n ttmattent. Tajerrumt akked illugan n tira id yexdem Mǧulǧud Mammeri lldint tiwwura ɣer tira taɣezfent. Aya yewwid tawefɣa n ugalen imenza s teqbaylit s demma n Said Sadi yuran ungal "askuti", Rachid Alich yuran ssin ungalen " asfel”, " fafa”. Si lǧera n ssin imyura-agi yerna-d Amar Mezdad yuran ungla " yiḍ d wass”. S wakka I yenǧer usalu I teskla taqabylit s yal udmawen-is ama d tamedyazt, ama d tullisin, ama d ungalan, ama d amzgun. Ayen akken yecban, lmuḥal ziɣ yuɣal ɣef yimmi n leqlam.
Deg isaggasen n 80
Ɣlin ifergan zdat n tidmi, zdat n tebɣest, zdat n tismin ɣef yidles aqbayli. Di lǧera n Idir nnulfan-d aṭas n iccanayen d trebuyaɛ irefden tizlit taqbaylit ɣer tqacuct am terbaɛt n imaziɣen imula, igudar, ifeguren, ineṣliyen, Agraw, Malika Dǧmrane, Sǧfiane, Amɣid, Takfarinas… Ccna amḥadi yuffa lebɣi-s deg irebbi n Matǧub Lǧunes, Ait Menguellet, Amar Kǧbbi yefkan lmun i wawal aqbayli akken ad yeferfer nnig zrubat yellan ammer ad yinni i leǧnas meṛṛa anwi id aqbayli, amek tella timadit taqbaylit. Ɣer lǧiha n temdyazt akked ccna yenulfa-d umezgun s teqbaylit imi i tekelt tamenzut tella-d tasuqilit ɣer teqbaylit n tcequft n Kateb Yacine "Mǧḥand ddem tabalizt-ik”. D anect-a meṛṛa id yeṣawḍen ɣer usaru amenzu s teqbaylit id yesukkes Bǧuguermǧunh seg ungal n Mǧulǧud Mammeri "tawrirt yettwattun”. Deg isaggasen n tmanyin taḥajurt ɣer tḥajur bedden imawlen n yedles am Salem Chaker ɣer usijhed n uɣrab n teqbaylit s unnadi deg tjerrumt-ines, d illugan n tira ines. Di tallit-nni i bdan ttnulfun-d imawalen s teqbaylit. Amezwaru seg-sen d win yexdem Mǧulǧud Mammerie "amawal amaziɣ atrar s taqbaylit d tenfransist”. UIamek ara d nezger tallit-agi n tmanyin melba ma nbered imawalen id yefɣen deg tasɣunt " tafsut " yecqan tusnakt mathematiques a beɛdda adlis n Hend Sadi "tusnakt s wurar”. Imawalen yecqan "tafizikt” akked " tasegda”  l’architecture. Deg yiseggasen-nni diɣen id yella usnulfu n waṭas n tesɣunin s tufra ttefraqen madden s ddew iciwi wa ɣer wa. Ahat gar tesɣunin tin yeṭṭfen lbal deg akken leqay ugbur-ines d tasɣunt "tafsut” deg ttarun imusnawan imeqranen n tmazɣa ɣer idisan n Salem Chakler, Said Sadi, Ferhat Mhenni, Mǧulǧud Mammeri. Tasɣunt-agi tukalal as yettuɛawed usezrireg akken ad ddlun yimeɣriyen fell-as imia d yiwet n tssadart n umezruy n umenuɣ ɣef yidles amaziɣ. Di lǧeṛa wanect-a id tenulfa diɣen tasɣunt tusnant "awal” yettwasnen di ddunit meṛṛa ɣef yella di lmendad Mǧulǧud Mammeri.
Ait Slimane Hamid Hǧcine. M
