Aselmed-a d win ara d-yillin ɣef teɣzi n 2 ɣer 6 n wagguren, u ad setfaydint deg-s 575 n tilawin deg yeḥricen yemgaraden gar-asent amcaḍ, aẓetta, abrudi … Leḥirefat-a d tid i tezmer tmeṭṭut ad tent-xeddem deg uxxam-is. Ad ner lwelha belli aselmed-agi n leḥirfat d win ara yesaɛden aṭas n tlawin d telmeẓyin yeqqimen deg uxxam, yettidiren deg tamiwin ibaɛden n tmurt n leqbayel, melba ma xelsent. Tilawin i teɛna temsalt d tid ara yenejmaɛen deg wazal n 12 yid-sent. S wakka ad sutrent aselmed i tnemhalt n leḥirfat n lwilaya. Si tama niḍen ad ner lwelha belli aselmed-a d win yaɛnan daɣen tilawin yesɛan aswir n leqraya i igerzen d tid yesɛan yakan agerdas le dittlṛme imi aselmed yaɛna aḥric n leḥsabat ne  la cǧmtttabilitẓ BT, d texegaṭ le ttrḥt-à-ttǧrter i lemd n usewejed n le certificat de maitrise ttrǧfessiǧnnelle d l’’infǧrmatique. Deg taggara ad nesemekti belli lwilaya n Tizi Wezzu d tin yesɛn azal 45 n yexxamen n uselmed.
Ain ZawiaTiwaculin deg yir taswiɛt Timzeduɣin n wazal n 10 n twaculin d tid yenṭaren mačči d kra deg taddart Ikǧubaen d-yezgan deg usamar n tɣiwant n ain zawia deg wunẓul n lwilaya n Tizi Wezzu. Tiwaculin-a d tid ur neẓri anida ara ddunt s sebba n iɣeblan deg ttidirent. Taswiɛt-a d tin yeǧan imezdaɣ deg ddurt yezrin ad reglan abrid n lwilaya w-128 I yettawin ɣer Buɣni, i lemend n usuter n temzduɣin i tewaculin-a. Am akken suturen tifrat n weɣbel n wesyax i yellan d sebba yesenṭṭaren timzeduɣin. Ad nar lewelha belli yiwet n tesqamut i d-yesdukelen iɣalen n uḥareb, srabes n tmezduɣt n tɣiwant d tin yerzan ɣer wemkan anida I d asent—d-iban belli aseyax d win yelḥan azal n 150 n m2, d win yessenṭeren 10 n tmezduɣin. Zira
Ma tecfiḍ ay amdakel ɣef yiḍ-nni amezwaru, ɣef tmuɣli tamezwarut, yuder ccfaṛ yuli, temmermeɣ d imeṭṭawen, uzzlen am waman, aman n igenni, aman n lebḥer, aman n ṣṣura … ad tuɣal ad d-teswawi lehwa taneggarut. Iḍ-agi ɣezzif fell-I, ad faṛsaɣ leḥbab n wul: lḥal iṛuḥ am acemma, d lewhi n leḥdac n yiḍ, qrib ad yemmlal wass d yiḍ am akka I d-nemlal. Nemlal-d s wallen, s tikti, s tira, s ṣṣut, s nnhati, s ssuṛa, s ubeḥri. Nessuk-d tamuɣli ɣef taddart bnan at Ṛebbi ɣef waman. Ixxamen tḥenncen, wa s idis n wa, xas ferqen-ten waman, ijemɛi-ten ṣṣut ubeḥri n lyali am wakken d asčenčen n tzebgatin n yelli Ɣriba. Tasusmi n yiḍ tecbeḥ s teftilin, s rriḥa n lehna, s rriḥa n liser. Imi ara sen-tesselfeḍ s tmuɣli am zun tebriḍ I yman-ik ɣef waman, ad tiliḍ akken kan telliḍ, am uqeclaw, fessus, akken i s-yehwa ad yurar d waman, rsen neɣ rwin kif kif. Iḍ-agi ɣezzif fell-I ad faṛsaɣ leḥbab d tirni: d asuden n yiwen yiḍ, d tamuɣli n yiwen yiḍ, d iḍes n yiwen yiḍ, d lemḥibba n yiwen yiḍ, d afares n lehna n yiwen yiḍ, d ccnawi n yiwen yiḍ, d azuzen n yiwen yiḍ, d ul n yiwen yiḍ.Ɣer-I d asayes, ɣer-s d afaṛes. D iḍ aneggaru, iḍ n lebɣi, iḍ n lembat, iḍ n uraju n win tuyes. Qim-d yid-I si leɛḍil, ad tɛeddi zzedwa n uḥemmel, zzedwa n targit, zzedwa n lemni.. iḍa-agi ɣezzif fell-I, ad cnuɣ taɣect n waman, ad iliɣ am waman, ad lḥuɣ tikli n waman yettecruruden am wecrred ufus-is ɣef leḥrir, ad iɛzizeɣ I tmuɣli, "ad rwunt tarda wallen-ik, a winna ḥemmlaɣ”. Islam Bessaci
Taddert n yigreb di tγiwant n Yillula Umalu,, tesudes-d yiwen n leqdic s wazal-is i wass n 04 d 05 yulyu 2011,s teγzi n sin n wussan ilmend n umuli wis n 49 n timunnent n tmurt n Lzzayer anda ar ad-ldin yiwen n usebdad n 46 n yimeγrasen i yeγlin d asfel i tlelli n tmurt n Lzzayer. Ass n 04 yulyu ad d-tillint temzikniyin, isura n tegrewla d waddal. Tasebḥit n wass n 05 yunyu, d tulya n usebdad n 46 n yimeγrasen s wudem unsib, syen a d-yilli usarag n umazray mass Zinedine Kacimi γef umezruy n temnaḍt n yillula umalu. Tameddit n wass mbaεd imekli a d-yilli umeslay anagi temǧignage γef yimeγrasen d xazabiyin ixedmen deg tallit-nni. γer tagara d tekfu s tmaγra n taddert. Iwesmekti kan, taγiwant n Yillula Umalu d tamnaḍt tamenzut deg-γlin waṭas n yimeγrasen, ger-asen γlin 740 d amdan, γef waya teṭṭef amḍiq amenzu i tmurt n Lzzeyar. Nǧra
Ayen Ilaqen:– Kra imurṣuyen uyaẓiḍ.– Tibṣelt i igezmen d tarqaqt.– Ticcert yezḍen – Lemleḥ, ifelfel aberkan, skenjbir, lmeɛdnus.100g n wudi, 2tɣenjayin n zzit.
Abrid aɣelnaw uṭṭun 09, i yellan gar Bgayet d Ṣṭif, yella deg-s lexsas d ameqqran. Ama seg tama n uxeddim-is, imi yeččuṛ d imedwab, d yiceqqiqen, ama seg tin n tafat i iɣaben meḥsub deg-s. Amedya d abrid yellan gar Bgayet d Tici. Neɣ ma tella ur tleḥḥu ara. Rnu ɣer waya, llan yimukan deg-s d amahi ameqqṛan ɣef yinehhaṛen. Amedya d aɣayan ḍirage i yellan deg temnaḍt iwumu qqaren At Ɛnan, i yettabaεen i tɣiwant n Yiderginen. Aɣayan-a, idewwer mliḥ, ula d tafat ur yesεi ara. Mebla ma nettu belli, d abrid i iḥezzqen mliḥ, armi ur zmirent ad mlilent deg-s snat n tkeṛyas. Ayen yessuhamen ugar, amek i ttɛeddayen syin-a yikamyunen imeqqṛanen? Acku amkan-nni, yettwassen s umahi-s, ṣṣawden dɣa kra n yinehhaṛen, semman-as "ṭṭuṛna n lmut”.
I yissali, deqs n yisehwa i d-yeḍṛan deg wadeg-nni. Ḍran-d yineggura ass n 04 akked 07 fuṛar yezrin. Deg-sen dɣa llan aṭas n yimejṛaḥ. Ad d-nesmekti d akken, abrid-a i yellan gar tɣiwant n tsexriwt d win n Ssuq Letnin i yettεeddayen seg win n Yiderginen, segmi yettwaxdem deg useggas n 1879, ar ass-a ulac d acu i ibeddlen deg-s. Γef usentel-a yenna-aɣ-d yiwen n yilemẓi seg tɣiwant n Yiderginen: "mačči d tikkelt mačči d snat i d-nehder ɣef uɣbel-a, isehwa deg ubrid-a ur ḥebbsen ara, ladɣa deg unebdu. Tecfam ahat ɣef wayen i yeḍṛan i umḍiq n uẓebbuc ilindi, imi i yegrareb. Ayagi mi ṭṭuqten wid yettεeddayen syin-a. Lameεna imasayen ur d-ggaren ara tamawt i waya, ḥacama tewweḍ tiyita ɣer yiɣes. Ihi ad d-nεiwed tiɣri i yimasayen i wakken ad xedmen abrid-a, ad t-swessεen, uqbel ad ifat lḥal ".K. K.
I lmend n usmekti wis 58 n tmenɣiwt n Lmulud At Caɛban, nesseqsa mmi-s Ali ɣef wanda yewweḍ leqdic n Tesbeddit Mǧulǧud Feraǧun imi d netta i d aselway-is. Ɣef waya, yenna-d: ’Tella-d Tesbeddit Mǧulǧud Feraǧun i yidles d usedwel, i d-ilulen deg useggas n 2012, i wakken ad d-tessifrir isem n Mǧulǧud Feraǧun akked leqdicat-is, ladɣa i tsutwin timeẓyanin. Aṭas n leqdicat i nexdem, ama d isaragen neɣ timsikniyin. Mačči kan dagi deg lwilayat n daxel, meɛna ula deg usammar, deg unẓul d umalu, am Batna, Wehran, Sṭif, Xennecla, Sɛida, Biskra akked tiyaḍ. Nezmer ad d-nini, nxeddem azal n 12 ɣer 15 n temliliyin deg useggas.
D Tasbeddit Mǧulǧud Feraǧun i yidles d usedwel i d-yeskecmen, i tikklet tamezwarut, amsuḍen n tira n umaru. Aṭas n yimussnawen n taɣult-agi i ixedmen akked Tesbeddit Mǧulǧud Feraǧun i wakken ad fken afus n tallelt i Mass Abdelwahab Medjadj, amaray amatu n Tesbeddit i yessawḍen ad yexdem azal n 5 000 n yisebtar gar wayen yura Mǧulǧud Feraǧun. Leqdic-agi, ad yili deg uẓeṭṭa inmetti i wid yebɣan ad t-yesseqdec, ama d inelmaden, isdawanen neɣ wid yettnadin s umata ɣef tira n Mǧulǧud Feraǧun. Iswi agejdan n Tesbeddit, d tullya n yiwen n wammas i medden anda ara yilin yidlisen n temkerḍit n Mǧulǧud Feraǧun, ayen yura d tɣawsiwin-is s umata. Deg useggas n 2019, teqdec Tesbeddit akked yiwen n umsuffeɣ i wakken ad d-swejden yiwen n usaru-arrat ɣef Mǧulǧud Feraǧun i lmend n umulli wis 60 n timunent n Lezzayer akked lmut n Mǧulǧud Feraǧun.
Ma ɣef yisenfaren ara d-yilin deg ussan i d-iteddun, ad d-nebder tuffɣa n tesɣunt taseklant Fǧurǧulǧu, asizreg n wungal ’La citẓ des rǧses, liḍre que Feraǧun aḍait titrẓ L’anniḍersaire’’, anda ara yili, diɣ, ciṭ n umeslay ɣef Etsukǧ Aǧyagi n tesdawit n Tǧkiǧ i yessuqlen u yesizergen deg Jattǧn ungal ’Le fils du ttauḍre’’ deg useggas n -I usmekti, i lmend n tuffɣa n wungal-agi, tella-d temlilit deg Tǧkiǧ anda teḥder Tesbeddit Mǧulǧud Feraǧun i yidles d usedwel. Am wakken ad yili usizreg-nniḍen sya ar anebdu n ’’Jǧurnal 1955/1962’’ anda ara d-ddun tikkelt-a iḍrisen yura Feraǧun deg meɣres, wid-nni ur d-neddi ara deg tezrigt n -Am wakken ara d-yili usizreg s taɛrabt n ’’Jǧurnal 1955/1962’’ i yettwaxedmen deg Maṣer. Llan diɣ aṭas n yisenfaren i useggas-agi n 2020, ara d-nini deg lweqt-nsen’’.Yesteqsa-t H. Mǧula
Ad tessuddes Texxamt n tfellaḥt n lwilaya n Tizi-Uzzu s lmendad n tenmehla n srabes n tfellaḥt n Tizi-Uzzu d Iferḥunen, yiwen n wass n tussna ad d-yilin ass-agi, 24 deg waggur n yulyu 2019, ɣef 10h n tsebḥit, deg taddart n Zubga, yettabaεen ɣer tɣiwant n Illilten.
Ad d-yili usentel n temlilit-agi ɣef yidles d wayen i icudden ɣer tfellaḥt n unetrum, neɣ Lḥebb Lemluk cerise. Ɣef waya dɣa, tger-d Texxamt n tfellaḥt n Tizi Uzzu tiɣri i yifellaḥen n temḍiqt-agi akken ad d-asen s ṭṭaqa, akken ad-d sfaydin seg temlilit-agi ideg ara yilin aṭas n yimussnawen n uḥric n tfellaḥt.
Ad-d-awin yimussnawen-agi awal ɣef useklu n lḥebb lemluk, d wazal n lɣella-agi, ama seg tama n tdawsa, ama seg tama n tdamsa. Am wakken ara mmeslayen diɣ ɣef wamek i ilaq ad d-tili tuẓut iwatan n useklu-agi, amek i t-fersen d wamek i t-leqmen.
Gar yimussnawen ara d-yessidren timlilit, ad naf Mass Kaci Bǧukhelfa, d amazzay, d amaswaḍ n wayen yeεnan yakk iberden n useḥbiber ɣef yimɣan d yisekla. Rnu ɣef waya d imeḍebber deg tenmehla n srabes n tfellaḥt n Tizi Uzzu.Ali Zalǧuk
I lmend n zerri n ṭam n yiseggasen segmi yemmut Muḥemmed Benḥanafi, awadem n tsekla d tmedyazt taqbaylit, yiwet seg tgejda yefkan tudert-nsen i rradyu n teqbaylit, thegga-d Ǧurida Sider, yiwen n usenfar asaru-arrat fell-as. Tessenked-d tazwart ɣef tikti n leqdic-a, ass-nni n 4 meɣres deg tiliẓri n Brtḍ, anda i d-fkan kra n yiwudam, inaẓuren d yimnadiyen, seg wid ixedmen d Benḥanafi, neɣ wid i t-yessnen, tinagiyin fell-as i temsuffeɣt Massa Sider. Taneggarut-a, tebges i leqdic-a, seg wasmi i d-tessuffeɣ adlis n tejmilt fell-as. Tikti, tusa-as-d seg Tfaska taɣelnawt n usaru amaziɣ, tenna ay  ɣer ala ur d-yettili ara usaru ɣef Benḥanafi i d-yewwin abrid n Si Muḥ Umḥend? Tenna-d "Ur yeshil ara akken ad texdmeḍ anadi ɣef yiwen am Benḥanafi, ladɣa ma d ayen yerzan asaru, yesran i waṭas n wallallen, itiknikiyen neɣ d wid n tedrimt”.
Maca, s tebɣest d lebɣi n tririt n tejmilt seg tama, d tririt n ureṭṭal seg tayeḍ, tessaweḍ ɣer lebɣi-s, acku akken i d-tenna Massa Sider, aṭas i tt-iɛawen Benḥanafi deg umaṭṭaf, telmed-d aṭas seg tussna-s, tamedyazt-is, d tudert-is s umata. Am wakken tella daɣen seg wid icerken amahil i waṭas n yiseggasen yid-s. Akken i iɛawen azal n ukkuẓ n tsutwin i d-iɛeddan seg uxxam n umaṭṭaf wis sin, I wakken ad nẓer azal ila urgaz-agi. Dɣa teṣber aṭas akken ad temmed aṣenfar-is. Asaru-a, yewwi-d ɣef tmeddurt n urgaz aseklan s umata, anwa-t, tudert-is di tegrawla, imi yekki d anesɣamu lkumisar deg tama n umalu, leqdic-is di rradyu tis snat i wazal n 45 n yiseggasen akked tudert-is deg temnaḍt n Medrissa deg Tyaret.
Ɣef way  ɣer armi d imir-a i tebges temsuffeɣt n umaṭṭaf wis sin i leqdic am wa, tenna belli "Ahat asmi yella yedder Benḥanafi, tili ur iqebbel ara, neɣ ur yettmuddu ara azal i wayen-nni, acku ur iḥemmel ara ad mmeslayen wiyaḍ s waṭas fell-as, yezga yeqqar anwa i ɣef tettmeslayeḍ”, ɛlaḥasab n Ǧurida i ixedmen yid-s. Tessarem d leqdic ara iɛejben wiyaḍ, acku akken tenna dima, ilaq d nekni ara ixedmen ayla-nneɣ , ad as-nefk lqima, u ad nesseḥbiber fell-as. Asaru, ur yettɛeṭṭil ara ad d-yeffeɣ, s sin n yiḥricen n 52 mn. Syin, ad d-yezzin i tzeɣwa n tẓuri d ccna. Khaled Achǧui
Mbeɛd ddeqs n yiseggasen n uraǧu, tberreḥ-d Tebniqt n teywalt n Bgayet deg yiwen n ulɣu d akken, ɣer taggara, ad d-sfaydint tɣiwanin n Yiderginen d Tsexriwt, deg usamar n Bgayet, s usenfar n tuqqna ɣer lgaz n temdint deg wakuden iqerben i d-itteddun. Iban-d d unsib waya mi d-yessawel lwali n Bgayet i yiselwayen n tɣiwanin-a i d-nebder, Massen Xalef d Buǧiṭ, akken kan ad asen-d-iberreḥ s telɣut. Yuɣ lḥal, akken i d-tewwi teɣbalut-nneɣ , yella yuzzel s timmad-is s usuter ɣur Uɣlif n wafud ẓnergie armi i as-t-id-qeblen. Deg wawal i d-fkan i tɣamsa seld timlilit-nni akked lwali, yesnemmer lmir n Tsexriwt Mass Mɛabed, yerna ibarek lgaz-a i yiɣermanen.
Akken ula d lmir n Yiderginen, ulamma yessarem ur ttilin ara abeɛda yisergal seg tama n yimezdaɣ mi ara d-yaweḍ lawan n usɛeddi n usenfar seg tferkiwin-nsen. Ilaq ad d-nini, yusa-d yisalli-a am tmuffirt yessefraḥen i yimezdaɣ n tɣiwanin-a acku tuɣ ur llin deg wahil n useggas-a. Seld mi d-yeffeɣ usenfar n lgaz i tɣiwant n Ayt Smaɛel, ara d-yettwawin si twilayt n Sṭif, aṭas i yellan ttmesteqsayen acu  ɣer ur d-ddint ara tɣiwanin n Tsexriwt d Yiderginen, neɣ daɣen ansi ara d-ɛeddin yijeɛbuben-nni n wurrig lgaz. Ma yella si tɣiwant n Ayt Smaɛel, amek ara yili lḥal d taddart n rrif, neɣ seg Suq Letnin i  ɣer i d-yewweḍ yakan usenfar n lgaz.
Tura ihi, seld asenseb n yisalli n tuffɣa n usenfar i tɣiwanin-a, yezmer lḥal seg Suq Letnin ara d-iɛeddi, ad d-ikemmel alamma d Tasexriwt. Yewwi-d ad d-nesmekti belli yettuneḥsab usamar n Bgayet gar tamiwin tineggura i d-yesfaydin s usenfar-a n wurrig agaman. Ula d imezdaɣ, ɣas ulamma umren, ḥsan iɛeṭṭel mliḥ wurrig-a ad yekcem s ixxamen-nsen di tmurt i yettwassnen tesnuzuy-it ula i tmura tiwerdanin.M. K.
Deg yiwen udewenni i texddem Tselwayt n Tudssa taɣelnawt n yimɛelmen d iṛemmasen izzayriyen i yiwen uɣmis, tuɣal-d s wawal tselwayt n Tudssa ɣer tezɣint crise tettidir tmurt n Lezzayer deg yiseggasen-agi ineggura, ladɣa ayen i icudden ɣer tdamsa n tmurt. Ɣef Leḥsab n Massa Samia El Makhlǧufi, taselwayt n Tudssa " Ad d-yili uneḥbus n qrib n umelyun n yixeddamen sya ɣer taggara n useggas-agi i deg i nella, ma yella ur d telli ara tifrat n tezɣint i ttidirent wazal n 5 800 n tkebbanit timeẓyanin d tlemmasin. "
Agemmuḍ-agi n yimeḍqan n uxeddim ara iruḥen, ad yernu ɣer 600 000 n yimeḍqan n uxeddim iḥebsen s ssebba n uɣlaq n 30 000 n tkebbaniyin timeẓyanin d tlemmasin gar waggur n fuṛaṛ d yulyu iɛeddan. Tger-d tiɣri tselwayt n Tudssa-agi i yimḍebbren teɛna temsalt akken ad d-rren lewhi-nnsen i tifrat n yiɣeblan meqqren i ttidirent tkebbanit-agi n tmurt d uxlaq n uxeddim i yelmeẓyen yesɛan tikebbaniyin. Dima ɣef Leḥsab n Massa Samia El Makhlǧufi " Azal n 5 800 n tkebbaniyin i yeseftayen deg taɣulin yemgaraden, ladɣa deg taɣult n lebni, tadawsa, tafellaḥt d temguri ara iɣelqen tiwwura-nnsent, d ayen ad d-yeglun s ustixer n qrib n umelyun n yixeddamen ".
Tenna-d daɣen d akken " Tamguri tazzayrit ur tezmir ara, akken yebɣu yili lḥal, ad tidir kan s 9 neɣ 10 n yigrawen imaguriyen yettabaɛen ɣer yimɛelmen imeqqṛanen. " D luluf n tkebbaniyin timeẓyanin, i d xelqen yilmeẓyen yesɛan tissugra, yettwaḥesben gar yinesmalen igejda n uxlaq n tbaɣurt sɛaya taɣelnawt, ass-a, twaxenqen akken iwata seg yal tama, dayen ad d-yeglun s uɣlaq-nnsent ma yella ur d-yessekcem ara iman-is Uwanak i tifrat n yiɣeblan yeṭṭuqten ɣef tkebbaniyin-agi. « Tuɣal-d s wawal daɣen ɣef wayen s wacu i d-glant temsalt n tejɛal i d-yellan i seg d-glant temsbaniyin seg 22 furar iɛeddan, dayen i d-ixelqen aṭas n yiɣeblan n tukci n tedrimt i tkebbaniyin timeẓyanin’’.
" D luluf n tkebbaniyin yesɛan ṭṭlaba, ufant-d iɣeblan meqqren deg unerḍul n tedrimt seg lbankat akken ad d- xedmet isenfar-nnsent, s ssebba n ṛṛayat i iḥuzan igrawen imeqqranen i ittekkan deg tjeɛɛal d tkerkas ". Tenna-d daɣen: " Tuget n yiḥricen n tdamsa ad ten-tḥaz tezɣint n cceḥa n tedrimt d usenqes deg usefti n Uwanak deg yisenfar imeqqranen’’.
Ɣas akken ɛeddan qrib kraḍ n yiseggasen segmi i d-iberreḥ uneɣlaf amenzwaru s tuɣalin n tutlayt n tmaziɣt d tunṣibt, maca leqdic deg unnar, ixuṣṣen nezzeh.
Abrid tura i yebda i tikli, imi aṭas n uxeddim i yurǧan akken ad d-tbin tmaziɣt d tidet d tutlayt tunṣibt deg unnar. Dɣa ussan-a, tceyyeɛ yiwen n lamer teɣlift n daxel i yiqerra n lwilayat, akken ad d-tili tira s tutlayt n tmaziɣt i tettlakin tiwilayin timeqqranin i d-iḥerren tilisa gar twilayt d tayeḍ tid i d-yettmagar umdan mi ara yekcem deg wakal n twilayt. Deg tebrat i yuzen umaray amatu n teɣlift-a, Ṣaleḥ Ddin Deḥmun, ass n 27 duǧember yezrin, yessuter deg-sen ad gen leqdic iwulmen i ccɣel-a, ad bdun seg tura i uheggi n usenfar-a unṣib deg yakk aɣiren n tmurt, seg 12 yennayer -Annect-a ad yili i lmend n usfugel n yennayer, ixef n useggas n yimaziɣen. Deg umeslay n umazan, yenna d akken leqdic-a amaynut yekcem gar tezwariyin ttriǧritẓs, acku tura tamaziɣt tuɣal d tutlayt taɣelnawt tunṣibt seg useggas n 2016, ɣef waya yessefk ad yili uɣiwel deg leqdicat yecban wi. Ladɣa deg wayen yarzan asuɣel n tettlakin n usnubget neɣ tideblanin.
Deg lamer-a yettuceyɛen, ddan-d akk yismawen n twilayin d twilayin tinesmigalin dẓlẓguẓs ttwarunt s tutlayt n tmaziɣt. Maca, ar tura ur neẓri ara s wanwi isekkilen ara yili ccɣel-a, ma yella s yisekkilen n tfineɣ akken i yennum useqqamu unnig n timmuzɣa yetteg s lemɛawna akked tdeblin timatuyin, imi yella-d yakan usuɣel n waṭas n tettlakin ɣer tmaziɣt s yisekkilen-a n tfineɣ. Neɣ wissen tikkelt-a, ma yella s yisekkilen n tlatinit, i yettwasemrasen ass-a deg tuget n tirawin yettilin s tmaziɣt, ama deg tesdwiyin, deg yiɣerbazen, neɣ deg yidlisen n tmaziɣt i d-yetteffɣen.
Ad yeldi uɣerbaz tiwwura-s i tuɣalin n yinelmaden ass n larebɛa, 4 deg cutember 2019, i lmend n useggas aɣurbiz 2019/-D inelmaden n uɣerbaz amenzu d wid n ulemmas akked wid n tesnawit ara yuɣalen deg wazemz-a, i d-isenṣeb uneɣlaf n usegmi. Ma d iselmaden, ad yaɣ lḥal uɣalen, imi nutni ad kecmen uqbel yinelmaden, ass n lḥedd, 1 deg cutember -Yetturaǧu, ad tebdu temsirt tamezwarut, s wudem unṣib, ass-nni n tuɣalin n yinelmaden, meḥsub ass n larebɛa, 4 deg cutember.
Ma d afraq akked usenzi n yidlisen, ilaq ad ifak uqbel deg wussan imenza n waggur n tuber i d-iteddun. Ma d tuɣalin n yixeddamen akked yinemhalen ad tili ass n lḥed, 25 ɣuct -Ma deg wayen yerzan leǧrida n yimuras n useggas-agi aɣurbiz amaynut, yefka-d uɣlif n usegmi aɣelnaw azemz n talliyin-agi. Imuras n ḥertadem lexrif, ad d-ilin aseggas-a seg wass n ttlata 29 tuber ɣer wass n lḥed 3 unbir 2019, wid n tegrest ccetwa, ad d-ilin tikkelt-a, seg wass n lexmis 19 duǧember 2019 alamma d ass n lḥed 5 yennayer -Imuras n tefsut, yetturaǧu ad d-ilin seg wass n lexmis 19 meɣres alamma d ass n lḥed 5 yebrir 2020, wid n unebdu ad d-ilin tazwara n yulyu. Am wakken i tetturaǧu tullya d uɛiwed n usexdem mise en serḍice n 656 n yisɣuren seg tuɣalin-agi n 4 cutember i d-iteddun. 426 d iɣerbazen imenza, 137 d iɣerbazen ilemmasen akked 93 n tesnawiyin, yettwaferqen ɣef 48 n lwilaya n tmurt n Lezzayer.A. A.
Ɣef wakken i d-yenna ussan-a yezrin uneɣlaf n umahil, n useqdec n tɣellist tinmettit, Mass Ḥasan Teǧǧani Haddam, ad yili kra n ubeddel deg uɣram n yisɛeddiyen insnujjyanen. Yenna-d aya deg wawal-is i d-yefka i tɣamsa di tama n Galma, i lmend n tirza i t-yewwin ɣer din imi, akken i d-iberreḥ, ttheggin deg ugezdu-is i usemres n sswami-a timaynutin akken ad ḍemnen aqɛad n tedrimt n Yisenduqen n ṭṭmana tinmettit.Yerna-d daɣen d akken ssuma n uɣram n yisɛeddiyen isnujjyanen ɣur yimsujjiyen imatuyen d wuzzigen « yeǧǧa-tt wakud acku tettuɣal i yiseggasen n 1980 ", am wakken i d-yessegza belli ad d-yeḍru uɛiwed n tmuɣli ɣef sswami n uɣram akken ad tezg akked tzemmar tidrimanin n Yisenduqen n ṭṭmana tinmettit. Rnu ɣer waya, ɣef wakken i d-yenna dima, yewwi-d ad d-yili uɛiwed-a n tmuɣli n uɣram ɣef leḥsab n wannect i d-sqamen yisɛeddiyen ɣur ṭṭebbat.
Seld ameslay-a ɣef « wuguren " n tedrimt n Yisenduqen n ṭṭmana tinmettit, aṭas n yimdanen i yettmesteqsayen si tura amek ara yili ubeddel-a, abeɛda igellilen seg-sen. «Nessaram d ayen ara yilin ɣef leḥsab n tdamsa n yal axxam d liḥala tinmettit n yal tawacult. Acku ma yella amek ara yili uɣram n win irekden si tama n tedrimt ara yili ɣef uẓawali, dinna d ugur, d lbaṭṭel ameqqran ", i d-yenna yiwen n uɣerman si Bgayet. Ad d-nesmekti ɣer taggara, d akken yebder-d uneɣlaf aheggi, deg wakuden i d-iteddun, n temliliyin ɣef tɣellist tinmettit akken ad yettwaldi uskasi azedgan ɣef taluft-a gar waṭas n tamiwin, akken ad suffɣen ɣer yisumar n tifrat yelhan, syinna ad ttwaseknen i snat n texxamin n uttarlaman, APN d Sẓnat.
I wakken ad d-afen tifrat i uɣbel n yiselmaden yellan deg umuɣ n tmeṛjiwt  liste d’attente , nnejmaεen yimutlayen ttǧrte-ttarǧles  n yiselmaden-a, akked yimasayen n uɣlif n usegmi. Ayagi imi ddeqs n yiselmaden i yettεassan ad asen-d-ssiwlen, meεna ur d-iban kra. Ama d wigad n uswir amezwaru, i d-yeffɣen deg useggas n 2018 neɣ d wid n uswir alemmas akked tsenawit, i d-yeffɣen deg useggas n -Rnu ɣer waya, ɣef leḥsab n yimutlayen n yiselmaden, llan imukan ideg xuṣṣen yiselmaden. Meεna imḍebbṛen n tenmehliwin n usegmi, ur d-ssawlen ara.
Seld amciweṛ gar yimutlayen n yiselmaden d yimasayen n uɣlif n usegmi, ineggura-a, nnan-asen-d belli ad ḥebsen asiwel i yiselmaden n umuɣ n tmeṛjiwt, seld 31 duǧember 2019, imi acḥal-ayagi segmi i d-yeffeɣ umuɣ-a. D ayen i yeǧǧan iselmaden i yellan sεan asirem ad xedmen, yeffeɣ-iten leεqel, ladɣa imi aseggas-a meḥsub yekfa. Seg tama-nniḍen, llan wid yumren s teɣtest-a, ladɣa inelmaden i d-yeffɣen seg tesdawit ur ufin ara axeddim. Acku ad asen-tettunefk tegnit ad tekkin deg temsizzelt i d-iteddun.
Ad d-nesmekti d akken iselmaden-a i rebḥen deg yiseggasen n 2017, 2018, ur qbilin ara s ṛṛay-a n yimasayen n uɣlif n usegmi. Ɣef waya i refden ula d nutni taɣtest belli ad uɣalen ɣer tikliwin, d yinejmuεen sdat n tenmehliwin n usegmi armi d ass ara d-rren i wayen i ssuturen. Ladɣa imi di lawan-a ideg nella, ssuturen akk abeddel, bɣan ad d-rren izerfan-nsen i iruḥen. Γef usentel-a, tenna-aɣ-d yiwet n tselmadt: "sin n yiseggasen-aya nekk ttεassaɣ ad i yi-d-ssiwlen, yal mi ara rzuɣ ɣer Tenmehla n Bgayet, qqaṛen-iyi-d ulac imukan, nekk di taddart anda i zedɣeɣ llan yimukan. Daymi i zriɣ belli kullec s tmussni, ihi d awezɣi ad nessusem ɣef uzref-nneɣ i ṛuḥen”.
Ulac d acu akk iweɛren deg ddunit am tegnit n ṭṭiq d waṭṭan, ladɣa ma tekka-d nnig-iɣil-ik. Asli Mǧhand, argaz bu 37 n yiseggasen, yessexdem akk ttawilat-is d tedrimt-is, armi ur yezmir ara ad iqabel iman-is. Daya i yessawḍen tawacult tameẓyant d tmeqqrant n Asli Mǧhand, ad d-tger tiɣri i yimezdaɣ n lwilaya n Tizi Uzzu i wakken ad ttekkin akk deg twizi n ujmeɛ n yidrimen i ilaqen i umuḍin-a. D mmi-s n taddart n Ikhelǧuiene deg tɣiwant n Ait Aissa Mimǧun, d ababat n sin n yigerdan. Ixeddem aṣeffi n yidamen seg useggas n 2015 deg ssbiṭer n Tizi Uzzu, d acu kan tikkelt-agi, ilaq-as ad yinig ɣer berra i wakken ad yexdem tamhelt n uleqqem n tegẓelt. Ass-nni n lǧemɛa, tameddit n wass, temlal teseqqamut n taddart-agi n Ikhelǧuiene d waṭas n tuddsiwin-nniḍen; tidukliwin, tiseqquma n tudar, iselwayen n tɣiwanin… Tettwasbed yiwet n teseqqamut ara d-yelhin s ujmeɛ n tedrimt-agi ilaqen. Dɣa syin i tebda twizi-agi n ujmeɛ n yidrimen, ama di ssuq n Tala Atmane, ama deg temdint n Tizi Uzzu. Yella-d diɣ usersi n wayen din n tbewwaḍin di tḥuna d leqhawi n lwilaya n Tizi Uzzu. "Asli Mǧhand, yeḥwaǧ lemɛawna-nwen” d wagi i d alugu n twizi-agi. Taɣiwant n Ait Aissa Mimǧun merra, tecmel i yiɣallen-is i wakken ad tefk asirem n tudert i mmi-s Mǧhand, i d-yessutren lemɛawna-s. Yal yiwen yebda s wayen iwumi yezmer, wa yerfed tibewaḍin, wa iɛawen s tedrimt-is, wayeḍ s ttawilat-is, iswi d yiwen d ajmeɛ n tedrimt ilaqen d usellek n Mǧhand. I wid yebɣan ad ɛiwen, ha-t-an usmiḍen n lbanka: 00200034034130010803 BNA n Tizi Uzzu. Nessaram-as ccfa d ḥellu i ASLI Mǧhand, akken gar-nneɣ ad ibedd.Adaǧun Abdelghani
Tadayṛa n Yiderginen, seg tid ikessben idigan icebḥen nezzeh deg twilayt n Bgayet, amedya d aceṛcur n Kefrida akked win n Umazzer. Rnu ɣer wigi, amkan iwumu qqaṛen Amḍiq n uẓebbuc, dɣa deg-s, tzad thuski. Imi tazeggzuyt n yimɣan d ttjuṛ, tjebbed tamuɣli n umdan s tduli-s taṛbiεit. Mabla ma nettu asif n waman i yettuɣalen d lemri n ccbaḥa n temnaḍt-nni, ladɣa ma terna-d fell-as tafat n tafukt. Lameεna, ayagi yakk, ur as-fkin ara yimḍebbṛen n tdayṛa d tɣiwant n Yiderginen azal imi rran-t d amkan n udeggeṛ n uhicuṛ, εedmen isem n ugama deg-s. Ad d-nesmekti d akken, ula d asif n Uɣeṛyun ur yeslik ara.
Acku ayen akk yettenḍeggaṛen deg Umḍiq n uzebbuc, ijemmeε-it wasif n Uɣeryun. Aneggaru-a, yuɣal d asif n umuṛej d uhicuṛ n lmaεeṣrat. « Ayen yessewhamen ugar, d amek i εemmden yimasayen n twennaḍt n twilayt n Bgayet i uxessar yecban wagi, di lawan anda i zemmren ad terren d adeg i tmerrit ". D awal n yiwen n umezdaɣ seg tɣiwant n Yiderginen. Seg tama-nniḍen, asif n Uɣeṛyun, yeṣṣawaḍ aman i yilel n Ssuq Letnin. S unamek wayeḍ, d amahi d ameqqṛan i ɣef nettmeslay.
Ama i twennaḍt, i yimdanen neɣ i tilmas esttAces i yettidiren deg yilel. Rnu ɣer waya, d anebdu i d-iteddun, ihi d tazmert n yimdanen i yellan deg urar. Di taggara, yewwi-d ad d-nebder belli, imezdaɣ n tɣiwanin n Yidergiben akked Ssuq Letnin, zgan d acekti, ahat ad d-sslen yimḍebbṛen n tɣiwanin-nsen, ad frun aɣbel n ugudu.K. K.
Macahu tellemcahu ad tt-yeḍbeε Ṛebbi d asaru. Yiwen urgaz yeqqar-as i mmi-s: "Ammi i wacu teṛṛiḍ akk medden d imeddukkal deg ur d-itekk nfaε? Ugadeɣ limmer ad ten-tiḥwiǧeḍ di tegnit n ddiq, yiwen ur ak-d-yeqqaṛ anεam. Mmi-s ur yesmeḥsis ara i wawal acku iɣil tizegzewt d leḥcic meṛṛa.Yeqqaṛ-as i baba-s: "Sεiɣ leḥbab yal amḍiq, mačči am kečč, ur tufiḍ ara win ara ak-iḥemmlen seg wakken teswaεreḍ timsal aṭas. Baba-s: "A mmi, nekk sεiɣ yiwen n uḥbib beṛka, deg-s lbaraka, jeṛṛbeɣ-t, ufiɣ-t d argaz. Yugi mmi-s ad yili d uḥdiq. Argaz terra-t tmara ad ixdem kra i wakken tabṛat-is ad d-taweḍ s allaɣ n win ara d-yeǧǧ d asalas n uxxam. Tusa-t-id tikti amzun-itt. Iddem ikerri, yezla-t, iɣumm-it s ubeḥnuq mellulen, yessames-it d idammen. Yuzzel ɣer mmi-s, yessawel-as: "Kker kker a mmi, teḍra-yi-d dagi taluft”. Ikker-d mmi-s s tɣawla: "Acu a baba d acu?” Nɣiɣ yiwen s ujenwi.
Tenɣiḍ -t? Anida-t?
Ṛwaḥ ad t-twaliḍ. Mi t-iwala mmi-s yexlaε, yenna-as: "A baba amek ara as-nexdem?”. Baba-s: "Ruḥ a mmi muqel-d albaεḍ seg leḥbab-ik i wakken ad aɣ-iεiwen ad t-nawi sanda ara t-nɣebbi”. Iruḥ uqcic ttnaṣfa n yiḍ, yezzi-d akk ɣef leḥbab-is, win iwumi yeḥka tadyant ad as-d-yerr: "Ala, ur zmireɣ ara i tigi”. Yuɣal-d uqcic s axxam. Baba-s: "Acimi akka ur d-tewwiḍ ara imεawnen?”. Mmi-s: "Ugin, uggaden”.
Amek ara nexdem ihi?
Ruḥ a baba ɣer Dda leflani, yak d aḥbib-ik. -Ad ruḥeɣ ala netta i sεiɣ. … Yettkemmil Yahia Yanes
Akemmel n uḥric 1u
Mi yewweḍ, yessawel-as, yeffeɣ-d, yenna-as: "D lxiṛ kan, acu i ak-id-yewwin di ttnaṣfa n yiḍ?”. Yerra-as: "Ay aḥbib, nɣiɣ argaz, aql-i ala nekk d mmi, ilaq win ara aɣ-d-iεiwnen di lbaḍna-agi”. Yerra-as uḥbib-ines: "Ṛǧu-yi akka amecwaṛ”. Qqimen netta d mmi-s ttṛaǧun armi a-t-a yeffeɣ-d. Iḥelles-d i uɣyul, yerna yewwi-d yid-s agelzim, amrar d wayen ara yeḥwiǧ. Mi wwḍen ɣer uxxam, yenṭeq s aḥbib-is: "Anida-t wagi tenɣiḍ?”. Yewwi-t urgaz ɣer umkan, yetti-d abeḥnuq-nni, dɣa iban-d ikerri s wacciwen-is. Yuɣal mmi-s yewhem, ur yefhim ara. Yenna-as: "A baba d acu-t wa?”. Baba-s: "A mmi wagi d ikerri, zliɣ-t i wakken ad d-tjeṛṛbeḍ leḥbab-ik n lekdeb, d uḥbib-iw n tidet, ihi awi-tt d tamsirt. Yenṭeq s aḥbib-is yenna-as: "Ma d kečč ad ak-yefk Ṛebbi lxiṛ, a-t-an ikerri imzel, awi-t s axxam-ik, ad teččen d warraw-ik". Taggara
Yiwen useggas kan ɣef timunent n tmurt n Lezzayer, ilul-d ukabar n Tirni n Yiɣallen Inemlayen yellan d anza n tnekra mgal adabu amesbaṭli n Ben Bella, d Bǧumediene. Ɣas ma deg umezruy amiran unṣib n tmurt n Lezzayer, tuget n tedyanin yesɛan assaɣ d umussu d tmagit amaziɣ, ttwafrent neɣ ttwaksent s lebɣi n ugraw n wejda yeṭṭfen adabu s yiɣil mbaɛd timunent n tmurt deg 05 seg yulyu 1962, maca tabɣest d lebɣi n yirgazen n Tmurt n Lezzayer, ladɣa irgazen n tmurt n Leqbayel, kren-d mgal tatut n umezruy aḥeqqani n tmurt i yettwabnan ɣef ṣṣaḥ. Mbaɛd taswiɛt anda lbaṭel d yiɣil uɣen amḍiq n talwit, mbaɛd taswiɛt anda agdud yessutur talwit seld n sebɛa d uzgen n yiseggasen n tegrawla i d-yeglan s wugar n umelyun d uzgen n lmuta, teɣli tmurt deg yir ifassen, yewwi-d Ad tuɣal ɣer yimawlan-is.
Deg umnaḍ-agi ideg i d-ban Hǧcine Ait Ahmed, yellan yakan d amazan n ugzdu n Sẓtif, i yeḥṣa d akken s kra n wazalen n tegrawla n 1954, anda i iruḥ ugdud d asfel.Yewwi-d useḥbiber ɣef wazalen-agi s ibeddi mgal imḍebbren n udabu amesbaṭli. Dɣa yessefhem-d deg 10 seg waggur n yulyu 1963 deg cfawat n umeɣnas n tegdud Ait Ahmed: " …Aql-iyin ass-a qesḍeɣ, ad d-naɣeɣ s wudem aserti ɛinani mgal adabu-a amesbaṭli axxedaɛ… D abrid awḥid i tuffɣa seg tegnit-agi yewwḍen ɣer lḥed-is… Aseqqamu Aɣelnaw n Yisegran ur tezmir ara ad ter tilisa i udabu amesbaṭli n unagraw. " Dagi i d-tban tmengla n ugrawliw Hǧcine Ait Ahmed.
Deg 28 seg waggur n cutember 1963, nnejmaɛen yimḍebren imezwura n tegrawla n lwilaya III d lwilaya IV, d irgazen n tsertit, deg yidigen n tɣiwant taqburt n Michelet. Gar wid-ak i ḥeḍren anejmuɛ-agi ad naf Hǧcine Ait Ahmed, Aknaner Mǧḥand Ǧulhadj, abugaṭu n yizerfan n umdan Ali Yaḥia Abdenǧur, Mǧurad Ǧussedik, Ait Medri Belaid, Agensas lieutenant Yaḥia Abdelḥfiḍ, d sin n yimeɣnasen n ukabar n Tegrawla Tanemnayt  Parti de la Rẓḍǧlutiǧn Sǧcialiste/PRS, Ali Ammar akked Abǧubekr Belaid d waṭas n yimeɣnasen yekkan deg Umussu n tegrawla n -Yella-d d unejmuɛ aneggaru n umussu uqbel taseɣrut tunṣibt azekka-ina n, 29 seg cutember 1963, deg temdint n Tizi Uzzu.
Akabar n Tirni n Yiɣallen Inemlayen, d akabar aserti amezwaru deg Lezzayer seld timunent. Yesɛa tiɣerɣert tamanaɣt i d-yugmen seg umezruy alqayan n tmetti tanemnayt n Lezzayer. Ɣas ma yella uqbel ukabar n Tegrawla Tanemnayt n wudem agrawliw Mǧhamed Bǧudiaf yettwasnen s umennuɣ-is aserti mgal timharsiwin yemgaraden. Acu kan akabar-agi n Tegrawla Tanemnayt ur yesɛi ara altaɣen igdudanen ma nesserewes-it d ukabar n Tirni n Yiɣallen Inemlayen.
Gar imenzayen n tɣerɣert n akabar n FFS, ad naf aɛawed n tmuɣli n uselḥu n wayen i d-teḥrez tegrawla i lfayda n ugdud, yettwaḥsaben d amasaḍ awḥid n tegrawla. Deg teswiɛt-nni, yessemres udabu ttawilat akk n useḥres d yiɣil mgal iɛeggalen n ukabar n FFS, akabar n Tegrawla Tanemnayt d ukabar n Tesdukla Tazzayrit i iqeddcen s tufra. Yella-d lḥers meqqren deg tmurt n Leqbayel ɣef uselway n ukabar Hǧcine Ait Ahmed.
Zgan ttawilat n tɣamsa tazayazt n Ben Bella d rregmat deg-s, akken ad yecɛel times gar yizzayriyen. Dɣa, qesden yimḍebbren n lwilayat ad rren talast i lbaṭel u udabu n Bǧumediene d Ben Bella. Tuɣal Tmurt n Leqbayel i tikkelt-nniḍen d annar n umennuɣ gar trebbuyaɛ n yiserdasen n ukabar n FFS akked yiɣallen n Tsardest n Teslullit Taɣelnawt, i yeskecmen agdud deg twaɣit tameqqrant n ṭrad tamaynut.
Deg yiwet n teswiɛt anda i d-yella uɣbel n tlisa gar tmurt n Merruk, ifures taswiɛt udabu akken ad yerr lḥedd i tegrawla, anda ula d iɣallen n FFS, ttwaceggɛen ɣer tlisa n tmurt n Merruk. Aya, yesseɣli ifadden n tsulta n FFS, deg waggur n unbir 1963, syin yella-d uneḥbus n Hǧcine Ait Ahmed deg 17 Tubeṛ -Ger waggur n yennayer d fuṛaṛ 1965 i yebda umtawa gar sin n yidisan n tmengla, anda ssawḍen ɣef umtawa u usuffeɣ n yimeḥbas imsertiyen, d usekcem n yimeɣnasen n ukabar n Tirni n Yiɣallen Inemlayen deg tudert turmidt. Ali Zalǧuk
Ma d aḥric wis sin n umtawa, yella-d ɣef wudem aserti seld asarag n Tefriqt-Tasyawit n Lezzayer deg taggara n yunyu 1965, anda i seṭɛerfen s wudem unṣib s ukabar n FFS, d akabar anemgal. Maca adabu n temsulta, ur yefki ara yakk tilelli n usemres n tsertit s wudem n tugdut, ladɣa seld aseɣḍel n udabu n Ben Bella sɣur Hǧuari Bǧumediene deg, 19 yunyu 1965, i yenɣan asirem n tugdut deg Lezzayer.
Yella lwali n Wehran Mass Ɛebdelqader Ǧellawi d unemhal n umaris aɣelnaw n timerrit d kra n yimasayen n twilayt deffir n beddu n umahil n lkar n "Wehran City Tǧur”, d lkar imerri amezwaru deg twilayt n Wehran. Yusa-d wayagi ɣef yiswi n unerfud n taɣult n timerrit di twilayt-a yettheggin ad d-tessuddes uraren n yilel agrakal deg unebdu n -D amaris aɣelnaw n tmerrit i d-yefkan tikti s uwellih n uneɣlaf n tmerrit d temguriyin timensayin. Ɣef waya, iwekked-d lwali n Wehran belli afurgu-a i yebdan ass n arim, 10 duǧember 2019, ad d-ittezzi i waṭas n yimeḍqan n Wehran, ineggura-a, ttufernen-d sɣur imazzagen n unnar n umezruy d tgemmi n Lezzayer.
Ma d anemhal n timerrit n Wehran, yenna-d « Tusa-d tikti seld mi d-terra Tenmehla-nneɣ asira aqdim n tmerrit, i yuɣalen d ayla n umaris, d ayen ara t-yeǧǧen ad t-yesseqdec i uwelleh n yiḥewwasen akked yimniren les guides ara yilin i lmend-nsen ". Ɣef wakken i d-tewwi teɣbalut-nneɣ , abrid ara tettawi lkar-a, ad yettɛedday ɣef 11 n yidgan inmazrayen deg temnaḍt n Wehran, ad ibeddu seg uzniq n Mǧhammed Khemisti, ɣer wammas n tkadidralt d leqṣer n yidles, syin ad ikemmel ɣer yiɣrem Sidi Lhewwari d tebḥirt «l’ẓtang" d lḥemmamat n Tturk, ad yaweḍ alamma d annar n waddal n yizgaren, syin ad yali ɣer temnaḍt "Igli yebhan” belle hǧrizǧn deg udrar n Mulay Ɛebdelqader, syin ad ikemmel ɣer lqelɛa n Santa Kruz d tmesgida tamasiḥit, u ad d-yuɣal alamma d talemmast n temdint s tikkin-ines ɣef frǧnt de mer. Khaled Achǧui
Akud n tuzzya-agi ad yaweḍ ɣer kraḍ n yisragen, ma d abeyyi n lexlaṣ ad yili d azamulan s 250 idinaren s uneḥsub n ubeyyi n unekcum ɣer lqelɛa n Santa Kruz s 80 idinaren, u ad ilin itikiyen uzzigen i yisdawanen d twaculin. I usmekti, afurgu-a d ameqqran d amaynut, ad yeǧǧ iḥewwasen ad rtiḥen daxel, ad ixeddem snat n tuzzyiwin i wass, tamezwarut ɣef 09h00, tis snat ɣef 14h30 n tmeddit. Iswi-ines d tukci n tegnit ama i yimdanen i izedɣen di Wehran, ama i wid i d-yettasen seg twilayin tiǧiratin, akken ad issinen imeḍqan inmazrayen n temnaḍt-a i d-yessebganen udem adelsan anmazray n Yihran. Rnu ɣer waya, ma tewweḍ s iswi-s tikti-a, ad d-rnun sin n yifurguten-nniḍen deg yizmaz i d-iteddun, ara irezzun ɣer yimeḍqan deg tamiwin ur nelli ara deg wahil n umezwaru-a, i d-yenna lwali n twilayt n Wehran.
Attttrendre la guitare d adlisfus i ulmad n tɣuri n uẓawan akked tyita n ugiṭar i d-yesuffeɣ i yiman-is uselmad n uẓawan Hǧcine Ǧuaguenini. Deg umnir-agi i d-yeffɣen i tikkelt-nniḍen deg tezrigt-is tis snat, ad naf 18 n tezlatin i yettwarun s uẓawan-nsent akked yisefra-nsent. Am wakken i d-yessegza uselmad-agi amek ara d-yili wurar n tgiṭart akked tɣuri n yimesla n uẓawan i wid yebɣan ad ten-lemden.
Gar tezlatin i d-yefren Hǧcine Ǧuaguenini, ad d-nebder Baba Inuba, Cfiɣ, Aya lxir-inu, Abeḥri n tmeddit, Ajeǧǧig n Idir, Ḥemmleɣ n Si Mǧh, A yemma ɛzizen ur ttru n Farid Ali, Linda n Les Abranis, Ay agellid mulana n Allaǧua Zerrǧuki, Lezzayer n Cherif Kheddam, Tabalizt n Ali Amrane, Mi ara d-yuɣal n Djamel Allam, Aqlalas n Mǧulǧud Assam, Anfet-iyi kan n Ali AMrane, Lbaz n Ideflawen, Gibraltar aẓawan n Djamel Allam. Mebɛd mi d-yessefhem umeskar isem akked wazal sɛant yakk tezmilin n uẓawan Dǧ, Rẓ, Mi, Fa, Sǧl, La d Si, iɛedda ɣer wamek i yezmer yiwen ad d-i  ɣer awalen n tezlit s uẓawan-is. Yal tizlit, tettwaru s wunuɣen-is akked yisefra-s deg yal asebtar. Yenna-d diɣ acu n ssenf uɣur teqqen yal tizlit akked unya-ines rythme.
Ɣer taggara, yefka-d umẓawan tadabut i umawal i yettwaseqdacen deg uẓawan yecban le SǧlfAge, la tablature, l’arttAge, la mesure, la ttartitiǧn, les temtts, chiffrage de la mesure…atg. S useqdec n udlisfus-agi, yal yiwen ara yerren ddehn-is u iḥemmel aẓawan d ugambar, yezmer ad d-yawi iman-is deg kra n wussan kan. Ihi, tirmit igerrzen.Hǧcine Mǧula
Ismawen i yessisnen tamurt n Leqbayel deg umaḍal s umata, ad qqimen i lebda ddren s ugerruj adelsan i d-ǧǧan. Mačči d ayagi kan, At Ɛebbas, seg wid yuraren nnuba tameqqṛant deg lgerra n Lezzayer, dɣa sεan ddeqs n yimeɣṛaṣen. Mebla ma nettu, lhiba d wazal i sεan, ama deg uḥric n tfellaḥt, neɣ di leṣnaf n tuččit. Rnu ɣer waya, sεan amezruy ula deg uḥric n txeyyaḍt d uzeṭṭa. Anda ddan yettban wayla-nsen, imi yemgarad ɣef wiyaḍ, yerna yewqem yegrurez, amedya d tiwwura n « Ɛebla ". D ayagi i εerḍen yimezdaɣ n temnaḍṭ-a, gar-asen wid n Yiɣil Ɛli, ad d-sneεten i umaḍal ass n, 15 tubeṛ yezrin, deg tnedlist taɣiwant n Yiɣil Ɛli.
Ad d-nesmekti d akken ttiεad-a texdem-it tddukkla « Adrar " n usegmi n tfellaḥt n Yiɣil Ɛli, s ufus n tallelt n tenmehla n tfellaḥt d tɣiwant n Yiɣil Ɛli, ilmend n usfuggel n wass amaḍalan n tuččit. Iswi n wid yekkin di temlilit-a, d asissen n ugerruj n temnaḍt-nsen i wid i d-yerzan, d usiweḍ n wayen i xeddmen i tmuṛa-nniḍen. Ayen yeṣṣefṛahen ugar, d amḍan n wid i d-yerran i tiɣṛi n uḥraz n tuččit. Usan-d dɣa ddeqs ad ḥeḍṛen dinna, imi llan seg wid yettaken azal i tezmert-nsen, ẓṛan azal n wayen yellan d agaman, ḥemmlen ad t-ččen. Ula d ifellaḥen n temnaḍṭ-a i d-isersen sselεa-nsen i lbiε, umren s tamawt i gren medden i sselεa-a, d wazal i as-fkan.
Ahat ula d nutni seg tama-nsen, rran-d i yisteqsiyen-nsen s tumert tageεmirt. Akken i neẓṛa, Iɣil Ɛli d tamurt n uzemmuṛ, ihi deg temlilit-a, yella zzit di ttiεad. Rnu ɣer waya, yella daɣen uyefki d wudi n tɣeṭṭen, ifelfel azeggaɣ aqeṛḥan, i yettwaxdamen kan deg At Ɛebbas, seqqdacen-t i usizweɣ n lmakla. Ula d tuččit tuzzigt n temnaḍṭ-a dɣa, teṭṭef amkan-is deg ufsar-a n sselεa, mebla ma nettu lfarina n uxeṛṛub d wayen-nniḍen. Ma yella deg wayen yeεnan taxeyyaḍṭ, teḥḍeṛ di ttiεad-a tddukkla « Tafat” n tullas n Yiɣil Ɛli, i usissen n wayen i xeddment. Ama d ibeṛnaṣ d tqeccabiyin, ama d iẓeṭwan, iwumi qqaṛen " Iḥembel " neɣ d tiqendyaṛ-nsen. Ula d ssxab s wacu xeddmen izraren n tullas, tefser-it-id yiwet n temɣaṛt i d-yusan seg taddart n Tqeṛṛabt. Axeddim-a i qrib yettwattu, teḥya-t-id temɣaṛt-a, i yesεan lebɣi yudef akkin i tlisa. Ama d wid i d-ifesren sselεa-nsen, ama d wid i d-yusan, umren ayendin s temlilit-a i yefkan azal i ugerruj n temnaḍṭ-a, d wid i t-ixeddmen.
Lḥif d waktayen n temẓi, d ayen ur itettu umdan. Yella win ur nessawaḍ ara ad ten-id-yejmeɛ ɣer yiwen umkan, yella win daɣen yessawaḍen ad ten-id-yejmel d taḥawact. D aya, i yexdem Arezqi Lɛifa Salmi, mi d-yegmer kra yellan d asmekti n temẓi-s, iga-as asefru-s deg tḥawact-is n tmedyazt. Dɣa, deg wussan-agi kan iɛeddan, i d-yessuffeɣ ɣer ssuq adlis amenzwaru n tmedyazt, i wummi isemma "Asmekti”. D yiwen wammud n yisefra n 116 n yisebtar, yettnuzu s wazal n 400 DA. Ma d tazwert n udlis-a, yexdem-as-tt uselmad Mass Racid Ḥusin Seḥnuni. "Asmekti”, d ammud n 60 n yisefra s snat n tutlayin: tamaziɣt d tefransist.
Yura-ten yakkan s teqbaylit, syin yessuqqel-iten i yiman-is ɣer tefransist, imi yella d aselmad n tefransist. Yefreq-it ɣef 6 n yiḥrcen-agi: Tayri, Lefraq n tayri, Ddunit d yiɣeblan-is, Lḥewj n yimawlan, Imdukal d wiyaḍ akked Ṛebbi/Ṣellaḥ d ssmaḥ. Tuget n yisefra yura, ttwarun s ṭṭabeɛ talɣa n yisefra n umedyaz Si Muḥend u Mḥend s kraḍ n tseddarin d 7-5-7 n tunṭiqin. Maca yella wanida ixulef lqaleb-agi, sya ɣer da. Am wakka, tuget n yisental i ɣef yessefra Mass Salmi deg udlis-a, cudden ɣer tmetti s umata. Ad d-nesmekti kan belli, Arezqi Lɛifa Salmi, d amedyaz d amaru. Ilul deg useggas n 1956 di taddart n Yiɣzer Necbel di tɣiwant n Buɣni di Tizi Uzzu. Yella yakkan d aselmad deg uɣerbaz alemmas, uqbel ad yeffeɣ ɣer tɣimit. Nessaram-as afud igerrzen ɣer sdat.A. A.
Massa Bǧuchafa, gar tlawin yecnan s teqbaylit s tebɣest. Asmi tebda ccna, mazal akukru n tmeṭṭut seg ccna d tẓuri akked tugdi i ireṣṣan di tmetti n lawan-nni, s lweḥc i d-yexleq rrebrab. Teḍfer Massa Bǧuchafa abrid-agi n ccna imi i t-tḥemmel, tefren ad tili d tagensast n tulawin akked tumast yettwakeblen. Yenna fell-as T.Djaǧut, aseggas n 1989 "D tacennayt i iceɛɛlen isuyas n tzeɣwa n ccna”. Isem-is aḥeqqani Zaina Nait Chabane, tlul deg useggas n 1964, deg tɣiwant n Yililten, Micli, deg Tizi Uzzu. Segmi tella d tamecṭuḥt, yezdeɣ-itt ccna, "Asmi sɛiɣ 4 neɣ 5 n yiseggasen, gganeɣ ttenkareɣ s rradyu tis snat, allal awḥid n teqbaylit imir-n, selleɣ i umezgun. Cfiɣ, yal taṣebḥit, tessakay-iyi-d yemma akken ad sleɣ i tezlit n Cherif Kheddam "Ṣbeḥ lxir ay udem n rrbeḥ”.
Tekker-d s tezlatin n Sliman Azem, Zerrǧuki Allaǧua, Hnifa, Bahia Farah, Matǧub d Aït Menguellet. Tebda s wurar n lxalat d ccnawi n tuddar s ubendayer. Syin tkemmel deg uɣerbaz, s tallelt n uselmad-is Rezig Kaci. yiwet n tikkelt tecna-d deg uɣerbaz n L.N.Yiraten, tizlit n Nǧra "Adrar n Ǧerǧer ɛlayen”, yeḥḍer Ṭaleb Rabeḥ, yessebɣes-itt, asmi i as-yenna tzemreḍ ad tuɣaleḍ d tacennayt tameqqrant. Dɣa syin i d-tebda, tcennu di tesdawit. Uqbel ad tinig ɣer Fransa, tecna deg tzeqqa n Mutualitẓ akked Allaǧua Bahlǧuli d Cherifa, s lmendad n rradyu Beur i d-iheggan tameɣra, seld amtawa gar umsuffeɣ Dadǧuche akked urgaz-is. Syin tessuffeɣ tizlit s ccna-ines di tmura-nniḍen, am Canada, USA, Belgique, Hǧllande, Marǧc, Australie …
Aṭas n tezlatin i as-yura urgaz-is M’hend Bǧuchafa. Tecna tuɣac n tmeɣriwin d lfuruḥ, d tid n ccḍeḥ, am Inebgawen, Ma tufiḍ, Yeǧǧa-yi. Maca ur tezgil ara tizlit tamḥaddit, anida terra tajmilt i Mulud Mɛemri, tecna daɣen Tiɣri i Yimaziɣen d tiyaḍ. Ass-a, tessaweḍ Massa Bǧuchafa 30 n yiseggasen n ccna. Ɣef waya, thegga-d yiwet n tmeɣra meqqren di tmurt n Fransa, deg tzeqqa n Cabaret sauḍage, ass n, 8 meɣres 2020, i usfugel n kraḍ n tmerwin n ubrid iḍulen i tuɣ deg tẓuri. Tefren 8 meɣres, ass agraɣlan n tmeṭṭut, akken ad as-terr tajmilt i tneggarut-a. Maca ɣur-s daɣen iṣenfaren, am tuzzya n ccna i tebɣa ad texdem deg waṭas n tamiwin n tmurt n Lezzayer. Aheggi n uḍebsi, anida ara d-tejmeɛ ddeqs n tezlatin i tecna ɣef teɣzi n umecwar-is, seg tid yufraren, ad tent-tesdakkel deg uḍebsi-a, s wallalen atraren.Kh. A.
Imi d Mulud Mɛemmeri i d-ineǧǧren abrid n uselmed n tmaziɣt s wudem atrar, ladɣa s tjerrumt, nesteqsa yiwen gar yiselmaden imezwura n tmaziɣt deg tesdawit ɣef wamek i ilaq ad yili useḥbiber ɣef tutlayt i wakken ad temneɛ seg nnger. Ha-tt-an tririt-is. ’Tamaziɣt, ass-a, amzun tettwakkes-d seg yimi n tatut. Awal-a, riɣ-t d tasemɣert i yimenza-nneɣ i yegren aẓru amezwaru i usenfar n tegert n wammud d usetrer d usimer n tussna d tmussnin uɣref. Syin akin, akin i wayen i d-yettwagemren seg tmussni n yimenza, akin i tikli –tewwi azgen n lqern aya deg usekles d usetrer d usnulfu deg tussna akked tsekla, akin i unekcum n tmaziɣt deg tesdawit d a tessaweḍ deg taɣult n tsekla tatrart ungal, tullist, arrazen yettfuktin deg kra din n temnaḍin, amzun, melmi kan,yettunefk-as i tutlayt-nneɣ ad tili d tutlayt tunṣibt deg snat n tmura Lezzayer akked Lmerruk.
Akin i wayen yellan yakan d tisuddwin tisegwin deg tesdawiyin, HCA, CNPLET, CRLCA, takadimit, tessaweḍ ad tekcem deg UgrawAferkan n Tutlayin, s timmad-is d tutlayt yettwasawalen gar tilas n wayen din d timura n Tferka Ugafa akked Ddaw Tneẓruft. Yettkan-d amzun tagnit-a i  ɣer tessaweḍ akka, d tiziwar tuɣalin. Maca aẓayeri i as-yettunefken, urɛad i d-yeflali deg ugni n tilawt, yeqqim d awal kan.Yessulef ad tili yiwet tsertit n tidet i usebded n tutlayt, i usefrek n tutlayt ara yilin d tasalelt iwatan i usenfali n yiḥulfan d tektiwin n tmeddurt tamirant, ara yeddun akked tallit deg nettidir ass-a.
Yessulef ad tili tsertit tazeddgant ara as-yessiɣen ugar n yiberdan tarrayin, ugar n wallalen, i unegmu n tantaliwin deg yal tamnaḍt, i usdukel n yirman imaynuten yettsemminin aktayen, i ufares n yizmamen iwatan tallit-nneɣ tasekla tatrart, tiẓuriwin timiranin, isura, izmamen n wurar i yimeẓẓyanen, i tikci n wazal n uselmed deg yiɣerbazen akked tsedawit.Yessefk daɣen – d ayen i d-neqqar yal mi aɣ-tettunefk tegnit―deg yal aswir n tmetti ad as-rren azal s timmad-is d tutlayt n tmurt-nneɣ , ad tt-qedcen i waken ad tefrek, ad tt-sqedcen, ad ssenfalayen yis-s tikta n uzeṭṭa n tegmat akked yizerfan n umdan, ad d-skeflen tamussni n Yimenza, ad tiẓid tussna n uzekka, ad tiẓid tudert, ad tizdig tegnewt iluɣentignewt tanemettit, tignewt tasertant, tignewt tamnezwut’’.Yesteqsa-t Hǧcine Mǧula
Tella-d temsikent n teklut n Mass Djamel Hǧceini deg Uxxam n yidles Mulud Mɛemmeri, ɣef teɣzi n ddurt seg 25 ar 31 deg yennayer -D timsikent anda i d-yewwin leqdic n umẓawan/amsuneɣ ɣef tlata n yisental igejdanen. D tamuɣli-s deg wayen yettwali, am wakken yeqqar netta s timmad-is ’Deg usuneɣ-iw, ttbeddileɣ ayen yesseḥzanen s wayen yessefraḥen.
Ihi, ɣef teɣzi n ddurt kamel, walan wid i d-yerzan ɣer Uxxam n yidles Mulud Mɛemmeri aṭas n tfelwiyin n teklut n Djamel Hǧceini i d-yesunɣen tamuɣli-s ɣef ugama akked twennaḍt. Mmalent-d tfelwiyin imekwan iqdimen i imechuren deg temdint n Tizi Uzzu, tudrin akked yixxamen n leqbayel. Ma d asentel aneggaru, yewwi-d ɣef ugama akked twennaḍt. Imi yella yesddukkel taklut akked uẓawan deg tudert-is, ihi yerna ciṭ n cbaḥa i temsikent-is imi iga assaɣ gar tmesliwt akked uwali s uẓawan i d-yessekles ɣef demma n waya.
Ɣef waya dɣa, yenna-aɣ-d: ’Tteɛraḍeɣ ad sunɣeɣ imesla u ad cnuɣ initen’’. Ilul Djamel Hǧceini deg useggas 1969 deg Yilulen Umalu, yesɛa Magister n uẓawan i d-yewwi deg Lezzayer tamanaɣt, ɣas ulamma yeḍfer deg tazwara ayen-nniḍen deg tesdawit n Tizi Uzzu. Yelmed taklut i yiman-is, acu kan aṭas i as-yefkan afus n tallelt ɣef teɣzi n umecwar-is.
Uli Rǧhde, d yiwet n Telmanit i iḥemmlen idles amaziɣ s umata. Tettlusa iselsa n leqbayel, yerna tcennu s teqbaylit. Nesseqsa-tt amek i twala izerfan n tmeṭṭut deg umaḍal s umata, ha-t-an wacu i d-tenna. ’Nebɛed aṭas ɣef umtawi dagi ɣur-neɣ deg Lalmany. Wammag deg umaḍal amaziɣ anef kan! Llan aṭas n yirgazen i yekkaten ɣef yizerfan n tmeṭṭut deg ddunit, acu kan aṭas diɣ n tlawin, ladɣa, tiyemmatin i d-yettrebbin arrac deg ccuq, u ttarrant tiḥdayin d tixeddamin n twacult. Zriɣ d acu i d-qqareɣ, imi ula d imawlan-iw, ur ssawḍen ara i wakken ad aɣ-ffken izerfan yemtawan, xas nutni d atraren u xas deg tmurt n Lalmany i nella. Acḥal n maḥyaf i tesɛedda yemma s lǧiha n temɣart-is.
Ass-a, la ttwaliɣ wid-nni i d-yekkren deg ccuq, ur zmiren ara i yiman-nsen; ur sɛin ara timunent-nsen. Aṭas deg-sen ur ssinen ara ad sewwen, ad ssirden iselsa-nsen neɣ ɛad ad izmiren i uxxam-nsen. Ttxellisen s urdi ameqqran i wakken ad ččen lmakla n berra n temɣawlit, ur nzeddig, ur nesɛi lbenna. Aṭas deg-sen i yessḥassfen ɣef ttrebga-agi, xas akken ẓran d ayen yelhan i asen-tebɣa tyemmat-sen deg uxemmem-is. Lameɛna, tidet kan, aɛdaw ameqqran n tmeṭṭut, d tameṭṭut s timmad-is.
Meḥsub nxus yir tamuɣli n yirgazen alamma nerna-d aqejjem d usemẓi n wazal n tmeṭṭut sɣur tameṭṭut. Zaɛma, nebɣa ad nili d tilelliyin, meɛna nekkat deg-sent imi llant d tilelliyin. Aya, dagi ɣur-neɣ, wammag ɣer Leqbayel neɣ ɣer Yimaziɣen s umata, la ttwaliɣ kter, ssarameɣ kan ad idiren akken iwata tilisa i asen-gan kra n wansayen n tmetti deg tudert-nsen. Yerna awal Amaziɣ, d argaz ilelli. Acu kan ur yettili ara d ilelli mebla tameṭṭut tilellit akked tutlayt-is’’. Hǧcine Mǧula
Mbeɛd igemmaḍ ur ngerrez n terbaɛt n Yilemẓiyen n Leqbayel, imi deg 10 n temliliyin texser 4, yeffeɣ-d ɣer tɣamsa uselway, Mass Crif Mellal, akken ad d-yessefhem kra n yiɛeqqayen i yimḥemmalen n terbaɛt ladɣa. Dɣa, ama deg BRTV neɣ deg umaṭṭaf wis sin, yerra-d ɣef ddeqs n yisteqsiyen, ad neɛreḍ ad d-nawi da agejdan.
Akken neẓra, niqal yeffeɣ-d wawal d akken temsebḍa tenmehla n JSK d usleɣmay Velud. Maca yeskaddeb Mass Mellal aya, yenna-d ɣas ma rfan seg ugemmuḍ am winna  akked Belɛebbas, ur d-yelli gar-asen wawal ɣef ugzam n wassaɣ. Isenfaren n yimal
Yebder-d Mellal isenfaren i d-itteddun n terbaɛt taqbaylit. Ama d anammas n usileɣ, i ɣef tella Ceḍital di lmendad, neɣ d axxam n tnezzut n terbaɛt. Yenna-d aql-iten ttazzalen akken ur ttɛeṭṭilen deg tlalit di sin.
Ifures Crif Mellal tagnit akken ad d-yessefhem nnuba n gma-s di terbaɛt, imi llan wid i as-yeqqaren d Ɣilas i d imḍebber n tidet, mačči d Crif. Yenna-d uselway, ɣas d tidet yettɛawan-it gma-s, ttemcawaren, rray aneggaru d netta kan i t-itteṭṭen.
Yewwi-d daɣen uselway Crif Mellal awal ɣef wid yebɣan ad t-ssabuṭin, ad rẓen tarbaɛt taqbaylit. Yenna-d imdanen-a ur bɣin mi ibeddel aṭas n tlufa daxel uxxam n JSK, imi llan rebbḥen-d adrim ɣef uɛrur n terbaɛt. Ɣef, wawal-is, yezmer ad tent-id-yefḍeḥ ɣer sdat.
Gadry seg yicennayen at lasel aferkan, i icennun seg wacḥal-aya tura tizlatin n uɣewwaɣ Lwennas Meɛtub. Nesteqsa-t di tdiwennit-a, yerra-aɣ-d.
Amek tesliḍ s Meɛtub Lwennas i tikkelt tamezwarut?Ahat yesḥeyyir waya, maca ssneɣ Meɛtub Lwennas deg wass n lexmis 25 yunyu 1998, deg uɣmis n tiliẓri n tmeddit, nekk lliɣ ɛad d agrud. Ass-nni i as-tettwacelqef tudert!
Syin akkin, tebdiḍ tettsaraxeḍ-t, tcennuḍ tizlatin-is. Neɣ amek? Syin akkin, ssneɣ tizlatin-is i igerrzen ayendin s ubrid n yemma i d-yettawin seg tikkelt ɣer tayeḍ tisfifin d timaynutin d ayla-s ɣer uxxam. Bdiɣ dindin cennuɣ-tent-id war ma nudaɣ akk ad tent-lemdeɣ tazwara. Deg-s d ccna mačči d aɛaned acku, akken ttwaliɣ, ulac win izemren ad iɛaned ayen ur nettwaɛanad. Iban-iyi-d dɣa, urǧin i d-yusa waya ɣer wallaɣ-iw. D acu kan, d tidet, ɛerrḍeɣ ad iliɣ d imekdi i tezlatin-is tinasliyin. Neɣ akken-nniḍen, ad d-iniɣ mi ara cennuɣ, neɣ tturareɣ-d tizmilin, xeddmeɣ ɣef leḥsab n wamek ttḥulfuɣ daxel-iw.
Neẓra yewɛer ad tecnuḍ s tutlayt ur tfehhmeḍ. Meslay-aneɣ-d ɣef waya d wayen i k-yerran ɣur Meɛtub Lwennas? Akken i ak-d-nniɣ yakan, mačči di ddhen-iw tazwara ad lemdeɣ tuɣac-is. Ḥemmleɣ-tent d tidet, maca urǧin sugneɣ-d ad lemdeɣ ad cennuɣ s tutlayt-a igerrzen, i yi-d-ibanen tewɛer imi d tanesbaɣurt. Ɣer taggara, iban-d ugemmuḍ-a. Tidet kan, qedceɣ maca war ma wwiɣ-d s lexber! Ma d ayen i yi-ijebden ɣer Meɛtub Lwennas, d tizlatin-is uqbel kullci, iban!, Yesɛa aɣanib weḥd-s, i tuɣ ur ssineɣ deg wayen iɛeddan, maca am wakken yettban-iyi-d d awaculan, n twacult. Amzun lliɣ ssneɣ-tent yakan deg waṭas-aya!
D anti-ten tezlatin-is i tcennuḍ s waṭas? I uzayez, ad d-iniɣ tizlatin i cennuɣ s waṭas d tid i d-yettbanen ḥemmlen-tent ugar medden, i d-yettawin taḥawact n umecwar n Meɛtub Lwennas.
Tesɛiḍ aṭas n yineḍfaren di Tmurt n Yizwawen d Tmazɣa. Awal-ik ɣef waya… Iban-iyi-d ur rǧiɣ, neɣ ur gziɣ ara amek zemreɣ ad sɛuɣ ineḍfaren. D acu kan, ahat yessaweḍ ad iḥaz uqeddic-iw, ad yeɛjeb ddeqs n yimdanen, acku ttawaḍen-iyi-d seg waṭas d aseggas tura, ar ass-a, yiznan n usebɣes, n usnemmer d yibeddi ɣur-i, seg waṭas n tamiwin. Ɛni, d ayen i yi-yesferḥen! D aya i yi-yeǧǧan ad d-snulfuɣ targa-w n YǧuTube taggara-a, acku buhan i yi-yessutren aya. Iban-d yewwi-d tili ahat ddiɣ-asen di lebɣi lawan-nni! Lḥasul, d iseɣ ɣur-i mi ḥsiɣ ɛejbeɣ i waṭas n Yizwawen, i yellan d aɣref n yirgazen d tlawin s ttzuxxuɣ aṭas, i ttqadareɣ, i ttɛuzzuɣ.
Yaḍra tesɛiḍ kra n yisenfaren? Taggara, ad d-iniɣ belli akken yella lḥal akked tuget n yirgazen d tlawin di ddunit, sɛiɣ ula d nekk isenfaren. Yiwen seg-sen d aheyyi n yigalaten di Lezzayer, send kullci, deg wul n Tmurt n leqbayel ɛzizen i cedhaɣ buhan. Maca, ahat daɣen anda-nniḍen, ma yella ad yekki waya deg usiweḍ n uqeddic, amezruy, amennuɣ, tiktiwin, izen n Meɛtub Lwennas akked yidles-is d win n yirgazen d tlawin i yennan UHU i lbaṭṭel, i yemmuten s yibeddi wala ma ddren knan!
Awal-ik n taggara… Awal-iw n taggara, ad d-iniɣ, akken i t-id-qqareɣ dima, tezmer Tmurt n leqbayel ad tzux s tarwa-s. Aɣref-a Amaziɣ i ttawiɣ i lebda deg wul-iw, d ttbut d akken nezmer ad nenɣ akk imazunen i nebɣa, s waṭas n tweḥcanit, maca d awezɣi ad nessusem iznan-nsen. Tanemmirt.Yesteqsa-t M. K.
Di lawan ideg kra n yidguden leḥḥun deg waṭas n tmura ɣef yir asefrek n yimḍebbren-nsen, llan ula d wid iluḥḥun ɣef d usenqes seg umihi n lḥamu i la yettidir umaḍal. Dɣa, ass n sem yezrin, 20 deg wayyur n cutember 2019, d imelyan n yimdanen i yeddan di tmura yemgaraden n umaḍal akken ad beggnen urrif-nsen seg tsertit tamirant i yettḍurrun takurt n Wakal. Deg yakk tiɣemmar n ddunit, ffɣen-d yigduden s iberdan nutni ttawin iberriḥen i yessawalen i uḥbas n twaɣit takulujit i la yettmaggan deg umaḍal akka tura, d ubeddel n tmuɣli tasertant sɣur yimasayen iɛlayanen n tmura.
Seg Hambǧurg di Telmant anda qeflen yiberdan s lɣaci, ɣer Ustralya d Sydney di Bangkǧk, ɛeddi akkin i Nairǧby, ffɣen-d akk s yiwen n wawal i uḥerrek tura i lfayda n tegnaw send ad ifit lḥal maḍi. Ɣef wayen i d-tewwi teɣbalut-nneɣ , d timeyyatin n tikliwin i d-yettwasuddsen deg umaḍal merra, rnu tuget seg-sent d isdawanen d yinelmaden i yellan deffir-sent. Dɣa, yeffeɣ yisalli di internet d akken di New Yǧrk yezmer lḥal wwḍen amelyun d kra n yinelmaden, seg 1 800 n yiɣerbazen izuyaz, i yelḥan i lmend n tmesbaniyin-a timaḍalanin.
D ayen yelhan, abeɛda ma neẓra d akken Marikan seg gar tmura i yessamasen aṭas tignaw. Rnu, ula d tuget n yimtawayen ɣef twennaḍt d usenqes seg uxdam n umunuksid n ukarbun, tetteffeɣ seg-sen. Ɣef tnaga n waṭas n yimeɣnasen d wid yesseḥbibiren ɣef twennaḍt, d asurif yelhan wayen akka gan yimdanen akken ad tbeddel ɣef tegnaw d twennaḍt-a deg umaḍal-a ideg nettidir. Ulamma aql-it taluft deg umsebḍi n yiberdan s anda ara terr. Ula di Fransa, yeṭṭaxxer uneɣlaf Nicǧlas Hulǧt seg udabu ɣef tmentilt imi yugi uwanek ad yeg kra n tigawin ilaqen i ubaɣur n twennaḍt.
Deg yiwen usarag i yexdem Pr Slimane Hachi i lmend n umulli wis 31 n tmettant Mulud Mɛemmeri, deg Uxxam n yidles n Tizi Uzzu, ass-nni n ttlata yezrin, yenna-d: ’Amahil n Mulud Mɛemmri, yerza s umata aseḥbiber ɣef tgemmi s yinadiyen-is akked leqdicat-is. Aya, yessaweḍ-it, dɣa, ad d-yessifrir ayen yellan yedreg deg tama-nni n Timimun leqdicat n tfellaḥt, tamedyazt, ansayen…. Ladɣa Ahellil i yuɣalen yekcem ɣer tgemmi tadelsant tamensayt n umaḍal deg UNESCǦ’’.
Ikemmel Pr Hachi deg wawal-is: ’Yebda leqdic-is deg yiseggasen n 1960 akked -D netta i d-ineǧǧren abrid-agi n useḥbiber ɣef tgemmi akked wiyaḍ. Ass-a, ddunit merra tedda deg lǧerras. D Lmulud At Mɛemmer i d ababat n telsasnet anthrǧttǧlǧgie deg Lezzayer akked Tefriq Ugafa s umata. Tura, tuɣal tgemmi tadelsant tamensayt d amennuɣ n talsa s umata armi yewweḍ ireṣṣa usiḥbiber ɣef tgemmi deg umtawa cǧnḍentiǧn n 2003 i d-tessuffeɣ l’UNESCǦ ɣef tgemmi tadelsant tamensayt immateriel. Ilaq ad nẓer d akken aḥareb ɣef tmagit, icudd daɣen ɣer tgemmi’’. H. M.
Teɣra Lynda Hantǧur tussna n tɣamsa deg tesdawit n Ben Ɛeknun di Lezzayer tamanaɣt deg wayen yerzan taɣamsa yuran. Deg tdiwennit-agi, newwi-d awal ɣef wungal-is "Iseflan n tudert” akked tira s umata.
Tefreḥ taddart. Tameṭṭut tameɣbunt tqeddec, tcebbeḥ i warraw-is, maca tettu iman-is, neɣ ahat d ayen-nniḍen: d lɛib ad tcebbeḥ i urgaz-is. Wagi d yiwen n ugdal i yellan deg tmetti n yimir-n. Ihi, ɣer tmeddit n wass tekcem tmeṭṭut ɣer texxamt akken ad d-tawi iɛdilen i yinebgawen i d-yeddan akked urgaz-is, teḍher-as tmeṭṭut, teqqim ɣef wussu, tcebbeḥ am teslit: terra amendil ɣef uqerru-is, truḥ ɣur-s tenna-as: " A tinebgit n lḥerma, a tin yeččuren d sser”. Tettmeslay-as s yisefra, tenwa d abrid i d as-iɛerqen imi i dterza ɣer texxamt-is. Terra-as d tnebgit-nni: " Abrid, ur i yi-yeɛriq ara, aql-i deg umḍiq-iw, nekk d tameṭṭut n ccix Kennu”. Syin mi teḥṣa Raju d takna i d as-d-yewwi, tefsex, dɣa tesleb…
Tewwiḍ-d awal s umata ɣef tmeḥqqranit mgal tameṭṭut… Deg wungal-agi, ur d-ttmeslayeɣ ara kan ɣef meḥyaf i d-yettilin sɣur timetti mgal tameṭṭut, acku meḥyaf, yettili-d gar tmeṭṭut akked tayeḍ. Tella yiwet n temsalt, ilaq ad nerr ddehn-nneɣ ɣur-s. Mi ara d-nettmeslay ɣef ddɣel ɣef tmeṭṭut, nezga neqqar-d d argaz i d sebba. Ala, ur ilaq ara ad nettu d akken ddɣel n tmeṭṭut ɣer tmeṭṭut, wagi yugar-itent merra. Mi ara nwali liḥalat n berru, nezga nettaf-d belli tettili-d tmeṭṭut tis kraḍet deg temsalt: d tamɣart-is, d tanudt-is neɣ d talwest-is. Nek jebdeɣ-d lwelha ɣef wanect-agi. Tella daɣen tmuḥeqqranit ɣef urgaz, amdya: Argaz ur yezmir ara ad d-yini belli yettwaḥqer sɣur tameṭṭut-is neɣ d uletma-s i iḥekkmen deg uxxam. Ihi, argaz yettwaḥqerr kter, imi ur yezmir ara ad yeffeɣ ɣer berra ad yini belli yettwaḥqer, d lɛib. Argaz, ur ilaq ara ad yili d aɛewwiq i tmeṭṭut. Ilaq ad ibedd ɣer tama-is, ad as-yefk tabɣest akken ad tennerni deg yisenfar-is.
Amek armi i d-terriḍ ungal-agi ɣer tmaziɣt? Nekk ur ɣriɣ ara tamaziɣt. Asmi i uriɣ tamacahut-agi, uriɣ-t s trumit. Syin, iruḥ ɣur-i Mass Saɛid Cemmax, yenna-yi-d: " Acimi ur tettaruḍ ara s tmaziɣt? Nniɣ-as: " Ur ssineɣ ara, ur ɣriɣ ara, yenna-ak: "Aru akken i tettmeslayeḍ. Taqbaylit-im teqɛed aru yis-s. Ilaq, ad nessimɣur tamkerḍit n tmaziɣt. Mačči d aman ara ternuḍ i tutlayin-nniḍen, ilaq ad tqeḍceḍ ɣef tutlayt-im”. Dɣa seg yimir-n, yexdem-iyi-d lḥir. Dɣa seg imir-n, bdiɣ ttaruɣ s tmaziɣt. Uriɣ-t akken i ttmeslayeɣ, syin akkin d yiwet n tnelmadt i yi-t-id-yuran, yesseɣta-iyi-t Takfarinas Nat Caɛban akked Ɛli Bexti. Ad-asen-iniɣ tanemmirt-nwen.
Awal n taggara… Win yettarun taqbaylit ur ixezzer ara ɣer tedrimt, axaṭer tira s teqbaylit d imenɣi. Ad d-iniɣ azemz n, 08 deg meɣres, mačči n ccḍeḥ. Azemz-agi, d imenɣi n tlawin. Ssarameɣ yal ass agraɣlan n tmeṭṭut, ad teffeɣ tektabt n tmezgun. Ma yella ɣef tira s tmaziɣt, ad d-iniɣ:”Ǧerǧer ay adrar n ṣsber, aẓar n tmazɣa ur yettɣar” Yamani Sǧuhila
Ddurt-agi yezrin i d-yeffeɣ walbum amezwaru n ucennay aqbayli Nǧurdine Akrǧure, ɣer tezrigin Tadukli Editiǧn. Ad naf deg CD 6 n tezlatin i d-yettmeslayen s umata ɣef tayri akked yiɣeblan i ttidiren yilmeẓyen n tura deg tmetti.
Deg tezlit tamezwarut iwumi yefka isem « Degǧuliw " i yellan diɣ d isem n walbum, yewwi-d awal ucennay Akrǧure ɣef tayri n tin iḥemmel i mazal yettawi-tt deg wul-is. Acu kan, tayri-agi ur tdum ara imi i t-teǧǧa tinna i ɣef yesleb, dɣa, dagi i d-yessenṭeq iḥulfan-is s tezlit iwumi yeqqar « Teǧǧa-yi ". Xas ulamma d nettat i t-yeǧǧan, meɛna ur tt-yesseḍlem ara s watas imi yerra kullec ɣef lmektub.
Ad nefhem aya mi ara as-tesleḍ i tezlit tis tlata iwumi yefka azwel « Lmektub ". Ɣef waya, dɣa, i yebɣa ad yuɣal d win-nniḍen i wakken ad tbeddel rray, ahat, ur tettruḥu ara, ad teqqim ad t-terǧu. Aya, ad t-naf deg tezlatin tis 4 akked tis 5 « Ad am-qqleɣ " d « Rǧu ". Akken yebɣu yili lḥal, teqqim neɣ truḥ, netta mazal-it yeɛceq-itt, mazal tasa tamcumt-nni, mazal udem-is deg wallen-is, ladɣa lexyal n lecfur-is imi i d-yessefra u iɣenna fell-asen deg tezlit taneggarut iwumi yeqqar « Lecfur-is ".
« Cennuɣ tawagennunit, meḥsub am yicennayen n dagi ɣur-neɣ n tama-agi n At Wagennun, yecban Fahem, Hamidǧuche, Ali Ferhati, Mǧh Ǧubelaid, Khelfaǧui d wiyaḍ ", i aɣ-d-yenna ucennay ajdid Nǧurdine Akrǧure i yesḥassfen aṭas ɣef wamek i yettili uḥric-agi n ccna deg unnar, ladɣa tamsalt n usekles akked usizreg. Hǧcine Mǧula
Ɣef waya, dɣa, ikemmel deg wawal-is « Seg useggas n 2016 i ttnadiɣ ɣef tezrigin ara d-yessuffɣen album-agi-inu. Meɛna sanida rriɣ, ad d-mmaggreɣ uguren, ladɣa tamsalt-agi n yidrimen. Armi d aseggas-agi i d-ufiɣ win ukud mmsefhameɣ, syin yessuffeɣ-it-id smana-agi iɛeddan ". Ilul Nǧurdine Akrǧure ass, 06/11/1982, deg taddart n Ililen, tama n Makǧuda.
Seld aṭas n uraju d leɛtab, tazzla seg, ɣer teẓrigin ara as-yilin i lmendad n usuffeɣ n udlis-is. Ar taggara, yeẓra tafat wungal "Deɛwessu n Lqayed” n Ccix Lyazid. Ɣas akken aṭas i yuzzel fell-as, maca yuɣal yessuffeɣ-it-id ɣef ddemma-ines, acku ɛlaḥsab-is ur yufi ara tallelt i uraju deg teẓrigin uɣur yennum yessuffiɣ-d yakan ifarisen-is, neɣ ɣer teẓrigin s umata i d-yessuffuɣen idlisen n tmaziɣt. D ayen i yeǧǧan Ccix Lyazid ad yesḥisef ɣef waya. S wungal-agi "Deɛwessu n Lqayed”, yewwi-d umeskar ɣef tedyanin yeḍran deg tama anida yezdeɣ, deg taddart Iɣil Umsed d tamiwin i as-d-yezzin am Uqbu d Ṣedduq.
Ccix Lyazid, yuɣal yis-neɣ ɣer tallit taqburt, ideg yedder Lqayed Ben Ɛli Crif deg temnaḍt-nsen, igmer-d tinagiyin ɣur yimɣaren d temɣarin i d-yecfan neɣ i asen-d-ḥkan ɣef talliyin-nni. Yefka azal n useggas di lweqt-is, gar unadi, agmar n yisallen d tnagiyin, akken ad yessiweḍ ad yekfu adlis-is deg tazwara n wayyur n yennayer yezrin, armi i d-yeffeɣ ass n, 24 deg furar -Yemmeslay-d ɣef maḥyaf i iga Lqayed Ben Ɛli Crif deg yiseggasen n 1870, d wamek yemxalaf d Ccix Aḥeddad yesnekren tanekra n 1871, d Lmeqrani.
Tacḍadt n lḥif yesbur Lqayed-agi ɣef yimezdaɣ. D adlis daɣen swayes yerra tajmilt i kra n yimdanen, gar-asen, setti-s, jeddi-s, baba-s d yemma-s d kra n yimɣaren n taddart. Ccix Lyazid, s yisem-is aḥeqqani Ben Henǧu Lyazid, aṭas i yeqdec deg tddukkliwin tidelsanin. Yunag ɣer tmurt n Merruk i wazal n 5 iseggasen. Yessuffeɣ-d yakan, "Isefra n tefsut” deg 2012, "Rreḥba n tneqqisin” deg 2017, "Ajellad d umyaru” deg -Ungal "Deɛwessu n Lqayed”, d tirmit-is tamezwarut deg tira n wungalen.
Nga yakan yid-s tadiwennit deg Uɣmis n Yimaziɣen deg waggur n Ɣuct 2019, yessegza-d leqdic-is d yiṣenfaren i t-yettrajun. Yenna-d ɣef uḥulfu-s, mi yewweḍ ɣer yiswi-s s tuffɣa n wungal yellan d targit, ɣas akken iɛetteb-it aṭas, maca yethenna wallaɣ-is, ikemmal yenna tamaziɣt teḥwaǧ tarwa-s, akken i teḥwaj at tdamsa i tallelt.Kh. A.
Deg tazwara n useggas-agi n 2019 i d-yessuffeɣ Saida Bǧuda 3 n yidlisen neɣ tesɣunin n yimeslayen inmidagen s teqbaylit. Yal adlis ɣur-s 30 n trastiwin i yinelmaden n uɣerbaz s umata. Ttwaheggant-d tesɣunin-a i lmendad n yal aswir n yinelmaden n uɣerbaz: inelmaden n uɣerbaz amenzu, wid n uɣerbaz alemmas akked yinelmaden n tesnawit. ’Imeslayen i sqedceɣ deg trasdiwin-agi d win i yellan deg yidlisen iɣurbizen. Yal aswir, ddmeɣ-d awal i yellan deg udlis-is. Akka ar ayaf unelmad amawal i yelmed neɣ ara yelmed deg uɣerbaz. Aya, yezmer ad as-yili d asmekti neɣ d areṣsi n wayen yeɣra yakan, mebla ma nudder-d urar d unecreḥ ara yaf deg trastiwin-agi’’, i aɣ-d-yenna Mass Bǧuda i d-yessewjaden yal letnayen yiwet trasta deg Uɣmis n yimaziɣen n La Dẓttḥche de kabylie. Deg uṭṭun-agi amezwaru, ad naf aṭas n tugniwin n yiɣersiwen akked ttɣawsiwin-nnḍen s yismawen-nsen. Ismawen ara yesnernin amawal n yinelmaden s umata, ladɣa, wid yellan akka deg temdinin neɣ inelmaden iɛerbawalen i d-yettafen ciṭ n uɣilif deg yimeslayen. Yezmer, diɣ, ad tili trasta-agi d alaɣmu ara yesseqdac uselmad deg uɣerbaz imi teɛna amawal aɣurbiz. Ad tt-tafem deg tnedlisin n Tizi Uzzu, s wazal n 100 idinaren.
Teḍra teqsidt, aggur iɛeddan, deg uɣerbaz agraɣlan azayri di tmanaɣt n tmurt n Fransa, mi teffeɣ yiwet n tnelmad seg uɣerbaz akken ad tẓal. Syin, tettwaḥbes ɣef leqraya i wazal n 7 n wussan sɣur tanemhalt n uɣerbaz, Massa Nadya Messasi. Mbaɛd tadyant-a, tegdel tnemhalt taẓallit i yinelmaden,i yiselmaden akked yixeddamen deg uɣerbaz.
Ddurt iɛeddan, temmeslay-d tneɣlaft n ttrebga Mass Nuriya Ben Ɣebrit ɣef wanect-a, tenna-d: "Ttruḥun-d yinelmaden ɣer uɣerbaz akken ad lemden timussniwin, ma yella d taẓallit, ad tili deg uxxam mačči deg uɣrbaz ’. Anect-a d ayen i d-ixelqen aṭas n wawal, ladɣa gar wid yessexdamen iẓedwa n internet: Gar wid iwumi yeɛjeb rray-agi, nnan-d d ayen yelhan limer ur nesekcam ara dyana deg yiɣerbazen. Si tama-nniḍen, llan wid i yugin rray-agi.
Aṭas n wawal i yuzlen sya u sya. Aṭas n wid ur neqqbil ara rray-agi. Ad d-nesmekti kan d akken aṭas n yizzayriyen ur nebɣi ara taneɣlaft n usedwel. Yal tikkelt, senqaden-tt di laryuy-is, ladɣa deg wayen yeɛnan ddin. Si tama-nniḍen, llan sandicat i d-yeskecmen iman-nsen, ula d nutni ffkan-d rray-nsen. Gar-asen Mesɛud Budiba s yisem n CNAPEST i d-yenna d akken ’taneɣlaft n ttrebga ur ilaq ara ad d-ffeɣ s rray yecban-wagi, ladɣa imi tamurt-nneɣ tleḥḥu ɣer tefranin, d ayen i d-yeglan s waṭas n wawal. Ikemmel, yerna-d: ’Ur ilaq ara ad nessekcem tasertit d wayen-nniḍen ɣer taɣult n ttrebga’’. Gar wa d wayeḍ: Wiss ma yella yiswi n uɣerbaz i tmussni neɣ i wayen-nniḍen?.
Tagi d yiwet n teqsiḍt, ḥekkun-tt-id γef yizirdi, deffir-s anamek neγ azal-is d ameqqran, d akken win yesεan lεib i d-ifeḍḥen tudet-ines, yettili-d d aεewwiq i lebda. Macahu tellemcahu ad tt-yeḍbeε Ṛebbi d asaru.Yiwet n tikkelt, iteddu yizirdi γer yiwet n tebḥirt deg udrar. Cwiṭ akken, iwala sin n yimdanen, la teddun. Yeẓra, ur t-ttağğaan ara kan akka: ad t-wwten. Yeffeγ-it leεqel sani ara yerr, sya d adrar sya d lkaf. Cwi tban-as-d d umatu yiwet n texjiḍt, ulamma d tamecṭuḥt. Yekcem γer-s, simmal ara εeddin yimdanen-nni. Maca, taxjiḍt, yeččuṛ-itt, ma d taseṭṭa-s seg wakken tugar-it, tettban-d γer beṛṛa, ur teffir acemma. Yeqqim sdaxel, ideɛεu ’Ya Ṛebbi ttxil-k, ur tt-walin ara’’. Σeddan yimdanen-nni, ur walan ara. Yeffeγ-d, yerra-d nehta. immuqel γer tseṭṭa-nni-ines, yenna-as: ’Ad akem-yekkes Ṛebbi neγ ad i yi-yekkes’’.Yahia Yanes Kh. A.
Yesla uneẓẓarfu n teɣdemt n Lezzayer ass-nni n, 16 duǧember yezrin, i lwali aqdim n Wehran Mǧulǧud Cherifi deg tedyant n utabeɛ-ines deg tsastant n tukci n leqwaɛi n wakal i Ali Haddad asmi yella uneggaru-a d aselway n tkebbunay tizzayriyin. Dɣa Mass Cerifi i iḥebsen leqdic-is d lwali kraḍ n wagguren-aya, slan-as i wazal n rebɛa n tsaɛtin, seld tullya n tsastanin yerzan asexser meqqren n tedrimt sɣur imasayen iqdimen i iɛeddan deg teɣdemt ussan yezrin, ɣef waya yetturaju ad as-alsen asiwel akken ad semmden yittafttaren-agi s ttbut. I usmekti, ɛeddan yakan sdat n ccreɛ lwaliyat iqdimen am Malek Buḍyaf, Sayf Islam Luḥ mmi-s n mmi-s n uneɣlaf aqdim, akken daɣen i yetturaju i tmesliwt n lwali aqdim n Tittaza akked win n Chlef, dima ɣef tmentilt n usexdem n tedrimt n ddewla i wayen ur nlaq ara.
Macahu tellemcahu ad tt-yeḍbeε Ṛebbi d asaru.Yettwessi umγar mmi-s: ’A mmi, γur-k ad d-tegneḍ siwa ma γef leḥrir, taduli-k d tarakna, γur-k ad d-teččeḍ siwa ma s uksum d wudi d tament, γur-k ad d-tsewqeḍ siwa ma sdat n tewwurt, atnan isurdiyen inu, ma d nekk a mmi tefna tudert-iw’’. Mi i yiweḍ umγar-nni leεfu n Ṛebbi, aqcic teffeγ fell-as lewṣaya-nni n baba-s, lmakla-s taguni-s d ssuq-is ala ttnefxa. Yuγal adrim-nni, tekfa, yeqqim akken d aẓawali win γer yerra yenna-as: ’Ulac’’. Armi i d-yemmekta yiwen n uḥbib n baba-s, iruḥ γur-s iεawed-as-d tamacahut, yeḍsa umγar-nni, yenna-as: ’Ur ttagad a mmi, baba-k yerra leḥsab-is, γas yemmut yeğğa-d awal d lmaεna γur-i. A ak-yeqqar baba-k, tura ha-tt tjerbeḍ?: A-ten-an idrimen-agi-inu γur-k, maca sya d tasawent, ur gan alamma yenγa-k naddam i wakken anda tufiḍ ad d-teγliḍ; ur tett alamma yenγa-k laẓ i wakken ad d-teččeḍ mebla ttnefxa, ma d ssuq, ffeγ γer beṛṛa ad d-teẓreḍ anda i wwḍen lecγwal. Yahia Yanes
Iɛawed yeḥya-d leqdic adelsan di tɣiwant n At Ɛissa Mimun, mbeɛd ussan n yimuras n unebdu. Ihi dɣa, tiddukkla tadelsant "Imnar n Tdukli” n tɣiwant-agi, thegga-d i tikkelt-nniḍen tiwwura yellin ttǧrtes ǧuḍertes ɣef tddukkla-a, leqdicat-is akked umezruy-is. Ad d-yili waya, taggara n ddurt-agi sdat-nneɣ lǧemɛa d ssebt 12 d 13 cutember 2019, deg uɣerbaz amenzu "Hacemi d warraw-is” n taddart n Tḥanut. Syin akkin, ad tebdu tallit n ujerred ɣer yisikwan ateliers ama d wid n tutlayin-a: tamaziɣt, tafransist akked teglizt ama d win terbaɛt n ccna chǧrale neɣ win n usuneɣ dessin.
Leqdic-a, ad d-yili ussan n 20, 21, 27 d 28 deg waggur-a n cutember ideg nella. Ma d beddu n leqraya, yetturaǧu ad yili ussan n 11 d12 tuber -Ɣer taggara, ad d-nesmekti kan belli aseggas iɛeddan, ugar n 60 n yigerdan i yeɣran deg yisikwan n tutlayin-a: tamaziɣt, tafransist akked teglizit. Imi isikwan-a n usuneɣ d terbaɛt n ccna d imaynuten, armi d aseggas-a i ten-id-rnan.
Uɣalent taggara-a tḥuna yesnuzun neɣ ixeddmen tuččit xfifen neɣ ayen iwumi ssawalen medden s yisem n Fast fǧǧd, deg temdint n Wehran d idgan n usemres war tuddsa, ur nesɛi ara tiwtilin iwatan i tigin n tgella iwulmen i yimdanen. Bdu seg tdersi n tezdeg akked leɣla d war aqader n usaḍuf n leqdic. Deg yiɣerman i yeččuren d imezdaɣ, ttlalent-d tḥuna-a am treɣla, imi d ibaṭimuten imaynuten yettwabnan, ɣer din i guǧǧan waṭas seg yimezdaɣ, am yiɣrem Lyasmis, Ṣṣabaḥ, Nnur… yettwassnen s tigti n tḥuna-a n tuččit fessusen.
Dɣa imalas yezrin, ffɣent kra n trebbaɛ n Tenmehla n tnezzut n twilayt n Wehran ɣer unnar, d ayen i ten-yeǧǧan ad bedden ɣef waṭas n twuɣa i ttgen wid ilan tiḥuna. Ufan ulac maḍi tawtilt tadawsant i uheggi n tuččiyin-a tifessasin. Amedya, deg yiwet n tḥanut deg tama n Ṣṣabaḥ, ufan ɣer yiwen asafar n lbaṭaṭa taqdimt i ixesren, yettwahegga wazal n 30 kilu deg-s i usexdem deg tuččit ara yettunefken i yimsebriden. Imraqben-agi, bedden daɣen ɣef lqella n tezdeg deg tgelliwin am rruz d cerba, ula d tuččiyin i swayes tettwassen temnaḍt n Wehran d twilayin n umalu am karantika, lɛeṣban, ur gerrzent ara i tuččit, acku wigi i tent-yettheggin, "ur xemmemen ara ɣef tdawsa n umdan, lhem-nsen amenzu d adrim swayes ara ččaren leǧyub-nsen”,; akken i d-nnan kra.
Ɣef waya, deg tuffɣa-a i tga Tenmehla n tnezzut n twilayt, temdel ugar n 13 n tḥuna, imi d amihi ɣef umdan d tdawsa-ines. Ladɣa ma neẓra belli ugtent tḥuna-a deg tamiwin ideg qqaren yinelmaden n uɣerbaz, neɣ anda llan sbiṭarat d kra n wammasen ideblanen. Yessefk ihi ad yili uxemmem ɣef teṣḥiḥt n bnadem uqbel ad ifat lawan, akken yella deg yinzi "Leḥder yugar leqḍeɛ”.
Khaled Achǧui: Taddart Iẓerruden, d yiwet gar tuddar n tɣiwant n Tirmitin deg wasun n Draɛ Ben Xedda. Tezga-d deg temnaḍt tis tlata n tɣiwant n Tirmitin i yessawaḍen ɣer taddart n Lbir deg tɣiwant n Suq Lexmis deg wasun n Mɛatqa. Seg tama n umalu n taddart-nneɣ , d taddart Iɛellalen, taddart n umeɣras Krim Belkacem, d asif i aɣ-icerken. Seg tama n usammer, d At Ɛrif, d asif diɣen i aɣ-yesdukklen. Seg ugafa, d taddart n umegdul i yuwin aseggas yezrin araz wis rebɛa n temsizzelt Rabeḥ Ɛisat.
Ma seg tama n unẓul, d tuddar n Lbir d At Ɛisa Uzyan deg tɣiwant n Mɛatqa i d-yezgan i taddart-nneɣ am wakken d afrag i usemmiḍ n Ǧerǧer. Amezwaru i izedɣen taddart, yeṭṭef tiɣilt am wakken i ɛemrent akk tuddar n tmurt n Leqbayel; tiɣilt iwumi neqqar ass-a " Iɣil Ufella” i yesɛan diɣen isem n "Tiɣilt Buras” am wakken i aɣ-d-qqaren yimɣaren n taddart. Deg tegrawla n 54, taddart Iẓerruden tefka-d 42 n yimeɣrasen i yellan d ufrinen ger warraw-is; maca mi tzureg tmurt, ur as-yuɣal ara lxir am tuddar akk n tmurt n Leqbayel.
Ha-t-a-n wayen yeǧǧan imezdaɣ-is ttunagen ama dagi deg tmurt ama ɣer tmura n lberrani. Deg wayen yeɛnan amḍan n yimezdaɣ, taddart Iẓerruden, d tis snat deg tɣiwant n Tirmitin umbaɛd taddart tameqqrant deg Tirmitin Ufella, s wazal n 3 000 n yimezdaɣ. Taddart Iẓerruden ass-a, d lmeyyat n yisdawanen, d lmeyyat n yilmeẓyen d telmeẓyin yal wa mucaɛ di lḥirfa-s: talaɣt, azeṭṭa, taxeyyaḍt, iqecwalen, ttrebga n tzizwa, ttrebga n lmal d waṭas n lḥirfat nniḍen. Taddart Iẓerruden, tettwassen diɣen s uɣerbal; akka kan i d-necfa, aṭas n twaculin i yettidiren yi-s.
Amek i d-yella umahil n leqdic-a? Acu i txedmem? Melmi i t-txedmem? Deg tazwara, axeddim, yettili-d yal lǧemɛa. Deg useggas-agi n 2019, ladɣa deg unebdu, axeddim yettili-d yal ass seg lxemsa n tmeddit akken alamma yezgen yiḍ neɣ tikwal alamma yuli wass. Nebda s usizdeg d ufrag n temqebrin n taddart, anǧar d usewseɛ n yiberdan, tukksa n yiḍumman, tuẓut n yisekla…; ma d acebbeḥ n taddart, d ayen i d-yellan deg useggas-agi n -Aṭas n yisenfaren i yettwaxedmen: lemqam n yimeɣrasen, tajmaɛt n taddart, tala, tifwarin n waman, acebbeḥ n yizenqan n taddart, imeḍqan izegzawen, axxam n tddukkla ara yili diɣen d tamkerḍit n taddart, imukan deg ara srusun yimdanen iḍumman-nsen…
Amek i yezmer leqdic am wa ad yesnerni tadamsa, tadawsa akked yidles deg tmetti? Seg tama n tdamsa, leqdic am wagi, yezmer ad yesnerni tuddar-nneɣ . Seg tama, ad yefk lebɣi i yimezdaɣ i wakken ur ttunagen ara ɣer temdinin; ihi, tuddar ad ɛemrent. Tin yernan ɣer-s, leqdic am wagi, ad yerr tuddar-nneɣ d imukan n tmerrit; ayen ara yellin tiwwura i yimawlan n lḥirfat n ufus akken ad d-ḥellin aɣrum-nsen s wayen ara iseḥbibren ɣef yidles-nsen, meḥsub tasekkurt timellalin. Seg tama n tdawsa, d ayen ibanen, tezdeg n tuddar-nneɣ d useḥbiber ɣef twennaḍt s umata, d ayen ara yesneɣsen seg waṭṭanen i d-itekken seg waṭas n wanawen n ubluleɣ. Seg tama tadelsant, leqdic am wagi, ad d-yerr azal i wansayen-nneɣ am tejmaɛt, tala, timecreḍt, tadukli gar yimdanen; war ma nettu aseqdec n tutlayt-nneɣ deg wayen akk ara yettwaxedmen deg taddart.
Yesteqsa-t H. M.
Gar yimeɣnasen n tigawt, i irefden amennuɣ s tira d uselmed n tutlayt tayemmat, yella uselmad d umaru Muḥend Gaya. Tayri-is i tmaziɣt d tmagit demmrent-t i wakken ad ikemmel amennuɣ n tikta, i d-yebda seg wasmi yella d ilemẓi, maca tura d amennuɣ s wudem-nniḍen; s tira s tmaziɣt d usizreg yis-s akked uselmed-ines, mbeɛd amecwar-is aɣezzfan deg ubrid n umennuɣ ɣef tutlayt d tmagit tamaziɣt, ama deg yikabaren n tsertit, ama d tddukkliwin tidelsanin neɣ deg yimussuyen-nniḍen. Muḥen Gaya, d yiwen n yilemẓi yeččuren d tabɣest akked timeɣnest n tmaziɣt. Yebda amennuɣ deg unnar deg umussu addukklan, imi yella d aɛeggal deg waṭas n tddukkliwin tidelsanin, gar-asent tiddukkla "Idles” akked "Tiɣzert”.
Ikemmel deg yikabaren n tsertit, gar-asen akabar n Yiɣallen inemlayen, Amussu adelsan amaziɣ, syin ikemmel-it deg tesbeddit Matub Lwennas akked Ugraw n umaḍal amazig, Tuddsa tazzayrit n yizerfan n umdan. Yebda tamaziɣt seg 1989 ar 1993, syin yuɣal d aselmad n tmaziɣt seg useggas n 1994 ar ass-a. Yella yesselmad taqbaylit deg Tegzirt n Fransa "AFKIF”. Yella diɣ d aneɣmas, imi yura deg uɣmis Iẓuran akked kra n tesɣunin-nniḍen s tmaziɣt acḥal d aseggas, yuɣal yeḥbes. Am wakken diɣ i ikemmel ulmud-is deg Useddu aɣelnaw n tutlayin d tɣermiwin n utram "INALCǦ”, i wakken ad yernu ad yerfed tamussni.
Ma deg uḥric n tira, ar tura ɣur-s kraḍ n yidlisen s tmaziɣt. Yura adlis-is amezwaru ɣef tedyanin n Tefsut taberkant n useggas n 2001, dɣa isemma-as "Amennuɣ n tidet”, ideg yules tidet n tedyant n tefsut 2001, imi yella imir d ameɣnas n tugdut. Syin akin, deg yennayer 2008, yerna yessuffeɣ-d adlis-is wis sin s tmaziɣt ɣef tudert d umennuɣ akked tmenɣiwt n ucennay Matub Lwennas, iwumi yefka azwel "Anazbay”. Adlis-agi, yusa-d d agummu n waṭas n yiseggasen n timeɣnest deg tsebeddit Matub Lwennas, i irefden isem n ucennay-agi amḥadi, am wakken, i yenwa bab-is ad as-yerr tajmilt s yiman-is, akken i d as-yessaweḍ i ucennay-agi yefkan tudert-is i tmaziɣt. Adaǧun Abdelghani
Mi yewweḍ Muḥend Gaya ɣer Fransa, yules-asen asizreg i sin-agi n yidlisen i d-yessuffeɣ yakan di 2006 d -Di yennayer 2019, yerna-d adlis-s wis kraḍ, i yellan d timsirin n tjerrumt n tmaziɣt, iga-as azwel "Timsirin n Tjeṛṛumt n Tmaziɣt ” Aḥric amezwaru. D adlis i d-ijemlen ddeqs n temsirin n tjerrumt, gar-asen-t agemmay, ilugan n tira, imqimen ilelliyen…atg, ara yilin d allal ussnan i yinelmaden d yiselmaden n tmziɣt. Sya ɣer sdat, yettheggi aḥric wis sin n udlis-agi n theṛrumt, ara d-yeffɣen deg wussan i d-iteddun ɣer tama n udlis-nniḍen n ulmad i yiḥaffaḍen n tmaziɣt. Afud igerrzen i umeskar.
Seld n usɛeẓẓeg n tmeẓẓuɣt n yimḍebbren n Tenmehla tazzayrit n waman ɣef wayen ssuturen ixeddamen, ladɣa timerna deg ssuma, xedmen yixeddamen-is asalag grAḍe, ass n acer d arim, 6, 7 seg waggur n tubeṛ -Yella-d ula d yiwen n unejmuɛ sdat n tenmehla-agi i d-yezgan deg tlemmast n temdint n Tizi Uzzu. Tigawt -agi timezgit n sin wussan i yal ddurt, tebda yakan seg 23 deg waggur n cutember iɛeddan, anda ssuturen aɛawed n tmuɣli deg uɣruḍ n yixeddamen anda i yettwali unmalu syndicat n yixeddamen, ddrus maḍi, u yewwi-d ad tili tmerna deg-s. Am waken ssutren daɣen yixeddamen-a agerrez n tewtilin n lxeddma. Ali Zalǧuk
Dɣa deg unejmuɛ i d-yellan sdat n tenmehla Tazzayrit n waman, heḍren-d yixeddamen aṭas ɣef yiɣeblan i d-ttmagaren deg yimeḍqan n uxeddim, yettilin deg lḥers meqqren deg kra n tegnatin, sdat n lɣiḍ n yimezdaɣ. Ɣef leḥsab n yimḍebbren n unmalu, lexṣas n ttawilat iwatan yeɛgeb aṭas axeddim, dayen i d-yettawin iɣeblan meqqren deg uxeddim. Nnan-d yimeḍebbren n tenmehla Tazzayrit n waman d akken s kra n wayen ssutren ixeddamen, d ayen yellan d sswab, d azref, maca ur zmiren ara ad xedmen acemma, dayen yeffɣen i lebɣi-nsen, imi d aɣbel yeɛnan yakk tamurt n Lezzayer. Sdat n usɛeẓẓeg n tmeẓẓuɣt i tikkelt-nniḍen n yimḍebbren teɛna temsalt, kecmen yixeddamen n tenmehla Tazzayrit n waman deg yiwen usalag war aneḥbus alamma rran-d yimḍebbren teɛna temsalt ɣer tuget n wayen ssutren.
Macahu tellemcahu ad tt-yeḍbeε Ṛebbi d asaru. Tagi γef yiwen n urgaz i yesεan nneyya tamsarit, acku ixeddem γef warraw-is, yeḍmeε ala deg win i t-id-ixelqen, mi i as-tenna tmeṭṭut-is: ’I tura kečč, akka kan ara teqqimeḍ d axeddam, ur tettnadiḍ ara γef ṛbeḥ-ik?’’Yerra-as: ’Ayen yellan fell-I, ad t-xeddmeγ, ayen-nniḍen γer Ṛebbi i yella, u yerna ma yebγa Ṛebbi ad rebḥeγ, ad d-yessiweḍ rbeḥ γer uxxam’’. Yiwet n tikkelt, truḥ tmeṭṭut-is γer lexla, ad tenqec. Ha-t-a tufa tasagimt ddaw n wakal teččuṛ d ddheb, seg wakken ulac deg-s nneyya d lxir, tuzzel γer watmaten-is tenna-asen: ’Rwaḥet ay atma, ufiγ agerruj, maca γurwat anwa ad ken-id-yeẓren γef wakal n urgaz-iw, ma ulac ad iẓer neγ ad icuk’’.
Tameddit deg yiḍ, ṣṣuben watmaten-is, skeflen-d asagem-nni, wwin-t γer uxxam-nsen. Mi wwḍen, smaren-t-id, afen-t yeččuṛ d izerman akk d tγirdmawin. Nann-as:’’Yyah, yyah, tebγiḍ ad aγ-tenγeḍ kemm d urgaz-im akken ad aγ-twertem’’. Nettat ur teẓri acemma acku deg uxxam-is i tella. Qqimen armi i neṣṣef yiḍ, ulin γer uxxam n wuletma-tsen, surgen-d asagem-nni seg cmini nnan-as: ’Mmtet tura, awer i d-tuγalem kemm wala argaz-im’’. Mi i d-yesla urgaz-is i kra yenγel-d si ssqef n uxxam-is, yekker-d, yaf-d taqaεet meṛṛa la tettmucεul s ddheb d lfeṭṭa, imuqel tameṭṭut-is yenna-as: ’Niγ nniγ-am asmi ara yi-d-yerẓeq Ṛebbi, yessen axxam’’. Yahia Yanes
Nura Idiri, d tanaẓurt tamsuneɣt Taqbaylit, d tamedyazt i ufan kra n tafat deg yifyar-nni imecṭaḥ mi ara ten-tettaru ɣef tferrawt tamellalt. Mi tt-nesteqsa ad nẓer tamuɣli-s, tettwali d akken deg umaḍal n tmedyazt, asefru d win akken i d-yettasen seg lqaɛ n wul i umedyaz. Aneggaru-a daɣen, d win yettḥulfun mliḥ-mliḥ s wayen i as-d-yezzin. Ɣur-s daɣen, asefru d awalen-nni i icudden aẓar ɣer yiẓuran, deg daxal n yal yiwet d yal yiwen.
Terna tenna-d: « Tamedyazt, d izen inefɛen timetti d wayen i aɣ-d-yezzin merra. Aredmani, ɣur-i tamedyezt d tafat, d ddwa ", akka i tettwali Nura tamedyazt, ama ɣef leḥsab n wayen i as-d-tewwi tẓuri-a i nettat, neɣ i twennaḍt-is d wid akk tessen. Gar wayen tessefra Nura Idiri, nezmer ad d-nebder kra n yizwal n yisefra-s, am "Tafsut”, "Targit”, "Ukiɣ-d deg umaḍal tedduɣ”, "Ḥemmleɣ tidderwect-iw”. Ɣer tama n usmedyez, Nura Idiri d tamsuneɣt daɣen i iḥemmlen ad d-terr deg tewriqt tugniwin tigamanin.
Am tmedyazt i tebda aṭas-aya, ula d asuneɣ, ddeqs-aya n yiseggasen segmi tger deg-s. Ayen yakk walant wallen-is, tezmer ad t-tecreḍ s ufus-is, s uɣanib d tferrawt. Dɣa, i lmend n teẓrigt tis mraw-sat n tfaska n tmedyazt tamaziɣt, i d-yellan deg Udrar n Fad d tajmilt i tmarut Kaysa Xalifi aseggas-a, thegga-d Massa Nura yiwet n tejmilt s tɣara-s nettat. Aya, mi tbudd yiwet n tfelwit d tabaḥant i twacult n Kaysa Xalifi, ideg nezmer ad nwali amek i d-tcebbeḥ s tẓuri udem n Kaysa, i aɣ-yeǧǧan ass n, 25 yunyu -Ula i yinaẓuren-nniḍen, tga ayendin d tijmilin s wunuɣ. Seg wayen tura tmedyazt Nura Idiri, ad nebḍu yid-wen taseddart-a seg usefru i tzewwel « Taqbaylit-iw ur teɛwiǧ ": "Suɛfeɣ tawaɣit, Ddiɣ-as deg lebɣi… Lasel acḥal yettru. Taqbaylit-iw Tezga tezreɛ talwit, Tezzi-d fell-i tmuɣli, Ass-a ad necfu. Taqbaylit-iw
Yettwassen Malek Ḥud s yisefra d tullisin, maca iger taggara-a ula deg wungal. Ihi i lmend n tsuffeɣt-a tamaynut nesteqsa-t, yerra-aɣ-d.
S kra n wawalen, ɣer wanida tcuddeḍ taqsiḍt-is?S yiwen n wawal, taqsiḍt n « Ccḍeb akked yiẓuran " teqqen ɣer tmaziɣt akked tidda-ines: tutlayt, amezruy, tamagit, taɣerma, insayen, imyayen… Seg wasmi i tebna ddunit, tura ɣef Umaziɣ ad yettnaɣ akken ad d-yeqqim ur inegger ara; ar ass-a netta d anaḍeḥ, urǧin yebri i ṭṭbel deg waman. Tamaziɣt, teḍra yid-s am useklu, yebḍa ɣef sin n yiḥricen: Tama n nnig n tmurt d ccḍeb, d taseṭṭa, d iferrawen, tettɣar, tɣelli-d ɣef tmurt, trekku, yettawi-tt waḍu. Tama tis snat tezga ddaw n tmurt, d iẓuran, ur tettbeddil ara, d tinna kan seg zik n zik. Ungal-a, yuwi-d awal ɣef wanect-agi akk.
Tgiḍ ussan yezrin timlilit d yimeɣriyen deg tnedlist Saɛid Meqbel. Amek tɛedda?Ass amenzu n wayyur-a n furar ɣef tis snat n tmeddit deg tnedlist Saɛid Muqbel n Tazaɣart Ḥammuc, nga yiwet n temlilit n usnuzu s ubuddu n yidlisen-nneɣ , nekk d umeddakkel ameɣnas n zik Ǧamal Arezqi. I yellan din ass-nni yiwen n umjahed aqdim n At Mlikec, Mezyan Ɛmiruc iwumi yura Ǧamal tanagit-is ɣef ṭṭrad 54--Nennegraw ddeqs yid-neɣ. Newwi-d awal d sin n yiselmaden n tsekla, yiwen n tesdawit n Tubiret, Mass Bellal Nurdin, wayeḍ n tesdawit n Bgayet Mass Ulebsir Karim i i yi-igan tazwart i ungal-iw, ɣef tsekla s umata. Seg melmi i tebda tsekla taqbaylit d wanda tuweḍ ass-a? Acu n wuguren i d-ttmmagaren ama imyura ama imsiẓrigen. Askasi yekka azal n snat n tsaɛtin. Ddeqs i d-yusan uɣen sin n yidlisen « Ccḍeb akked yiẓuran " inu, « Akal d wawal " n Djamal Arezki.
Amek tga tmuɣli-k ɣef tsekla taqbaylit taggara-a? Anwa ara kem-yamnen a ddunit mi tuweḍ tsekla taqbaylit ɣer uswir am wa? Aseggas-a 15 n yizwal n wungalen i d-yeffɣen s teqbaylit, amḍan-a yugar win n teɛrabt akked win n tefransist deg tmurt-nneɣ . Teggra-d tura ɣer tɣara n ufares aseklan. D akud ara d-yerren s lexbar ɣef wayen yuklalen ad yerfed isem n tsekla d wayen-nniḍen ur nefki ara akk anzi ɣer wayen iwumi neqqar « tasekla ". Akka tura, llan aṭas n wid yettarun idlisen s teqbaylit. Teḍra yid-neɣ am win yekkaten ad d-yeɣrem akud-nni i aɣ-deggren metɛemda wid yettḍebbiren fell-aneɣ. Ssarameɣ, ad tkemmel tegnit akka neɣ ugar ma Leqbayel beggsen-d ad qqaren ayen i d-iteffɣen s tutlayt-nsen.
Tanemmirt-ik.
