Awal-ik n taggara…Anawen akken ma llan n tsekla, ternuḍ tiẓuriyin merra am tmezgunt, ssinima, taklut, ccna ttḥuddun tutlayt ɣef nnger-is i ttnadin kra n urbaɛ ad d-yeḍru ɣef yiqerray-nsen. A win yufan inaẓuren-a deg tal taɣult, ad d-dhun akken i iwata deg umahil-nsen n usnulfu, ma d wiyiḍ ad ten-ssebɣasen s wayen iwumi zemren ladɣa taɣuri n yidlisen i d-iteffɣen imi fell-as i d-newwi awal. Tanemmirt i kečč, tanemmirt i uɣmis, tanemmirt i yimeɣriyen ur nettakk afus. Ttraǧuɣ timuɣliwin-nsen mi ara fakken s tɣuri n ungal « Ccḍeb akked yiẓuran ". Yesteqsa-t M. K.
Mazal, ar ass-a, ulac d acu i ibedlen deg sbiṭer n tarrawt n Terga Uzemmur segmi yettwaldi deg useggas n -Γas ma yella rezzun-d ɣuṛ-s seg yal amḍiq n twilayt, tikwal ula seg beṛṛa-is, ameεna liḥala-ines ur telli d tin yeṣṣefṛaḥen. Ad d-nesmekti d akken sbiṭer-a, mačči kan i tarrawt n tullas, meεna i udawi n lehlakat i icudden ɣer tmeṭṭut s umata, am waṭṭan n uxenzir n lwelda, d yidmaren. S unamek-nniḍen, tullas yettdawin deg-s, ḥwaǧent aḥader, d usayes, mačči d astehzi ideg llant tura. Seg yiwet n tama, ur ufint ara tullas timuḍan iman-nsent dinna, acku addad n temεict yexṣeṛ mliḥ. Amedya, win n tguni. Imi deg yiwen n umeṭṭraḥ, gganent armi d ukuẓ n tullas.
Rnu i waya, ssemliliyen deg yiwet n tzeqqa, tid yurwen, tid i ixedmen attaṛaṣyun, d tid yettεassan ad -telḥeq nnuba-nsent ad cerrgent. Ula d naddam ur tezmir yiwet ad testaεfu, imi yeṭṭuqet umeslay di tzeqqa. Mebla ma nettu tuččit i d-ttaken i yimuḍan, imi mačči d ayen yezmer ad yessebleε yiwen. Seg tama-nniḍen, tezdeg iɣab yisem-is deg wadeg-nni, ama d taduli, ama d abduz. Ula d beṛṛa n sbiṭaṛ ur yeslik ara. Dɣa ur zmirent tullas ad ldint ula d ṭṭwiqan, yuɣ lḥal tfuḥ lḥala.
« Limer teḥbes temsalt dagi, yezmer yiwen ad yesbeṛ ", i aɣ-d-tenna yiwet n tmuḍint i d-yekksen aculliḍ kyste  seg lwalda-s, imi i nesteqsa ɣef uswir n uxeddim deg sbiṭer, dɣa tkemmel deg wawal-is tenna-d: « qqimeɣ acḥal n wakud, ttεessaɣ nnuba-w ad telḥeq, i wakken ad cerrgeɣ. Meɛna imi i d-yelḥeq wass-nni, ayen i sεeddaɣ yugar leqṛiḥ n waṭṭan. Nekk ad tεeggideɣ, tifremliyin, yiwet ur d-trezzu ɣuṛ-i. Ula mi ara ad d-yelḥeq lawan i wakken ad wteɣ tissegnit n ussenqes n ṣṣṭer, d tid yuḍnen i yettṛuḥun ttḥellilent deg-sent i wakken ad d-ṛuḥent, amzun ur yelli d axeddim-nsent. Ma yella d amsujji, iεedda-d ɣur-i ala yiwet n tikkelt".
D tidet, amḍan n tullas i d-irezzun ɣer sbiṭer n Terga Uzemmur d ameqqṛan, yerna aneggaru-a ur yezmir ad yerfed buhan, lameεna ayɣeṛ ur d-rennun ara yimḍebbṛen i teεna temsalt sbiṭarat-nniḍen, ahat ad yenqes leḥṛis ɣef yimuḍan?
Ffɣen-d yiselmaden n uswir amenzu deg waṭas n twilayin, imalas yezrin, akken ad ssutren aseɛdel-nsen d yiswiren n uɣerbaz alemmas d tesnawit deg waṭas n lecɣal yerzan amahil-nsen, imi ttwalin belli iselmaden yettmahilen deg uswir-a adday, yettili-d fell-asen lḥerṣ ugar n yiswiren-nniḍen. Gar tmental i ten-yeǧǧan ad bedden sdat n teɣlift n usegmi akked tenmehliwin n usedwel d waṭas n yiɣerbazen deg wakal n tmurt, nnan belli ttwaɛezlen, tidersi n tcehrit-nsen, sswayeɛ i qeddcen seg ṣṣbeḥ alamma d tameddit, rnu ɣer waya taɛessast n yinelmaden deg ubaraz d usečču d yidgan-nniḍen n uɣerbaz.
D ayen i ten-yeǧǧan ad farṣen tagnit n wass aɣelnaw n uselmad i d-yettezzin yal ass n 5 tuber n yal aseggas, ad gen abeddi-nsen azekka-nni akken ad d-sbegnen lɣiḍ-nsen. Ad ssiwḍen, diɣ, isuturen-nsen ɣer yimasayen yeṭṭfen taɣult n leqraya, ad d-muqlen ɣur-sen, ad snefsusin fell-asen taɛkemt d wuguren. Gar wuguren daɣen i ten-yerḥan d aheggi n tfertin n tɣuri deg uxxam s tira n ufus i wugar n 10 n yilmuden: gar-asen wid ur nelli d taɣult-nsen am usuneɣ, tusnakt, aẓawan d waddal akked ṭaẓẓayt n temsirin ɣef uswir n unelmad. Ma d asuter agejdan i refden, uɣur i d-ssawlen deg yiẓedwa inmettiyen i yakk iselmaden n uswir-a adday, d akken d lawan ad ddukklen deg tṣeddart n uxeddim akked uswir n uɣerbaz alemmas, acku, ɛlaḥsab-nsen, leɛtab i ttenɛettaben yugar tacehrit i ttaɣen. Kh. A.
«Ibeddi-a n yiseɣ, ur ttekkant ara deg-s tenmaliwin les syndicats, akken ur d-yettili ara ubeddel n tigawt. Ma nuɣal-d ɣer wuguren, neṭṭalab aseɛdel d yiswiren inaflayen, tukksa n tɛessast d usenqes n sswayeɛ n uxeddim, aɛiwed i wahil n tsuta tis snat d tuɣalin ɣer talɣa n uselmed sḍis n yiseggasen deg uɣerbaz amenzu, d ayen ara yekksen taččart n tneɣriyin", i d-yenna yiwen n uselmad. Iselmaden igensasen, gan ineqqisen ara yettunefken i yinemhalen n usedwel n twilayin merra, seg tama-nsen wigi, ad t-ssiwḍen i uneɣlaf n usedwal. Deg uraǧu n tririt yelhan, myefken asiher i yibeddiyen d tuffɣiwin-nniḍen.
Yetturaǧu ad d-tili tfaska taɣelnawt tis ukkuẓet n tmedyazt tamaziɣt deg waɣir n Tubiret. D timlilit ara d-theggi Tiddukkla Tadelsant Amaziɣ n taddart n At Leqsar, seg wass n 19 ar 22 meɣres 2020 i d-iteddun. D tagnit daɣen, akken yis-s ad tuɣal tejmilt i yiwet seg tgejda n tmedyazt taqbaylit, seg yimenza irefden asefru, yis-s i iḥureb ɣef yidles d tmagit, wagi d Mǧhamed Benhamadǧuche yettwassnen s yisem n Ben Mǧhammed neɣ Ben. Yelha ma ttilint-d akka tejmilin am tigi i wudmawen urɛad teǧǧa tudert, mačči ḥala ma tewwi-ten tmettant, akken qqaren "Asmi yedder yectaq aɛeqqa n ttmer, mi yemmut ɛellqen-as aɛerjun”. Akken ad iḥulfu s wazal ila leqdic d wayen iga ɣef lǧal n yidles amaziɣ. Tafaska-a n Tubiret, ad d-ilin deg-s isuḍaf n uttekki am tfaskiwin d-ssuddusent tddukkliwin-nniḍen n tmurt n leqbayel, ur nettaf ara aṭas n umgired.
Tameddit n wass-nni n lǧemɛa iɛeddan, 2 ɣuct 2019, temlal tasa d way turew deg uɣerbaz amenzu n taddart n Lemṣella, di tɣiwant n Yilula Umalu.
D tagnit ideg mlalen akk yinelmaden ɣer tama n yiselmaden-nsen ɣer tama diɣ n yimawlan-nsen. Ala acmumeḥ d lferḥ i d-yettbanen ɣef wudmawen, ma d ilsawen ur cuḥḥen ara i uqessar d usmekti n wayen sɛeddan akk yinelmaden yeɣran deg uɣerbaz-agi. Tebda tfugla-agi i d-yettwasuddsen i lmend n yinelmaden n taddart-a, i d-yufraren deg yikayaden-agi unṣiben. Mbeɛd awal n tazwara, n uselway n tddukkla tadelsant Tiɣilt, i d-iheggan leqdic-agi. Yesseḥres deg umeslay-is ɣef wazal n usebɣes n yinelmaden-agi d usirem n umecwar aɣezzfan di leqraya-nsen.
Ttwaferqen warrazen d yigerdasen n usebɣes ɣef merra yinelmaden n taddart-agi i d-yufraren s yigemmaḍ yelhan deg tlata ikayaden unṣiben i useggas-agi aɣurbiz 2018/-Fkan azal n 12 n warrazen, 7 seg-sen i yinelmaden i d-yewwin akayad n uswir wis 5, 3 n warrazen-nniḍen i yinelmaden i d-yewwin akayad n BEM ɣer tama sin n warrazen i yettunefken i wid i d-irebḥen akayad n BAC.
Am wakken diɣ i d-llan kra n leqdicat idelsanen-nniḍen ɣer tama n ufraq n warrazen-agi. Ad d-nesmekti kan belli d taddart n Lemṣella i d-yettheggin yal aseggas tameɣra n tbexsisin, maca tezgel tazrigt n yilindi, tili ara d-yilin d tis -Ma d tazrigt tis 13, ad tili aseggas-a ussan n 29 d 30 ɣuct -Adaǧun Ghani
Macahu tellemcahu ad tt-yeḍbeε Ṛebbi d asaru. Qarren wat zik, tella yiwet n tmeṭṭut d tamattart, meḥsub tettmetra, maca d aggur di ṣsifa-s, d tuḥdiqt d timsetḥit. Ihi mi i tt-iwala ugellid, yenna-as: ’A taqcict, seg wass-a d tasawant, yekfa fell-am lḥif-agi n tuttra, ad kem-aγeγ, ad tuγaleḍ d tameṭṭut-iw’’. Tefreḥ tmeṭṭut, ur tumin i iṣaren, armi tikwal teqqar-as amer d targit i la ttarguγ. Σeddan yiseggassen, nnan-as yixeddamen-is I ugellid: ’A sidi, nsel i tmeṭṭut-ik, thedder deg uxxam. Ɛni yella yid-s walbaεḍ?’’ Ṣselṭan iwhem! Iεus-itt armi d yiwen wass iwala-tt di yal tamḍiqt di leqser, tessers cwiṭ n kra: ya d aγrum, ya d seksu, ya d iniγman neγ d lebsa, dγa ad d-ttεeddi γef yimeḍqan-nni, ad tessawal: ’Ṭεam n Ṛebbi ya lmumnin, ṣadaqa i wudem n Ṛebbi’’. Yeffeγ-d γur-s ugellid, yenna-as: ’Yak a tameṭṭut, γileγ ifuk fell-am lḥif, acimi akka!’’ Tameṭṭut: ’Annaγ ay agellid, tannumi, d yir aṭṭan’’. Yerra-as: ’Ruḥ ihi ad tkemmleḍ ccγel tennumeḍ. Yahia Yanes
Tessuddes-d tddukla n yimezlan d yirmuden n yilmeẓyen n temdint n Tegzirt, « Taɛeqquct n yiri n yilel n Tegzirt " s lemɛawna n tddukkla talsawit, « Tiddukla tazzayrit n tgemmi n twennaṭ d izerfan n umdan " n temdint n Tizi Uzzu d Waggur azeggaɣ azzayri yiwet n teɣlamt tasejjant si tṣebḥit armi d tamedit n wass-nni n sem, 14 furar 2020, deg uɣerbaz amenzu "Muḥamed Ahras” n taddart n Tifra. Anda i d-yella udawi baṭel i yimdanen i d-yerzan s waṭas di tsaɛtin timezwura n wass. Am wakken i d-yella, daɣen, unadi ara d-ibeggnen ma yella kra lehlak I yesɛa umdan-nni netta ur yeɛlim ara. ama s tukksa n yidammen, neɣ s tmacint.
Deg yiseggasen-agi ineggura, yella-d lḥir meqqren sɣur imezdaɣ n tɣiwant n Mɛatqa, akken ad beddlen udem n tɣiwanin n dayra-nsen yenḥafen s waṭas. Dɣa seg tectliwin n usizdeg n tudrin, i d-iḥellan imeḍqan deg temsizzelt n taddart tazedgant, ɣer tiwizi n useḥbiber ɣef twenaḍt, d tfaskiwin n tzemmurt n ufexxar. Tikkelt-agi, d taddart n Yiɣil n Teqḍibin yettabaɛen ɣer tɣiwant n Mɛatqa, i d-yefkan afus n tallelt i tɣiwant, s tukci n wakal i lebni n unnar n ddabex uḍar, deg umḍiq iwumi qqaren Assif. Deg tazwara n ddurt iɛeddan, heggan-d yimezdaɣ n taddart n Yiɣil n Teqḍibin d yimezdaɣ n tudrin n Iberquqen tiwizi i usewseɛ d uwenneɛ n unnar-agi n ddabex uḍar, anda smarsen yakk ttawilat iwatan yellan gar yifassen-nsen, akken ad fkan tagnit i yilmeẓyen n tɣiwant, ad tturaren deg-s. Seg lǧiha-nsen, ferḥen nezzeh yimezdaɣ n tɣiwant n Mɛatqa seg tcetliwt-agi n Yiɣil n Teqḍibin. Ula d aselway n Useqqamu aɣerfan Aɣiwan n Mɛatqa, Mass Laguel Lyes, ibeggen-d lferḥ-is s tigawt-agi, u yewɛed s uwenneɛ akken iwata annar-agi n ddabax uḍar i la ttraǧun yilmeẓyen n tɣiwant ugar n 30 d aseggas aya. Ad d-nesmekti kkan d akken dayra n Mɛatqa yesɛan ugar n 54 000 n yimezdaɣ, ur tesɛi ara ar ass-a annar n ddabex uḍar iwatan. Ala yiwen n umḍiq kan i yellan anda tturaren, ula d winna ur iwulem ara, ur yeqɛid ara. Yerna ffkan-t i lebni n usenfar n Sbitar n dayra n Mɛatqa.
Seld 5 n yiseggasen segmi yeḥbes usenfar n usiweḍ n lgaz agaman seg Tala Ifassen ɣer tɣiwant n Ayt Smaɛel, a-t-an berrḥent-d kra n teɣbula s userreḥ i tedrimt ara d-yawin akemmel n lecɣal. Ilaq ad d-nini d akken ulamma aẓeṭṭa n ubḍaw yella yettmagga deg wakuden iɛeddan di kra n tuddar n tɣiwant, maca asenfar n tiwin n uqadus ara d-yasen ɣer Uswel, seg Tala n Yifassen, yella yewḥel. Iqeddicen-nni dɣa i yellan ttmaggan deg yiberdan, gan-d ayendin d uguren i yimezdaɣ. Tikwal, ttilin d amihi fell-asen, abeɛda arrac imecṭaḥ i izemren ad ɣlin, seg tikkelt ɣer tayeḍ, deg yiḍerfan yettwaɣzan.
Rnu-as attwiɣ n yiberdan i yesserfan nezzeh inehharen n yikerrusen. Ula d iqeddacen n termisin ur ttarran ara abrid amek i t-ttuɣ, mi ara kfun lecɣal-nsen. Maca tura, ad snuffsen yimezdaɣ xersum s yisalli n userreḥ n usenfar ara asen-ibeddlen kra di tɣara n tudert, ara asen-yekksen kra n tɛekmin i niqal ttidiren seg lgaz n tqerɛet. «Seld annect-nni d araǧu, yettwakkes dayen lqid ɣef usenfar-a n usiweḍ n lgaz i tɣiwant-nneɣ . Mazal ad aɣ-d-mlen amek ara tili tura akken ad nwali tirmisin deg unnar", i aɣ-d-yenna uselway n tɣiwant n Ayt Smaɛel, Mass Sadeq Rebbaɛi. Ad d-nesmekti d akken seg Sṭif i d-tewwi tɣiwant n Ayt Smaɛel, acku tezdi tilisa akked twilayt-a.
Dɣa, tuqqna ad d-tas ɣef teɣzi n wazal n 15 n yikilumitren akken ad tessečč ayen yettqaraben ɣer 3 000 n yixxamen. Kra n yiɣermanen ssarmen lemmer i d-yeḍra waya deg unebdu yezrin. «Lemmer ur sweḥlen ara asenfar-a ɣur-nneɣ iseggasen-a ineggura, tili tagrest-a nesɛedda-tt teḥma akken iwulem", i iwala yiwen n umezdaɣ.
Deg yiseggasen-agi ineggura, yella-d lḥir meqqren seg teseqquma n tudrin i usizdeg d ugerrez n tmurt n Leqbayen.
Ayen i d-yefkan afud deg waya, d tamsizzelt n Aissat Rabaḥ i d-yettheggi Useqqamu Aɣerfan n Lwilaya n Tizi Uzzu, i d-ixelqen tismin ɣer wayen igerrzen. Dɣa, ilul-d lḥir, tikelt-agi, ɣer teseqqamut n taddart n At Zɛim s tallelt n yimezdaɣ. D taddart i d-yezgan 4 n yikulimitren ɣer unẓul n tɣiwant n Mɛatqa, i d-yessuddsen tacemlit n usizdeg d ugerrez n taddart. D tacemlit i yettilin sin n wussan deg yal ddurt, deg wass n Sem d Sed. I uttekki deg temsizzelt n taddart zeddigen deg ugezdu, aṭas n leqdicat i d-yellan deg unnar, s tallelt n Useqqamu Aɣerfan n Lwilaya n Tizi-Uzzu, Aseqqamu Aɣerfan Aɣiwan n Mɛatqa, imɛelmen n taddart. Gar leqdicat-agi, ad naf asenfar n lebni n tuget n yizenqan n taddart s wuzru i wumi qqaren s trumit " Ardǧise «, d asenfar i d-yefka Useqqamu Aɣerfan n Lwilaya n Tizi-Uzzu, daɣen asenfar n usiweḍ n waman, trisiti d lgaz ɣer yal ixxamen imaynuten ur nesɛi ara isenfaren-agi igejdanen. Daɣen, llan yisenfaren n lebni n tliwa deg tlemmast n taddart d lebni n yiɣeṛban n yimeḍqan i d-yettsaxan, wigi d isenfaren i d-yettunefken sɣur Useqqamu Aɣerfan n Mɛatqa.
Deg tcemlit-agi n taddart, ttekkant, tikelta-agi, ula d tilawin, sddaw n leɛnaya n tddukkla tamaynut n tlawin yettusemman Ixulaf n At Zɛim, i d-yefkan afud meqqren deg leqdicat n usizdeg d ugerrez, ladɣa s tiktiwin timaynutin deg useḥbiber ɣef twennadt. Rnu ɣef waya, tiẓẓin n yijeǧǧigen deg yal tiɣmert n taddart. Ayen i d-yefkan udem igerrzen i yizenqan-is. Yal taggara n ddurt, ad ddukklen yimezdaɣ n taddart meẓẓi meqqer, am tmeṭṭut am urgaz, deg yiwet n twizi meqqren, iswi-ines awḥid, agerrez n wudem n taddart. Ayen igerrzen deg leqdicat yecban wigi, d tadukli i d-yettlalen, i yettnernin seg wass ɣer wayeḍ, deg lfayda n umdan, syin n twacult, ɣer tmetti d talsa sumata. Deg tirza-nneɣ ɣer yizenqan n taddart, nufa lḥan yimezdaɣ deg ugerrez n taddart, wa d lebni n yiɣeṛban, wa deg usizdeg n yizenqan, yiwen yettreqqim iɣeṛban n tala. Ayen yelhan yakk deg waya, tuget n yisufer n ugerrez, ttwaksen-d seg ugama, ama d asɣar, talaxt, lmuɣri, usbiɣ, azṛu…Ali Zalǧuk
Tella-d di taggara n ddurt iɛeddan, tezrigt tis tlata n rreḥba n udlis i warrac deg taddart n Uɛfir deg tɣiwant n Bujimaɛ. Ass-nni n lǧemɛa d ssebt 27-28/09/2019, imezdaɣ n taddart n Uɛfir n Bujimaɛ, llan di ttiɛad u deg yirebbi n yidles s umata d udlis s wuzzig. Mebeɛd tazrigt tamezwarut n 2016 d tis snat n 2018, i iɛeddan deg tegnatin igerrzen, tefka afud meqqren i tddukkla tadelsant "Amnir” n tama n Uεfir n Bujimaε, i wakken ad suddsen tazrigt-a tamaynut. D ashier i d-yettwaheggan s tallelt n Tenmehla n yidles n Tizi Uzzu, tin n usegmi d usedwel ɣer tama n Useqqmu Aɣerfan n Lwilaya n Tizi Uzzu, d wiyaḍ. Yella-d leqdic-agi adelsan n sin wussan, deg uɣerbaz amezwaru "Addar Belɛid” yellan deg tama-agi n Uεfir, anda i txeddem ddeqs n yirmad tddukkla-agi tadigant, di yal tikkelt.
D Rreḥba n udlis deg tezrigt-is tis kraḍet, ideg ttekkint wazal n 12 n tezrigin, i ixedmen timsikniyin s usenzi n yidlisen. Ad d-nedber gar-asent; Tamagit, El Amel, Richa Elsam, Jelis…atg. Am wakken daɣen, i d-llan wazal n 15 yimyura, yettarun i ugrud, i yessenzen s ubuddu idlisen-nsen, s tutlayin-a yemgaraden tamaziɣt, tafransist d taɛrabt, i d-yerzan seg waṭas n tamiwin n lwilaya n Tizi Uzzu. Ad d-nebder gar-asen: Tinhinan Ḥarrac, Ali Ḥeǧǧaz, Racid Buxerrub, Ḥusin Luni…atg. Imsuddsen n rreḥba-a, heggan-d leqdicat-nniḍen, i d-yellan deg wahil n tezrigt-a, anda ara naf sin n yisaragen ɣef tfelsafit, yiwen ɣef tfelsafit s umata sɣur Mass Ḥerrac Ḥmed, yellan d aselmad n tfelsafit yeffɣen ɣer tasaɣt.
wis sin, yella-d ɣef tfelsafit n ugrud, sɣur Massa Marie-Laure Duttin, d taɛeggalt di tddukkla "Algerie-France Amitiẓ”. Am wakken daɣen, ara naf isikwan ateliers n usuneɣ akked tɣuri, ɣer tama n umseḍsi akked useḥḥar d wayen-nniḍen. Yella-d diɣ, usarag s ssenf n table rǧnde, sɣur tezrigt La Pensẓe, i yettarun i ugrud, yezzi-d deg-s wawal ɣef wazal n udlis n ugrud. Bɣan yiεeggalen n tddukkla-agi "Amnir”, ad ẓẓun tikti n udlis, tayri n tɣuri ɣer warrac imecṭaḥ, d asebɣes daɣen i yimura yettarun i tsuta-agi. Ma ɣer taggara n ttiɛad-agi, fkan arrazen d igerdazen n usebɣes i warrac i d-yufraren deg n temsizliyin, i xedmen yakkan.
Am yal aseggas, ḍeṛṛunt aṭaṣ n txeṣṣaṛin di tegrest, ama d isehwa n yiberdan, aṭṭerdeq n tbutayin n lgaz, neɣ d axnaq n yimdanen s wayen i iteddun s yis-s. Amedya, d tin yeḍṛan di Xeṛṛaṭa, ass n 13 unbir yezrin. Taluft-a, tamentilt-is d lgaz, dɣa qrib i tegla s teṛwiḥin n 6 n yimdanen seg yiwet n twacult. Γef leḥsab n teɣbalut-nneɣ , tadyant-a, teḍṛa di temnaḍt n Yijermunen, taɣiwant n Xeṛṛaṭa. Ɣef 02: 00 n tnezzayt, yekker leεyaḍ gar yimεacren n twacult-a, seld mi slan s wayen yeḍṛan. Imir-n kan i ssawlen i yiqeddacen n Uḥuddu aɣarim. Ineggura-a leḥqen-d di lawan, dɣa ṣṣawḍen selken-ten-id seg lmut timḥettemt. I yisalli, deg wid i ixenqen llan kṛad n yirgazen, d kṛaḍ n tullas. Ma yella d leεmeṛ sεan seg 33 armi d 76 n yiseggasen.
Ad d-nesmekti d akken, ɣef leḥsab n yisallen i aɣ-d-yewwḍen, iεeggalen n twacult-a, ur ssensen ara lgaz uqbel ad gnen, nutni ur zrin ara belli llan yiteyyuten i yessuffuɣen. Daymi ur faqen ara, armi i d-ufan iman-nsen wa yeṣreε, wa yemlelli. Wwin-ten yiqeddacen n Uḥuddu aɣarim s uɣiwel ɣer sbiṭer n Xeṛṛata, anda i asen-xedmen ayen i ilaqen. Ma yella seg tama n tɣellist, ttweṣṣin yiqeddacen n Uḥuddu aɣarim iɣermanen ad ḥaddren iman-nsen, acku lgaz n umunuksid n kaṛbun, ur iṛeḥḥem ara. Ihi yewwi-d fell-asen ad ttaǧǧan tiṭwiqin i ubeḥri, ad snusun ayen akk i iteddun s lgaz deg uxxam uqbel taguni. Rnu i waya, yal yiwen yellan sdat yimseḥmuchauffage, ma yella iwala times-is d tawṛaɣt, ad t-yessens, ad iwali d acu d aɣilif. Akken qqaṛen At zik aḥader yeɣleb aqader.
Tgellu-d twaɣit n tmes s umihi i umaḍal s umata. D tawaɣit i d-yettawin lemḍerra i umdan daɣen, imi deg kra n tamiwin tkeččem ula ɣer tuddar, tessexsar kra ara taf sdat-s. Yal aseggas tḥeggeṣ tiẓegwa, isekla d yimɣan. Ma d ssebbat d tidak dima, ma mačči d timental n ugama, d amdan i yettilin deffir n twaɣit. D igiman n yigeṭṭaren i ireqqen yal anebdu, ur ikeffu ara dɣa alamma berrḥent-d tenmehliwin n uḥuddu aɣarim s yigmaḍ i d-tessegra, ad ggarent tiɣri i leɛqel d leḥder. Dɣa deg twilayt n Wehran, tefka-d, seg tama-s, Tenmehla n uḥuddu aɣarim leḥsab n tjumma i tesserɣ tmes deg unebdu-a s 121 igeṭṭaren, seg umenzu n yulyu 2019 armi d 8 cutamber -Khaled Achǧui
Tenna-d d akken ɣas meqqer wuṭṭun-a, maca ur d-glint ara s txeṣṣarin timeqqranin i izemren ad ḍurrent amdan, acku tuget n tmess i inetren, tella-d deg tẓegwa. Seg tama-s temmeslay-d Massa Ḥalima.Ḥ, timḍebbert n uḥareb, ɣef yimihiyen n tmes, tenna-d 121-agi n yigeṭṭaren, 48 deg-sen d tiẓegwa timeqqranen i yerɣan, 63 n yigeṭtaren deg yimukan ur nelli d tiẓegwa, yexlan seg yimezdaɣ. Terna tenna-d belli "ma nesserwes amḍan-a ɣer win n yilindi, ad t-naf yuli mliḥ aseggas-a, imi ilindi tenker tmes 13 n tikkal kan, tegla s 12 n yigeṭṭaren, ma d timental ur banent ara”. Tiɣiwanin yenneḍruran s waṭas i tḥuza tmes-a, ad naf Busfer, Msergin, Arzew d Gdeyel. Ma d aggur ideg i tzad s waṭas tmes, d aggur n yulyu, imi tessaweḍ tečča 107 n yigeṭṭaren. Annect-a, yeǧǧa tanmehla-a ad d-tger tiɣri i uḥader, akken ad qqiment tẓegwa cebḥent, ur reqqen ara yisekla ladɣa wid ur d-nettuɣal ara seld timerɣiwt-nsen.
Ɣef leḥsab n yiqeddacen n Uḥuddu aɣarim, tendeh tmes deg semmus n yimukan yemgeraden di twilayt n Bgayet. Ar tura mazal ur d-tban tmentilt n undah-a, lameεna ssegran-d axeṣṣar deg yimeḍqan-a, ladɣa arɣay n ttjur d yimɣan.
Ula d Taɣiwant n Melbu ur teslik ara seg uxeṣṣaṛ-a, imi rɣant deg-s ugar n 8 000 m2 ɣef 22:-Imezdaɣ n tɣiwant-a s umata, irekb-iten zzεaf d ameqqṛan, acku ur ẓṛin ara d anwa i deffir n temsalt-a, i yellan d tementilt n uṛɣu n teẓgi tacebḥant i d-yezzin i tɣiwant n Melbu. Gar-asen aselway, d yimeltaɣen n tddukkla Awal Yessawal, i yesnemmren iqeddacen n Uḥuddu aɣarim ɣef ufus n tallelt i asen-fkan i yimezdaɣ n temnaḍt-a, armi ṣṣawḍen ssensen times-a uqbel ad d-teglu s temḍerrit-nniḍen.
Seg tama tayeḍ, deg temnaḍt n Tizi Ḥmed, deg tɣiwant n Ticci, yewweḍ ureqqas n umihi ɣer tseddart taεlayant. Tadyant teḍṛa ɣef 01:45 n tnezzayt, yerna times qrib tečča ula d ixxamen meḥsub, limer mačči d tiḥerci n yimezdaɣ, d ixeddamen n Uḥuddu aɣarim, i yessqedcen ugar n 7 n yikamyunen n ussens n tmes, acku deg yiḍ-nni yeqwa mliḥ waḍu. Lameεna ɣas gan ayen ilaqen, times tessreɣ ugar n 9 n yihekṭaṛen.
Deg tdiwennit-a, yewwi-d awal Daǧud Mekhǧus ɣef tirmit-ines deg leqdic adelsan, deg tira, tamuɣli-s ɣef tsekla d temsal-nniḍen.
Amek i d-tufiḍ iman-ik deg uḥric-agi n tira?Tussa-yi-d tikti n tira, asmi i bdiɣ axeddim d anawer deg uɣerbaz. Lliɣ jemεeɣ-d timucuha n zik-nni sɣur temɣarin d yimɣaren n taddart. Skelseɣ-tent deg tesfifin n zik, umebεed ttaruɣ-tent ɣef lkaɣeḍ, akken armi i d-jemεeɣ aṭas n tmucuha. D acu kan imiren, ruḥeɣ unageɣ ɣer Lezzayer ɣer, sbiṭer n Dwira, acku nekk rɣiɣ asmi lliɣ d amecṭuḥ. Rɣiɣ asmi sɛiɣ 8 n wagguren di leεmer-iw. Rɣiɣ, nekk mazal-iyi la ttmurudeɣ deg waguns. Baba, fell-as as-yeεfu, ur yezmir ara ad i yi-idawi di tallit-nni, acku aṭas n yigerdan i yesεa. Ad yawi aɣrum neɣ ad yi-idawi d. Acu, yexdem ayen yellan fell-as: yewwi-yi ɣer Ɛennaba anda i llan Icenwiten. D sbiṭer n tlemmast n Ɛennba, anda i qqimeɣ dinna aṭas n yiseggasen. Mi akken i d-uɣaleɣ, ufiɣ-d tisfifin-nni yakk rɣant, mugent d iɣed deg wakal. Acḥal i ttruɣ fell-asent, iɣaḍ-iyi lḥal … Syin, lemdeɣ-d aṭas ɣef teskla taqbaylit. Yal yal mi ara d-xelseɣ, ad d-ddmeɣ kra n usurdi, ad d-aɣeɣ yis-sen idlisen, am tesɣunin Asalu, abc, atg. Ttaɣeɣ-d ayen yeεnan yakk tamaziɣt. Akken i d-xelqen HCA, ttawin-iyi-d yimeddukal-iw idlisen i d-yeffɣen syin. Acḥal ferḥeɣ s yimeddukkal-iw, yal yiwen deg-sen deg mi ara iruḥ ad yinig ɣer Lezzayer, ad d-yeglu s yidlisen-inekk, acku ẓran belli nekk ḥemmleɣ aṭas ad ɣreɣ idlisen n tmaziɣt. D acu ula ad nekk, yal mi ara ɣreɣ adlis, ad t-muddeɣ i wayeḍ. Lḥaṣun, imir-nni ula d nekk εemdeɣ-t, bɣiɣ medden yakk ad issinen tutlayt-nsen tamaziɣt.
Ma yella wamek ad aɣ-d-tefkeḍ agzul ɣef wayen txeddmeḍ neɣ ɣef wayen tetturuḍ…Uriɣ ungal Ussan n Tayri deg Fransa. Deg tallit-nni, lliɣ d aεeggal n tddukkla n tmerrit n tɣiwant Ulgrej amaray amatu, yerna xedmeɣ d anawer deg uɣerbaz. Nexdem d waṭas n tddukkliwin i yellan deg tmurt-nneɣ , ama d tiddukkla n tiklat Leqser n Bgayet, tiddukkla n Itri n Uqbu, tin n Timimun n adrar, SDH Wehran neɣ tin n later n Bgayet. Lḥaṣun aṭas i neqdec i nexden yid-sen, syin neqdec d yiwwet n tddukkla n tmurt n fransa qqaren-as Abbẓ Pierre d tayeḍ, qqaren-as Gẓnẓratiǧn 2010 n fransa diɣ. Imiren, nesεa yiwen uselway n tɣiwant-nneɣ , iḥemmel axeddim yid-nneɣ , akk d tddukkliwin i yellan. Akken akken armi i d-nebna 18 yixxamen i yimeεḍar d yiẓawaliyen, nerna-d Auberge i yilemẓiyin akked yimukan anda tturaren warrac imecṭaḥ d waṭas n tɣawsiwin-nniḍen. Neεreḍ, ad nreqqeε ixxamen n zik n leqbayel deg tudrin n tɣiwant. Lḥasun, nniɣ-ak-d aṭas n leqdic i nexdem ladɣa leqdicat n tddukkliwin-ayi n berra ddaw leεnaya n uneɣlaf n daxel n Lezzayer. Akken ẓran yiεgalen-nni n tddukkla Gẓnẓratiǧn 2010 d iεeggalen n Abbẓ Pierre n Fransa leqdic-iw yelha, yerna xedmeɣ-d talilt chǧrale i yinelmaden yeqqaren deg uɣerbaz anda i xeddmeɣ, bɣan ad i yi-rren tajmilt ad i yi-awin ɣer Fransa, ad i yi-dawin, ad i yi-kksen cwami-nni n tirɣi i d-ibanen deg wudem-iw azelmaḍ d ufus-iw. Syin ruḥeɣ ɣer Fransa tikelt tamezwarut, qqimeɣ kan kra wussan. Iẓerr-iyi ṭbib ameqqran. Tikelt tis snat, qqimeɣ qrib 8 n waguren anda i d-yessicbiḥ udem-iw akked ufus-iw. Asmi i ruḥeɣ ɣer din i tikelt tis snat, cfiɣ ass amezwaru i kecmeɣ ɣer sbiṭer, iḍ-nni amezwaru i bdiɣ ttaruɣ ungal-iw amenzu, tusa-yi-d tikti. Yerna akken i d-ffɣeɣ syin, kra n wussan, tettawi-yi-d tddukkla La Gẓnẓratiǧn 2010 imussnawen, imura d inaẓuren ɣer tddukkli, dinna i d-lemdeɣ amek ara aruɣ ungal akken iwata. Ttasent-iyi-d tektiwin n tira, uriɣ qrib 3 wungalen. Yerna ttruḥuɣ ɣer ACB anda i d-ufiɣ aṭas n tɣawsiwin ayen yeεnnan iɣriben d inaẓur-nneɣ . Rniɣ-d tamussni n tira tamεemmrit.
Amek liḥala n tmaziɣt deg lwilaya n Sṭif?Deg lawilaya n ṣṭif, la tetteddu tmaziɣt ɣas ulamma am yifker. D acu, qqaren-tt warrac deg lakul amenzu akked uɣerbaz alemmas.
D acu twalaḍ deg tsekla tamaziɣt s umata?D acu ulac imeɣriyen aṭas. Mmalen ɣer tutlayt-nniḍen am taεrabt. Dɣa aṭas i yi-d-yesteqsan ɣef wacu  ɣer ur ttaruɣ ara s taεrabt. Nekk, qqareɣ-asen yal ass nekk ttaruɣ taqbaylit axaṭer d aqbayli. Taεrabt, tesεa imawlan-is nekk imawlan-iw d taqbaylit d tamaziɣt s umata. Tasekla n tmaziɣt ɣas akken la tleḥḥu, d acu kan ilaq ad tili tkadimit i wakken ad teddukkel s yiwwet n tira. Tira-s s tlaṭinit i wakken ad teddu ɣer sdat. Ilaq ad tesεu imeɣriyen yal yiwen ilaq ad yesεu adlis n tmaziɣt deg uxxam-is ass-a, azekka ad t-ddmen warraw-is, ad t-ɣren.
Kra n yisenfaren-ik sya d afella…Isenfaren-iw, sin wungalen yiwen yekfa ad yeffeɣ deg wagguren i d-iteddun, azwel-ines Tawenza Umesbrid. Ma yella d wayeḍ, qrib ad yekfu azwel-ines Tizwal Uɣerbas. Rnu sεiɣ ammud n yisefra, yekfa azwel-ines Amsedrar. Aql-i leḥḥuɣ ɣas nekk d aawali, yerna d amuḍin ɣef tmaziɣt. Kkateɣ ad rnuɣ, ad neǧǧreɣ abrid ɣer sdat. Ɣas nufa-d isennanen, d acu tella tebɣest, tmeɣnest d leḥmala n uẓar -nneɣ i wakken tutlayt ur tettmettat ara sya ɣer sdat.Yesteqsa-t Hǧcine Mǧula
I lmend n wass aɣelnaw n yimeɣraṣ, thegga-d tesnawit n Maεuc Idris n Lbeṛǧ Mira, ass n, 18 fuṛar yezrin, yiwet n temsizzelt s wazal-is. Taneggarut-a, tella d tagnit i wakken ad walin yinelmaden n uswir aneggaru i yettheggin aswir-nsen, ladɣa imi ur d-yeggri ara waṭaṣ i ukayad n taggara n useggas. Am wakken i tella daɣen d ttiεad i d-yessemlalen inelmaden d yiselmaden n ukuẓet n tnawiyin. Rnu i tin n umeɣṛaṣ Maεuc Idris, tettekka tesnawit n umeɣṛaṣ Xaled Mesεud, n Yiderginen, d tin n umeɣṛaṣ Ɛebban Ṛemḍan n Melbu akked tinna n umeɣṛaṣ Ḥusin At Ḥmed n At Smaεel.
Seld awal n unemhal n tsenawit n Lbeṛǧ Mira i yessṛeḥben s yinebgawen-is d wawal n kra n yimasayen n tesnawiyin-nniḍen, εeddan srid ɣer ttiεad n temsizzelt. Ad d-nesmekti d akken timsizzelt-a, tella-d deg sin n yiḥricen. Tamezwarut, d temsizzelt taggagt, tis snat d tin n usuneɣ. Di tmezwarut dɣa, ama d tinegwa tiseklanin neɣ d tid icudden ɣer tussna, llant akk di ttiεad. I yisalli d tasnawit n Lberǧ Mira i d-yusan deg umḍiq amezwaru, s 63 n tenqiḍin. Ayen yeṣṣefṛaḥen ugar d tanqiḍt n Tmaziɣt, imi wwin-d 10/-Teḍfer-itt-id tasnawit n Yiderginen, i d-yusan deg umḍiq wis sin. Ma yella d Tasnawit n At Smaεel, teṭṭef amḍiq aneggaru s 36 n tenqiḍin kan. Agemmuḍ-a, yessewhem inelmaden d yiselmaden n At Smaεel s umata. Γef usentel-a dɣa yenna-aɣ-d yiwen n uselmad: « sḥasfeɣ nezzeh, acku aswir n warrac-nneɣ n zik, yemgarad ɣef win n warrac n tallit-a. Ilaq ad ḥṣun yimawlan belli ula d nutni uraren nnuba tameqqṛant deg waya, imi bran i yifassen-nsen deg wayen yeεnan leqṛaya n warraw-nsen. Nessaram s tidet, ad tbeddel tegnit deg tesnawit n Ḥusin At Ḥmed ".
Ma yella deg temsizzelt n usuneɣ, d anelmad Xaled Xaled, seg tesnawit n Yiderginen, i d-yezgan deg umḍiq amezwaru. Seg tama-nniḍen, ddeqs n leqdicat idelsanen i d-yellan di ttiεad. Ama d ticeqqufin n umezgun, neɣ d tignatin n ccna. Ula d tufsirin n tewlafin n yimeɣṛasen akked yidlisin n umezruy, sεan amur-nsen di temlilt-a. Aredmani, ulac win i d-yeffɣen seg ttiεad-a, mebla ma yerna-d cwit n tmussni i wallaɣ-is. Mebla ma nettu, ula d Imjuhad n temnaḍt-a, εerḍen-ten-id ɣer temlilt-a i wakken ad d-mudden tanaga-nsen ɣef umezruy n temnaḍt-nsen di tegrawla. Γer taggara, fkan arrazen i wid i d-yufraren d tnagiwin n usnemmer i wid ittekkan. K. K.
Macahu, tellemcahu ad tt-yeḍbeε Ṛebbi d asaru. Qqarren zzman, yella yiwen n umdan d amesbaṭli acku d bab n draε u yesεa adrim swayes yuγ akk imdanen. Uuγalen s ddaw n ufus-is. Ihi, ṛṛay d ṛṛay-is γas γer yiγzer awal d awal-is,γas ma yexser. Win ad d-yekkin mgal ines, ad as-iceyyeε iḍan-is, ad sεeddin fell-as lbaṭel. Yiwen n umdan, yesεa tabγest d akuraji, yugi ad yuγal am wiyaḍ d axeddam-is, neγ xersum ad yessusem am umeγbun n taddart-nni yečča lḥif d tmara. Ihi, win akka, wayeḍ akka ulamma argaz akuraji ur yexdim ara kra, maca ur yekni ara i ddel, yerna at taddart yettban belli ḥemmlen-t γas ur d-sbeggnen ara ayen-nni. Si tama-s, amcum-nni ur t-yeεğib ara lḥal. Xedmen-as yiwet n tcerket i ukuraji-nni akken ad d-tesweqqɛen.
Yewweḍ γer sdat n lqaḍi, yenna-as: ’A leflani, aql-ak cetkan-d fell-ak at taddart belli la tzerεeḍ ccwal di tseqqamut, tebγiḍ ad tfarqeḍ tacemli’’. Akuraji: ’A sidi lqaḍi, nekk d amdan urğin nwiγ lexsara i yiwen, ruḥ steqsi imeγban yugten di taddart ad a k-inin’’. Lqaḍi iṣṣub-d γer taddart, yejmeε-d at taddart, la ten-yesteqsay. Seg wakken yaf-d lḥal yeggul deg-sen umcum-nni, cehden-d akken yebγa netta, yal yiwen akken i as-yemehmuh. Mi akken kfan, yenṭeq umcum nni: ’Twalaḍ a sidi lqaḍi, acu I d-qqarren?’’ Lqaḍi yaf-d lḥal yeḥdeq yessen: ’Ala, ur walaγ ara, sliγ kan’’. Amcum: ’Amek?’’ Lqaḍi: ’Sliγ i lehduṛ-nsen, maca ur walaγ ara ulawen-nsen’’. Yahia Yanes Nisma Tigrine
Lhan yinelmaden n tesdawit n tubiret ass-nni n ttlata, 15 tuber 2019, akken ad d-inin ’Ala i tefranin n 12 duǧember i d-iteddun’’, ’I rrwaḥ n yizamulen n unagraw’’. Am wakken i ṭṭalaben, diɣ, ’Asuffeɣ n yimeḥbas n rray’’. Ffyen-d yinelmaden n tesdawit Akli Muḥend Ulḥagǧ akken uɣen tannumi s umgired n tektiwin d wannayen iwraɣen, izeggaɣen d izegzawen. Dduklen-d akken ad d-inin ulac tifranin di yir tignatin yecban tigi. Ssuturen daɣen aqlaɛ n udabu seg yiẓuran imi dayen yeqqur. Ur ttun ara diɣ amennuy-nsen mgal tuddsiwin imi, ɣur-sen, tigi squcdent-d seg udabu. ’Ihi, ad ruhent akken ara iruh uẓar-nsent, akken ad teǧǧuǧeg tesdawit’’, i iwala yiwen unelmad. Ṭṭuqten yinelmaden yeddan si tesdawit armi d lwilaya akken ṭṭuqtent tektiwin-nsen. Ad nerr tamawt d akken ɣer tama n yinelmaden, lḥan kra n yimezday d imeɣnasen akken ad ffken afud i yilelliyen n tubiret. Tella-d tikli deg tegnatin igerrzen nezzeh ɣas ulamma aṭas i yelḥan deg-s s wulɣuten i yessawalen i ubeddel, tugdut d tlelli. Ṭṭerḍiqent tuyɣac n Maɛtub, Ideflawen d Uleḥlu amzun d Ǧerǧer s timmad-is i icennun.
Yeffeɣ-d udlis amaynut deg wussan-agi, d yiwen wammud n tullisin i tura Massa Rabha Aïssǧu. D afaris-is amenzu ara d-tessiẓreg, yeffeɣ-d wammud ɣer teẓrigin Achab. Ddant-d deg-s tẓat n tullisin, s yisental yemgaraden, am; A Fa, Lemri, Tameɣra, Tiziri, Timerǧiwt, Tamwarebt, Ttxil-k a mmi. Dɣa d "Timerǧiwt” i tefren d asentel ara d-yeddun ɣef teɣlaft n udlis. Daxel n udlis-a, tenǧeɛ tmarut yiwet n taluft i mazal fell-as askasi di tmetti, yal wa d tamuɣli-s ɣef wamek i tt-yettwali, tagi d tamsalt n tmeṭṭut d uzref-is i urɛad i d-nban akken ilaq di tmetti n wass-a. Ma nudef s telqayt ɣer ugbur n tullisin, ad naf lwelha n tmarut, tcudd srid ɣer maḥyaf s tewsatin-is yakk i d-iḍerrun mgal tameṭṭut. "Seg wakken tuɣal di rrif, tikwal tameṭṭut mi ara tili s tadist, ad teḥṣu tettraǧu taqcict, ɣur-s ayagi icuba nnger, acku nettat ur as-tefki ara tmeddurt azref-is, amek ara d-tɣur d yelli-s!
Ma teḥṣa am nettat ara tidir!”. Annect-a, yezga d ttbut, ladɣa di tmetti n tallit taqburt. D timsal-agi yakk i d-tessegza Massa Rabha deg tullisin-is. Iswi-s, d asiweḍ n yizen i umdan s umata, ad as-tili tameṭṭut d amdan, d rruḥ, d leqdic, d iḥulfan, d tayri, d asnulfu, d tameddurt s timmad-is. Neddem-d ammud-a i d-tsedda deg yiwet seg tullisin-is. Hat-a-n wayen i tenna "…Mi tekfa ameslay teɣli di ddker armi tencef, tafekka-s tezzizrir d tidiwin. Tuɣal tekker, tuẓa ɣer yiwen ṭṭaq d amecṭuḥ, qqaren-as ṭṭaq n uɣrib, tserreḥ s ṭṭelq n taɣect-is: – A Belwid ɛzizen, anida telliḍ? Melmi ara ak-id-iger ubrid, melmi ara tfak lɣerba fell-aɣ? Tessawel azal n tlata n yiberdan. Tessawal, allen-is cerrwent d imeṭṭi. Tuɣal tessusem, teṭṭef-d ijifer n lfuḍa-s, tesfeḍ yis-s udem-is, teffeɣ-d, tkemmel abrid-is…”. Aɣanib d tutlayt i tessemres tmarut, ttwagzan, imi ur d-tgir ara aṭas n wawalen imaynuten. Ɣef waya ara yishil i yimeɣri, am win yennumen taɣuri s tutlayt n Dda Lmulud, am wid urɛad i d-skeflen ccbaḥa n tsekla taqbaylit d yisental yemgaraden i ɣef d-ttawin yidlisen-is.Kh. A.
Yessuffeɣ-d uselmad n tmaziɣt Adel Bachǧuche, adlis-is wis sin deg wussan-a, ɣer teẓrigin Tira. Sin n wagguren kan segmi i d-yessuffeɣ "Tamudemt n tfertin n temsirin”, iḍfer-it-id gma-s s usentel "Timsirin – Iluɣma – Aseɣti n yiluɣma”. Imi ameskar d aselmad yellan deg unnar, yefren ad d-yawi s leqdic-is amaynut ɣef uselmed, akken ad yessiǧhed ugar tamkerḍit n yidlisen n uselmed, acku d annar yesran i tektabin, akken ad yennerni. Ula d imazzagen n tutlayt seg yimesnilsanen d yiselmaden n tesdawit, xeddmen-d tizrawin u ssuffuɣen-d idlisen deg taɣult-a. Adlis-a, yebḍa-t Adel ɣef kraḍ n yiḥricen igejdanen: Timsirin + iluɣma + aseɣti n yiluɣma. D adlis yerzan ahil n uswir wis sin alemmas, n tsuta tis snat. Uqbel yal tamsirt, yettili uḍris, sakin ad d-ḍefrent temsirin n yiferdisen n tutlayt, am tjerrumt, tirawalt d tseftit.
Ɣer taggara n yal tamsirt, ad naf asiteg d yiluɣma. Ineggura-a, ttwaseɣtan deg uḥric aneggaru n udlis. Yerra umeskar lwelha-s ɣer kra n yiḥricen ilan azal deg uselmed s usenfar, am tegnit n tmenna, tamsirt n tmedyezt, tagnit n useɣred akked kra n temsirin n umawal. Ma neddem-d amedya n Tegnit n tmenna, ad t-naf d aḥric s wazal-is deg uselmed atrar, irennun-d abaɣur seg waṭas n tamiwin i unelmad. Nezmer ad as-nsemmi tanfalit s timawit, yezmer ad tt-ibedd uselmad ɣef tɣawsiwin-a; tugniwin, aḍris yuran neɣ ayen yettwali yerna isell-as audiǧ ḍisuelle. Ma d tizemmar i  ɣer ara yessiweḍ, ɣef wakken i d-yedda deg udlis n Adel Bachǧuche; "Tettrebbi anelmad ɣef tmussni n tutlayt akken ad tt-yettmeslay ɣef yiles, asenfali s timawit war uguren, tettekkes leḥya ɣef unelmad ma yella ur yennum ara yettmeslay, tettrebbi-t ad yettqadar tawala-s nnuba-s deg tmeslayt”. Kh. A.
Seg zik n zik, ssuturen deg tudrin n leqbayel Anẓar yal tikkelt mi ara teẓruref lqaɛa; mi ara tuɣal tmurt d aɣurar. Tisirit-a, teqqen ɣer tedyant n ugellid n waman Anẓar akked yiwet n teqcict i yugin niqal ad t-taɣ deg tazwara. Tameṭṭut-a, tezga tesucuf deg yiwen wasif, yal mi ara d-iṣubb ugellid n waman Anẓar, ad teffer iman-is. Yiwen wass yenna-s: ’Ad d-tefkeḍ ayen bɣiɣ, neɣ ad am-kkseɣ aman’’. Tugi teqcict ccerṭ n Ugellid, dɣa yekker yebren taxatemt, din-din yeqqur wasif. Deg taggara, teqbel teqcict lebɣi n Ugellid, syin uɣalen-d waman s amekkan-nsen. Ha-tt-an s tewzel tsirit-a. Seg yimir, ssuturen Anẓar yal tikkelt mi ara teqqar lqaɛa, meḥsub ur d-yewwit ara ugeffur deg lawan-is. Ddurt-a dɣa, yella-d usuter neɣ lxedma n Unẓar deg waṭas n tudrin n leqbayel.
Nnejmaɛent temɣarin, fkant ttiɛad i usiher-a. Mi d-yewweḍ wass-nni, cebbḥent i uɣenǧa, rrant-t am wakken d tislit ara fkent d tarzeft i Ugellid n waman Anẓar anda ara ssutrent tiririt n tunṭict-a, meḥsub ad d-iserreḥ i waman ageffur. Ad ttɛeddayent axxxam axxam, ad d-jemɛent isufar n tgella i wakken ad xedment azekka-nni imensi n Unẓar. Timɣarin-a, ttawint arrac imecṭaḥ i yettɣennin yid-sent, ssuturen ageffur deg Ugellid n waman Anẓar. Ɣef wakken i aɣ-d-nnant temɣarin-a, ttawint igerdan axater d nutni i yesɛan nneyya, ad ten-iqader Unẓar u ad t-ɣiḍen imi meẓẓiyit, dɣa ad asen-yeddu deg lebɣi, ad d-yewwet ugeffur. Ladɣa imi timɣarin-nni kkaten igerdan-agi s uẓegduf, yiwen n yimɣi i iteqqsen mliḥ, syin ad ttrun warrac mi ara yennal yimɣi-agi taglimt-nsen. Akka, ara d-tettru tegnawt fell-asen, ɣef leḥsab n tsirit.
Ma d asuter n Unẓar, yettili-d s usefru-a deg waṭas n temnaḍin: ’Anẓar, anẓar, A Rebbi, sseww-itt ar aẓar. Ad teww nneɛma n udrar, Ad ternu tin n uzaɣar. Axenǧa, yetteqliliḥ, Nnig n uxxam Uqiliḥ, A Rebbi, seww-itt-id Mliḥ’’. Akken yebɣu yili lḥal, awi-d ukan ad yili ugeffur, ladɣa ma neẓra d akken tettekk-d tidet seg yimi n ugrud. Akka, dɣa, i deɛɛunt temɣarin ’A Rebbi, ur aɣ-ttqassa ara ɣef wudem n llufan’’. Tisirit, d tisirit, akka ay tga, yerna d tigejdit n yal idles, xas ur tt-numin ara. Hǧcine Mǧula
Macahu tellemcahu ad tt-yeḍbeε Ṛebbi d asaru. Yiwen wass iεedda-d umqerqur, tenṭeq ɣur-s tɣirdemt tenna-as: " A timjellebt”. Terra-as-d: "Acu a tiɣirdemt?”.Tenna-as: " La t-ttwaliḍ asif iḥemel, nekk ilaq ad zeggreɣ ɣer tama-nniḍen. Tura ma ulac uɣilif, ad i yi-tzeggreḍ”. Ulac uɣilif, d acu kan ugadeɣ ad i yi-teqseḍ.
Annaɣ a timjellebt, ma qqseɣ-kem, ad temteḍ, uma temmuteḍ, ad d-tɣerqeḍ deg wasif, ma tɣerqeḍ ddiɣ yid-m. Ihi, ɣas ur ttagaḍ. Ulac win ara ihudden axxam i deg yella, ulac win ara yessegrirben ṭumubil deg i yedda. Twala temjellebt d tidet, dɣa tenna-as: " Ihi, ali-d ɣef waεrur-iw ad kem-zeggreɣ”. Tuli tɣirdemt, terkeb, teqlaε temjellebt, truḥ qbala ɣer tama-nniḍen, akken kan wwḍen ɣer ttnaṣif, teqqes tɣirdemt timejɛebt. Taneggarut-a, tenna-as: "Annaɣ a tiɣerdemt”. Terra-as-d tɣirdemt: " Akka a timjellebt”.
I tura a tiɣirdemt, uqbel ad mmteɣ yerna ad tedduḍ ula d kemm, sfehmi-y-id amek? Yahia Yanes
A timjellebt, nekk yexleq-iyi-d Ṛebbi ad qqseɣ, ad qqseɣ ɣas azal d ṛruḥ-iw.
Seg yisental i ɣef ttmeslayen yimdanen ussan-a, imi d ayen i ten-iceɣben, d ssuma n tfakturin n trisiti i yulin nezzeh. Ladɣa, deg ukṛadyur-a aneggaru. Ayen i ten-yeǧǧan wehmen ugar, amek armi d tura i teεlay ssuma n lexlas, di lawan anda ur seddayen ara medden trisiti s waṭas. Rnu i waya, tamsalt-a, tusa-d deg wakud anda i d-yennulfa waṭṭan n Kuṛunu, dɣa ula d ssumma n uttitṛul tuder-d. Γef leḥsab n udiwenni i d-newwi akked kra deg-sen, qqaṛen-d belli d imḍebbṛen n SǦNELGAZ i d ssebba n waya. Ayagi imi, ttεeṭṭilen ugar n ukradyur i wakken ad ceyyεen i medden tifakturin-nsen. Yerna tamsalt-a, d ayen i ten-isuεden s tidet, acku imir-n, yettekcam umsuder cǧnsǧmmateur deg uḥric wiss kṛad, neɣ deg win n ukuẓ n lexlaṣ. Ɣef usentel-a, yenna-aɣ-d yiwen: «Mačči d tikkelt i tɛeṭṭel tfakturt i wakken ad telḥeq, yerna imir-n d nukni i yettxelliṣen aɛeṭṭel-a.
Ayen i ɣef sḥassfeɣ ugar, llan wid ur nefhim amek i xeddmen leḥsab n ssuma n trisiti, ihi ur ẓrin belli aɛeṭṭel-a ur yelli i ubaɣuṛ-nsen". Ddeqs n tnagiwin n yimdanen i aɣ-d-iwekkden d akken s tidet yella waya, ula d tuddsa Tazzayrit n uḥuddu ɣef umsuder, deg usebter-is, temmeslay-d ɣef uɣbel-a. Ad d-nesmekti d akken, yella-d umeslay daɣen, belli rnan ula i tẓeṭṭaṭ taxe ɣef tnezduɣt, imi tuli seg 150 n yidinaṛen, armi d 600 n yidinaṛen. Ayagi, mebla aṣexbeṛ n medden. Ula d ineggura-a seg tama-nsen, ssuturen sɣur yimasayen di Sǧnelgaz, ad d-seggzin taluft-a n ubeddel, d tmentilt-is.K. K.
Tineggura-a, anida tezzi tiṭ-ik ama deg yiberdan neɣ deg yimukan-nniḍen, ala tiqerɛatin d tebwaḍin n uttlastik ara d-temlileḍ. Ulac tardast deg wakal n tmurt, ur tḥuza ara taluft-agi n yiḍuman n uttlastik. Win iwumi tenniḍ, ad ak-yini: « Mačči d nekk ara d-iqeɛden tamurt! ". Yal wa yettara-d ṭṭlam ɣef wayeḍ; imezdaɣ qqaren-d d tiɣiwanin ur nxeddem ara axeddim-nsent, nutenti si tama-nsent, ur sawḍent ara ɣer lebɣi-nsent, yerna seḍlament imezdaɣ. Ma d tiddukliwin i iqedcen deg uḥric n twennaḍt, ula d nutenti sḥasfent ɣef liḥala n twennaḍt di tmurt, xeddment ahat nnig tezmert-nsent. Ula d asmi i yuɣalen yiḍuman d idrimen, ur cliɛen ara yimdanen, imi d tidet d idrimen-nsen i ṭeggiren mačči d iḍuman-nsen! Adaǧun Abdelghani
Mbeɛd mi d-yessawel uɣlif n twennaḍt ɣer tḥawact n yiḍuman deg wakal aɣelnaw, tettwalqeḍ-d tnecta tasmekta n 474,38 n yiṭunen yiḍuman n uttlastik. D tigawt taɣelnawt iwumi semman « Aggur War Attlastik ". Tebda, ass n 21 cutember yezrin, ad tkemmel alamma d ass-a n, 21 tuber -Ad d-yili uḍfar n tigawt-a taɣelnawt, sɣur teseqqamut n uḍfar d uktazel, yetabaɛen ɣer uɣlif n twennaḍt. Am wakken, i ssawḍen ad d-suddsen azal n 69 n yisaragen d yimyaggren deg yakk timnaḍin n tmurt, i usefhem i medden ɣef wazal d wamek ilaq ɣef umdan ad iseḥbiber ɣef ugama d twennaḍt. Rnu ɣer wahil uzzig i d-yellan i yigerdan inelmaden n uɣerbaz, ɣef teɣzi n 3 ssmanat n tigawt-agi. Yella-d deg-s uttekki n tmetti taɣarimt ur yesɛin tamtilt, ama d tiddukkliwin tisadarin ttrǧfessiǧnnelles, ama d tid n twennaḍt d yilemẓiyen, ama d tigrawin n yiskutiyen, ama d imezrawen isdawanen, tiseqquma n tuddar neɣ n yimḍqan, iɣerbazen d udmawen n tmetti yettwassnen ɣer yidis n yiduba idiganen d yiɣsuren n ufran d wallus n usseqdec n wafrasen.I lmend n waya, daɣ deg lwilaya n Ǧiǧel d Ɛennaba, nulfan-d kra n tkebbaniyin i lmend n ulqaḍ n yiḍuman n uttlastik, ara d-ixelqen ama d imekwan n uxeddim, ama d asizdeg n twennaḍt. Am wakken daɣen i d-heggan ticemliyin n uqɛad n kra n yimukan deg kra n lwilayat n unẓul n tmurt i wakken ad d-yili wallus n useqdec n wafrasen n uttlastik, yernu iger-d uɣlif n twennaḍt tiɣri i yimdanen terza temsalt akken ad sseftin deg uḥric-agi i d-isekcamen idrimen.
Segmi yettwabna Umezgun n tzegzewt deg taddart n Ayt Ɛisa, taɣiwant n Uweqqas, ayendin d armuden i n-yettwaheggan s uɛraḍ n waṭas n yinaẓuren yemgaraden, ama d tirebbuyaɛ n umezgun, d icennayen, d imsaragen neɣ d imalasen. Ussan-a dɣa, yendeh deg ubraḥ warmud adelsan, ladɣa asenɛet n tceqqufin n umezgumm seg tmeddit d asawen. Ihi, i lmend n teẓrigt tis semmus n wuḍan n umezgun n Ayt Ɛisa, thegga-d tddukkla tadigant armud ideg i d-ttwasneɛtent ddeqs n tceqqufin deg yiḍ, mi d-rrant i tiɣri n tddukkla « Tadukkli " trebbuɛay yemgaraden n twilayt n Bgayet. Ama d tarbaɛt n Ticci n Mass Sɛidi, neɣ d tin iwumi ssawalen Ifeṭṭiwjen n temnaḍt n Tmeẓrit.
Daɣen, ula d acennay Lwennas Tagrawla, yewwi-d ass-nni kra n ccnawi berra i ubeḥri. Kra n wussan ɣer sdat, tettwahegga-d rreḥba n ccna sɣur unaẓur Azal Belqadi, seld winna n Tyaqut, Lwennas Gerruj d Arezqi Yaɛla. Imir-nni, nezmer ad d-nini ala tizlit taɣerfant i d-yettwawin i uzayez. Ddurt yezrin daɣen, muggen deg umezgun n Buṭeɣwa sin n yiḥuna ateliers s tallelt n kra n tddukkliwin n Bgayet. D ayen i yeǧǧan ad yili umalas Fares Idir d inebgi n yiḍ-nni, ideg i d-yessawel timucuha i warrac. Ayendin d annecraḥ i yezmer ad yettwaɛqel deg wudmawen n yigerdan di teswiɛin-nni. Yewwi-d ad d-nesmekti d akken yella-d lebni n umezgun-a azegzaw s tedrimt d ufus n yiɣermanen kan. D isenfaren am wi i yelha ad nettwali di Tmurt n Yiqbayliyen.
Iɣil Ɛli d yiwet n temnaḍt anda ṭṭuqten mliḥ yiḥerqan n uzemmur, ladɣa imi lqiεan-nsen kkawen, mačči d wid isellḥen i tuẓẓut n ddeqs n tidal, d yigumma. D ayen i yeǧǧan imezdaɣ n temnaḍt n At Ɛebbas s umata, rran-tt i tuẓẓut n yileqqamen n uzemmur. Imi ineggura-a, ttwinniεen deg lqiqan-nsen akken ilaq, yerna ula d lɣella tettili s buhan. Aseggas-a dɣa, yugar wid iεeddan, acku urwent tzemrin d yileqqamen armi celxen. Rnu i waya, ula d lɣella n useggas-a tufrar, meḥsub yiwen n uqenṭaṛ yerra-d armi d 26 n llitrat.
Ula d wid yesεan s buhan, ṣṣawḍen senzen-t d iεeqqayen. Ad d-nesmekti d akken, kilu n llḥeb n uzemmur, yelḥeq armi d 80 n yidinaṛen aseggas-a. S unamek-nniḍen, tuli ssuma-s cwit ma yella nmuqel ɣer useggas yezrin, anda i yenza s 70 n yidinaṛen i kilu. Ma yella seg tama n zzit, d anemgal. Meḥsub tuder-d ssuma-s mliḥ tikkelt-agi. Aṛiḍa, deg kra n temnaḍin yettnuzu s 500 n yidinaṛen kan i litra, ma yella deg tiyaḍ, 600 neɣ 700 n yidinaṛen i litra. Aredmani, yettuṛaǧu ad d-yader deg ussan i d-iteddun,ɣef leḥsab n wid yesεan tarmit deg unnar.
Γef usentel-a newwi-d ameslay akked Dda Ɛetman, d yiwen n ufellaḥ i d-yeggaren aɣrum-is seg lbiε n zzit uzemmur. Dda Ɛetman, iteṭṭef-d iεemmalen n uzemmur, ileqqeḍ-iten. Ayagi, i wakken ad yessenz zzit-nni, ad iεeyyec s yidrimen-is tawacult-is. Dɣa yenna-aɣ-d: « Nekni deg tmurt-nneɣ , ur tettali ara nezzeh ssuma n zzit, acku meḥsub ulac axxam ur neksib ddeqs-is. Aseggas-a dɣa, ad neḥmed rebbi, tella mliḥ lɣella. Ihi sεan akk medden, armi sseggran nnig n wayen i yeḥwaǧen, ihi sennzen-t.
Imi yeṭṭuqet zzit di leswaq, tuder-d ssuma-s. Meεna seg tama-nneɣ nekni s yifellaḥen, mačči dayen yeffɣen fell-aɣ". Ikemmel deg wawal-is: « Amek akka segmi ara d-yali wass nekni d axeddim. Nqubel aṣemmiḍ, nerna leεtab n uleqqaḍ. Lameεna nesnuzu-t s 500 n yidinaṛen? Lameεna limer i d-tusa tmurt d tin iweqqmen, ilaq ur nettaf ara iεewwiqen am wigi. Ula d lbiε, ur nettaf ara iwumi ad t-nesenz ".
Taddart n Wizran am tuddar akk n tmurt n Leqbayel, d yiwet n taddart tameqqrant. Akken i d-ḥkan yimɣaren n taddart-a, semman-as «Wizran", d yiwen n umdan iwumi qqaren Aεednan akked d umeddakkel-is, leḥḥun leḥḥun deg teẓgi armi i d-ssawḍen ɣer umkan-a n Wizran, yenṭeq Uεednan yenna i umeddakkel-is: «Wissen isem-is umḍiq-a ideg nella!" Yerra-as urfiq-is: «Wi yeẓran!" Seg wass-nni yeqqim akka yisem n taddart d Wizran. Llan, wid i d-yennan semman-as Wizran imi imezdaɣ-is imezwura, d At n tebɣest am yihran  izmawen .
Am wakken yella yiwen n unnar ideg tturaren yilmeẓyen ddabex n uḍar. Degt lemmast n taddart, ad naf yiwet n lqahwa akked sebεa n tḥuna. Iseggasen-a ineggura, slulen-kra n yilmeẓyen yeɣran yiwet n tddukkla iwumi semman: Itri n tlelli, d yiwet n tuddsai iqeddcen aṭas ɣef wansayen n lejdud-nneɣ , am wakken daɣen tettεawan imezdaɣ n taddart deg yal tagnit. Wizran, d yiwet n taddart yeččuren d tiliwa yecban Tala n Melyu, Ajejḍar…atg. Mmalen yimezdaɣ-is s waṭas ɣer tfellaḥat: ulac win ur neksib tazemmurt, ama deg yiḥerqan neɣ tama n uxxam-is.
Mucaεet taddart n Wizran, deg umezruy, s 86 n yimeɣrasen i yeɣlin d asfel deg lgirra n 1954 mgal acengu afransis, meḍlen deg tmeqbert n ccuhada daxel n taddart-a. GM. Aḍris-a, uran-t-id yinelmaden n useggas wis sin, aɣerbaz alemmas 11 yimeɣrasen Tiɣilt Buceqfa. Aseggas aɣurbiz 2019 / -Ismawen n yinelmaden, Ğεefri Tilelli, Ɛisani Tafat, Twati Cahra, Bensaleḥ Ḥusam.Adel Bachǧuche
Ayen yelhan deg temsalt n tmaziɣt deg uɣerbaz, d tarmit-a i d-negmer. Amecwar i d-nedda di tttidagujit yelha. Simmal nsuruf, simmal ttbanen-d wuguren n tidet i ɣef ilaq ad nadin yimassanen, yal yiwen deg taɣult-is. Yegget umahil. Llant kra n temsal tigejdanin, rzant arraten n ulmud d tarrayin n uselmed: Iselmaden mazal εad i sεin adlis n tjerrumt taɣurbizt. Ihallen n uselmed, bdan ṣeffun, tebda tzerri deg-sen tafat, maca mazal deg-sen afras d telqim. Yezmer ad beddlen seg uẓar ma tella tmuɣli talqayant ara d-yemlen iberdan iwulmen, ama i uselmed n tutlayt n tyemmat, ama i tutlayt tis-snat. Idlisen diɣen, ttbeddilen i lmend n yihallen. Tura, tarmit temla-aɣ-d acḥal i texser tarrayt-nni n usemnenni n waṭas n yilsawen deg yiwen udlis am winna n uswir wis-4 alemmas. Taluft n tarrayin n uselmed, ula d nutenti d taluft meqqren. Tebda tṣeffu deg wallaɣen, maca mazal amahil fell-as. Ilaq ad yekfu uṭebbeε, ad nekcem deg tallit n uselmed n tidet. Yessefk, yal yiwen iqeddcen deg unnar, ad yeqbel ad yekcem deg usileɣ imezgi akken ad yezmer ad yes  ɣer tamaziɣt s ubrid ussnan i yeddan d yimir-a.Yesteqsa-ten Hǧcine Mǧula
Yemgarad wamek ara d-yili umager d usfugel n yennayer n useggas-a. Deg yixxamen, tiddukkliwin tidelsanin, tizeɣwa n ccna, iɣerbazen…atg. Lḥasun ad yili s lferḥ n yimdanen, imi d ass n lfal amerbuḥ i d-igellun s usfillet yelhan d lxir d lbaraka. Ɣef waya, yessuddes-d Umaris aɣelnaw n yidles d wulɣu, i lmend n umager n yennayer 2969, yiwet n tuzzya n tẓuri n ccna d uẓawan n terbaɛt tamaḍlant Tinariwin deg tlata n twilayin meqqren n tmurt. Deg Lezzayer tamanaɣt, deg usamer u deg umalu. Tarbaɛt Tinariwin, d tin yettwassnen deg umaḍal s taɣulin n uẓawan yufraren i txeddem deg Rruk, El bluz d uẓawan amensay atergi, imi xilla n warrazen imaḍlanen i d-tḥerr yakan. Tebda tuzzya seg Sirta, deg temdint n Qsenṭina, ass-nni n amhad 3 yennayer 2019 deg tzeqqa Aḥmed Bay. Syin tkemmel azuzen deg tmanaɣt deg tzeqqa meqqren Aṭlas, ass n sed 5 yennayer -Yetturaǧu ad tessali ass-a n arim deg tmanaɣt n umalu n tmurt, deg tzeqqa n El Maɣreb deg Wehran ɣef tis 17h00 n tmeddit.
I lmed n usmekti wis 60 n tmettant n umeɣnas yellan d aɛeggal asebdad n ukabar n Yitri n Tefriqt n Uqafa daɣen d amaray Amatu n ukabar-agi, wagi d Imache Amar, tuɣal-as tejmilt meqqren, ass n Sem, 07 seg Furar 2020, deg taddart-is n At Masbaḥ i d-yezgan deg tɣiwant n At Dwala.
Imache Amar, d yiwen gar yimḥaddiyen imeqqranen n yigduden yettwaḥqren deg umaḍal, d yiwen yekkaten ɣef tmental tuɣdimin. Yebda umennuɣ-is asertan deg yiseggasen 1920, armi d amennuɣ amrig deg waggur n unbir n useggas n -Yella gar yimenza i yebdan mgal tiktiwin n temnukda d temharsiwin yemgaraden. Yugi lḥers d lbaṭel mgal igduden yellan s ddaw uɣmar n wiyaḍ. Imdanen i t-ixulḍen, ama asmi yunag ɣer Fransa neɣ asmi i d-yuɣal ɣer Tmurt, daɣen ɣef wayen uran yimussnawen n umezruy, gelmen-t-id d akken yella d argaz d wawal, i ireznen mliḥ deg lecɣal-is. Yerna yesɛa yiwet n tmuɣli wessiɛen, yettwali ladɣa ɣer sdat. Yeẓra amek ara ddunt tedyanin ɣer sdat. Amedya deg udlis i yura deg useggas n 1937 iwumi isemma " l’Algẓrie au Carrefǧur ", iwumi i d-ɛaweden diɣ warraw-is deg useggas n 2012, yehder-d ɣef waṭas n temsalt i d-yeḍran mbaɛd, ama ɣef yizerfan n warrac, izerfan n tmeṭṭut d usemguri n tmurt n Lezzayer. Dayen dɣa i ɣef i d-yuɣal mmi-s deg wawal i d-yenna deg tejmilt-agi i as-yuɣalen.
Isem-is yura deg yisebtar n umezruy s waman n wurraɣ, d awezɣiɣ ad yettwamḥu seg yixemmimen n ugdud amaziɣ, yeḥsan s tɣeṛsawt n Imache Amar, asaḍ n udrar n Ǧerǧer. Yebda umahil n umeɣnas s tlallit n ukabar n Yitri n Tefriqt n Ugafa deg useggas n 1926, deg tmurt n Fransa, syin, ḥebsen akabar-agi deg useggas n 1929, maca amennuɣ-is asartan ur yeḥbis ara. Dɣa, yuɣal-d ukabar-agi s yisem-nniḍen deg useggas 1933 i yewwin isem n ukabar n Tmanagt n Yitri n Tefriqt Ugafa. Deg waggur n unbir, seg useggas n 1934, i tikkelt-nniḍen yettwaḥbes ukabar n Tmanagt n Yitri n Tefriqt Ugafa, yerna wwin tuget n yimḍebbren n ukabar-agi ɣer lḥebs, anda ḥekmen fell-asen s sḍis n wagguren n lḥebs d 2 000 n Francs n lxeṭya i yal yiwen seg yimḍebbren n ukabar-agi. Deg waggur n maggu 1935, yeffeɣ-d seg lḥebs, Imache Amar, yuɣal srid ɣef uqerru n Ukabar i iqeddcen s tuffra kan. Deg udlis n Imache Chabane, yeɣal-d s wawal ɣef yiɣeblan yezgan gar baba-s d Messali Lhadj, ur yebɣin ara ayen yexddem, ladɣa ad d-yili ɣef uqerru n Ukabar, ayen iwumi semman mbaɛd « le zaɛimizm ".
Seg yisental i ɣef ttmeslayen medden ussan-a, d liḥala n tegnawt i iqessḥen nezzeh, armi tugi ad tebru i yimeṭṭawen-is. D tidet ur teqqim tegnawt teεdel akken i tella zik, imi deg tallit-a, tamurt ur teksib ara 4 n tsemhuyin saisǧns . Lameεna, ayen ideg nella aseggas-a, yugar wid yezrin. Meḥsub deg yiseggasen iεeddan, deg wayyur n fuṛaṛ, tekkat-d lehwa. Rnu i waya tifesniwin n lḥamu deg-s, εedlent. Ma yella d aseggas-a, tifesniwin tiεlayanin, lehqent armi d 26 deg twilayin n ugafa n tmurt, ad as-yini yiwen deg unebdu i nella. Ahat ula d ayen i iḍeṛṛun deg tallunt  esttace , am uxemmuj aberkan, d tamentilt n ubeddel n unezwi climat . Γas ma yella mgaradent tmentilin ɣef leḥsab n tmuɣliwin n medden, dɣa wa yeqqar texṣeṛ liḥala n lqaεa. Wayeḍ yeqqaṛ d Bab n Yigenwan i yerfan ɣef medden. Wiyaḍ seg tama-nsen, nnan-d belli tamentilt n waya, d tiẓegwa n yemɣan i yerɣan uɣalent d iɣed, akked tuẓẓut n ttjuṛ ideg stehzan yimdanen.
Meεna, yella yiwen n uḥulfu i ten-yezdin, imi akken ma llan kukran imal i yettraǧun ma tkemmel akka. Aredmani, uzzlen yimezdaɣ deg tuddar ɣer tẓallit, ahat ad isel Yellu i wayen ssuturen, ad tebru tegnawt i waman-is, amedya d taɣiwant n Yiɣil Ɛli. Ma yella deg taddart n At Saci, nnejmaεen At taddart, ffɣen-d s ṛṛay, belli ad uɣalen ɣer leεwayed n lejdud-nneɣ . Ad d-ḥyun ansay n unẓaṛ. D arrac n taddart imecṭaḥ, ara yessutren i Yellu anẓaṛ. Acku nutni mazal sɛan nniya, mazal ulawen-nsen zeddig. Ahat ad d-imuqqel Ṛebbi i wudmawen-nsen, ad yebru i ugeffur. Ad d-nesmekti d akken, ula d arrac imecṭaḥ umren ayendin, dɣa d wagi tura i d ameslay-nsen. Ayagi imi, d tagnit i ucmumeḥ seg tama, seg tama-nniḍen, ad issinen yiwen seg wansayen n yimezwura-nneɣ .K. K.
Aǧuizet Kader, d yiwen gar yicennayen iqdimen, i yeffren iman-nsen acḥal d aseggas, syin yuɣal-d ɣer ccna n teqbaylit, mbeɛd 27 n yiseggasen. Deg yiseggasen n 80, i yebda amecwar-is di ccna, imir yella d ilemẓi, yessaramen ad yili d acennay. Yella yumen belli yal amdan mi ara d-ilal ad yebɣu ad d-yeffeɣ d kra: d acennay, d amejjay, d aselmad… Ula d netta akken i tt-yessarem i teffeɣ, yedder lweqt armi i d-yufa iman-is d acennay. D tizlatin n Ḥamiduc, i t-id-ijebden ɣer ccna, dɣa yuɣal yettɣenni tizlatin-is.
Ulamma yebda ccna deg yiseggasen n 1980, maca i yiman-is kan, yeqqim 27 n ssna n tsusmi. Deg useggas n 1991, yeskles tasfift-is tamenzut deg yiɛezzugen, maca ur tt-id-yessuffeɣ ara imi di tallit-nni yekukra, yerna yesɛa uguren. Syin akkin, ikemmel kan deg ccna n tmeɣriwin sya u sya. Armi d aseggas n 2018, i d-yuɣal s wudem unṣib ɣer ccna s tesfift iwumi isemma iḍelli, i d-yeffɣen ɣer tezrigin New Music n Yiɛeẓẓugen.
Amek i d-nenna ussan yezrin, llan yiɣerbazen di Xeṛṛaṭa ur uklalen ara isem n uɣerbaz, acku ur ksiben ara ula d ttawilat imecṭah i ilaqen ad d-ttuhiggin i yinelmaden iṭuṭiḥen, ladɣa taɣellist, tezdeg, d umḍiq i iwulmen i tɣuri. Imawlan n yigerdan-a, fernen ad gren dderya-nsen deg yir addad, axir ma qqimen deg yixammen-nsen, ad semḥen di tmussni. Ɣef waya i ṣebren i wayen yellan. Meεna deg yimuṛas-a, furṣen tagnit i wakken ad qeɛεden ayen i d-yewwi ad yettwaqeεεed, daymi dduklen ddeqs deg-sen deg kra n yiɣerbazen di Xeṛṛata, i wakken ad d-ssizedgen kra deg-sen. Amedya d ayen i gan deg uɣerbaz amenzu n taddart n Ṭtabya deg tɣiwant n Xeṛṛata. Dɣa, dehnen leḥyuḍ-is, berrzen tineɣriyin, yerna ssizedgen-tent i wakken ad tteklen d akken arraw-nsen deg laman ara ilin di tuɣalin-a. Seg tama-nniḍen, deg tɣiwant n Draε n Lqayed, texdem tddukkla n yibabaten n warrac akked kra n yimezdaɣ n taddart n Ṣṣnaḍla leqdic igerrzen. Qeεɛden aɣerbaz alemmas n Xennic Sliman i wakken ad t-id-afen yinelmaden d yiselmaden ihegga. Iqeddicen-a, εejben nezzeh imezdaɣ n tuddar-a, acku iswi-nsen d yiwen; ad ḍemnen tudert yelhan i unelmad, i wakken ad ssiwḍen ɣer yigemmaḍ igerrzen. Ad nekfu s wawal n yiwen n uselmad i yellan d ababat daɣen: «Nessaram leqdicat am wigi ad ttilin mkul taggara n ddurt. Imi ayen yelhan yelha, am wakken i ssarameɣ ula d iɣerbazen-nniḍen ad ḍefṛen tikti-agi".
Ur wwiḍen ara sḍis n wagguren segmi i d-yella usewseɛ n tama n wadda n umraḥ n yimrigen neɣ "Place d’arme” akken i yettwassen, d asenfar i yeččan azal n 6 n yimelyaren. Almi taggara-a uɣalen yimdanen ttcetkayen seg waṭas n lixsas i d-yellan deg umkan. Yeldi ass n umenzu n unbir 2018 yezrin, newwi-d fell-as dɣa awal deg Uɣmis n yimaziɣen, d lwali n Wehran i t-yeldin, u deg umeslay-is lawan-nni, yesseḥres akken ad yettwaḥader wadeg-a, ad yettwasizdeg akken ilaq u ad yili deg-s laman.
Annect-a merra d taɣiwant n Wehran i d-yewwi ad tt-testeklef yis-s, ma neẓra d akken d amkan i d-yezgan di tlemmast n temdint rnu yecbeḥ, d ayen ara d-ijebden ladɣa tiwaculin ad qqiment di laman. Maca, segmi yebda waggur n Remḍan, imdanen tteffɣen deg yiḍ ad kksen ɣef lxaṭer-nsen u ad ttun aẓummu d laẓ n wass kamel. Tiwaculin i ifernen amkan-a i usteɛfu, zgant d acetki seg lixsas n tafat imi tuget n llambat i as-d-yezzin, xsint yakk, rnu ɣur-s lixsas n laman imi ur nettaf ula d yiwen seg yiɣallen n laman dinna seg lxemsa n tmeddit d asawen, ladɣa tura aql-aɣ deg waggur n Remḍan, ma d imdanen yal wa anda iḥemmel ad yawi abrid-is deg yiḍ. Khaled Achǧui
Ula d tifewwaṛin-nni n waman yellan di tlemmast i d-yettaken initen icebḥen, seg waggur-nni amenzu ur d-ssuffuɣent ara aman. Dɣa asteqsi i d-yettuɣalen dima, ay  ɣer yal mi ara d-tili tullya n kra n uṣenfar i lfayda n yimdanen ur d-yettili ara uḍfar-ines akken ad yeqqim kan akken yella d amaynut? D anwa i d ssebba neɣ d anwa ur nxeddem ara ixeddim-is, d wacu i ilaqen akken ad yekfu lḥif n uḍegger n udrim deg ulac? Iban yakk d akken yal yiwen s uḥric-is n tuzzma am umasay am umdan s timmad-is. Ali Zalǧuk
Ha-tt-an dima tmurt n Lezzayer gar tmura i yeṭṭfen imeḍqan imenza deg wayen yeɛnan ibaxixen n ubrid. Ɣef leḥsab n wulɣu n Ulemmas aɣelnaw n uḥezzeb d laman deg yibardan, i d d-yefkan igemmaḍ s waccu i d-glan ibaxixen n ubrid deg useggas n 2018, ad naf azal n 3 091 n lmuta, d 30 561 n yimejraḥ deg 21 568 n yibaxixen n ubrid i yettwajerden. Ɣef wakken i d-yenna unemhal n Ulemmas aɣelnaw n uḥezzeb d laman n yibardan, Mass Ahmed n Ait El Hǧcine, i d ihedren deg umaṭṭaf n Radyu taɣelnaw, yettkemil usubbu deg umḍan n lmuta seg yibaxixen n ubrid ma neserwes d umḍan n useggas n 2016 anda llan 4 500 n lmuta. Ma deg useggas 2017, ad naf 3 600 n lmuta. Yella-d, ihi, usubbu s wazal n 8,36 % deg umḍan n lmuta. Dɣa ɣef leḥsab n yimḍebber amezwaru n Ulemmas, ugar n 90% n yibaxixen n ubrid, ssebba-nsen d imdanen, ladɣa ayen i icudden ɣer uqadar n yilugan n tenhart iwatan. Ugar 25% nniḍen, yerza zyada deg uɣiwel n yimsebriden. Deg wawal-is, yenna d akken ugar n 45% n yibaxixen, xeddmen-ten yilmẓeyen yesɛan sddaw n 29 n yiseggasen deg leɛmer-nsen, anda ara naf 23,49 %, sɛan kan turagt n tenhart ur nɛeda ara sin n yiseggasen. Ma d ayen yeɛnan ttawilat n usiweḍ meqqren d ikumya, d nutni i d-igellun s waṭas n lmuta deg yibaxixen n ubrid. Ɣef waya, dɣa, i teddem tenmehla n Ulemmas aɣelnaw n uḥezzeb d laman n yibardan, aṭas n leblanat akken ad tessiweḍ deg usenqes n twaɣiyin n yiberdan.
Tuɣal tura am wakken d lɛadda. Yal mi ara d-yaweḍ waggur n Remḍan, ad alint ssumat n yisufar n wučči. D tagnit anda ttfarasen kra n yimetjaren akken ad senzen s leswami ɣlayen. Deq leswaq, nufa mgaradent leswami n yisufar, yal yiwen s lebɣi-s: Wa yesnerna deg ssuma, wayeḍ yeǧǧa-tt akken tella. Xas ulamma tenna-d tneɣlaft n tjara d akken ssumat n lxuḍra, lfakya akked uksum ad subbent, maca deg unnar, nettwali d ayen-nniḍen i iḍerrun.
D ayen ara yeǧǧen ameɣbun, ur yettizmir ara ad d-yaɣ ula d isufar i yettuḥesben d igejdanen n tgella. Seg tama-s, tiddukkla yettḥaraben ɣef umsider, ur tessusem ara imi d-tenna deg yiwen wulɣu "ma yella win iwalan ametjar ur iquder ara ssumat i d-tefka tneɣlaft, ad aɣ-d-yessiwel akken ad d-yeccetki”. Ɣef waya, dɣa, nesteqsa kra n yimsewqen, a-t-an wayen i d-nnan: "Ulint ssumat mačči d izli, ladɣa ussan-agi imezwura. Dɣa, ttmer, ur tezmireḍ ara ad t-tennaleḍ”. Ma H. G, tkemmel yenna-d: "Mi i d-yewweḍ waggur n Remḍan, aṭas n yimdanen i itteffeɣ leɛqel, ttaɣen kulec amzun akken ad tekfu lxuḍra-agi. Ma yella wid teɛna temsalt di lwilaya, ilaq fell-asen ad d-ffɣen akken ad ɛassen wigi ixeddmen leswami akken i d asen-yehwa acku di yal tamnadt amek ara tent-tafeḍ, ur ɛdilent ara”. Ma d wayeḍ iwala d akken: "Ula d imdanen, ilaq ula d nutni ur ttaɣen ara mi ara walin kra iɛedda tilas, syin akin taɣawsa-nni, ad tṣub di ssuma, imi akka i bɣa. Ula d wid yettɛassan, ulac-iten deg unnar. Teḥsiḍ kan d anect-agi ara yilin!” Sǧuhila Yamani
Lgaz d yiwen n usafar yettselliken amdan seg tsuqas n tasmuḍi n wussan d wuḍan n ccetwa. Yettuneḥsab d allal i ssexdament twaculin deg yixxamen i umager n usemmiḍ d ugris i swayes i d-tgellu tegrest yal mi ara d-zzin wussan-is.
Ttafen-t yimdanen d amwanes, ladɣa deg wuḍan n ccetwa isemmaḍen, yesseḥmaw axxam ɣef tikkelt. Deg yiseggasen-a ineggura, aṭas n tamiwin n tmurt i mazal ur yekcim usafar-a, ssawaḍen kra n yimezdaɣ armi gezzmen iberdan, zun d tawsit n usuter i tuqqna n tnezduɣin-nsen s lgaz, i ubaɣur akk yesɛa. Maca, seg tama-nniḍen, ɣur-s lmaḍerrat, ur nenekker ara belli d allal amihan, i izemren ad yessiweḍ amdan alamma d tamettant, ma ur yeḍfir ara tarrayin n usemres-ines, neɣ ur iḥuder ara. Yal aseggas, mi ara tebdu tegrest, deg wussan-is imenza, ttɣawalen yimdanen ɣer ucɛal n lgaz deg yixxamen, ula d aneggaru-a seg tama-s, yettɣawal ɣer uḥwaṣ n terwiḥin i yestehzayen deg useqdec-is tikwal. Yessegray-d s twuɣa. Ɣef waya, tettheggi-d Tenmehla n Sǧnelgaz n Lezzayer tamanaɣt tama n Guẓ de Cǧnstantine, tuffɣiwin n yiqeddacen-is ɣer yiɣerbazen, akken ad ssegzi u ad fken iwellihen ɣef wamek ilaq ad ḥadren iman-nsen yinelmaden seg tamiwin-nsen, ad ssiwḍen isallen-a i twaculin-nsen.
Tuɣal-d tddukkla tadelsant "Itri Uzekka” n taddart n Yixelwiyen di tɣiwant n At Ɛissa Mimun, ɣer leqdic adelsan mbeɛd mi gersen leqdicat-is i kra n wagguren. Ussan-agi ineggura, gren-d tikti d tamaynut, yeffɣen i wahil-nsen adelsan n useggas, gar tejmilin, timsizzliyin, tifugliwin…atg. Ulamma, aẓar n tikti yuɣ amkan gar yiswiyen n tddukkla-a, maca armi d tikkelt-agi i ssawḍen ad tt-ṛessin deg unnar. Dɣa, i lmend n ukraḍyur wis ukkuẓ n useggas-agi n 2019, thegga-d tddukkla-a ahil meqqren n usileɣ n yiɛeggalen n umussu aduklan.
Yetturaǧu ad d-ilint temliliyin-agi n usileɣ deg rebɛa n taɣulin yemxalafen, gar tuber, unbir akked duǧember. Asileɣ amenzu, ara d-yilin ɣef usbeddi n usenfar aduklan, ad d-yili ussan n 04 d 05 deg waggur-a n tuber i d-teddun. D aduktur Cennan Areẓqi, aselmad n tesdawit n Tizi Uzzu, ara d-yilin ɣef lmendad n usileɣ-agi n yiɛeggalen n waṭas n tddukkliwin tidelsanin. D netta diɣ, ara yilin d imsileɣ n usileɣ wis sin, ara d-yilin ɣef useḥbiber ɣef twennaḍt. Asileɣ-agi n sin wussan 14 d 15 unbir 2019, ad yezzi wawal deg-s ɣef usentel-agi: "Asegmi n twennaḍt, i lmend n unegmu idumen”, ideg ara d-yefk Mass Cennan iwellihen d wamek i ilaq ad nseḥbiber ɣef ugama ideg nettidir.
Mi yessuli usileɣ-agi, yetturaǧu ad tili tuffɣa s annar, ara d-yilin ɣer tkebbanit n usefreg n yiḍuman "Aluḍerttlast”, i d-yezgan deg Tala Ɛetman. Ma d asileɣ wis kraḍ, ad d-yili ussan n 01 d 02 duǧamber -Tikkelt-agi, ad yili usileɣ n umussu aduklan ɣef umnir n tikli deg udrar randǧnnẓes. D Mass Lewnis Tǧuati, d aɛeggal n tddukkla n twennaḍt Guraya, ara d-yilin ɣef lmendad n usileɣ-agi. Am wakken diɣ, i yetturaǧu ad d-tili tuffɣa s adrar deffir kan n usileɣ-agi, i wakken ad d-yili usnas deg unnar n wayen xedmen deg usileɣ-a n sin wussan. Asileɣ aneggaru, ad yili d asuffeɣ n tanant n tsellak timenza secǧurisme, ara yeddun ɣef tegzi n waggur. Adaǧun Abdelghani
Ad tebdu ass n 15 unbir, ad tessali ass n 15 duǧember -D Mass Ali Xeddam, imsileɣ aɣelnaw n tsellak timenza u d aselway n Waggur azeggaɣ azzayri n tama-a n At Ɛisa Mimun. D netta, ara yilin d imsileɣ n tanant-agi n secǧurisme. Ɣer taggara, ad d-nesmekti belli d axxam n yilmeẓyen Dib Ali n At Ɛisa Mimun ideg ara d-ilint temliliyin-agi n usileɣ. D tiddukkliwin tidelsanin n tɣiwant-a ɣer tama n tiyaḍ, i yetturaǧun ad sfaydint seg usileɣ-agi. Am wakken diɣen i zemren ad jerden yimdanen-nniḍen iman-nsen i wakken ad ttekkin. I wugar n yisallen ad siwlen ɣer wuṭṭun-a: 0775 98 92 -Tennulfa-d iseggasen-a ineggura yiwet n tjara tamaynut i yuɣen aẓar deg waṭas n tudrin n Tmurt n Yiqbayliyen; ta d asenzi n yiɣiɣden i d-yettaǧǧa wayen yettwaserɣen. Deg tɣiwant n Ayt Smaɛel, i yeggugen s wazal n 65 n yikilumitren ɣer usamar n Bgayet, yuɣal warmud-a iḥuza akk imdanen d yakk tiḥricin n tmetti. D aẓawali neɣ d amerkanti, d agrud neɣ d ilemẓi, d tameṭṭut neɣ d argaz, merra-nsen, gren deg-s akken ad asen-d-uɣalen yidrimen send asenzi n tneɣda-nni i wid i d-irezzun beddemma ɣer tuddar akken ad tt-aɣen. Ɣas ahat yal amdur leɛmer issemras tjara-a, maca d tilawin akked yigerdan i yezgan deg-s ɣef teɣzi n umalas.
D tilawin, acku d nutenti i yessewwayen tal taɣawsa deg ukanun n uxxam, ma d igerdan, llan rezzun beddemma ɣer teẓgi akken ad d-ḥerqen isɣaren d kra n yimɣan, am tidekt. Ma yella zik tuɣ ur sɛin azal yiɣiɣden armi teddun deg yiḍumman, ass-a deg wussan caḍen wid iẓerren deg-sen agerruj meskud ayen i asen-ggaren d adrim i wayyur yettɛawan-iten ad sgerrzen addad-nsen n tudert n yal ass. Imi tikwal,llan wid yesnuzuyen s wugar n 2 000 n yidinaren i wayyur. Ma d ssuma n yiɣiɣden-nni, tettbeddil ɣef leḥsab n tɣara-nsen. Amedya, iɣiɣden i ɣef tseɣleb tebrek, xeddmen 20 armi d 40 n yidinaren i ukilu.
Ma yella d wid yesfan, ttnuzun 60 armi d 100 n yidinaren/akilu. Mi ara d-yerzu s tkerrust-is win i ten-yettaɣen, ad tafeḍ yal amezdaɣ acu i as-yessumur d ayen akken i d-yejmeɛ. « Yelha mi nufa ɣer wanda ara nerr iɣiɣden-nneɣ , rnu s uxelles. Ddurt iɛeddan i senzeɣ kra n wayen i d-ḥewwzeɣ deg yiculliḍen s wazal n 600 n yidinaren ", i aɣ-d-tenna yiwet n tmeṭṭut seg Ayt Smaɛel.M. K.
Ass-nni n ssebt, 23 deg unbir deg-i nella, i d-yeffeɣ, dagi deg tmurt akked Fransa, walbum amaynut n ucennay ameqqran Zedek Mǧulǧud iwumi isemma Neɣ ḍelmeɣ! Mbeɛd mi tettuwexxer tuffɣa n walbum-agi i ilaqen ad d-yeffeɣ deg waggur n yulyu yezrin, ha-t-an yewweḍ-d lawan-is i waggur-a n unbir -Deg-s ad naf 14 n tezlatin i d-yettmeslayen ɣef waṭas n yisental i yuɣ tannumi ucennay aqbayi Zedek Mǧulǧud yettawi-d awal fell-asen, yecban tutlayt, tamurt, tirrugza, tayemmat, tagmat d wayen-nniḍen: meḥsub ayen yakk i icudden ɣer tmetti s umata.
Deg tezlatin n tikkelt-a, u xas ulamma Zedek yeqqim d Zedek akken i yuɣen yid-s tannumi wid i as-isellen, meɛna yella-d umaynut deg useqdec n wallalen atraren deg uẓawan-is. Yedda uẓawan s wallalen n tallit-a, ur yeqqim ara kan deg ugambar-nni-ines. Aya, yefka udem atrar i ccna-s. I wakken yessaweḍ ɣer uswir-a deg useqqɛed n tezlatin seg tama n uẓawan, yessawel i wid teɛna temsal am Allaǧua Bahlǧuli, Mǧkrane Adlani, Malik Kerrǧuche…atg.
Am wakken i d-yextar, diɣ, imẓawanen imeqqranen i yekkan deg leqdic-agi azeddgan. Seg tama n uɣanib, ad t-naf yedda deg ubrid n wayen akken i icennu yakan, xas ulamma yesnerna-as acemma deg tiwḍin-is ɣer tmeẓẓuɣt. Ahat, ad ilin wid ara as-yinin ibeddel ciṭ deg uẓawan, maca, mi ara tesleḍ i tɣessa n tezlit, ad tt-tafeḍ tennerna s tidet, acu kan ur tbeddel ara seg uẓar-is. Deg walbum-agi, nezmer ad d-nini belli yejmeɛ-d akk aɣanib n umecwa-is ɣer yiwen umekkan. "Yejmeɛ-itt-id am lḥenni”, akken qqaren. Seg tama n usefru, mazal-it yeqqaz irennu deg usekfel n wawalen iqdimen akked useqdec s tḥerci n wawalen atraren. Yeẓra amek u anda i d-yettaf awalen iqburen. Yessen amek ara ten-id-yessekfel mi ara yaf asentel i yeffɣen fell-as.
Tikkelt-a, yerza ɣer Ubrid aqdim i wakken ad t-id-yeglem u ad as-d-yesmekti ayendin n yiḥulfan n temẓi. Din i as-yeḥka tameḍrurt-is, s usḥissef, i ubrid-nni aqdim ladɣa imi i d-yemmekti tuɛciqt-is. Am wakken, diɣ, i d-yegmer kra n wawalen iqburen s usuzen deg tezlit "I mimmi”, ladɣa deg wayen yeɛnan tineqqisin-nni n zik i d-ssawalent temɣarin. Seg wayen yerzan awalen atraren, ad ten-naf keccmen-d sya ɣer da, anda kan wulmen, ladɣa deg tezlatin timḥaddiyin s umata. Seg tama n tnaṣlit akked yizamulen n trrugza ɣer yimaziɣen s umata, yefka-d agzul fell-asen deg tezlit iwumi isemma "D Yennayer”. Hǧcine Mǧula
Ula d iẓawanen n tezlit-a, mgaraden: ttaken acbih n tamiwin-nsen. Ma seg tama n tezlit tamḥaddit "A yemma yemma’’, ad naf asteqsi-a, i d-yettuɣal kan ɣef teɣzi n usefru "Acu yuɣen tamurt-iw? Acku, ɣef wakken i t-id-yenna "Tesserxas deg warraw-is”. Am wakken, daɣen, "Ssnen abrid, xḍan-as”. I wigi yakk, yerra-asen-d s tezlit "Awer timlilit”, anda i d-yenna: "Zik, nettemlili-d ɣer ṣṣaḥ, d tinna i aɣ-yesddukkulen. Nettawi-tt-id am leslaḥ, nessergagay iɛdawen. Tura, nettemlili-d ɣer ccḍeḥ, ha-tt-an din a Muḥ Uḥsen. Win ur tɣaḍ Teqbaylit, awer timlilit”. Ha-tent-in tezlatin n walbum-agi: A yemma yemma, Awer timlilit, Awi-d ukan, Am yimeslab, Winna, Dda Lḥafiḍ, Ifuk uṣerbek, Abrid aqdim, I mimmi, Ɛzizu, Aḍu-nni, Tabaḥant-iw, Ad iniɣ, D Yennayer.
Aṭas n tudrin n leqbayel i d-yeggaren Anẓar, yal tikkel mi ara tili lqaɛa yeṭṭef-itt uɣurar, ssuturen deg-s i wakken ad asen-d-yefk ageffur ad swent tfarkiwin-nsen. Yella unsay-agi si zzman n zik ɣar tmetti taqbaylit. Yettili-d s ucebbeḥen n uɣenja am teslit, ad t-fken i warrac imecṭaḥ, ad d-zzin i tzenqatin n taddart s ccna-agi: « Anẓar, Anẓar a Rebbi seww-itt ar aẓar, ad teww nneεma n udrar, ad ternu tin n uzaɣar ". Dayen i ssutren ula d imezdaɣ n taddart n At Sɛid, i d-yezgan di tɣiwant n Mizrana, dayra n Tegzirt.
Maca, nutni xtaren aya s tmamekt -nniḍen, tagi d yiwet n lweɛda i d-ǧǧan lejdud-nsen ugar n 700 n yiseggasen-aya ɣer deffir iwumi ssawalen « Nwal " i d-yettilin deg yiwen umekkan i d-yegan di tiɣilt, iwaɛan ɣer lebḥar iwumi qqaren Tawwurt n Mḥend Uḥend. Amekan-agi, yesɛa azal d ameqqṛan ɣar yimezdaɣ n taddart-agi, acku yekcem deg umezruy n tmurt n Lezzayer. Llan-d, eg-s, waṭas n yimennuɣen di tallit-nni n Ṛuman, n Ṭurk, n Fṛansa…atg.
Gar-asen win i d-yellan akked Yiṭurkiyen,deg useggas n 1 825 anda mmuten azal n 300 n yimjuhad. Taṣebḥit n wass-nni n sem, 21 furar 2020, heggant tlawin n taddart aɣṛum aquṛan, taḥbult, lexfaf akkedtgella-nniḥn, syin ṭṭfent abrid ɣer umekkan, ceɛlent-as ticemaɛin, ɣṛant-d lfatiḥa. Azekka-nni, swejdent-d tibaqiyin n seksu, sseččent yal win i d-yerzan. Ula d wid ur d-nruḥ, yewweḍ-asen ɣer yixxamen. Dɛant ɣar sidi Rebbi, ad tili lweɛda-agi d tin yettḥaraben, ad yekkes takawt wa d-yefk lehwa, ad sswent tebḥirin. Yacine Meghzifene
I lmend n wass agraɣlan n tutlayt tayemmat, i d-yettuɣalen di 21 furar n yal aseggas, ddeqs i yellan di ttiɛad i sfuggel-is.
Ama d tiddukkliwin, d tiɣiwanin, neɣ d tuddsiwin yemgaraden, yal yiwet thegga-d ahil beddemma akken ad as-fkent azal i yuklal wass-a ara sfugglen yakk yiɣerfan deg umaḍal. Deg wayen i yeṭṭafaren armuden n usfuggel n wass-a, ihegga-d dɣa Useqqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa ahil n kraḍ n wussan, 20, 21 d 22 furar, deg ugezdu n Tɣerdayt. Deg-s ad ilin ddeqs n warmuden. Deg Uqbu, theyya-d tddukkla Itri Adelsan n Uqbu ahil d amerkanti ɣef teɣzi n kraḍ n wussan. Ad d-nebder seg-s asiwel n tmucuha, isaragen, amezgun akked tmenna n yisefra. Deg temkarḍit tagejdant n Tɣuri n temdin n Tizi Uzzu, thegga-d Tenmehla n yidles ahil d ameqqran, ideg i d-llan kra n yisaragen d tnezzuyin s ubuddu n yimura. Deg-s d asfuggel n wass n tutlayt tayemmat, deg-s d asfuggel n umulli wis 4 n usenṣeb n tamaziɣt. Yettwawi-n wawal ɣef wacu i d-yewwi usenṣeb n tmaziɣt, tutlayt tayemmat, d wacu i d azal n usuqel seg tutlayin tiberraniyin ɣer tutlayt n Teqbayli/Tamaziɣt s umata. Yella-d waya akked Massen Ḥamid Bilek, Ḥasan Ḥelwan d Yusef Merraḥi. Seg wayen i d-yellan di Fransa, ad d-nebder armud i d-thegga tddukkla SFK, mi tenced amaru Fahim Mesɛuden ad d-yeg asarag. Tusa-d ta d tagnit akken ad d-yemmeslay ula ɣef udlis-is amaynut "Iziran n temẓi ", i d-yessuffeɣ ussan-a yezrin kan ɣer teẓrigin Ccix Muḥend Ulḥusin. Ad yemmag usarag-d ass n sed 07 di meɣres -Di Muntryal, tamurt n Kanada, llan deg usihar kra n Yiqbayliyen n dinna, ladɣa wid i d-yezzin i uɣerbaz n teqbaylit-tamaziɣt INAS, i iqeddcen ayendin i usider n tutlayt d uselmed-is i tarwa i d-yettnekkaren dinna. Din dɣa, yettwasuddes-d usarag ɣef userwes gar kra n tutlayin sɣur Mass Lhacmi Twahri. Taɣal-as tejmilt
I lmend n usmekti n wass agraɣlan n tutlayt n tyemmat, i d-yettilin yal ass 21 deg waggur n furar, tesfugel lwilaya n Tizi Uzzu ttiεad-agi akken ilaq lḥal tikkelt-agi. Aṭas n yidisan i d-iheggan ass adelsan i lmend n usmekti-agi. Gar wid I t-id-yessuddsen ad d-nebder Tanmehla n Yidles, Axxam n Yidles n Tizi Uzzu, tasdawit n Tizi Uzzu, Tanmehla n usegmi aɣelnaw, Taṣweḍt n tmaziɣt… atg. Heggan-d yiwen leqdic d anesbaɣur, i d-yellan ass-nni n lexmis, 20 deg furar 2020, deg tzeqqa tameqqrant n Uxxam n yidles Mulud At Mεemmer n Tizi Uzzu. Aseggas-agi, gan-as tajmilt i tmedyazt Bǧurai Djedjiga, i d-yefkan aṭas i tsekla d yidles amaziɣ; icewwiqen, isefra, tibuɣarin…atg. Gar wayen i d-yufraren deg wahil yettwaxedmen aseggas-agi sɣur yimsuddsen-agi, yella-d d anesbaɣur, imi llan-d waṭas n leqdicat idelsanen ɣef teɣzi n wass-nni. Ad d-nebder timsikent i d-heggan waṭas n yiɣerbazen ilemmasen n liwilaya n Tizi Uzzu i ittekkan deg tmeɣra-a. Tella tin n lmakla, tin n yidlisen, tin n wallalen iqburen…atg. Am waken I d-yella usenɛed n usaru "Tallit taqdimt”, syin akkin d tajmilt s timmad-is, anda i tfures tanagit tnemhalt n yidles ad d-awi abruy seg umecwar n tẓuri n Massa Bǧurai d wayen i d-tefka i teqbaylit. Si 10h30 armi d 12h00, d askan n yimuhal d yiremmad n kra n yiɣerbazen ilemmasen n Tizi Uzzu, gar-asen Mulud Ferɛun n Tizi Uzzu, win n Tassadurt, aɣerbaz alemmas Rakem n Tala Amara d uɣerbaz n sin yimeɣrasen Tellal Mǧhamed n Uqawej. Gar wayen i d-sneɛten, ad d-nebder tamezgun, ccnawi, ccḍaḥ d zwağ aqbur n Leqbayel, icewwiqen, tibuɣarin, tamedyazt, timseɛraq…atg. Ɣer taggara maḍi, yella-d usebɣes s yigerdasen i kra n win ittekkan deg leqdic-agi adelsan. M. K. / Gh. A.
Deg tudert n yal ass, ur yeẓṛi yiwen d acu i izemren ad d-yeḍṛu seg teswiεt ɣeṛ tayeḍ. Daymi i yelha uḥader, akken qqaṛen yimezwura "Aḥader yeɣleb aqader”. Γas ma yella amdan yettkukru tuqqsa mi ara yerzu ɣer tezgi, ama d tin n uzrem, neɣ d tin n tɣirdemt, lameεna amahi n tuqqsa-a yella ula deg yixxamen. D ayen i yeḍṛan d yilemẓi K.Wahib seg taddart n At Tεisiwt, taɣiwant n At Smaεel, i yesεan 17 n yiseggasen. Dɣa, am yal ass, seld tuččit n yimensi, yeffeɣ uqcic-a i wakken ad iwanes imeddukkal-is, imi ttnejmaεen yal tameddit ttqeṣṣiren. Lameεna tikkelt-a, ur yerzi ara ɣur-sen, acku yeffeɣ-d kan amnaṛ n tewwurt n uxxam, iḥus i kra i t-ikerrcen seg tefdent-is. Imir-n yecεel Wahib tafat n usawal-is yufa-tt d tiɣerdemt i t-yeqqsen.
Γef leḥsab n teɣbalut-nneɣ , ccil ur iḥus ara Wahib i leqriḥ ameqqṛan imir-n, meḥsub d ayen yezmer ad yeṣbeṛ yiwen, lameεna akken i ttεeddayent temrac i yettḥulfu s uḍaṛ-is ifeccel. D ayen i t-yeǧǧan iger teɣṛi i wat uxxam. Nutni seg tama-nsen refden-t ɣer sbiṭaṛ. Ad d-nesmekti d akken deg ubrid-is yemlelli, yerna yettara Imi yelḥeq ɣer dinna, iḥus i yiman-is yefcel akk. Rnu i waya, yuɣal ur yezmir i leqṛiḥ-nni, yebɣa kan ad yeqmec allen-is ad igen. Ula d aḍaṛ-is yuɣal ur yettḩussu ara yis-s. Kksen-as idammen s tazzla, xedmen-as asiṛum. Imi i d-ffɣen igemmaḍ n yidammen, ttwekkden belli d tuqqsa n tɣirdemt, fkan-as ddwa iwulmen. Yerna ǧǧan-t deg sbiṭaṛ iḍ-nni, armi d azekka-nni, imi iḥulfa i yiman-is yeḥla i t-id-ssufɣen.
Imawlan-is, d yimedukkal-is, umren ayen din imi yeslek. Di taggara ad nekfu s wawal n uletma-s dɣa tenna-aɣ-d: «Ulac d acu isehlen am lmut, ɣas ma yella s tacart, lameεna yelha win yettḥadaren iman-is".
"Leḥder yugar leqḍeɛ”. D inzi-a n at zik i d-yeggran ad t-sxedmen yimdanen, akken ad ḥadren iman-nsen mgal aṭṭan amihan cǧḍid-19, i d-yeččan amaḍal ussan-a. Imi urɛad i as-d-ufan yimussnawen d yimnadiyen n tujjya asafar n uḥbas-ines. Anfafad n Cǧrǧna, yebda-d taggara n waggur n duǧember 2019, deg tmurt n Ccinwa, syin yeḥrured ɣer tmura-nniḍen, armi yelseq ass-a deg 113 n tmura, ɣef leḥsab i d-tmud tuddsa tamaḍlant n tdawsa. Dɣa iberreḥ-d unemhal amatu n Tuddsa ass-nni n amhad s uṣennef n waṭṭan-agi d aṭṭan amaḍlan amihan, ma nwala simmal yettnernay, qrib ad yaɣ akk amaḍal. Yewwi-d ɣef tmura ad ḥerzent s uḥader iwulmen, ma d imdanen ad ḍefren tarrayin ilaqen n usizdeg.
Ar tura, banent-d deg umaḍal azal n 124 101 n liḥalat, yenɣa 4 566 n yimdanen. D tamurt n Ccinwa ideg i d-yebda i yeṭṭef s waṭas, s 80 787 liḥalat, mmuten 3 151, jjin 61 -Deg Lurutt, ufan-d 22 307 liḥalat, mmuten gar-asen 930 d amdan. D tamurt n Ṭṭelyan i yenṭerren s waṭas mbeɛd Ccinwa, s 12 462 liḥalat, mmuten gar-asen 827 yimuḍan. Syin d tamurt n Iran, s 9 000 imuḍan, mmuten 354 deg-sen. Teṭṭafar-itt-id Kurya n wadda, s 7 577 liḥalat d 60 n yimettanen. Tamurt n Listtan, s 2 128 liḥalat d 47 n yimettanen. Timura n Albanie, SuAde, Irlande, Belgique, Panama d Bulgarie, banent-d liḥalat timezwura n wid yemmuten taggara n ddurt-agi kan.
Ma d timura n Hundǧras, Bǧuliḍie, Cṛte d’iḍǧire d Turquie, banent-d liḥalat n waṭṭan timezwura. Deg tmurt n Fransa, yuli umḍan n wid yemmuten ɣer 48, gar 2 281 n wid yeṭṭef unfafad n cǧḍid--Deg Lezzayer, ar wass n amhad, 26 n yimdanen i yekcem waṭṭan, 2 n yirgazen i yemmuten. Ɣef waya i d-yettili leḥder meqqren s umdal n yiɣerbazen d tesdawiyin, inurar n ddabex, d yidgan ideg d-ttemlilin s waṭas yimdanen. Deg Tizi Uzzu, ar yiḍelli, banen-d 3 n yimuḍan i t-ihelken. Ha-ten-in deg sbiter CHU Nedir Med n temdint-a. Kh. A.
Asenfar n useggem d tduli n wannaren, yeffeɣ-d i waṭas n tɣiwanin tallit-a taneggarut, gar-asent taɣiwant n Yiderginen i d-yezgan s tebɛed n wazal n 45 n yikilumitren ɣer Usamar n Bgayet. Dɣa, seld kra n uɛeṭṭel i icudden abeɛda ɣer lexsas n tedrimt, qrib yekfa usenfar s timmad, n tduli n unnar agejdan, imi temmug yakan tduli. ’Tura akka, nezmer ad d-nini amur ameqqran n lecɣal yemmug meskud qqimen-d kan sin. Yettusemma, tura mi nessa taduli i unnar, yeqqim-d kan usbedd n yijqa n tafat akked cwiṭ n ureqqeɛ daxel n unnar ", i aɣ-d-yenna yiwen seg yimḍebbren n tɣiwant n Yiderginen. Yewwi-d ad d-nini xussen ayendin yimeḍqan d tzeɣwa ideg zemren ad d-sbeyyinen tizemmar-nsen yilemẓiyen n tɣiwant-a n Yiderginen, ama d ayen yerzan ɣer uḥric n waddal, isilaɣ, ɣer yidles d yiḥricen-nniḍen. Ɣef waya areqqeɛ n unnar-nsen aɣiwan i d-yezgan di tlemmast n Yiderginen, ad ten-yeǧǧ xersum ad ssemrasen addal n ddabex n uḍar s wugar n rraḥa d tɣellist. Tugart-tugart ma neẓra belli deg wayaqeddac, llan ur ttheyyin s waṭas tiberziwin tǧurnǧis acku ur sɛin annar iwulmen, neɣ ma heyyan-d ad d-heyyin anda-nniḍen. « Aṭas-aya nettraǧu annar-nneɣ deg waddad igerrzen am wa. Tura yella wamek ara nesṭuqqut seg warmuden inaddalen. D ayen iseg ara d-sfaydin ama d arrac imecṭaḥ neɣ d ilemẓiyen ", i d-yenna yiwen seg Yiderginen. Ad d-nesmekti d akken yeffeɣ-d usenfar-a i tɣiwant n Yiderginen s yidrimen n wayen iwumi qqaren FCCL. Yekker-d s wazal n 43 n yimelyan n dinar, neɣ ugar n 04 n yimelyaren n santim. Deg-s, gar cwiṭ n waṭas, taduli n unnar s ugazun, abnaw n ufrag d tseddarin, asbedd n unagraw n ujmaɛ n waman n ugeffur, asbedd n tafat d ubnaw n texxamin n usteɛfu d ucuccef.M. K.
Yeffeɣ yisalli ussan yezrin ɣef tukerḍiwin i d-yettilin deg ssuq n Xeṛṛata, imi aṭaṣ n medden i yettwakren: Wagi yetwaker-as usawal, wayeḍ d idrimen, ula d tullas dɣa, ur slikent ara.
Tamsalt-a, tesnerna-d aṭaṣ n tuggdi deg wulawen n yimezdaɣ, daymi i sxebṛen iɣallen n laman i wakken ad ḥeṛsen taεessast di ssuq-a, i d-yeḍḥan d amahi ɣef wid i d-irezzun ɣer dinna, ama seg tɣiwanin n tdayṛa n Xeṛṛata, ama seg tid-nniḍen am At Smaεel, akked Tṣexṛiwt. Ccil ulac wid ur nesli ara s tukerḍiwin-a. Imakaren ur ugaden ara, d anemgal, kemmlen di lecɣal-nsen.
Dɣa ddurt yezrin, yessawel yiwen n umɣar i yiqeddacen n yiɣallen n laman, acku yella win i as-yukren ugar n umelyun. Yerna amakar-a, yekkes-asen-t-id seg lǧib-is srid, ifaṛeṣ tagnit imi d amɣar ur yezmir ad yazzel deffir-s. Lameεna, tumert n ubandi-a ur tdum ara bezzaf, imi seld tanaga n umɣaṛ-a, i yeṣṣawḍen yefka tiweṣṣaf n umdan i t-yukren i yittulisen, ineggura-a uzzlen i uḥeffu fell-as. Di taggara ufan-t, imir-n i yebɣa ad d-yeffeɣ seg ssuq ad yerwel.
Ad d-nesmekti d akken, ula d imezdaɣ xedmen ayen ilaqen, s umecṭuḥ s umeqqṛan. Asaru-a, yekfa s tumert, imi amakar-a d win i yesεan abrid ixemjen, yerna mačči di Xeṛṛata i yezdeɣ, meεna di temdint n Bgayet. Lḥaṣul, iεedda di ccṛaε di teɣdemt n Xeṛṛata, anda i yeḥkem fell-as uselway-is s sin n yiseggasen d lḥebs, akkeḍ sin n yimelyan d idrimen.K. K.
Iberreḥ-d ass-nni n lḥed di Lezzayer tamaneɣt, uneɣlaf n Usegmi aɣelnaw, Abdelhakim Belabed belli atug n urbaḥ deg ukayad n n taggara n ulmud n uɣerbaz amenzu yewweḍ ɣer 83,31%, deg wakal n tmurt. Yerna yenna-d, agemmuḍ-agi, d ayen yettwaqbalen.
Deg yiwen n usarag n tɣamsa, i iga i lmend n beddu n yikayaden n Lbak, isegza-d uneɣlaf belli agemmuḍ-agi yewweḍ ɣer 94,90% deg 48 n lwilayat, mi ara d-nseddu atug n uɛeddi atug n rrbeḥ deg yikayaden rnu-as talemmast n uktazal imezgi. Ad nesmekti kan belli -655 n yinelmaden i yeqqaren deg 18 000 n yiɣerbazen imenza yellan di tmurt. Ddeqs daɣen n yiɣerbazen i d-yewwin agemmuḍ n 100%.
Tizi Uzzu deg umḍiq amezwaru i tikkelt tis 11
Ass-nni n lḥed yezrin, mi i d-banen yigemmaḍ n ukayad n taggara n uswir amenzu n useggas aɣurbiz 2018-2019, yeḍḥa-d belli d lwilaya n Tizi Uzzu i d-yufraren i tikkelt tis 11, ta deffir ta.
Imi seg useggas n 2008, d nettat i yettaṭṭafen taqacut n umyezwar deg yigemmaḍ n tlata n yikayaden n taggara n useggas, gar-asen akayad-agi n 5e. Deg wayen yerzan igemmaḍ n lwilaya n Tizi Uzzu, Ɛlaḥsab n unemhal n usegmi-ines, azal n 17 865 i ijerden iman-nsen deg umuɣen n usεeddi n ukayad-a, yerna sεeddan-t akk. Leḥsab n wid i t-id-yewwin yelḥaq 16 879, s lqidar n 91, 11%, ma yella s wid iɛeddan s asuffeɣ ttassage yewweḍ ɣer 96,64%.
Azal n 222 n yiɣerbazen imenza, ɣef 624 n yiɣerbazen, i d-iḥellan 100% deg ukayad-agi, s lqidar n 35,56%. Azal daɣen n 30 n yinelmaden i d-yewwin tazmilt n 10/10 deg ukayad-agi, ma 24 n yinelmaden i d-yewwin tazmilt n 9,9 d wugar n 851 n yimsizewren sɛan ugar n 9,-Ma deg umyezwar n lwilayt deg yigemmaḍ n ukayad-agi, i tikkelt tis 11 d lwilaya n Tizi Uzzu, i d-yettifriren deg umḍiq amezwaru. Ad d-nesmekti kan, belli inelmaden-agi i yesɛan tazmilt n 5/10 neɣ ugar neɣ wid iɛeddan s usuffeɣ ad ruḥen deg wussan-agi ad jerden iman-nsen deg useggas amezwaru deg uɣerbaz alemmas. Ma deg wayen yerzan igemmaḍ n ukayad n BEM, yetturaǧu ad bannen ass, 01 yulyu 2019, ma d wid n BAC ad ilin ass n, 20 yulyu i d-iteddun.Adaǧun Abdelghani
Am wass yecban iḍelli, 15 deg meɣres, i yettwanɣa Mǧulǧud Feraǧun deg Lezzayer tamanaɣt sɣur tuddsa ǦAS, netta akked xemsa-nniḍen n yixeddamen. I lmend n usmekti wis 58 n tmenɣiwt-is, ihi, thegga-d tddukkli, yewwin isem-is, yiwen wahil d anesbaɣur deg taddart n umaru, Tizi Hibel, taɣiwant n At Meḥmud deg lɛerc n At Dwala.
